## 7TH-01 对角线中 / The Secret of the Diagonal

**37**：……妈妈，我不明白。\
**37**: Mama, I have a question.

**37**：为什么大家都讨厌“无理数”？\
**37**: Why don't people like the "irrational numbers"?

站在沙滩上的女性回过身来，望向年幼的女孩儿。\
The woman turns around, gazing her daughter with warm affection.

**77**：嗯……你也讨厌无理数吗，37？\
**77**: Mmm, do you feel the same about them, 37?

**37**：有一点儿……\
**37**: Mmm, maybe a little?

37低下头，踢走了脚下一块不规则的石子。\
37 looks down and kicks away a pebble.

**37**：我可以数出3，我可以数出17，但是我永远无法数出0.01001000100001……更不用说拿它计算了。\
**37**: You see, Mama. I can count to 3, and to 17, but I can never count to something like 0.01001000100001, let alone use it in calculations.

**37**：这些无限不循环小数会让结果变得一团糟，整个式子的简洁和优雅都会被毁掉，我不喜欢它们。\
**37**: The endless, non-repeating decimals would make a mess of the results, and I can't keep the equations as simple and elegant as I want.

**77**：——但你最爱的图形圆，它的周长与直径之比也是个无理数，不是吗？\
**77**: But your favorite, the circle—the ratio of its circumference to diameter is also an irrational number, is it not?

**37**：不，π是特殊的，我知道它是如何得来的，知道它代表的含义，我也能把它加入到计算中来。还有e，lg2，√2……\
**37**: π is special. I know how it was found and what it represents, so I trust it and use it in my calculations. The same with e, log2, and √2.

**37**：可是，只有很少的无理数能像这样。\
**37**: But not many irrational numbers are this convenient to work with.

**37**：那些完全无规律的、无法化简的、无限延伸的数字，我写不下它们，数不出它们，无法计算它们。\
**37**: Some have no patterns, no simplest forms, and no end. I can't work out their digits, write them out, or calculate them.

**37**：它们只是古怪地盘踞于数轴上，像神话里不可被神杀死的蛇足巨人癸干忒斯。\
**37**: Not only are they impossible to pinpoint on the number axis, but there's an infinite amount of these irrational numbers!

**77**：……哈哈。\
**77**: Haha.

**37**：……妈妈，你为什么要笑？\
**37**: What's so funny, Mama?

**77**：笑你这么聪明，又这么笨，我的女儿。\
**77**: You're a clever, silly goose, my dear.

**77**：你只是还不够了解它们——而不是讨厌它们。\
**77**: You don't dislike them. You just don't understand them enough.

那位修长的女性俯下身，拾起沙滩上的一根被海潮泡软的树枝。\
Leaning down, she picks up a soggy twig.

柔软的树枝划过由沙子构成的集合。\
Her hand moves, sliding the tip of the twig across the sand.

四条等长的边，两条交错的对角线。\
Four equal perpendicular lines are drawn, with two more diagonal lines intersecting in the middle.

一个规整的方形。\
It is the shape of the familiar square.

**77**：来看看我们熟悉的老朋友吧。\
**77**: Take our old friend √2 for instance.

**77**：√2，一个无理数，是纯粹算术上可得的结论，它等价于“在a和b都是整数的情况下，2不可能被表达成（a/b)²的形式。”\
**77**: The irrationality of this number can be proven through basic arithmetic, as it cannot be expressed as an irreducible fraction of integers a/b ...

**77**：我们不需要任何关于无理数的知识，就可以使用归谬法证明这一点。\
**77**: A simple proof by contradiction is enough, with no knowledge of irrational numbers required.

**77**：然而，我们却可以轻易地在正方形的对角线上看到这个不可数的数字。这意味着——\
**77**: The presence of √2 is prevalent in nature, and it is particularly noticeable along the diagonals of a square. This means—

**37**：——我知道！\
**37**: Oh, I know!

**37**：这意味着，毕达哥拉斯以整数比为基石构建的数论是不牢靠的！\
**37**: This means the system built solely on the ratio of integers was flawed!

**77**：是的。这是一个简明、优美的定理，也是古代数学最好的成就之一。许多数正是不可通约的，而√2只是其中最显眼的一个。\
**77**: Yes. √2 is simple, elegant, and one of the greatest discoveries in mathematics. It showed the existence of infinite incommensurable numbers, with √2 being the most obvious one to find.

**77**：它的发现摧毁了由整数比搭建的古典王国，也催生了使数学分析转向现代的突破性革命，揭开了更深邃的新一页。\
**77**: This was how the tower of old ideas crumbled, paving the way for revolutionary breakthroughs that catapulted mathematical analysis into uncharted frontiers.

**77**：它向我们证明了，在我们脚下除去由尺规丈量的坚实大地之外，还有一个捉摸不透的神秘王国。它不可度量，不可通约，不可穷尽。\
**77**: We discovered a kingdom beyond our traditional methods—one that is immeasurable, incommensurable, and inexhaustible.

**77**：——而开启这个王国的钥匙，就光明正大地潜藏在正方形的对角线中。\
**77**: And the key to its gates is hidden in plain sight—in the diagonal of a square.

**37**：无……理的王国？\
**37**: A kingdom of irrationality?

女孩入迷地点点头，一如既往，她理解得很迅速。\
The girl listens intently. As always, she understands quickly.

**37**：我明白了，妈妈，永远都有超出我们认知之外的数字……这就是无理数的意义。\
**37**: I see now, Mama. We are not all-knowing beings. There will always be numbers beyond our awareness. Such is the nature of irrational numbers.

**37**：所以……只要增进对它的了解，我们也一定能和无理数成为朋友！\
**37**: So, if we get to know the irrational numbers better, we can be friends with them, too!

**37**：——可是，你还没有回答我，岛上的人们为什么都讨厌它？\
**37**: But, you haven't told me why people on the island hate them.

**77**：……\
**77**: ...

她看不清母亲的面容。\
The image of her mother's face fractures.

只是记得回忆的最后，她嘴角的弧度柔和，神情平静——近乎怜悯。\
But her smile is clear—gentle, quiet, and almost ... pitying.

**37**：……妈妈？\
**37**: Mama?

特效-一个破碎的特效，复用1.3的幻境破碎，代指梦境结束。

**苏菲亚**：——！\
**Sophia**: ...!

**苏菲亚**：37……你醒来了？\
**Sophia**: 37, you're awake!

床榻上的女孩突然坐了起来，双眼直直地向空气中望去。\
The girl sits upright in bed, her eyes staring into the air in dismay.

**37**：……\
**37**: ...

**37**：现在是什么时间，苏菲亚？\
**37**: Sophia, how long was I out?

**苏菲亚**：你昏迷了一个星期，这段时间……\
**Sophia**: You've been in a coma for a week. We ...

仓促的布料摩挲声

友人的话语被打断了。37仓促地掀开被子，向挂着布帘的门洞跑去。\
Her words are cut off as 37 jumps off the bed, rushing her way out.

**苏菲亚**：等一下，37，你还没有完全康复——！\
**Sophia**: No, stop! You're not well yet!

**37**：不，已经没有时间了！\
**37**: There's no time!

**37**：我得去找6……我得快一点，快点去告诉大家——\
**37**: I have to find 6. I have to tell them now—

**37**：——我们的“圆”破碎了。\
**37**: Our "circle" has been broken.

## 7TH-02 蓝与灰 / The Blue and the Grey

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：一切如常……吗？\
**Vertin**: Nothing's happening?

真理的殿堂与往日无异。\
The Hall of Truth is as crowded as ever.

仍挤满了太多的争辩，太多的嘈杂，太多的异见。\
Ideas, noises, and arguments are all crammed into one space.

**？？？**：——维尔汀小姐，请您专心一些！\
**???**: Ms. Vertin, your attention, please!

**？？？**：这次问询事关您和您同伴的命运，您应当清楚。\
**???**: This is a public inquiry, and your answer determines the fate of you and your friends.

**？？？**：我们将就一周前的坐标泄露事件，对贵方及重塑之手所造成的危害予以集体表决。\
**???**: There will be a vote on your punishment, considering the leak of the island's coordinates and the damages caused by you and Manus Vindictae.

**？？？**：而您在过去两个小时里查看了十次手腕上的计时器——请恕我直言，还有什么，比即将落下的判决更加重要？\
**???**: Yet, in the past two hours, you've looked at your watch ten times. Forgive me for being blunt. What could possibly bother you more than your sentence?

**维尔汀**：……抱歉。\
**Vertin**: My apologies.

台下响起了轻微的咋舌声。\
A mocking click of the tongue can be heard from the crowd.

**210**：你该让她看的，888。很显然，时间的刻度也是一类数字。\
**210**: Let her look, 888. Doesn't it occur to you that time is also in the form of numbers?

**210**：——也许她只是在等待自己的幸运数降临呢？\
**210**: Perhaps she's waiting for her lucky number to come.

210的发言引起了一阵窃笑。\
His words cause a ripple of chuckles throughout the hall.

人们在此刻正需要这样轻松的调剂，如同弦不能一直被紧绷着。\
Clearly, after hours of debate and discussion, this lighthearted moment brings a much-needed sense of relief.

**210**：而且，我们又得出了什么重要的结论呢？\
**210**: Besides, what conclusions have the good people here made?

**210**：过去一周发生的种种摩擦，使我们不得不聚集在这里，讨论着这些话题：在圣地暴毙的重塑门徒、被阻断的戈尔贡洋流、进犯岛屿的人类军队。\
**210**: We were brought together in this great hall today, for misfortunes have struck us in the past week: Manus followers were found dead in our sacred place, the Gorgon Current was cut off, and a human army has invaded our land.

**210**：还有随之而来的国际领土的纠纷，外部政体的威胁，岛上访客的冲突。\
**210**: There were also the territorial disputes, the threats from external powers, and the conflicts between our guests.

**210**：很显然，这些客人给我们带来了超乎想象的“礼物”。\
**210**: As you can see, our guests have brought us quite the unexpected "gifts."

**210**：那么，我们究竟该信任谁的说辞——是基金会，还是重塑之手？\
**210**: They will give us their explanations. But whose words should we trust—those of the Foundation, or Manus Vindictae?

辩论家半鞠一躬，将手引向高台左侧。\
He bows slightly, gesturing to the left of the stage.

**维尔汀**：……我愿在真理之石前立誓，我对这一次的泄露事件毫不知情。\
**Vertin**: I swear on the Stone of Truth that I have no knowledge of the leak.

**维尔汀**：我们从未将任何信息泄露给人类的军队，圣洛夫基金会也正在外界积极调停领土纠纷。\
**Vertin**: We never gave any information to the humans. As we speak, the St. Pavlov Foundation is taking measures to mediate the territorial disputes from outside the island.

**888**：但你将这里的情况如实汇报给了基金会。\
**888**: But you did report everything here to the Foundation.

**888**：此后信息的去向，您并不知情，对吗？\
**888**: And you don't know what they did with the information, do you?

**维尔汀**：……是的。\
**Vertin**: Right.

**210**：——我们有什么理由不怀疑她们呢？谁都知道，基金会是一个亲近人类的组织！\
**210**: A questionable defense, a doubtful explanation. Why should we trust her? We all know that the Foundation is closely associated with the humans.

**210**：监守自盗，自导自演，毫无敬畏，蔑视誓言……世俗的王冠数易其主，唯有人类的恶行始终如一。\
**210**: They are the false friends of the arcanists, with their crocodile tears and broken vows. While many may have changed over time, their nefarious human taint lingers.

**210**：而且，我们为什么要向一个落后于我们7年的组织，寻求对抗“流溢”的知识与经验呢？\
**210**: Besides, why should we seek collaboration and assistance from an organization that's seven years behind us on the study of the "Emanation"?

教众们在熙攘声中骚动了起来。\
His words evoke a murmur of agreement.

**210**：可是兄弟们、姐妹们，别急着掷出你手上涂着灰白格子的卵石。再看看我们的老朋友，重塑之手吧。\
**210**: But rush not, brothers and sisters! The moment of decision has not yet arrived. Let's give our old friend Manus Vindictae a fair and equal hearing before casting our pebbles into the pot.

报幕者伸出右手，引向高台的另一侧。\
He stretches out his right hand, directing the audience's attention across the stage.

那里端坐着一抹蓝黑相间的身影。\
On the right, there sits a quiet figure in black and blue.

**阿尔卡纳**：……\
**Arcana**: ...

**210**：诚然，基金会对“流溢”的认知落后我们7年。\
**210**: Indeed, the Foundation's understanding of the "Emanation" is seven years behind ours.

**210**：可重塑之手的访客不要说数学素养了，连基本的语言能力都没有。\
**210**: However, our Manus friends here are unable to speak at all, let alone understand complex mathematical principles.

**210**：——请问阿尔卡纳小姐，您要如何解释，您的门徒成批暴毙于我们的圣地入口？\
**210**: Please enlighten us, Ms. Arcana. Why were swaths of your followers found dead at the door of our sacred place?

**210**：难道是我们的数学课程终于叫他们发了疯，非得像那些殉道者一样，一头撞死在真理的门前？\
**210**: Did our math lessons drive them to madness, causing them to bash their heads against the gate of Truth like martyrs?

**阿尔卡纳**：——正是如此。\
**Arcana**: So it would seem.

**教众Ⅱ**：……什么？\
**Believer II**: What?

断言的干脆足以令信仰者们诧异。\
Her quick and straight answer causes a commotion in the crowd.

而岛外的来客只是轻轻合上了手里的书本。\
Yet she only gently closes the book on her lap, uncaring of the suspicious stares around her.

**阿尔卡纳**：诚然，我们的追随者缺乏一些知识的传承……\
**Arcana**: One must confess that our followers were ill-prepared to take on the wisdom of the island.

**阿尔卡纳**：但我们与贵学派合作的诚意是毋庸置疑的。\
**Arcana**: But we didst come seek mutual development with sincerity.

**阿尔卡纳**：对诸位所鄙夷但仍需依存的现象世界领域，我们也予以了不吝的物质资助。\
**Arcana**: I trust you are aware of the assistance we have provided o'er the years in this World of Matters, which you, though reluctantly, relied upon.

**阿尔卡纳**：至于这场论辩——\
**Arcana**: As to this debate,

**阿尔卡纳**：我恰好听过一个应景的故事，也许能与诸位分享。\
**Arcana**: I was once told a story that now seems fitting to recount.

她的目光望向高台。\
Her gaze falls on the bench.

金发的法官端坐其上，争辩开始以来，他还未置一词。\
The fair-haired judge has not spoken a word since the debate began.

**6**：……请说。\
**6**: Pray, share with us.

**阿尔卡纳**：感谢您慷慨的容许。\
**Arcana**: Thank you kindly.

**阿尔卡纳**：这是一个关于“圆”的古老传说。拜访此地之前，一位年轻的艺术家曾将它分享于我。\
**Arcana**: 'Tis the story of the "circle." A young artist told it to me before I arrived on this island.

**阿尔卡纳**：在远古时期，第一个有智慧的心灵从蒙昧中苏醒。\
**Arcana**: In the ancient past, amid a world of primitive instincts and ignorance, the first intelligent mind awaken'd.

**阿尔卡纳**：它对这世界感到恐惧，意外自然远比它强大。在自然之中，它的自我渺小得难以感知。\
**Arcana**: Overwhelmed by the enormity of nature and dismayed by its own insignificance, the creature was shaken to its core.

**阿尔卡纳**：为了表达这种违抗的决心，它便在自己周围画上一个魔力圈，以此来将自己与外界区隔开来。\
**Arcana**: In an act of defiance, it drew a magick circle, shielding its powerless self from the formidable world beyond.

**阿尔卡纳**：最原始的巫术诞生了，造物开始以内在的灵性来反抗外界现象的压力。\
**Arcana**: This was the first magick, when the primitive man mastered the pneuma within and wielded it against the relentless forces of nature.

**阿尔卡纳**：在抗争的过程中，造物更清楚地认识到了自身的边界。\
**Arcana**: In that process, man hath gained a deeper understanding of the boundaries and limitations of its power.

**阿尔卡纳**：这就是最初的“圆”。\
**Arcana**: This is the tale of the first "circle."

**阿尔卡纳**：它庇护了我们。一如今日，诸位仍享受着它的恩泽。\
**Arcana**: The "circle" shielded us, and its protection benefits thee to this day.

**阿尔卡纳**：而我感到有趣的是，在这个故事里——\
**Arcana**: What I find intriguing in this story:

**阿尔卡纳**：人自身的存在、界限和证明，都仰赖于这个圆而确立。\
**Arcana**: Man hath established its existence, recognized its boundaries, and learned the purpose of life, all by relying upon this very circle.

“——砰！”\
Bang!

厅堂的门被撞开了，一个气喘吁吁的虚弱身影靠在了门框上。\
The hall gate bursts open. The intruder with a small figure leans weakly against the doorframe.

**37**：呼，呼……\
**37**: *panting*

**维尔汀**：——37？\
**Vertin**: 37?

近一半的信仰者们站了起来，望向这位许久未见的质数。\
All eyes are fixed on the young girl; some have even risen to their feet in surprise.

其中包括那位高堂之上的领袖。\
The leader on the bench breaks the silence.

**6**：37，发生什么事了？\
**6**: What's wrong, 37?

**37**：岛……\
**37**: The island ...

她苍白的嘴唇嗫喏着，终于吐出了第一个音节。\
Her pale lips tremble, struggling to get the words out.

**37**：我们的岛……生病了。\
**37**: Our island has fallen ill.

一阵鸦默雀静。仿佛这兀自闯入的话题与小岛并无干系。\
Even the slightest sound is gone. An eerie silence descends upon the hall.

“——砰！”\
Thud!

沉闷的异响，比撞门声来得更响亮，更近。\
Another dull, muffled thump, as if something's struck a hard surface.

现在，另一半的信仰者们也站了起来。他们困惑地望向声音的来源——头上的穹顶。\
But it's enough to get the rest of the crowd to their feet. They look up at the roof—the thud came from up there.

“——砰、砰砰砰砰！”\
Thud, thud thud thud!

撞击声应和着他们的疑问。\
More thumps follow.

就像一名不得章法的鼓手，正在天球形状的穹顶上狂乱地敲击。\
It's as if the hall has turned into a drum, with an out-of-control drummer playing frantically on the dome.

**教众Ⅳ**：见鬼，这里到底发生什么事了？！\
**Believer IV**: Argh, what is going on?!

**教众Ⅳ**：外面是下冰雹了吗？\
**Believer IV**: Is that a hailstorm?

**苏菲亚**：不，我想——并不是……\
**Sophia**: No, I don't think so.

没有数字的除错师在大厅外张望，担忧却不敢跟上友人的脚步。\
Standing outside the gate, the numberless Corrector looks up at the sky.

她站得更远，望得更清，也因此目睹了事情的全貌。\
Being barred from entering the hall, she can see better from where she stands.

**苏菲亚**：好像，是阿其翁……\
**Sophia**: Those are Abraxases,

**苏菲亚**：它们……从空中摔下来了？\
**Sophia**: falling from the sky.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

抬起手腕，确认表带——几乎是下意识的动作。\
Another look at the watch—it's become something of a habit over the last few hours.

是的，这就是那个她一直等待着的、最重要的时刻。\
This is it. The long-anticipated moment has finally arrived.

**维尔汀**：……是“暴雨”。\
**Vertin**: It's the "Storm."

**维尔汀**：这个时代的“暴雨”……到来了。\
**Vertin**: The "Storm" of this era is here.

## 7TH-03 石钟之下 / Bring the Gavel Down

**教众Ⅱ**：维尔汀小姐，您是说“流溢”发生了……？\
**Believer II**: Ms. Vertin, did you just say the "Emanation" has happened?

**教众Ⅱ**：在这个时间？\
**Believer II**: Just now?

**维尔汀**：……准确来说，是24小时倒计时开始了。\
**Vertin**: More precisely, its 24-hour countdown has begun.

**维尔汀**：每个时代的“暴雨”正式落下前，有一段缓冲期。暴雨症候将从临界点逐渐扩散至全球，具体症状和程度暂未发现规律。\
**Vertin**: There's always a buffer period before the "Storm," during which the Storm Syndrome gradually spreads from the Critical Point across the globe. The symptoms are different every time, and we have yet to discern a pattern.

**维尔汀**：在拉普拉斯科算中心的协助下，我们可以提前24小时预告“暴雨”将至。\
**Vertin**: With the help of Laplace Scientific Computing Center, the best we can do now is to send a 24-hour warning prior to the "Storm."

**维尔汀**：……又一分钟过去了。\
**Vertin**: Another minute has passed.

厅堂被素色袍子们怀疑的讨论声填满。\
The hall is once again filled with the whispers of the white robes.

对于一座以观测“流溢”为使命的小岛而言，目前的状况超出了他们的预想。\
On this island dedicated solely to the study of the "Emanation," the situation has far surpassed their imaginations.

**888**：——请诸位不要离开座位，表决尚未结束！\
**888**: Please remain seated, everyone. We are still in the middle of a vote!

**888**：这座岛屿并不会受“流溢”影响。我们应当继续先前的议题，得到结论后，再转向新的领域。\
**888**: The "Emanation" holds no influence on this island. The discussion must continue until a satisfactory conclusion is reached. No other subjects shall be brought up until then.

集会的协理人抬高了声音，盖住了喧嚣的一隅。\
The banshee, acting as Custodian of the assembly, raises her voice, drowning out the arguments.

这是她职责所在——让表决顺利进行。\
Despite the unforeseen turn of events, she remains committed to her duty—the debate must go on.

**888**：37——你先到这儿来。有人能给她拿个毯子吗？\
**888**: Come here, 37. Can someone please bring her a blanket?

顾及那抹虚弱的身影，她将声音放得很低。\
Her voice softens as she looks at the frail, slender girl in front of her.

**888**：42，你去和苏菲亚看看那些阿其翁的情况。\
**888**: 42, go with Sophia and check on those Abraxases.

**教众Ⅰ**：……\
**Believer I**: ...

被念及数字的男性教众鞠了一躬，快步跑出去。\
The man bows and leaves.

穹顶又恢复了它的秩序。\
Order is restored under the dome once more.

**210**：噢，这实际上是个好消息。\
**210**: Ah, good news, good news indeed!

**210**：——我们不用再表决了，不是吗？\
**210**: We are freed from the pain of choosing whom to blame, are we not?

**888**：——什么？\
**888**: What?

修辞学家抬起手，笑容可谓清爽。\
The rhetorician raises a hand with a triumphant smile.

一如既往，他带来一个创新的议题，或者又一次哗众取宠的尝试。\
As usual, he's offering a new perspective, or what some might call another attempt at stirring up the crowd.

**210**：“流溢”就要到来了，灵性的潮水将涌流、倾泻、漫过一切。\
**210**: The "Emanation" is coming. The tides of pneuma will pour from above and wash away all trivialities.

**210**：届时，无论是外部世界的人类军队，还是历史空间上的某个政权，以及他们带来的无尽纷扰。\
**210**: By then, human intruders and the international powers of this era, along with the turmoil they brought,

**210**：——所有令人不快的一切，都会化为地面上的油污，被整齐地冲入沟渠。\
**210**: will all be dissolved and poured into the ditches like gunk.

**210**：而我们也终将放下这些无尽的琐碎，重新回到对“本质”的研究中。\
**210**: And we will regain our shores and return to the study of essence and Forms.

沉默。\
His words are met with silence.

沉默源于思辨——对这些抛却现象世界的人们而言，210的话语是有道理的。\
The crowd is lost in thought. Having long detached themselves from the phenomenal world, 210's words are striking a chord.

**37**：不，这次不一样！\
**37**: No, it's different this time!

而后，一个娇小的身影站了起来。\
The petite figure stands on her feet.

37没有披上那条毯子，她尚未康复的脸色也依然苍白。\
She is pale as snow from her coma, and did not bother to put on the blanket given to her.

**37**：——这座岛生病了！\
**37**: The island has fallen ill!

**37**：它正变得臃肿、滞重、迟钝，向下坠落到无明的现象世界中。\
**37**: It's getting bloated, stagnant, and sluggish, drifting into the World of Matters where ignorance reigns.

**37**：很快，灵性的潮水就会漫过我们——正如漫过现象世界的每片碎屑。\
**37**: Soon, the tides of pneuma will wash over us, sweeping away the fragments of the phenomenal world.

**教众Ⅳ**：——什么？！\
**Believer IV**: What did you say?!

**教众Ⅳ**：也就是说，我们所有人都会被“流溢”带走？这——\
**Believer IV**: In other words, we will all be taken by the "Emanation"? This ...

**教众Ⅴ**：这太荒谬了……！\
**Believer V**: This is unthinkable!

这不是一个好消息。\
This is terrible news, one that nobody wants to hear right now.

这是一枚炸弹，意想不到的——侵入了这个圆形的厅堂。\
The impact is like a bomb going off, the crowd is buzzing with fearful whispers.

37旁边的年长女性站了起来，怀中还抱着那条不曾派上用场的毯子。\
The lady next to 37 stands up, still holding the unused blanket.

**教众Ⅱ**：……37，你才刚刚醒来，身体还很虚弱。\
**Believer II**: 37, you just woke up from a coma. You're not well.

**教众Ⅱ**：你需要再休息一会吗？\
**Believer II**: Why don't you take another rest?

**37**：不，不，我不需要休息。我到这儿来，就是为了说这件事。\
**37**: No, no time for that. I'm here to warn you.

**37**：我感知不到无限定者的气息了，以前从来没有发生过这种事！\
**37**: Apeiron is gone. I can no longer sense It. This has never happened before!

**888**：——为什么你这么惊讶，37？\
**888**: Why are you so surprised, 37?

平静的疑问，并不带任何额外的情绪。\
The question is asked softly, but it cuts like ice.

**888**：我以为你知道原因。\
**888**: You should know the reason of Its alienation.

**888**：毕竟，是你擅自把外人带入了圣地。你违背了教典的训诫，激怒了无限定者。\
**888**: You brought outsiders to the sacred place. You betrayed the Scriptures' teachings and angered Apeiron!

**37**：——！\
**37**: ...!

**888**：当然，这是一个武断的推论。——重塑之手同样未经允许侵入了圣地。\
**888**: Of course, I may have jumped to this accusation, as Manus Vindictae also intruded our sacred place without permission.

**888**：我们也没有任何岛屿将被“流溢”淹没的证据，37的举证并不完备。\
**888**: People! As of now, there's no proof that the "Emanation" will influence the island. 37's account is lacking.

**888**：由此，诸位应该意识到，过去的事件依然疑点重重，且对学派造成了不可挽回的损失。\
**888**: And we are still plagued by suspicions, accusations, and the damages done to our home.

**888**：眼下我们应当继续讯问，然后做出如何对待基金会和重塑之手的访客的表决——\
**888**: We are to proceed with the hearing and reach a final verdict on both the Foundation and Manus Vindictae.

将集会带回正轨的努力失败了——近一半教众突然将目光移向门口。\
The attempt to refocus the assembly fails as half the audience turns their attention to the gate.

在那里，先前离开的使者去而复返，正不知所措地踟躇着。\
Sophia has returned, standing hesitantly in front of the entrance.

**苏菲亚**：……很抱歉，非常抱歉，我本不该擅自踏入真理的殿堂……\
**Sophia**: I'm sorry. Please forgive me. I shouldn't have intruded the Hall of Truth, but ...

接二连三的打断让协理人感到恼火，但她及时注意到了除错师神色的反常。\
Though irritated by the constant interruptions, the Custodian immediately notices her peculiar expression.

**888**：苏菲亚，你不是在和42调查阿其翁吗？\
**888**: Sophia, weren't you and 42 checking on the Abraxases?

**888**：发生了什么事？\
**888**: What is the matter?

除错师的声音震颤着，她的手局促地在空气中比划。\
The Corrector gestures in the air, her voice shaking.

**苏菲亚**：阿其翁们的样子很奇怪！它们的喙……不，它们的整个头部，都在不断地滴落油彩——\
**Sophia**: The Abraxases don't look right! Their beaks, no, their entire heads are melting into oil paints.

**苏菲亚**：还有42，我们本来正在沙滩上勘察。可是他突然——\
**Sophia**: And 42 ... We were on the beach, suddenly, he ...

未尽的话语堵在嘴边。\
Her words trail off.

通过敞开的大门，鸟群的尖叫声清晰可闻。\
Beyond the open gate, the screeching of the bird monsters completes her sentence.

而另一名使者越过苏菲亚，癫狂而愤慨地冲进讲厅。五颜六色的油彩从他的面庞上淌落，在真理的殿堂上汇成一汪小小的水潭。\
The other believer appears behind her, shoving Sophia aside as he flails and stumbles into the hall. His face is melting, colorful oil paints forming a puddle on the floor.

**教众Ⅰ**：哈哈哈！哈哈哈哈！我明白了，我全都明白了！\
**Believer I**: Hahaha! Now I see, it finally all makes sense!

**教众Ⅰ**：从来没有真理，也没有超验！！！一切都是假的！是影子！是火光，是碎屑！\
**Believer I**: There never was the Truth, nor the transcendental! Everything is a lie! Nothing but shadows on walls, flickers of fire, and fragments of reality!

**教众Ⅰ**：没有人可以从虚无中幸免！这座岛注定将在矛盾中覆灭！！！\
**Believer I**: No one will survive the oblivion! The island will be destroyed amid its conflict!

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**维尔汀**：这是……这个时代的暴雨症候？\
**Vertin**: Is that the Storm Syndrome?

**888**：42，你的脸——\
**888**: 42, your face ...

没有理会同伴的呼喊，男人口齿不清地大笑着，手里凝聚着神秘术的辉光。\
Completely disregarding those around him, he bursts into maniacal laughter, casting an arcane glow in his palms.

他跳上了石制的坐席，掀翻了一连串照明的火炬。\
He jumps onto a seat and knocks over a row of torches.

**教众Ⅰ**：没有——人——\
**Believer I**: NO ONE!

**维尔汀**：888女士，请不要再尝试和他对话！\
**Vertin**: 888, stop conversing with him!

**维尔汀**：——立刻制伏他！\
**Vertin**: We must subdue him, now!

**维尔汀**：这是暴雨症候——！\
**Vertin**: He has the Storm Syndrome!

**维尔汀**：诸位，请听我说，37的话是正确的。小岛发生了某种变化，你们免疫“流溢”的能力衰减了！\
**Vertin**: Please, listen, everyone. 37 is right. Something's changed on this island. Your immunity to the "Emanation" has been weakened!

地板上，男人的狂笑已经平息下去，但他脸上的油彩依然骇人。\
42 lies motionless on the floor, his face still a mess of colorful paint.

而在他的四周，惊愕和疑虑的声浪一波盖过一波，几乎掀翻圆形穹顶。\
Fear and uncertainty quickly arise around him.

**教众Ⅳ**：这不可能，在之前的八次“流溢”里，从没有出现这种状况！\
**Believer IV**: How? That's never happened in the last eight times!

**210**：这是个无效归纳，朋友。即使你此生从未见过紫色的牛，也不能证明紫色的牛就是不存在的。\
**210**: A feeble induction, my friend. Just because you've never seen a purple cow, doesn't mean it doesn't exist.

**教众Ⅳ**：现在是谈论逻辑的时候吗？！42已经字面意义上地“流溢”了！\
**Believer IV**: Must we talk of logic now?! 42 has literally been "emanated"!

**教众Ⅱ**：——先是军队，再是“流溢”……自从那些外人来到了岛上，坏事就没有停止过。\
**Believer II**: First the army, then the "Emanation." Everything's been falling apart since the outsiders arrived on this island.

**教众Ⅱ**：基金会和重塑之手，总有一方理应为这些事负责。\
**Believer II**: The Foundation and Manus Vindictae—one of them must answer for this.

**教众Ⅳ**：那你也应当问问37和数字“0”，她们在圣地都做了些什么，才触怒了无限定者！\
**Believer IV**: Then you should also ask 37 and number "0" what they've done in the sacred place to anger Apeiron so much!

**37**：我……\
**37**: I ...

**维尔汀**：——不，不是37，我告诉过你们！是重塑之手。\
**Vertin**: No, 37 didn't cause this. I told you. It was Manus Vindictae!

**维尔汀**：重塑之手违背石环的协定，发动了自杀式袭击，他们侵入了你们的圣地——\
**Vertin**: They broke the peace agreement and launched suicide attacks. They forced their way into the cave.

**教众Ⅳ**：在这一件事上，你们二者同罪！\
**Believer IV**: You and them are equally responsible on this matter!

**教众Ⅳ**：而他们至少付出了生命作为代价，你却还好好活着，不是吗？\
**Believer IV**: They at least paid with their lives. What about you?

**教众Ⅳ**：你声称42的异变是“流溢”带来的癔症，但我们要如何确定，这不是你们神秘术的伎俩？！\
**Believer IV**: You claim that 42's abnormality was caused by the "Emanation," but how are we to believe that it isn't, in fact, the work of your arcane skills?

**教众Ⅳ**：维尔汀小姐，在你的随身物品中，有一枚金色的采样仪器。——烦请告诉我，你们基金会又想从这里找到什么东西？\
**Believer IV**: As we went through your belongings, Ms. Vertin, we found a golden sampling device. Enlighten us: What exactly is the Foundation looking for here?

**维尔汀**：那是——\
**Vertin**: That's ...

**阿尔卡纳**：呵呵……\
**Arcana**: Heh-heh.

笑声从厅堂的另一侧传来。\
From the other side of the hall comes a soft chuckle.

**阿尔卡纳**：很好，很好，维尔汀。\
**Arcana**: Good, Vertin. Good.

**阿尔卡纳**：再多说一点，再多做一点……\
**Arcana**: Let the confrontations be louder and the struggles be harder.

**阿尔卡纳**：让我看看你会为此被改变成何种姿态。\
**Arcana**: I wonder what shall come of this.

**6**：——安静！\
**6**: Silence!

石钟截断了这场争论。\
The gavel slams down with a heavy, undeniable thud.

一直沉默的领袖从高台上站起，他的面容前所未有地凝重。\
The host of the assembly rises to his feet, his face unusually grave.

**6**：争辩到此为止。\
**6**: The debate will end now.

**6**：过去我们未曾达成一致，如今一切的议论也已毫无意义。岛屿有更紧急的状况要处理。\
**6**: Since we were unable to come to an agreement, further discussion is pointless. There are more pressing matters to attend to.

**6**：公民大会就此结束。对圣洛夫基金会和重塑之手的结论，将由我直接裁断。\
**6**: This will be the end of the assembly, and my decision will be the final ruling:

**6**：——请你们双方立刻离开岛屿，马上。\
**6**: I demand that both parties leave this island at once.

没有任何修辞，他的话语言简意赅。\
The decision is clear and final.

6代表着调和，独裁和武断很少出现在这个数字身上。\
As the number of reconciliation, 6 has been mindful of his use of unilateral authority.

但这次没有任何人提出异议。\
Yet, there are no objections this time.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

厅堂陷入了长久的沉默，这沉默是为了逼迫。\
The hall falls into a silence—a silence that demands a decision.

该怎么做？\
What to do?

这将是个重大损失，关于“暴雨”的交流刚刚开始，洞穴深处的奥秘也尚未揭开。\
Leaving the island would be a huge loss. The discussion about the "Storm" has only just begun, and the depths of the cave is yet to be explored.

而且，重塑之手的领袖——她还在这里。\
Worst of all, the leader of Manus Vindictae—she can't be left here with the School of Apeiron.

她会接受这个结果吗？她意犹未尽吗？\
Will she accept the verdict? Will she appeal?

——她究竟带着怎样的目的来到岛上？\
Just what exactly is she after?

这是一场无声的零和博弈，先应答的一方率先出局。\
It's a zero-sum game, where the first one to react is more likely to lose.

现在，不妨等待。\
The best course of action is to wait.

**阿尔卡纳**：……当然，我尊重每一位同胞的意见。\
**Arcana**: The decisions of my fellow brethren shall be respected.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：我也认同您的判断。\
**Vertin**: I also agree with your verdict.

这是一个尚可接受的结论，一切只是回到了原点。\
The outcome is still acceptable, things will just go back to square one.

过往关于“暴雨”的探讨，对非对称核素R的采样，已经给后续的调查带来了足够多的线索。\
Besides, the concepts exchanged on the "Storm" and the samples of asymmetrical nuclide R are already significant advancements for subsequent research.

更重要的是——即使不能达成合作，也必须阻止这个纯血神秘学家团体倒向重塑之手。\
More importantly, if the School of Apeiron cannot form an alliance with the Foundation, they must be stopped from joining forces with the enemy instead.

这是一个率先表决的机会，它将挽救局势于被动之中。\
This is a chance to take the initiative and avoid being caught in a reactive position.

要做的只是，站起来，点点头。\
All that's needed is to stand up and nod.

**维尔汀**：——我同意您的判断。\
**Vertin**: I respectfully accept your verdict.

同意是容易的，因为造成问题从来不在这一点。\
Agreeing was the easy part.

问题是——她会怎么选择？\
Now comes the real issue—what will she choose to do?

**阿尔卡纳**：我的选择和维尔汀一样。\
**Arcana**: My choice matches that of Vertin's.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

她轻而易举地接受了，一如接受将鲜血滴上石环。\
She casually agrees, just as she did when asked to pledge on the stone bangles.

**阿尔卡纳**：——仅有一个小小的疑虑。\
**Arcana**: But may I ask for one small doubt to be dispelled?

**阿尔卡纳**：在我和维尔汀小姐一同离去后，贵派真的不需要我们提供援助吗？\
**Arcana**: Ms. Vertin and I will depart ere long. Do you truly not desirest aid from us?

**6**：……感谢您的关心。\
**6**: You're kind to ask, miss.

**6**：诚然，庇佑我们的圆遭遇了扰乱，但这只是现象世界的一次风浪。\
**6**: It is true that our circle has been disturbed, but we see it as a mere turbulence of the phenomenal world.

**6**：我们是手握尺规之人，圆心不会因此偏移，形状也不会因此流变。\
**6**: He who holds the compass decides the circle. This will not shift the center of our focus, nor change the shape of our beliefs.

领袖俯下身去，将手覆在42的额头上。\
6 bends down, laying his hand on 42's forehead.

**6**：Μηδὲν ἄγαν.\
**6**: Μηδὲν ἄγαν.

**教众Ⅰ**：……\
**Believer I**: ...

**教众Ⅰ**：……呼。\
**Believer I**: *breathes peacefully*

**维尔汀**：——他用神秘术消解了暴雨症候？！\
**Vertin**: He purged the Storm Syndrome with an arcane skill?!

**维尔汀**：这是……可能的吗？\
**Vertin**: I never thought it'd be possible.

领袖重新起身，平静地面向众人。\
The leader straightens up, looking as composed as ever.

**6**：……42只是需要智识的净化，正如这座岛屿一样。\
**6**: The light of intelligence has cleansed 42 of confusion. It is also what the island needs.

**6**：这件事会得到妥善的解决，我此前的决断，亦不会改变。\
**6**: The incident will be properly handled, and my ruling stays unchanged.

**6**：——请阿尔卡纳小姐理解。\
**6**: I expect your words to be matched by actions, Ms. Arcana.

他的语气只剩下冰冷的警戒。\
His tone is cold, leaving no room for negotiation.

**阿尔卡纳**：当然，为什么不呢？您的族群有自己的规则。\
**Arcana**: Certainly. It was a fair and just decision,

**阿尔卡纳**：只是我们也需要一些启程的时间……尤其是在这样可悲的坏天气里。\
**Arcana**: if only one could depart amidst such unfavorable weather.

**阿尔卡纳**：——我想维尔汀也会同意的，不是吗？\
**Arcana**: I presume Ms. Vertin will also appreciate more time to prepare for the journey, what sayest thou?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

她的笑容依然亲切，商谈的口吻像进行一场友人聚会。\
It is a reasonable request, and her expression is nothing but decent and sincere.

**6**：……在这个沙漏流尽前，你们有两个小时用来撤离。\
**6**: The hourglass empties in two hours. Please leave before that.

**维尔汀**：……感谢您周到的安排。\
**Vertin**: Thank you for your thoughtful consideration.

无人再提出质疑，所有数字都默认了领袖的裁决。\
The decision is met with no further objection from the people.

6收起了沙漏，将目光投向缄默的席座。\
6 puts away the hourglass and looks at the silent audience.

**6**：……那么，在这场会议的最后，我想引用一个故事。\
**6**: Lastly, I would like to share a story,

**6**：作为这起事件的收尾，也作为对阿尔卡纳小姐此前分享的回应。\
**6**: to conclude today's meeting, and respond to Ms. Arcana's tale.

**阿尔卡纳**：我很荣幸。\
**Arcana**: I am most honored.

领袖抬起手，面向厅堂的众人。\
The leader raises his hands and faces the people.

**6**：我也听过这个关于圆的传说，但它尚有后续。\
**6**: I, too, have heard the story of the first circle. But in my version, more followed.

**6**：在这个故事里，人们畏惧自然，违抗自然，躲避自然。\
**6**: The first of man were intimidated by the enormity of nature and constantly tried to defy and escape it.

**6**：我们的先祖则选择转向自然，到自然中去。而它也接纳了我们，以它的崇高和广博。\
**6**: Our ancestors, however, had the opposite reaction. They found solace in nature, which welcomed them with a nourishing embrace, sharing its vastness and sublimity without reservation.

**6**：完满的融合出现了，圆不再代表对立和拮抗。\
**6**: It was the perfect harmony. The moment the circle ceased to represent confrontation and avoidance.

**6**：我们沐浴在阿波罗之星的启示下，漫步于海滩的和谐与静美中，以此获得智识的升华和灵魂的共振。\
**6**: As we bathed in Apollo's illumination and wandered the tranquil shores, our souls resonated, and we were lifted to a higher wisdom.

**6**：由此，我们克服恐惧，摆脱蒙昧，欣赏到万事万物的形式与本质。\
**6**: This was how we conquered our fears, emerged from ignorance, and allowed ourselves to indulge on the essence and Forms.

**6**：这就是“古典的人”。\
**6**: This was the rise of the "classic man."

**6**：——和解的勇气、和平的决心、献身的精神，并不比违抗和怀疑来得更加低微。\
**6**: May you all be blessed with the courage for reconciliation, the determination for peace, and the devotion to nature—qualities no less noble than caution and defiance.

**6**：散会。\
**6**: You may all leave now.

**37**：——请再等一下！\
**37**: Please, just a moment!

清亮的声音打断了领袖的步伐。\
A clear voice rings across the hall, stopping 6 in his tracks.

她倏地自高台上站起，袍角在空中划出一道尖锐的弧线。\
Her robe flutters as she stands up on the high podium.

**37**：我会修好我们的圆！\
**37**: I will fix our circle!

**37**：888说的是对的，是我触怒了无限定者，我应该为此负责。\
**37**: 888 was right. I have enraged Apeiron. I am responsible.

**37**：我会再去一次圣地——我会去通过无限定者的考验，恳请祂分享神圣光明的诺斯，使我们求得关于本质的真理。\
**37**: I will go back to the sacred place, pass Its test, and ask It to share the divine light of Gnosis, so we can learn the Truth about the essence.

**37**：——我会弥补我的过失，我保证！\
**37**: I will make up for what I've done, I promise!

离开的脚步停顿了，6转过身来，望向那枚目光坚定的星星。\
6 turns around, his eyes meeting the gaze of the determined star.

**6**：……上一次有人通过这个仪式，还是三个世纪前。\
**6**: It has been three hundred years since the last challenger had their success in the cave.

**6**：37，你是否知悉，即使你不用参加试炼，我们也有其他途径完成岛屿的净化？\
**6**: 37, are you aware that we have other means to cleanse the island, even if you don't bring the matter to Apeiron?

**37**：我知道。\
**37**: Yes, I'm aware.

**6**：……那么，你是否知悉，倘若在无限定者的考验中失败，你将面临什么？\
**6**: Then are you aware of the price you will pay, should you fail Its test?

**37**：——我知道。\
**37**: Yes, I am.

**6**：……那么，我许可了。\
**6**: Then you shall have my blessing.

没有再理会厅堂里的质疑。\
He leaves, ignoring the murmurs of shock.

石钟敲响了自己的尾音。\
The gavel is thus brought down.

这场无尽的论辩终结于人为的句号。\
The long debate has finally come to an end.

## 7TH-04 证明的开端 / The Beginning of a Proof

剧情场景-岛屿-传道者之厅外-天色差分（是一个比较独特的光线，比如玫瑰紫）

**十四行诗**：……总部传来了通告，这一次“暴雨”的临界点是维也纳。\
**Sonetto**: The headquarters has issued a notice. The Critical Point of the "Storm" is in Vienna.

第一助手放下了手中的无线电小姐，凝重地转过身来。\
The chief assistant puts down Ms. Radio and turns around with a somber expression.

**十四行诗**：暴雨症候是面部出现油画变形，少数扩散到躯干，同时伴随战争狂热的神经谵妄症。\
**Sonetto**: This type of Storm Syndrome involves a bodily transformation into oil paintings, primarily affecting the face but sometimes spreading to the torso. It is often accompanied by delirium and an intense obsession with war.

**十四行诗**：“暴雨”发生的原因和1929年高度相似。重塑之手引发国际局势的震荡，加速了当前时代的崩溃。\
**Sonetto**: Like the "Storm" of 1929, it was accelerated by social upheavals resulting from the constant tensions Manus Vindictae created between nations.

**维尔汀**：这个时代……\
**Vertin**: This era ...

天空的颜色不同以往。\
The color of the sky has changed.

时代狂热的癔症已经蔓延到了这座与世隔绝的小岛。\
The Storm Syndrome has finally reached this island.

所幸，同伴们一切无恙。\
No one on the team's caught it yet, but that could soon change.

**星锑**：要我说，这也太荒唐了——\
**Regulus**: This is absurd!

长达一周的地下监禁没能挫伤摇滚海盗的志气，她的包里装满了鼓鼓囊囊的炼金材料。\
With a bag filled with alchemy materials over her shoulders, the young pirate remains spirited despite a week in underground captivity.

**星锑**：我们好不容易找到了一个免疫“暴雨”的地点，然后它突然就像没了气的皮球一样失效了？\
**Regulus**: We went through all that trouble, sweated our guts out, and finally got to a place where the "Storm" can be kept out. But now you're telling me that immunity is going to disappear like a fart in the wind?

**星锑**：我本来还想多待一会儿，再带点阿其翁嚼剩的炼金材料和残典回去……\
**Regulus**: I was planning to stay here for a while. There might be alchemic materials and pieces of books the Abraxases left behind from their meals.

**星锑**：该死，这一点也不科学……！\
**Regulus**: Ugh! Now that is frustrating, mate!

**十四行诗**：我想……也许因为这是神秘学？\
**Sonetto**: *sigh* Such is the nature of arcanum?

**维尔汀**：准确来说，不是失效，而是衰减。目前被“暴雨症候”影响的区域仅限沙滩，传道者之厅附近的区域还是安全的。\
**Vertin**: The immunity hasn't "disappeared." It's just waning. For now, only the beach has lost the effect. We're still safe around the Hall of Apeiron.

**红弩箭**：但谁也不能保证这个圈会不会继续缩水，对吧？\
**Lilya**: But there's no guarantee that we'll be safe here forever, right?

**红弩箭**：哈，和芝诺的生存模拟考试似的。\
**Lilya**: Hah. Reminds me of Zeno's survival test.

**维尔汀**：……我和十四行诗曾经推断，这座岛上有一个环绕全岛的大型神秘术式。\
**Vertin**: Sonetto and I talked about this. We think the island is protected by a large-scale arcane ritual.

**维尔汀**：岛屿的衰竭可能与它的变动有关。尽管我不知道原理……\
**Vertin**: The sudden decay of the island's "Storm" immunity might be the result of its changes, though I'm unsure of the specifics.

**星锑**：但他们总会做点什么，对吧？那个发型和摇滚明星似的领袖，他总该有点办法吧？\
**Regulus**: Those people are doing something about it, right? That leader with the rock star hair—shouldn't he be taking action by now?

**维尔汀**：……公民大会后，6召集了所有整数。他们似乎准备进行一个集体净化仪式。\
**Vertin**: 6 has gathered all integers after the assembly. They're going to perform a mass cleansing ceremony.

**维尔汀**：37也提出了一个试炼仪式，我想学派内部有足够的应对手段。\
**Vertin**: 37 also mentioned a test. I think they have more than one way to deal with the changes.

**APPLe**：据APPLe某所知，与世隔绝的纯血神秘学家团体，大多都有着自己的秘传仪式。\
**APPLe**: To the best of this APPLe's knowledge, secluded pure-blood arcanist groups often have rituals that they keep to themselves.

**APPLe**：阿派朗学派传授的真理是理智化的，奉行的教条却是宗教式的，他们的神秘术传承或许就与后者有关。\
**APPLe**: These islanders impart Truth based on intellect and rationality, yet their doctrines are highly religious. Perhaps their arcane skills are passed down in a religious manner.

**红弩箭**：哇哦，听起来可真是神秘啊——该不会是将所有人关在一起做数学题吧？\
**Lilya**: Oh, very mysterious, very arcane. I hope they're not all huddled together doing math at a time like this.

**红弩箭**：比起这些，头儿。\
**Lilya**: And I'm more worried about us, Captain.

红弩箭收起了吊儿郎当的神情，语气前所未有地凝重。\
Lilya changes her tone, unusually serious.

**红弩箭**：——是阿尔卡纳主动索要了撤离时间，对吗？\
**Lilya**: Arcana asked for more time for both sides to withdraw, didn't she?

**维尔汀**：是的。6预留的时间是两小时，也就是说……\
**Vertin**: Yes. 6 gave us two hours to leave. That is to say ...

**维尔汀**：——“暴雨”倒计时跳到20：00时，我们必须离开岛屿。\
**Vertin**: We must set out when the "Storm" countdown reaches 20:00.

**红弩箭**：在那之前，你手上的石环依然有效，对吗？\
**Lilya**: And before that, the stone bangle on your wrist still works, right?

**维尔汀**：……嗯，我能够感知到这一点。\
**Vertin**: Yes. I can feel it.

**维尔汀**：如果我有与阿尔卡纳开战的念头，它便会灼烧我。\
**Vertin**: It would scald me whenever I thought about going to war with them.

**红弩箭**：哈，明白了。\
**Lilya**: Hah. I see.

**红弩箭**：看来我们只能在这2小时里执行计划了。\
**Lilya**: So we only have two hours for the plan.

**星锑**：……计划？什么计划？\
**Regulus**: Plan? What plan?

**星锑**：我们现在不是要……开溜吗？\
**Regulus**: Aren't we sneaking away from all this?

**十四行诗**：抱歉，星锑，你的住处和我们相距甚远，有一些信息我还没有来得及通知你。\
**Sonetto**: Sorry, Regulus, your, uhm, "accommodation" was a long way from ours, so we haven't given you the latest updates.

**十四行诗**：简单来说——\
**Sonetto**: To put it simply ...

**37**：——你们想去哪儿？\
**37**: Where are you going?

**十四行诗**：唔！\
**Sonetto**: Uhm!

唐突出现的少女吓了所有人一跳。\
The sudden appearance of the girl startles the crowd.

37一脸好奇地站着，一如既往，她的步伐悄无声息。\
37 stands there with a curious look on her face.

**十四行诗**：呃，37小姐，我们……\
**Sonetto**: Ahh, 37, we ...

**维尔汀**：——我们在谈论如何离开的问题，37。\
**Vertin**: We are discussing how to leave this place, 37.

**星锑**：对极了，我正想说呢！你们心急火燎地赶我们离开，可我们连艘像样的船都没有。\
**Regulus**: Precisely! I was just about to say, your chief wants us gone in a jiffy, but we don't even have a piece of wood to sail with!

**星锑**：维尔汀正准备把我们全部装进箱子里，然后游泳横渡爱琴海呢。——对吧，维尔汀？\
**Regulus**: Vertin is sizing us up to see if we can fit in her suitcase. She's going to swim across the Aegean Sea using her tiny arms! Right, Vertin?

星锑挤挤眼睛，热切地用胳膊肘捅了过来。\
Regulus squints and eagerly pokes her elbow in.

**维尔汀**：……是的。\
**Vertin**: Right.

**37**：嗯……听起来很棒！\
**37**: Hmm. Sounds like a lot of fun!

**37**：那你应该从海滩北角的高地上向南跳水，那里在传道者之厅的切线上，一定能让这趟旅途顺利！\
**37**: Then you must leave from the north side of the beach, jump off the cliff there, and head south. The cliff is on the tangent line of the Hall of Apeiron, which is a good sign for your journey!

37点了点头，非常认真地予以了数学上的建议。\
She nods confidently, fully convinced of her own conclusion.

**37**：我可以带你们去找入水的好地方——不过，得等维尔汀和我从那个地方回来！\
**37**: I will show you where to jump. But you'll have to wait till Vertin and I return.

**维尔汀**：……我？去哪里？\
**Vertin**: Me? Where are we going?

**37**：这是什么问题？\
**37**: What kind of question is that?

**37**：只有那一个地方是值得去的，不是吗？\
**37**: The only place worth going.

她张开了手，嗓音雀跃，语调轻快，一如既往。\
She extends her hand with a light and happy tone.

**37**：——当然是作为独一无二的0，和我一起再去面见无限定者！\
**37**: You're the one and only 0. We'll go see Apeiron together!

剧情场景-岛屿-居民区洞穴

**玛尔塔**：……你不去找37吗？\
**Marta**: Aren't you going to look for 37?

**玛尔塔**：明明她昏迷不醒时，是你寸步不离地照看她。\
**Marta**: You took such good care of her while she was in a coma.

阴影中的人颤抖了一下。\
In the darkness, the figure trembles ever so slightly.

也仅仅如此。\
She tries to steady herself.

**苏菲亚**：……我不知道……\
**Sophia**: I don't know.

**苏菲亚**：我不知道，玛尔塔女士。\
**Sophia**: I don't know what I should do, Madam Marta.

**苏菲亚**：37要去参加那个试炼，但我，我完全帮不上忙。\
**Sophia**: She's going back to the cave for the test, where I can't help her.

她低下头，努力使自己颤抖的双手交握。\
She looks down, trying her best to press her shaking hands together.

**苏菲亚**：我只能为她祈祷……但对于她所要做和将要做的事，我全都一无所知。\
**Sophia**: All I can do is pray for her, for I have no adequate knowledge or power to assist her.

**苏菲亚**：——从来如此。\
**Sophia**: As ever.

**玛尔塔**：也许您不用太过担忧。\
**Marta**: Perhaps you needn't worry so much.

**玛尔塔**：37会安然无事的，她是被真理眷顾的孩子。\
**Marta**: 37 is the one favored by Truth. She will be fine.

**苏菲亚**：……我知道，可是……\
**Sophia**: I know. It's just ...

苏菲亚深深地叹了一口气，将脸埋在手掌中。\
Sophia lets out a long, helpless sigh and buries her face deep in her palms.

**苏菲亚**：可是，她也是一个人。会受伤，会流血，会死亡。\
**Sophia**: She is also of mortal flesh. She could get hurt, bleed, or die.

她堪堪移开了目光，不再望向那片自己短暂缺席的海角。\
She avoids looking at the beach, seeing it as a battlefield where she lacks the skills to engage.

**苏菲亚**：……玛尔塔女士，您来到学派的时间太短，不知道无限定者的考验意味着什么。\
**Sophia**: You haven't been with us for long, Madam Marta. Apeiron and Its test might be new to you.

**苏菲亚**：我们提出猜想，完善证明，在尺规构建的方圆之地筑起大厦，划定属于“人”的可知疆域。\
**Sophia**: Here on this island, we spent years theorizing, proving, and constructing models based on our mortal comprehension, defining the boundaries of what man is capable of understanding.

**苏菲亚**：可在“本质”的领域上，我们并无能力断言。因而，我们在神庙前匍匐询问，所求之事是否正确。\
**Sophia**: But when it comes to the "essence" and "Forms," we are unable to make any definitive statements. So we humbly approach the temple and inquire about the correctness of our beliefs.

**苏菲亚**：洞穴的回音将回答您“是”或者“否”。\
**Sophia**: And our answer is delivered as a "yes" or "no," reverberating in the form of echoes.

**玛尔塔**：……这即是6所说的，“向无限定者检验证明……”？\
**Marta**: Is that the "submission of proof" 6 mentioned before?

除错师点了点头，她雀跃的友人同样精于此道。\
The Corrector nods, knowing her friend has a natural talent for this.

**苏菲亚**：……检验一个人本质的数字，是最微不足道的。检验发生过的事实真假，亦是容易的裁决。\
**Sophia**: Validating one's essence and soul with a number and verifying the authenticity of one's claims are simple feats for us.

**苏菲亚**：然而，无限定者的试炼却不一样。\
**Sophia**: But Apeiron's test is different.

**苏菲亚**：“通过考验的人将会获得超越一切的真理。”\
**Sophia**: "Those who succeed will obtain the transcendental Truth."

**苏菲亚**：“倘若失败，也会为此付出最为可怖的代价。”\
**Sophia**: "Those who fail will pay a terrible price."

**玛尔塔**：……！\
**Marta**: ...!

**苏菲亚**：一切事物都有着边界。\
**Sophia**: Everything has its limits and boundaries.

**苏菲亚**：试图染指自己限度之外的人，必将招致灾祸。\
**Sophia**: Those who overstep their bounds will only court their own misfortune.

**苏菲亚**：因此，我们必须竭尽所能，我们必须心存敬畏。让灵魂适度于躯体，令万物免于过度。\
**Sophia**: We must respect and be wary of our limits, so our souls will be adequate for our bodies, and all things be refrained from excess.

**苏菲亚**：“无限”并非我们能踏足的领域。它只属于那些古老而神秘的不可说者。我们唯有仰望，祈祷，崇敬。\
**Sophia**: The "boundless," "limitless," and "infinity" are not of our realm to tread. They belong only to ancient beings that we cannot utter. We can only stand in awe, offering our admiration, humility, and reverence.

**苏菲亚**：现在，37却要叩响祂的大门，恳求祂分享那超越的真理。如果她失败了，如果她没能承受住无限——\
**Sophia**: Now 37 is going to knock on Its door and ask to be indulged with the transcendental Truth. But, if she fails, if she can't bear the weight of the boundless infinity ...

她很难再说下去了。\
She can't go on.

**苏菲亚**：……我多么希望我知道更好的方法，或者我能够替她前往……\
**Sophia**: I wish I knew a better way, or could even do it in her place.

**苏菲亚**：可是，只能是她，只能是37……\
**Sophia**: But only she can do it. It has to be her, 37.

剧情场景-岛屿-传道者之厅外-天色差分（是一个比较独特的光线，比如玫瑰紫）

**37**：我确信这是一个完美的解法，可以一劳永逸地解决我们所有的问题！\
**37**: I'm sure this is the perfect solution to finally put an end to all our problems!

**37**：无限定者会回答通过考验者的一个问题，任何你绝不能靠自己回答出的问题，甚至是关于“本质”和“一切”的问题！\
**37**: If I pass the test, Apeiron will grant me the answer to one question. It can be any question I don't have an answer to, even about the "essence" and "everything."

**37**：——至少妈妈是这么告诉我的。\
**37**: At least that's what Mama told me.

37笃定地点了点头，显然这一规则是不证自明的。\
37 nods with confidence.

**37**：我想，只要我挑选了合适的问题，无论是“流溢”的谜团、现象世界的纷扰，还是这儿的危机，都会立刻找到解决的方法！\
**37**: I just have to choose the right question to ask, and we will be rid of all the troubles. Whether it be the "Emanation," the turmoil of the phenomenal world, or the dangers threatening the island, all will be gone!

**37**：6也认可了我的提议。所以，维尔汀——\
**37**: I have 6's blessing. He agrees with me. So, Vertin ...

**星锑**：等等，你可不要拐骗我们的舵手！\
**Regulus**: Ah-uh, not so fast! You can't just steal away our helmswoman like that!

**星锑**：这个仪式肯定是有风险的，对吧？万一维尔汀回不来了，谁来带我们游泳横渡爱琴海？\
**Regulus**: This "thing," it's too good to be without any risks, don't you think? What if Vertin doesn't make it back? Huh? Who's going to swim us across the sea then?

**37**：嗯？对我的确比较危险，但对0来说就不一样了，因为0乘以任何数都是0。\
**37**: Hmm? It could be risky, but not for Vertin, only for me. 0 multiplied by any number will still be 0.

**37**：这一点已经确切验证过了！\
**37**: And we have validated that proof!

**星锑**：嘿，这可不是一个充分的论据。再说，我根本不觉得维尔汀是0——\
**Regulus**: Well, that's not good enough for this Pirate! Besides, Vertin doesn't seem like a 0 to me.

**维尔汀**：——没关系，星锑，我想那里的确不会对我有影响。\
**Vertin**: It's okay, Regulus. I think I'll be safe there.

**维尔汀**：但这不是对你们很重要的仪式吗？你知道我并未立下誓言，也没有加入学派。\
**Vertin**: But 37, isn't this a sacred test for your people? I have never taken the oath. I'm not one of you.

**37**：不，那都不重要，维尔汀。\
**37**: That does not matter, Vertin.

37摇了摇头，她的目光依然坚定。\
She gently shakes her head in determination.

**37**：进入神庙后，不可以回头。我们不能在追寻真理的道路上半途而废。\
**37**: But you must know that once we enter the temple, we cannot turn back. The path to the Truth is a one-way road.

**37**：我们上次的验证被打断了，不是吗？你的问题没有问出，我也还没有得到答案。\
**37**: Our last visit was interrupted, remember? You didn't get to ask your question, and I didn't get my answer.

**37**：……而我的问题，已经不必问了。\
**37**: And now, I don't need to ask my question anymore.

她咬紧嘴唇，抱住了自己的双臂。\
She bites her lip, holding her own arms tight.

**37**：你们是对的，维尔汀，现象世界的纷扰可以影响“本质”……没有比发生在这儿的事，和这场“流溢”，更能证明这一点了。\
**37**: You and your friends were right, Vertin. The discord in the phenomenal world does have an effect on essence and Forms. No one can argue against this when facing the "Emanation."

**37**：我只是想要知道的更多……你应当也一样。\
**37**: But there's more I'd like to know, and I believe you feel the same.

**37**：——我会去告诉6的，我也会去告诉所有人的。我会说服他们的，因为这是正确的。\
**37**: I will tell 6 that you're coming with me. I will tell everyone and persuade them, because this is the right thing to do.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**十四行诗**：……不用担心，司辰。我和红弩箭小姐会负责做好撤离的所有准备。\
**Sonetto**: Go, Timekeeper. While you're out, Lilya and I will ready us for evacuation.

**红弩箭**：是啊，联络总部的交接工作——谁干都一样。\
**Lilya**: We will liaise with the Foundation from here.

**维尔汀**：……明白了，我和你去见无限定者。\
**Vertin**: Thank you both. I'm ready.

**维尔汀**：只是我还有一个疑问，37。\
**Vertin**: Before we go, 37, I have a question.

**37**：嗯哼？\
**37**: Hmm?

是的，这的确是一个机会。\
A golden opportunity has arisen.

一个千载难逢的、追上重塑之手的机会。\
This could be a chance to level the playing field against Manus Vindictae.

**维尔汀**：——你说，通过考验的试炼者，无限定者将回答他的一个问题。\
**Vertin**: You just said that Apeiron will grant an answer to whoever passes the test.

**维尔汀**：那么，假如有这么一个问题。\
**Vertin**: Will It answer my question?

**维尔汀**：倘若我直接询问“免疫‘暴雨’的方法”……祂是否也可以回答？\
**Vertin**: If I asked for a way to become immune to the "Storm"?

## 7TH-05 四次方程 / Four Cross-Checks

**研究员Ⅰ**：有眼无珠的**们，该死的、愚蠢的、狭隘的人类中心主义者们——\
**Researcher I**: Damn! You narcissistic, fat-headed, humanocentrist freaks!

**研究员Ⅰ**：你们都疯了！你们才是疯子，而我，我会证明我是对的——\
**Researcher I**: You are the crazy ones! And I, I will prove myself right!

**研究员Ⅱ**：该死，快把马修带回康复中心去！他受那面具影响太深了！\
**Researcher II**: Seriously!? Can someone please bring Matthew back to the rehab center? That mask has made him crazy!

研究员狂乱挥舞着手臂，在混乱之上制造新的混乱。\
The researcher's arms flail wildly as he stumbles across the shiny silver floor, adding more to the chaos.

泛着理性光泽的银色地面上，一瓶被投掷的酒精瓶燃起蓝色的火苗。\
Amidst the mayhem, a bottle of alcohol on the ground bursts into bright blue flames.

而后，一双钢铁的脚步迈过了它。\
And then, two metal feet stomp across the fire without hesitation.

**露西**：有进展吗？\
**Lucy**: Any progress?

**破译组长**：没有。我们召集了所有破译术式的专家，但他们没有任何发现，甚至连念咒后的不适感都没有。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Not much. We've called all the experts here, but so far it's been a waste of time. Not even a bodily reaction when reciting the text.

**破译组长**：它不属于任何一种已知的语言，也不符合寻常的拼写规则。\
**Cryptography Lead**: It doesn't belong to any known language, nor follow any linguistic rules.

**破译组长**：不少人认为是咒文抄错了，因为这项报告并不是资深调查员传回的，而是一个新手调查员借由自己的神秘术——\
**Cryptography Lead**: Many are starting to doubt the accuracy of the incantation. After all, it was copied down by a novice investigator with her arcane skill, not her supervisor.

门被推开了。\
The door is pushed open.

这个偌大的房间如今挤满了人。\
The spacious room is now packed with people.

人群的最中央是一部电台。\
They're all gathered around a radio on the table.

**联络员Ⅰ**：马库斯小姐，您听写的这份咒文确实属实，对吗？\
**Liaison Staff I**: Ms. Marcus, can you confirm that the incantation you dictated was correct?

**马库斯**：我……\
**Marcus**: I ...

**联络员Ⅰ**：再次确认，您在一名纯血神秘学家的显像神秘术中看见了阿尔卡纳施术的场景，对吗？\
**Liaison Staff I**: We also learned that you witnessed a visual recording of Arcana performing her arcane skill, depicted through images recreated by a pure-blooded arcanist. Is that right?

**马库斯**：是的，准确来说，是在卡卡尼亚小姐的镜子神秘术中，看见了前重塑之手成员伊索尔德的回忆。\
**Marcus**: Yes, to be precise, I saw it in the memories of Isolde, a former member of Manus Vindictae, using Ms. Kakania's arcane mirror.

**联络员Ⅰ**：您能保证那名前重塑成员的回忆是准确的吗？\
**Liaison Staff I**: Can you attest to the accuracy of this memory?

**马库斯**：……我不能。\
**Marcus**: I can't say.

**联络员Ⅰ**：您能保证卡卡尼亚小姐的镜中成像是客观、真实、未造成任何歪曲的吗？\
**Liaison Staff I**: Do you deem the reflection of Ms. Kakania's arcane mirror to be accurate, factual, and without misinterpretation?

**马库斯**：……我不知道。\
**Marcus**: I'm not sure.

**联络员Ⅰ**：您能保证自己的阅读神秘术，是准确公正的，并且在摘录时不会造成偏差吗？\
**Liaison Staff I**: Can you confirm that your arcane skill, "Read," was performed correctly, and provided an unbiased, objective, and flawless interpretation?

**马库斯**：我，我也不知道……\
**Marcus**: I, I don't know about that either.

**马库斯**：但是，我看到了画面，我还听到了她吟唱的声音——\
**Marcus**: But I saw it with my own eyes. I heard the chanting.

**马库斯**：我的确不知道那是什么语言，但我标注的音标是准确的——！\
**Marcus**: I don't know what language that was, but that's how I heard it, and I've written it down phonetically!

**联络员Ⅰ**：无需紧张，我们只是在核查当时的情况。\
**Liaison Staff I**: Please calm down. We are only verifying the details.

**联络员Ⅰ**：基金会已派遣特别行动队赶往维也纳，请您务必把咒文涉及的两名神秘学家一并带回。\
**Liaison Staff I**: The Foundation has dispatched a special operations squad to you in Vienna. Please make sure the two other arcanists involved will return to the Foundation with you.

**马库斯**：……我……明白。\
**Marcus**: I ... Understood.

连线结束了，联络员摘下了耳机。\
The call ends. The liaison removes the headset.

这不是一个理想的结果，破译小组成员的脸色并不比金属更像人类。\
The result is far from ideal. Her face is pale, as lifeless as her mechanical colleagues.

**？？？**：……所以，我们要解读的就是这个？\
**???**: This? Is this it?

一道刺耳的讥讽拨开空气，唐突地挤到人群前列。\
A sarcastic voice cuts through the air as a man pushes through to the front.

**哑谜**：“一个古老的奇迹，一个拯救的魔圈！”\
**Enigma**: "An ancient miracle, a circle of salvation!"

**哑谜**：/eɪ u:.nə 'sa.kəʊ/ ... A tuna psycho?\
**Enigma**: /eɪ u:.nə 'sa.kəʊ/ ... a Tuna Psycho?

**哑谜**：一句意义不明的，用神秘术阅读的神秘术呈现的神秘学家回忆里的神秘术咒文。\
**Enigma**: An inexplicable incantation transcribed by an arcanist based on what she saw in the memory of another arcanist recreated by yet another arcanist.

**哑谜**：神秘的四次方——多么精妙啊。而你们竟然还在谈论什么“客观还原”……\
**Enigma**: That's as convoluted as a dream within a dream within a dream. To think they wanted an "objective restoration."

**哑谜**：试问，假如灵知可以交叉检验，还是交叉检验四次的话，它为什么还没替代科学呢？\
**Enigma**: I mean, if Gnosis is so reliable and can really cross-check not only once, but FOUR times, it should have long replaced science by now.

**哑谜**：我们为什么还没有全部下岗，让一群猴子来打字机上演奏莎士比亚呢？\
**Enigma**: With this level of uncertainty, we might have better luck asking typewriter monkeys to randomly give us the answer to the "Storm" immunity!

**破译组长**：阿德勒？！你应该不在破译组的名单上——\
**Cryptography Lead**: Adler?! Why are you here?

**露西**：我让他来的。\
**Lucy**: I requested his participation on the cryptography team.

**露西**：虽然他是人类，但他在密码学上颇有建树。\
**Lucy**: He is a human, but he excels in the field of cryptography.

**破译组长**：可是……\
**Cryptography Lead**: But ...

男人阴沉地往前走了一步。\
The man takes a grim step forward.

**哑谜**：为什么我不能来？\
**Enigma**: And why can't I be here?

**哑谜**：因为我的姐姐是格蕾塔·霍夫曼？\
**Enigma**: Is it because Greta Hofmann's my sister?

**哑谜**：而这是她——一个品行高洁的、富有献身精神的调查员，为了人类神圣的使命，拼上性命从雨幕中拿到的术式？\
**Enigma**: And this—is this what a respectable and honorable member of the Foundation gave her life to retrieve? Is this the ritual she died for?

**哑谜**：——噢，我忘了，她没有拿到，是她的学生拿到了。\
**Enigma**: Oh, riiight. It wasn't even her who retrieved the ritual. It was her student.

**露西**：你还不是正式成员，随时可以退出破译小组。\
**Lucy**: You are not currently on the official roster. You can leave at any time.

**哑谜**：退出？为什么？\
**Enigma**: Leave? Why should I leave?

**哑谜**：——我有权知道我姐姐为什么而死！\
**Enigma**: I have every right to know what my sister died for!

**哑谜**：好啊，朋友们，解吧，来解这个神秘四次方的术式吧！看看我们最终会得到什么——\
**Enigma**: Well, now. Get to work, people. Let's decipher this great mystery and see what it'll bring us.

**哑谜**：是拯救，还是虚无？\
**Enigma**: Salvation, or oblivion?

他冷笑着离开了，手中还挥舞着那张写着咒文的纸条。\
He leaves sneering, waving the note with the phonetic spelling in his hand.

这场闹剧溅起的水花逐渐平息。\
The farce is finally over. The room is at peace again.

破译小组的成员们凝重地望向总负责人，似乎在等待一个结论。\
The cryptography team turns to the robot, awaiting her instructions.

**露西**：继续破译。\
**Lucy**: Return to your stations, please.

**露西**：在穷尽所有可能性之前，我们不能断言这份免疫“暴雨”的咒文是无效的。\
**Lucy**: Let us not dismiss its credibility until we have exhausted every possibility.

**露西**：还有——\
**Lucy**: Also ...

她平静地转过头来。\
She calmly turns her head.

**露西**：把阿德勒·霍夫曼加在破译组的名单上。\
**Lucy**: Add Adler Hofmann into the cryptography team roster.

破译组长的电路波动了一瞬。然后，它快步追出了门，紧随着它新上任的组员离开。\
The cryptography lead hesitates for a moment, surprised. Nevertheless, he nods and quickly leaves the room.

墙上的内线电话响了。\
The phone on the wall, used for internal communication, begins to ring.

**联络员Ⅰ**：你好，这里是“暴雨”观测与研究中心。\
**Liaison Staff I**: "Storm" Observation and Research Center.

**联络员Ⅰ**：……明白了，我会转达露西女士。\
**Liaison Staff I**: Noted. I will make sure Ms. Lucy is aware of that.

联络员放下了电话，以某种征询的表情望向总负责人。她年轻的脸上有一丝微末的惊慌。\
The liaison puts down the phone and turns to the robot, a flicker of panic on her face.

**露西**：发生什么事了？\
**Lucy**: What is the matter?

**联络员Ⅰ**：是康复中心的电话，关于之前重塑面具的研究……\
**Liaison Staff I**: It's a call from the rehab center, about the previous study on the Manus mask.

**联络员Ⅰ**：……女士，我想您最好亲自去看一看。\
**Liaison Staff I**: Ma'am, I think you should go see this in person.

剧情场景-康复中心走廊

**助理希曼**：……好的，马修研究员。现在请告诉我们，你还听到了什么？\
**Assistant Simone**: Very good, Matthew. Now tell us, what did you hear?

狭窄的走廊外站满了警卫。\
The already narrow corridor is now filled with security guards.

这是警备级别最高的一间病房，和病患的一切交流都需隔着钢化加固的三层玻璃进行。\
The room they're guarding is heavily secured, isolated behind three layers of tempered glass.

病房中坐着一个男人，一个戴着面具的男人。\
A patient sits in the room with a mask on his face.

**研究员Ⅰ**：那些声音——那些几不可闻的呢喃，那些嗡嗡的、蠕动的、可怕的耳语，一直在我脑子里！\
**Researcher I**: Voices, those voices! The inaudible murmurs, the frightening whispers, they worm into my ears!

**研究员Ⅰ**：我告诉过你们，我写下过它们！可你们认为我只是罹患“狂躁症”的疾病……哈，哈哈哈哈！\
**Researcher I**: I told you before. I wrote about this before! But you dismissed them as manic episodes. Haha, hahahaha!

**助理希曼**：所以你戴上了面具？\
**Assistant Simone**: Did you put on the mask?

**研究员Ⅰ**：是的，我总得证实我的猜想！\
**Researcher I**: Yes. How else would I know that I was right?

**研究员Ⅰ**：——现在好了，我从未听得这么清楚过，那些声音就在我的脑仁里叫嚣，就在这儿！\
**Researcher I**: And now I know! And never have I heard them so clearly. They are screaming inside my head!

**研究员Ⅰ**：它诱惑我，给予我承诺，代价是把脑子抛在后头！聆听那位仁慈的、独一无二的母亲的声音！\
**Researcher I**: Their temptations, their promises! I just have to let go of my brain. Can you hear it? The benevolent Mother is speaking!

研究员的手指用力地掐紧自己的皮肉，似乎在克制某种冲动。\
His nails dig deep into his palms, as if fighting an overwhelming impulse.

**研究员Ⅰ**：我笃定我现在能写出一篇最棒的论文！\
**Researcher I**: Now, I can write the ultimate paper!

**助理希曼**：“母亲”指的是？\
**Assistant Simone**: Who is this "Mother"?

玻璃被猛地拍响了。研究员惊恐地张开嘴，徒劳地在光滑的镜面玻璃上磨砺指甲。\
She is answered by a loud crash. The researcher throws himself against the glass, gasping in horror and scratching helplessly at the surface.

**研究员Ⅰ**：不，我不能再说了！它们注意到我了，它们朝着这儿过来了——\
**Researcher I**: No, I can't say any more! They see me. They've come for me.

**研究员Ⅰ**：——你们得立刻杀了我！\
**Researcher I**: Kill me! Kill me now!

告诫已经太晚，男人的脑袋在玻璃之后突兀地炸开了。\
It is too late to beg for mercy. His scream is abruptly silenced as his head explodes open behind the glass barrier.

鲜血和脑浆溅在了刚刚加固的玻璃上，一个新生者自他的躯体中出现。\
Amidst the splatter of blood and brain, a new being emerges from the remnants of his flesh.

**重塑·门徒**：ㄏㄡˇ——！\
**Manus Follower**: *roar*

尖锐的警报声响了起来。

那里，还在敲击着玻璃的已是那手持三角铁的门徒。他的口中哀鸣不止，犹如新生儿发出第一道啼哭。\
The alarm blares loudly.

剧情场景-康复中心走廊\
A Manus follower wriggles up from the bloody floor, holding a triangle in hand. He lets out a loud cry, reminiscent of a newborn's first wail.

伴着玻璃的钝响声，助理结束了内线通讯，望向站在旁边的总负责人。\
The liaison ends the call, cutting off the horrid sounds on the other end of the phone.

**露西**：立刻终止对重塑之手面具的一切研究，这一方向的危害程度已经超过了其潜在价值。\
**Lucy**: Suspend all research on the Manus mask at once. Its dangers far outweigh the potential benefits.

**露西**：永久封存所有相关用具，并将本次事件的脱敏信息通报全员，以防再出现研究员私自佩戴它的情况。\
**Lucy**: Seal away all equipment and share only a controlled account of the incident with others. We cannot afford to have another researcher try on the mask again.

**露西**：——然后，清理现场。\
**Lucy**: Now. Clean this up.

**拉普拉斯安全员**：收到。\
**Laplace Safety Officer**: Yes, ma'am.

随着气密门的开启，一队装备齐全的警卫冒着催眠烟雾冲进房间。\
The airlock door hisses open, a squad of armed guards storms into the room under the cover of sleeping gas.

镜面玻璃的另一侧，机器背过身去，将头脑中又一堆标记着“‘暴雨’研究”的数据归入了废弃区域。\
On the other side of the glass, the robot turns away from the scene, categorizing yet another set of "Storm" research data as irrelevant and filing it away as waste in her memory.

**露西**：嗯。\
**Lucy**: Hm.

**露西**：又一个完全错误的方向。\
**Lucy**: Another dead end.

## 7TH-06 傲慢与偏见 / Pride and Prejudice

一段意义不明的咒文。\
An unknown incantation.

一个被证实相当有害的面具。\
A mask that has proven to be extremely dangerous.

这就是当前“暴雨”研究的全部对象。\
These are the only leads they currently have on the "Storm."

**露西**：……\
**Lucy**: ...

钢铁拼接的手拿起了一叠文件。\
Her metallic fingers pick up another stack of files.

那是先前针对重塑面具的化验报告，它证实并记录了“非对称核素R”的存在。\
These are the test results of the Manus mask, confirming the presence of asymmetrical nuclide R.

机器望着它，条屏若有所思地闪了闪。\
The robot studies them carefully. The slit on her face pulses in contemplation.

**露西**：希曼，委托给司辰的采样工作有进展吗？\
**Lucy**: What is the status of the sampling, Simone? Any updates from the Timekeeper?

**助理希曼**：暂时没有。因为岛民对基金会的不信任，自上次收集到一管样品后，司辰一直没能找到第二个独立行动的时机。\
**Assistant Simone**: For the moment, no. The people on the island are still suspicious of the Foundation's motives, so she hasn't had a second chance to collect any samples.

**助理希曼**：不过，在一个小时前的最后一次通讯里，她提到自己将再度前往地底。\
**Assistant Simone**: But she has called in an hour ago. We were informed that she will return to the cave shortly.

**助理希曼**：另外，她特意提醒我们，小岛免疫“暴雨”的区域发生了衰减，幸存区似乎不是绝对的。\
**Assistant Simone**: She also warned us that the immunity zone on the island appears to be shrinking. The safe zone is not stable.

**露西**：……嗯。\
**Lucy**: Hm.

机器今日并未装配表情，助理只能从那道条屏中判断总负责人的心境。\
The robot did not put on a face today. Simone can only read her mood from the narrow slit.

**助理希曼**：……您有什么发现吗？\
**Assistant Simone**: Ma'am, have you noticed something?

**露西**：不相干，希曼。\
**Lucy**: They are unrelated, Simone.

**露西**：面具和咒文是不相干的，尽管它们都来自于重塑之手。\
**Lucy**: The mask and the incantation are indeed related to Manus Vindictae, but they are unrelated to each other.

她将眼前已被封存的重塑面具移到一边。\
She moves the sealed Manus mask aside.

**露西**：假设维也纳调查员传回的一切报告为真，那这里有一个显著的疑问。\
**Lucy**: If the account of the Vienna investigator is correct, one cannot help but question:

**露西**：——阿尔卡纳为何不直接分发面具给伊索尔德和她的兄长？\
**Lucy**: Why would Arcana not simply give the masks to Isolde and her brother?

**助理希曼**：……马库斯调查员传回的报告是非常不完整的，我们很难据此推断当时的实际情况。\
**Assistant Simone**: Investigator Marcus's report was highly lacking, making it challenging for us to infer what truly happened.

**露西**：噢，我想“报告不完整”是个无用的假设。因为我们只能依据已知的信息做出推断。\
**Lucy**: I suppose we can be skeptical that the report is incomplete. But it is all we have for now.

**露西**：实际上，她很好地完成了工作。\
**Lucy**: She did a good job. I could not have asked for more.

**露西**：我们都听到了那句话：“一个古老的奇迹，一个拯救的魔圈。”\
**Lucy**: We all heard it. "An ancient miracle, a circle of salvation."

机器伸出手，在空中画下了一个相似的圆圈。\
The robot extends her hand, drawing an imaginary circle in the air.

**露西**：重塑之手的领袖要展示奇迹——面具并不算一个奇迹。\
**Lucy**: The leader of Manus Vindictae promised a miracle, but the mask is far from it.

**露西**：它只是一个工具，用来控制和挑选那些已经臣服的信众。马修用他自己为我们证明了这一点。\
**Lucy**: The mask is a tool of control, designed to identify and enslave the believers. Matthew has demonstrated its effects for us.

**露西**：但这个术式不一样。\
**Lucy**: But this ritual is different.

**助理希曼**：……您是说，这个术式也许是比面具更加深奥的存在？\
**Assistant Simone**: Do you mean the ritual is more sophisticated than the mask?

机器赞许地点了点头。\
The robot nods approvingly.

**露西**：或许如此，但也并非绝对。\
**Lucy**: Perhaps, but it is not entirely definitive.

**露西**：维也纳的调查员卓越地完成了任务。面具已被证实没有研究价值，免疫“暴雨”只是它诸多功能中一个甜蜜的诱饵。\
**Lucy**: The investigators in Vienna completed their mission spectacularly, and now Matthew has proven that the mask is useless for our purposes. Its immunity was only a cover for its other functions.

**露西**：它的副作用巨大且不可消除。即使我们解明了原理，也无法将重塑之手的手段用诸于全部同僚。\
**Lucy**: And the mask has powerful and irreversible side effects. Even if we find out how it protects the wearer from the "Storm," we cannot use it on our colleagues.

总负责人拿起那张并不很长的纸条。\
She picks up the scrip.

**露西**：如果这条咒语被证实为真……\
**Lucy**: If this incantation is verified to be true,

**露西**：——那么它就是普罗米修斯窃取的火种本身。\
**Lucy**: it will be our Promethean fire.

**哑谜**：这个术式是没用的。\
**Enigma**: This ritual is useless to us.

**哑谜**：不要再白费力气了，这么解下去是不会有什么结果的。\
**Enigma**: Save yourself the trouble. We're not getting anywhere with this.

**破译组长**：——什么？\
**Cryptography Lead**: What?

各式仪器堆满了房间。\
The room is cluttered with all sorts of sophisticated equipment.

模拟答案的稿纸从桌上一路积压到地上，研究员们已许久没从书堆中抬起头来。\
The floor is littered with scrap paper. The researchers haven't lifted their heads or taken a break for quite some time.

破译组长拿着刚泡好的咖啡，感到某根电路正无声地在脑中熔断。\
The cryptography lead stares at Enigma, a fresh cup of coffee in his hand. His patience is wearing thin as the metaphorical string labeled "tolerance" in his mind is finally about to snap.

**破译组长**：什么意思，阿德勒？什么叫这个术式是错的？\
**Cryptography Lead**: Explain yourself, Adler. What do you mean the ritual is useless?

**破译组长**：伙计，你才在椅子上坐下了几分钟？我刚泡的咖啡都还没凉——\
**Cryptography Lead**: You barely sat down! My coffee's still hot!

密码专家阴沉地拿起一叠纸，将它强行塞到了组长的怀里。\
The cryptographer solemnly hands the lead a stack of papers from his desk.

**哑谜**：我不需要浪费时间研究，这是很简单的逻辑推断。\
**Enigma**: I don't need to waste any more time. It's simple logic.

**哑谜**：现有的信息并不支持密码学上的破译。我们所做的只是在浩瀚如烟的典籍中穷举，试图找出它是哪一种语言或密文。\
**Enigma**: The current information is insufficient for cryptographic decryption. We're attempting an exhaustive brute force, comparing every ancient text and record to find the language or corresponding text. It's like looking for a needle in a colossal haystack.

**哑谜**：然而，即使我们侥幸地匹配上，也没有人能够验证它。研究是不可能从这个方向上突破的——\
**Enigma**: Even if we stumble onto a match, none of us can validate such a thing. A breakthrough in this regard is simply not possible—

**研究员Ⅱ**：是吗？\
**Researcher II**: You can't be serious.

有人推开了桌子，从房间的另一头站了起来，手里还紧紧地握着一支圆珠笔。\
Across the room, a man stands up abruptly from his chair, clenching a pen in his hand.

**研究员Ⅱ**：——你用什么做出的论断？你解明这个咒语的运作原理了吗？\
**Researcher II**: And what is the basis of your reasoning? Have you figured out the mechanics behind the ritual?

**哑谜**：我不需要理解神秘学，这只是最基础的推理。它……\
**Enigma**: I didn't need to understand the intricacies of arcanum to deduce this. It was simple log- ...

**研究员Ⅱ**：所以你甚至没有试图去理解它。仅仅是从自己高贵的人类逻辑出发，就否定了我们所有人的努力。\
**Researcher II**: So you never even tried to understand it. With your supposedly superior human reasoning, you dismissed all of our dedication and hard work, just like that.

**研究员Ⅱ**：——你以为你是谁？\
**Researcher II**: Who the f*** do you think you are!?

没给所有人反应时间。研究员径直冲到哑谜的面前，狠狠给了他一拳。\
Before anyone can react, the researcher lunges at Enigma and punches him right in the face.

**哑谜**：……啊？\
**Enigma**: Wh—?

哑谜错愕地抬起手，捂住火辣辣的脸颊，表情比起愤怒毋宁说是震惊。\
Enigma brings a hand up to his cheek, looking more confused than angry.

**研究员Ⅱ**：马修说得对，你们这些傲慢的呆子、白痴、蠢货、傻瓜——\
**Researcher II**: Matthew was right. You arrogant fools, clueless morons!

**研究员Ⅱ**：我受够你们这些自以为是的人类中心主义者了，给我下地狱去吧！\
**Researcher II**: Get out of my face, you humanocentric narcissist. Go to hell!

研究员怒吼着砍来，将圆珠笔挥出了博伊刀的气势。\
The researcher snarls, brandishing his pen like a soldier brandishing a dagger.

囿于科研工作者的宿疾，他挥了空。\
Much to his frustration, his swing loses power mid-air—another casualty of the neck and shoulder pain that plagues this office.

哑谜堪堪躲过了这一袭击，他的神情只剩下了茫然。\
Enigma narrowly avoids the attack, bewildered by the turn of events.

**哑谜**：有必要这样吗？我只是告诉你我的成果——\
**Enigma**: Was this really necessary? I was just sharing my conclusion.

**破译组长**：该死，是重塑面具的影响！我该想到的，他和马修是同一个实验室的研究员，他之前也一定接触过面具——\
**Cryptography Lead**: Ugh, it was the mask! I should've thought of that. He worked in the same lab as Matthew, and he must've been exposed to the mask.

**哑谜**：但这不合理啊！威廉姆斯的指标一直很正常，这副作用还有潜伏期吗？！\
**Enigma**: But his physical exam seemed fine. Is there an incubation period!?

**破译组长**：他都在你面前发疯了，你还在乎什么合不合理？！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Does he seem fine to you now? Huh?

**破译组长**：不，威廉姆斯，放下那台康威V代自动机！那是“暴雨”发生后全球仅剩的一台了！！\
**Cryptography Lead**: No, Williams, put that down! That's the only Conway Automaton V left after the "Storm"!

回应它的是：一句怒吼、一阵短促的风声、金属和墙壁的碰撞声。\
He is met with a guttural growl, followed by the deafening crash of metal against wall.

那台机器贴着它的头顶飞了过去，在墙上摔了个稀巴烂。\
The machine whizzes past his head and shatters to pieces on impact.

破译组长头痛欲裂，它挣扎着冲到了门口，按下了墙上硕大的红色按钮。\
The cryptography lead can feel his sanity teetering on the brink. He staggers towards the door, frantically smacking the big red button on the wall.

**破译组长**：——警卫！警卫！我们需要帮助！！！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Security! Security! We've got a code red!!!

**露西**：所以，这会给破译工作带来什么影响？\
**Lucy**: So, what are the implications for the decryption?

**破译组长**：……没有产生预期以外的影响。我们及时制伏了威廉姆斯，而且他砸的那台康威V代自动机本来也派不上用场。\
**Cryptography Lead**: There were no unintended consequences. We were able to control Williams in time, and the Conway Automaton V he destroyed wasn't useful to our work anyway.

**露西**：喔，很高兴你们最小化了损失。\
**Lucy**: I am glad you kept the damages to a minimum.

露西合上了手里的装置电脑，转过身来。\
Lucy turns off the screen in front of her and turns around.

**露西**：鉴于你还站在这里，我是否可以认为，你打算进一步向我汇报工作，乌尔里希先生？\
**Lucy**: Since you are still here, Mr. Ulrich, I take it as a sign that you have more to report?

走廊上的一角，一场控诉正蓄势待发。\
In a secluded area of the hallway, an emotionally charged complaint is about to take place.

破译组长的声音压得很低。经历了之前的混乱，它看起来十分狼狈。\
The cryptography lead tries to keep his voice low, looking completely disheveled from the turmoil he has just endured.

**破译组长**：……威廉姆斯是一个意外，比他更不可控的是阿德勒，我必须向您说明他的问题。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Williams was merely an accident, ma'am, but Adler is a loose cannon on the team. We need to talk about this.

**破译组长**：很抱歉，直到现在，我依旧不明白为何您要让他加入。\
**Cryptography Lead**: With all due respect, I still don't understand why you put him on the team.

**破译组长**：也许他确实为科算中心做出了卓越的贡献。但那是八年前的事了。现在他不只是该死的失败主义者，还是个坚定的人类主义者。\
**Cryptography Lead**: He may have made his contributions to Laplace, but that was eight years ago. Now he's just an irritating defeatist and a staunch supporter of humanocentrism.

磁流体恼怒不已地闪烁着，没留意到自己的情绪正在勇攀高峰。\
Every particle of ferrofluid in his helmet is vibrating with rage, his voice rising involuntarily.

**破译组长**：他从不理解神秘学，也从未尝试过理解它。直到现在还试图活在“暴雨”前的世界里，不愿接受他熟悉的旧世界已经变为一滩油污！\
**Cryptography Lead**: He never understood the arcanum, or tried. He's still stuck in the time before the first "Storm" and refuses to acknowledge that his small, beautiful world is gone!

**破译组长**：这样的人对术式破译能有什么帮助？\
**Cryptography Lead**: How can someone like that help us?

这样的质问通常源于怀疑、压力，还有诸多复杂的因素。于是露西停顿了一下，像是在思考一个有意义的回答。\
The robot senses his doubt and frustration—there may be more sentiments and underlying issues at play. She pauses for a moment before answering, as if deep in thought.

**露西**：噢，所以阿德勒·霍夫曼研究员并没有丧失行动能力。\
**Lucy**: I understand your concern, but I have not heard anything about the incapacitation of Adler Hofmann.

**破译组长**：什么？……当然，他只是挨了一拳，最多破了点皮。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Incapaci—What? He got a few scratches at most. The guy barely touched him.

**露西**：很好，那你还要和我汇报什么？\
**Lucy**: So he is fine. I am glad we agree. Is there anything else you would like to report?

**破译组长**：……\
**Cryptography Lead**: ...

机器等待了5秒，对方没有做出应答。\
The robot waits 5 seconds for an answer. But there isn't one.

她将之视为一个可以进入“回复”阶段的信号。\
This must be the social cue that it is her turn to speak.

**露西**：正因为不理解神秘学，他才能用人类的思维去看待神秘术的效用，让研究沿着我们需要的方向前进。\
**Lucy**: His lack of knowledge on arcanum is exactly why we need him. His human perspective will offer valuable insights on arcane rituals.

**露西**：——这个术式后续的应用不能只局限于神秘学家的范畴。\
**Lucy**: The results of this study will not only be used to save arcanists,

**露西**：因为我们要拯救的不仅是神秘学家，还有同样在这个世界上生活着的人类。\
**Lucy**: but also humans who share the same world with us.

破译组长显然还想再说什么，但机器已经回答完了问题。\
The cryptography lead tries to argue further, but Lucy is certain the issue has been sufficiently addressed.

**露西**：我们的时间有限，先生，而你只关乎私人恩怨和族群冲突的报告已经占用了我2分37秒的时间。\
**Lucy**: We are racing against the clock, mister, and your report on personal disputes and racial conflicts has wasted 2 minutes and 37 seconds of our time.

**露西**：如果他不配合工作，你有权将他踢出破译组，这是你的职责。\
**Lucy**: If he refuses to cooperate, you have every right to remove him from the team. That is your responsibility.

**露西**：——喔。\
**Lucy**: Oh.

被提到名字的组员从走廊拐角处走了过来。他脸色发青，眉头紧皱，手中还紧紧攥着一摞演算纸。\
From the other end of the corridor, the subject of their argument approaches, looking deeply upset and clutching a stack of papers.

显然，他聆听了这场争论的全程。\
Clearly, he has heard every word they just said.

**露西**：很高兴看到你的确没有丧失行动能力，阿德勒研究员。\
**Lucy**: I am relieved that you survived your altercation.

**露西**：——你想要汇报什么？\
**Lucy**: What would you like to report?

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

**破译组长**：……\
**Cryptography Lead**: ...

组长和组员的目光不期而遇地在空中交汇，为双方的职场生涯带来毁灭性的尴尬一秒。\
Their eyes meet, making both of them squirm uncomfortably. This is undoubtedly one of the most awkward moments in both of their careers.

最后，是乌尔里希率先迈开了离开的脚步。\
After a prolonged silence, Ulrich steps back and walks away.

哑谜没有再回头确认这一点。他压低声音，开始了自己的汇报。\
Without even looking back at him, Enigma begins his report in a low voice.

**哑谜**：我已经受够了在无望的方向上浪费时间，女士。先前面具研究的失败已经让太多同僚发了疯。\
**Enigma**: I'm fed up with wasting time, ma'am. The setback with the mask has already driven too many people insane.

**哑谜**：——所以您最好看看这个。\
**Enigma**: That's why you should take a look at this.

他递上了那叠文件。\
He hands the stack of files to Lucy.

**哑谜**：我在逻辑上证明了当前的研究是无意义的，咒语的长度不足以支持密码学上的破译。\
**Enigma**: I can logically deduce that our current direction is another dead end. The incantation isn't long enough for cryptographic decryption.

**哑谜**：我们只能寄希望于典籍。也许某本古老的手抄本里、遗迹的石碑上、某个强大神秘学家的记忆中，有类似语言的记录。\
**Enigma**: We will have to turn to ancient records. Perhaps we'll find something in age-old manuscripts, in tablet inscriptions, or in the memories of powerful arcanists.

**哑谜**：可即使找到了，我们也无法证实——因为我们中没有人会使用这个术式。\
**Enigma**: But even if we find it, we can't validate it because none of us can cast the skill.

机器正仔细地查阅着文件，没有打断他的失败主义发言。\
The robot remains silent during his pessimistic remarks, flipping through each page of the file.

**哑谜**：低阶的神秘学家无法使用高阶的神秘术，即使他们完全清楚每个字母的念法、每个单词的含义。\
**Enigma**: Low-ranking arcanists can't cast high-ranking skills, even if they know the exact pronunciation and meaning of the incantation.

**哑谜**：灵知即是如此不讲道理。它依赖于直觉领略，而非更有迹可循的智力理解。它取决于个人经验和能力的参差，也没有普遍推广性。\
**Enigma**: Gnosis is beyond reason like that and cannot be debated. It stems from raw intuition rather than logic and intellect, is shaped by personal experiences and natural abilities, and cannot be intentionally replicated.

**哑谜**：或者让我说得更直接一些——它取决于血统的纯度。\
**Enigma**: And the most determining factor—it relies on the arcanist's purity of blood.

**哑谜**：而您指望的这个术式，这句据说能创造奇迹的咒语。它来自重塑之手的领袖，一个能力完全在我们认知范围外的纯血神秘学家。\
**Enigma**: The miracle ritual you hold such hopes for belongs to the leader of Manus Vindictae, a pure-blooded arcanist whose power is beyond our imagination.

**哑谜**：就像是让一个幼儿园的孩子去回答哥德巴赫猜想，这个难题早就超出了我们所有人的能力限度！\
**Enigma**: It's like asking a toddler to solve Goldbach's conjecture. It's completely beyond the boundaries of our limits!

**露西**：但你不是神秘学家。\
**Lucy**: But you are not an arcanist.

**露西**：你为什么要在意他们的规则？\
**Lucy**: Why should you play by their rules?

**哑谜**：…………\
**Enigma**: ...

男人被噎住了，他没有想到这番陈辞会引来这样的反问。\
The man is taken aback by her question. It's something he's never considered before.

**露西**：神秘学家的确存在神秘术运用上的巨大差距，这和他们的血统有关。\
**Lucy**: You are right. Arcanists differ due to their purity of blood.

**露西**：关于这一点，兔毛手袋研究员已经给我提交了一份详细的报告，论证了血统纯度和施术能力的线性关系，并发表了比你过激十倍的批判性言论。\
**Lucy**: Researcher Medicine Pocket has already reported the linear correlation between the bloodline of an arcanist and their abilities, and has drawn a conclusion ten times more extreme.

**哑谜**：……那您应该接受，这是它的专业领域。\
**Enigma**: Then you should listen. That's their area of expertise.

机器人转动了一下脖子——也许这可以被称为“摇头”。\
Her neck moves subtly, almost like shaking her head.

**露西**：破译小组的成员没有能力检验这个术式，我们完全清楚这一点。\
**Lucy**: We know that our cryptographers do not have the power to validate the ritual.

**露西**：但我也不期望你们立即检验它——而是仅仅去构想实践该目标的可能性，作为一个小组。\
**Lucy**: And we do not expect you to do that. All I ask of you is to come up with a feasible plan, and to do it as a team.

现在再说小组合作有些迟了，哑谜只是把头撇向了一边。\
Enigma turns away, repulsed at the mention of "team."

露西看完了哑谜提交的报告，将它还给了对方。\
Lucy finishes reading the report and hands it back to him.

**露西**：你的推断的确符合逻辑，但它没有实际作用。\
**Lucy**: Your deduction is logical, but not practical or actionable.

**露西**：——因此，我想我最好还是把它还给你。\
**Lucy**: So I should return this to you.

**哑谜**：……什么？\
**Enigma**: What?

闪烁的条屏像机械脸上的一个模糊的微笑。\
The glow in her eye slit is strangely reassuring, almost like a smile.

她抬头望向窗外。\
She looks out of the window.

**露西**：我很欣赏你特有的逻辑思维能力，阿德勒研究员。但这不代表你一定要受限于此。\
**Lucy**: Your logic is impressive, Adler. But do not let it limit your thinking.

**露西**：你说到神秘学家的能力限度——逻辑也有它的限度，不是吗？\
**Lucy**: You spoke of the boundaries of arcane power, but logic has its limits too, no?

**露西**：获得知识的路径有许多种。直觉的洞悉，逻辑的觉察，经验的推演，他人的传授。\
**Lucy**: Knowledge can be obtained through various means, such as intuition, logical reasoning, empirical observations, and teachings from others.

**露西**：你们不是这条道路上唯一的求证小组。如果你们失败了，还有其他人。如果这个方向不行，还有下一个。这次“暴雨”不行，还有下一次。\
**Lucy**: Your team is not the only one cracking the ritual through their own means. If you fail, we will turn to the others. And if that approach is wrong, we will try another. If no solution is found before the "Storm," we will simply wait for the next one.

**露西**：重要的是，我们必须前进，不计代价地前进。我们必须找到那条行之有效的道路——不然只能任由这场雨将我们冲刷。\
**Lucy**: What matters is we keep moving forward, no matter the cost. We must keep to the path, or we will be swept away like dust in the rain.

研究员罕见地沉默了。\
For once, the researcher does not argue.

而后，他喃喃地开口了，近乎自言自语。\
He whispers, as if talking to himself.

**哑谜**：……即使失败了，也还有其他人。\
**Enigma**: If one team fails, you can still turn to the others.

**哑谜**：那为什么偏偏是格蕾塔？\
**Enigma**: Then why? Why did it have to be Greta?

**露西**：……什么？\
**Lucy**: What?

**哑谜**：……没什么，只是一个不合逻辑的无效问题。\
**Enigma**: Forget it. Just a bitter, irrational thought.

**哑谜**：我的尝试到此为止了，希望您的“其他人”能有所突破。\
**Enigma**: This marks the end of my efforts. Hopefully, "the others" will bring you the needed breakthroughs.

男人饱含怒气地离开了。\
The man walks away in anger.

而后，他突然想到一个问题。\
But after only a few steps, a question comes to mind.

**哑谜**：——您一直在这儿等待什么？\
**Enigma**: You've been waiting here for a while. Are you expecting someone?

**哑谜**：您不是会浪费时间聆听下属抱怨的人，这里一定有什么是值得您关注的。\
**Enigma**: You aren't the type to waste time listening to us whine, so there must be something here worthy of your attention.

**哑谜**：——是有人已经接近成功了吗？\
**Enigma**: Is someone close to a breakthrough?

**露西**：噢，没有你想得那么复杂。\
**Lucy**: Nothing of the sort.

**露西**：我只是在充电，这里有一个公共的电源插头，先生。\
**Lucy**: I am recharging. We have a public power outlet here.

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

她活动了一下金属的关节。\
She moves her joints as if standing for so long has stiffened her body.

**露西**：不过我的确也在等待。\
**Lucy**: But I am indeed waiting.

**露西**：——白色石屋的鸽子，它们飞来了。\
**Lucy**: The doves of the White Stone House are here.

振翅声自空中传来。\
The sound of flapping wings fills the air.

在研究员惊愕的目光中，那石膏质感的造物停留在了钢铁的指尖上。\
The researcher is astonished as the creature, with a texture similar to plaster, perches on her metal finger.

**露西**：很好。\
**Lucy**: Good.

**露西**：——更接近限度之人向我们提供了帮助。\
**Lucy**: Someone closer to the "limit" has given us aid.

## 7TH-07 米诺陶迷宫 / Maze of The Minotaur

**红弩箭**：芝诺那边的答复如何？\
**Lilya**: Any news from Zeno?

剧情场景-岛屿-传道者之厅外-天色差分（是一个比较独特的光线，比如玫瑰紫）

**十四行诗**：接应的步骤正有序进行，他们会在两小时内完成部署。\
**Sonetto**: They are moving as planned. The deployment will be complete within two hours.

**十四行诗**：……阿尔卡纳有什么动作吗？\
**Sonetto**: What about Arcana?

**红弩箭**：老样子，像块蓝黑色的礁石，站在海角上吹咸风。\
**Lilya**: Same old. Standing still on the rock as if she's a part of it. Soaking up the salt in the wind, I guess.

十四行诗调整了一下通讯器的位置，让输出设备中红弩箭的声音更加清晰。\
Sonetto fiddles with the communication device, making sure Lilya's voice is loud and clear.

现在站在一旁的星锑也可以听得清楚了。\
Now Regulus can hear their exchange with perfect clarity.

**红弩箭**：——她可真会挑地方。在岛屿视野最好的高地，从这儿看，我们所有人的动向在她眼中一览无遗。\
**Lilya**: She's found herself a good spot, overlooking all of us from up there.

**红弩箭**：无论是那些数字人前往的岛屿中心，还是维尔汀和37她们进入的洞穴入口，亦或是被“暴雨”影响的沙滩和海岸……尽收眼底。\
**Lilya**: The center of the island where the "number people" are heading, the entrance to the cave where Vertin and 37 are going, and the beaches in the "Storm" ... Nothing escapes her sight.

**星锑**：喔！也许她只是在规划逃跑路线呢？\
**Regulus**: Ha! Impressive! Maybe she's planning her escape?

**红弩箭**：啊哈，如果哪天我们和重塑之手举办游泳竞技赛，我一定推荐你参加，星锑。\
**Lilya**: Is she also going to swim? Hah, it seems like we're in for a swimming competition.

**红弩箭**：——让“乌龟”游得快一点儿，以上是我衷心的建议。\
**Lilya**: Speaking of which, it would be nice if those "tortoise" slowpokes could swim a little faster!

通讯结束了，飞行女巫的注意力回到了监视任务中。\
She hangs up and resumes surveillance of her target.

这注定是人人自危的两小时。\
The next two hours are critical.

岛民们正在筹备自救的净化仪式，外来者则在做撤离前的最后准备。\
The islanders are busy with the cleansing ceremony, while the outsiders are preparing for their departure.

**星锑**：唔，十四行诗，我已经明白你们的计划了。\
**Regulus**: Look, Sonetto, I understand your plan now.

**星锑**：但我还是有点儿——呃，我是说，有一点点担心……\
**Regulus**: But I still can't shake off a bad feeling about all this.

**十四行诗**：别担心，星锑，我们已经练习了很多次。\
**Sonetto**: Don't worry, Regulus. We have gone over this many times.

**十四行诗**：误差在0.00025%以下，我有成功的信心。\
**Sonetto**: The margin of error should be below 0.00025%. I'm confident that it will work.

**星锑**：我知道，我知道！我相信你，我不需要这么详细的数字！\
