**Regulus**: I know, I know! Spare me with the numbers. I know I can rely on you!

数字过敏者飞快地摆手，试图把那一串漂浮的零从自己的大脑中轰出去。\
She waves her hand quickly, as if swatting away the numbers like flies.

**星锑**：——我担心的是维尔汀。两个小时足够她从地底返回吗？\
**Regulus**: I'm still worried about Vertin. Will she make it back in two hours?

**星锑**：如果她没有及时回来，我们就得自己掌舵了，是这样吧？\
**Regulus**: If she doesn't come back in time, who's going to take charge and guide us? We'll have to steer our own course, won't we?

**十四行诗**：是的。\
**Sonetto**: Yes.

十四行诗严谨地点了点头。\
Sonetto nods.

**十四行诗**：科算中心正在搜集一切和“暴雨”有关的线索，非对称核素R已经是一个了不起的突破。\
**Sonetto**: Laplace is gathering every piece of information they can find on the "Storm." The discovery of the asymmetrical nuclide R was already a remarkable breakthrough.

**十四行诗**：如果司辰在洞穴能有新的发现，我想也一定会对科算中心的免疫“暴雨”研究有所帮助。\
**Sonetto**: It would help the immunity research a lot if the Timekeeper could find something useful in that cave.

对摇滚海盗来说，这番官方回答收效甚微。很显然，她还是更愿意相信自己的经验。\
The pirate is not satisfied with the answer. Evidently, she has a strong opinion on the matter.

**星锑**：唔，我对那地方可没有什么好的回忆。\
**Regulus**: Hmm. I don't think she's going to have a lovely time there, judging by what happened to me last time.

——作为待在地下时间最久的人，她无疑拥有这份发言权。\
Having spent the longest time there, she's undoubtedly the most qualified to comment on the subject.

**星锑**：这仪式压根全是疑点！先不说风险，光是这个“通过试炼的人就能得到任何一个问题的解答”的说法……\
**Regulus**: Is it just me, or do you also find this a bit fishy? The dangers aside, using an "answer" as a reward?

**星锑**：难道他们崇奉的这个“无线电者”，是一台自动答录机吗？\
**Regulus**: What?! Is this deity some sort of answering machine?

**APPLe**：实际上，无限定者是古希腊哲学家阿那克西曼德提出的一个哲学概念，用来指代世界的“本源”。\
**APPLe**: In fact, Apeiron is a philosophical concept introduced by the ancient Greek philosopher Anaximander, which means "the origin of everything."

**APPLe**：它是不定和无限制的物质实在，万物产生于它，也复归于它。\
**APPLe**: It is the physical manifestation of the "boundless," the "indeterminate," and the "infinite." Everything arises from it and returns to it.

**APPLe**：不过在这座岛屿的教众心中，它似乎有更实际的含义。\
**APPLe**: But it appears to serve a more practical purpose for the believers on this island.

**十四行诗**：我咨询过玛尔塔女士。她告诉我，即使是用最接近本质的“数字”，人们能获取的知识也终究是有限度的。\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Marta told me about this. There are limits to the knowledge one can acquire, even when using "numbers," which are considered closest to the essence.

**十四行诗**：而无限定者是无边界、无限制的存在。要获得超越自身限度的知识，就需要求得祂的帮助。\
**Sonetto**: But Apeiron is a boundless, limitless existence. If we wish to seek knowledge beyond our own limitations, we must turn to It for help.

公认的好学生正认真回忆着从教典中听来的内容。\
She faithfully recites what she learned from the teachings of Apeiron.

APPLe抖了抖领结，似乎很赞同她及时的补充。\
APPLe adjusts his bow tie, grateful for her contribution.

**APPLe**：依据APPLe某所知，越是古老、定义模糊、不可查鉴的特殊存在，便越有可能拥有难被证实的神秘学能量。\
**APPLe**: To the best of this APPLe's recollection, the more ancient, abstract, and intangible an entity is, the more likely it possesses arcane powers beyond our fathom.

**APPLe**：借由与伟大存在的交感，崇奉者们获取超越性的灵知指引。\
**APPLe**: By communing with the supreme existences through sympathetic magic, worshipers could gain the guidance of their transcendental Gnosis.

**APPLe**：同时，祂们也会从崇奉者身上收取代价。\
**APPLe**: They would, of course, exact a price from the worshipers as well.

**十四行诗**：……代价？\
**Sonetto**: Price?

这一名词令她短暂地错愕。\
Just hearing the word makes her heart sink.

**十四行诗**：APPLe先生，您能说得再详细一点吗？\
**Sonetto**: Could you be more specific on that, Mr. APPLe?

**十四行诗**：——祂们收取的代价，具体是什么？是生命吗？还是……\
**Sonetto**: What's the price? Lives? Or ...

**十四行诗**：其他的东西？\
**Sonetto**: Something else?

剧情场景-黑屏

**37**：维尔汀，跳过来——\
**37**: Vertin, jump over here!

剧情场景-洞穴-迷宫试炼地。一个洞穴场景，类似1.4抽象王国，但是四壁更白，中间有写着数字的透明方块（为四阶幻方），方块散落开来。

**37**：做得好！现在你所在的数字是1——\
**37**: Very good! Now you are on number 1.

**37**：接下来跳到7！这只是个四阶幻方，你只要每四步加起来等于34就好了！\
**37**: And you should jump to 7! This is a 4 by 4 magic square. You just need to make sure every 4 steps you take adds up to 34.

世界在脚下摇摇欲坠，每一步都伴随着踩空的风险。\
Howling wind fills the air. The unstable footing is the only solid thing they can rely on.

前往洞穴深处的道路已不同以往。\
The path into the cave is completely different than before.

透明的无限台阶消失了，也不再有飞舞的金色曲线。目所能及是空旷的四壁，以及脚下写着数字的方砖。\
The transparent stairs are gone, as are the swirling golden lines in the air. Now only cold rock walls surround them, and numbered bricks lie beneath their feet.

这是一个史无前例的跳房子游戏。\
It's a game of hopscotch unlike any other.

**维尔汀**：我不明白，37。上次我和你来到地底时，还不是这样的——\
**Vertin**: I don't understand, 37. This place was different the last time we were here.

**37**：嗯，因为试炼已经开始了！求知的道路总是比起检验更曲折一些。\
**37**: It has changed because the test has begun! The path to new knowledge is always harder than verifying a known result.

**37**：别担心，这就像克里特国王的米诺陶迷宫，我们总会抵达最深处的！\
**37**: Don't worry. This is like a labyrinth with a Minotaur. There is always a way to the center.

**维尔汀**：……但进入米诺陶迷宫的人不都是祭品吗？\
**Vertin**: But weren't those labyrinth walkers offerings to the Minotaur?

可惜，她根本没有在意。\
Unfortunately, she doesn't seem to care or be concerned at all.

**37**：现在我们要完成这个幻方！维尔汀，接下来跳到10——\
**37**: Now we're going to solve the magic square! Vertin, the next number is 10.

——呼！\
Whoosh!

风声从耳边划过，世界在眼前扭曲。\
The world churns around them, a space is revealed.

幻方完成的一刻，迷宫的造型再次改变了。\
As the magic square is solved, the maze shifts once more.

**37**：噢不！它变成幻圆了，我们得重新计算！\
**37**: Oh, no. It turned into a magic circle! We have to calculate again.

**37**：但这也很简单，只需要将每一层圆周上的数字加在一起，使之等于每条直径上的数字与圆心之和。\
**37**: This one's easy. The sum of the numbers on each circle should be equal to the sum of the numbers on its diameter plus the number in the middle.

**37**：只是从方换成了圆，没有什么难的。\
**37**: We're just going from a square to a circle. It's not that difficult.

**37**：现在你站的数字是32，我们需要找到17或者21——\
**37**: You are now on 32. We need to find 17 or 21.

她专注于心算，没有注意到身后的异样。\
Completely absorbed in solving the puzzle, she doesn't notice what's coming up behind her.

写着数字“21”的几何体窃笑着砸了过来，热情的姿态让人想到岛屿上某个21乘以10倍的三位数。\
A geometric figure with the number "21" hurtles toward her. For a moment, she thought she heard it chuckle.

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**维尔汀**：注意安全，37!\
**Vertin**: Careful, 37!

**维尔汀**：这些数字是活的，我们得先把它们复位！\
**Vertin**: The numbers are coming to life. We need to put them back in place!

剧情场景-洞穴-迷宫试炼地中心-幻圆差分，幻圆复位。\
The ground ceases to shake, and everything comes to a standstill once again. The numbers have returned to their original positions.

震动消失了，所有数字都回归了本位。

37蹦蹦跳跳地越过了它们，直奔圆心处的出口。\
37 breezes past them with a cheerful smile, making a beeline for the exit.

**37**：我早说过，这并不耗费什么时间～!\
**37**: Like I said, it's not that big of a deal!

**37**：——嗯？\
**37**: Hm?

她骤然停下了脚步。\
She stops.

那道通往迷宫深处的门前站着一个熟悉身影。\
Before the gate stands a familiar figure.

**37**：喔！我本来以为这里出现的会是福特圈、魔群，或者希尔伯特的无限旅馆之类的东西。\
**37**: I thought the next question would be the Ford Circle, the Monster Group, or Hilbert's Infinite Grand Hotel.

**37**：——结果居然是6！\
**37**: I never thought it would be 6!

**37**：你好，6！你是真的6吗？\
**37**: Hello, 6! Are you the real thing?

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

**6**：我是真正的6。\
**6**: Yes, I'm the real 6.

**37**：唔，这可不一定。在本质面前，我们都是墙上的倒影，你又怎么能断言你是真正的6呢？\
**37**: Mm. I wouldn't be so sure. When it comes to the essence, we are all shadows cast on a wall by a flickering fire. How do you know you're the real 6?

**6**：……呵。\
**6**: Heh.

这可真是不得了，就连37也后退了一步。\
That was too much to take in. Even 37 can't help but step back.

**37**：呃，你刚刚是笑了吗？\
**37**: Urh, did you just smile?

**37**：好吧，现在我必须怀疑你不是真的6了。\
**37**: Hmm. Now I very much doubt that you are real.

**6**：我没有笑。而且，我是真正的6。\
**6**: I didn't. And I am the true 6.

**6**：这道门是由每一代的6来守护的，37。\
**6**: This gate has always been guarded by a 6.

领袖又恢复了往日的无表情。\
The leader reverts back to a blank expression.

37对于熟人的出现显然不甚高兴。\
37 doesn't seem too thrilled to see her friend here.

**37**：我有不好的预感——我料定这道题会非常简单！\
**37**: I have a bad feeling about this—I think the question we're about to answer will be very simple!

**37**：你肯定只会走一个形式，然后就把我们放过去，是吗？你最擅长做的就是这种事。\
**37**: It's just a formality, isn't it? You'll ask a question and let us through. I've seen you do that on other tests before.

**6**：形式也是非常重要的。\
**6**: Formality is also important.

**37**：不，本质才是最重要的，只有本质！\
**37**: No, only the essence is important, only the Forms are important!

6不置可否地摇摇头，不再继续这场争辩。\
6 shakes his head, showing no inclination to continue the debate.

**6**：——我要问的的确是关乎本质的问题，37。\
**6**: This is a question about the essence and Forms, 37.

**6**：这非常重要，请你认真聆听。\
**6**: Please pay heed to it.

**6**：至于维尔汀小姐，你不用作答，只需旁听。\
**6**: As for Ms. Vertin, we only expect you to lend a patient ear.

**维尔汀**：好。\
**Vertin**: Very well.

37则慎重地望着6，露出了在科塔博斯上迎接泼葡萄酒挑战时的神情。\
37 looks at 6 with determination, the same look she had when she faced that challenge in the game of kottabos.

她有信心答出任何一道难题。\
She's confident that she can solve any problem that comes her way.

**6**：——37。\
**6**: 37.

**6**：假如你索求的真理，造成了你自身信仰的覆灭。\
**6**: If your pursuit of Truth were to lead to the destruction of your faith and beliefs,

**6**：即使如此，你也要前进吗？\
**6**: would you still keep going?

**37**：……什么？\
**37**: What?

她发自内心地惊讶出声。\
She exclaims involuntarily.

**37**：——这是什么问题？\
**37**: What kind of question is that?

## 7TH-08 德尔斐神谕 / Oracles at Delphi

剧情场景-洞穴-迷宫试炼地中心-幻圆差分。幻圆复位。

**37**：假如我索求的真理，造成了我自身信仰的覆灭……这是什么问题？\
**37**: If my pursuit of Truth will be the destruction of my beliefs?

37连连摇头，这比重塑访客提交的习题本还要令她困惑。\
She shakes her head repeatedly, looking more perplexed than when she checked the Manus followers' math homework.

**37**：我信仰的就是真理，为什么真理会因为真理覆灭？\
**37**: I came for the Truth, and my faith is the Truth. Why would the Truth be destroyed by the Truth?

**37**：如果是我之前算错了，那么就再来一次！\
**37**: If it's because I did the calculation wrong, I'll go back and do it again!

**37**：下一次，下一次我总会算得更好。\
**37**: And next time, I will do better!

毫无犹豫的回答，门前的法官也为此多了片刻的沉默。\
An answer without hesitation, causing the gatekeeper to pause for an extra moment of silence.

**6**：如果真理的本质就是没有真理呢？\
**6**: What if the essence of Truth is there is no "Truth"?

**37**：唔，那不也还是一种真理吗？虚无也依然是一个确定的答案，不是吗？\
**37**: Hm, isn't that also a form of the "Truth"? Its non-existence is an answer in itself, is it not?

**37**：为什么你说话像210一样？你真的是6吗？\
**37**: You're speaking like 210. Are you really 6?

37显然对这番诡辩一般的对话失去了耐心。\
37 has clearly run out of patience with the sophistry.

她恼怒地盯着6，不确定这是否是某种捉弄人的把戏。\
She stares at 6 in annoyance, trying to detect any sign on his face that he might be playing a joke on her.

**6**：……那么，我换一个更具体的问题，你可以把它当做寓言故事来听。\
**6**: I should be more specific. You may see it as another allegory.

**6**：在通往真理的道上有一扇门。假如打开这扇门，你就能获得你索求的真理。\
**6**: A gate stands before you. Open it, you will find the "Truth" you seek.

**6**：而同时，它也将造成你熟悉世界的覆灭。——你会打开它吗？\
**6**: But at the same time, the world as you know it will crumble. Will you still open it?

37眨了眨眼睛，让答案再次准确，坚定地脱口而出。\
37 blinks. This time, her answer is even more clear and resolute.

**37**：——当然！\
**37**: Yes!

**37**：如果世界会因为真理而改变，就说明之前的世界错了，不是吗？\
**37**: If my world changes because the Truth is revealed, doesn't that mean my previous understanding was wrong and should be corrected?

**37**：假如那的确是真理，为什么要让正确为错误让步呢？\
**37**: If what's behind the gate is really the Truth, why would I give up the Truth for falsehood?

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**6**：……我明白了。\
**6**: I see.

**6**：那么，作为通过问答的奖励，我将这个术式赠予你。\
**6**: You've passed. As a reward, I will bestow upon you this sacred ritual.

**6**：它能帮助你跨越与伟大存在交感时的灵性鸿沟。\
**6**: It will bridge the gap between you and the supreme existence during communion.

一只镶着金边的卷轴，被守门人递给此次答题的胜利者。\
A gilded scroll is presented to her.

而胜利者只是拧紧了眉毛。\
But the winner only furrows her brows even harder.

**37**：这就结束了？你甚至没有问出一个真正构成问题的问题！\
**37**: Was that it? You didn't even ask a question that posed a real challenge!

**37**：看吧，维尔汀，我就知道6只会走个形式。\
**37**: See, Vertin? I knew this was just a formality.

**37**：维尔汀？\
**37**: Vertin?

**维尔汀**：……不，37。我想这个问题……\
**Vertin**: No, 37, I think this question ...

**6**：37。\
**6**: 37.

6突兀地开口，打断了对话继续。\
6 interjects.

**6**：我还有一句箴言要告诉你。\
**6**: There are some words I'd like to share with you.

**6**：这不是出于6的立场，而是我个人……一个曾经名叫“亚齐”的人。\
**6**: Not as 6, but myself, who used to live under the name "Atticus."

**6**：我们都读过苏格拉底的故事，真理与政治并不相容。\
**6**: We know the story of Socrates's life, how Truth and politics are at odds with each other.

**6**：——置身事外的智慧，与亲临其中的苦难，你只能选择一个。\
**6**: Either be wise, uninvolved, and look on; or be practical, involved, and suffer.

**6**：希望到了那个时候，你不要忘记今天的回答。\
**6**: I hope you will remember your answer when the defining moment comes for you.

领袖离开了。\
He leaves.

这是场不甚满意的问答游戏，她撇了撇嘴，但仍然把战利品紧紧握在手中。\
The game has been a disappointment. 37 frowns in frustration, but she keeps a tight grip on the scroll.

圆心的入口向她们敞开，这场试炼的前方依然迷雾重重。\
The gate in the center of the circle has swung open, but the path ahead is still shrouded in mist.

**37**：快走吧，维尔汀，我们还没抵达迷宫深处呢。\
**37**: We should go, Vertin. There's a long way ahead.

**37**：——真希望下一关会有趣一点。\
**37**: I hope the next question will be more fun.

剧情场景-洞穴-迷宫试炼地中心-幻圆差分，在上一张复位幻圆的基础上，中心出现一扇门，差分工作量小。

**37**：嗯，果然没什么难的！就和妈妈告诉我的一样。\
**37**: Nothing I haven't expected so far! Just like what Mom told me.

**37**：这只是个游戏，就像打水漂、跳房子、科塔博斯……我一直很擅长游戏。\
**37**: They're just games, like skipping rocks, kottabos, and hopscotch. I've always been good at games!

**37**：噢，是那扇门！维尔汀，我们就要抵达迷宫深处了！\
**37**: Look, there's the gate, Vertin. We're almost at the end!

37志得意满地拍拍手，将又一道解开的谜题抛诸身后。\
37 claps her hands with satisfaction, having resolved yet another obstacle.

同行者的脚步却远不如她雀跃。\
But her companion is much more pensive.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**37**：——维尔汀，你怎么了？自从见到6后，你就变得很沉默。\
**37**: What's the matter, Vertin? You've been quiet since we met 6.

**37**：可你是数字0，不是数字6，你不应该和他进行通分！\
**37**: But you're number 0, not 6. You have no common factor with him.

**维尔汀**：……不，我只是在想……\
**Vertin**: No, I'm only thinking ...

**维尔汀**：机会只有一次，你已经想好一会儿要问什么问题了吗？\
**Vertin**: What's the question you're going to ask? We've only got one chance.

**37**：当然，是问那个最重要的问题！\
**37**: The most important question of all, of course!

**维尔汀**：……关于流溢“本质”的问题，是吗？\
**Vertin**: About the "essence" of the "Emanation," right?

可以预想到的回答。\
It was not a hard guess.

对于这座小岛的居民来说，关于本质的问题，从来都是一切问题中最为重要的。\
The islanders devote their lives to the study and service of "the essence." Nothing is more important than this question.

本质通达一切，相比起来，其它所有都是现象世界的碎屑。\
The "essence" reveals the ultimate truth that underlies all existence. Everything else is just fragments of the phenomenal world.

尽管它不像“免疫研究”那么迫切，但得知“暴雨”的本质也会对研究有所帮助。\
It might not directly solve the issue of the "Storm" immunity, but knowing its nature will certainly help with that aspect.

——更何况，它事关于一切迷雾的真相。\
And it's the key to solving not just one problem, but many others.

**37**：嗯……关于本质的问题是很重要。\
**37**: Well, the essence of it is important.

**37**：可是，我们总有一天会发现它的。因为它就在那儿，不是吗？\
**37**: But one day, we will eventually come to understand it. Even if we leave it alone for now, it will still be there, yes?

**维尔汀**：嗯？\
**Vertin**: I think so?

出乎意料地，37并没有第一时间肯定。\
She seems to have something else in mind.

**37**：我一直在想星锑上次说过的话……即使真理已经近在眼前，但倘若不是亲自求证来的答案，她宁愿选择放弃。\
**37**: I can't stop thinking about Regulus. Despite being so close to the answer, she turned back in the cave, determined to earn the answer rather than receive it on a silver platter.

**37**：这就像捂住耳朵，不去听取德尔斐神庙的神谕——果然是无理数的想法！\
**37**: It's like covering your ears in front of the oracles at Delphi! How typical of an irrational number.

**37**：可是，她也是对的，不是吗？没有任何一条教典规定不能这么做。\
**37**: But she was also right, wasn't she? None of the precepts forbids one from doing so.

**37**：也许她会掉队，会分心，会慢一些，但最终我们都会抵达真理……没有什么根本的不同。\
**37**: People like her may fall behind or get distracted along the way, learning at a slower pace. But in the end, we will all converge. It doesn't matter if some arrive sooner than others.

**维尔汀**：……所以，你不准备直接询问关于“本质”的问题？\
**Vertin**: So, are you going to ask something else?

这一次，她点了点头。\
This time she nods.

**37**：是的，我想到了一个更合适的问题！\
**37**: Yes, I have come up with a better question!

**37**：一个一劳永逸解决这儿危机的问题，一个能自“流溢”中打捞起所有人的问题！\
**37**: A question that will solve all our problems once and for all, and free everyone from the "Emanation"!

**37**：尽管没有那么深远，但它也是个好问题。\
**37**: It's not as profound as my first question, but it's an equally good one.

**维尔汀**：……我明白了。\
**Vertin**: I see.

**维尔汀**：那么，我想我就在这里停下了。\
**Vertin**: I will stop here then.

**37**：——嗯？\
**37**: Hm?

她转过身来，微微睁大了眼睛。\
She turns around, eyes wide with surprise.

**37**：维尔汀，你也要像星锑一样半路折返吗？\
**37**: Vertin, are you turning back like Regulus?

**37**：可你是0，不是无理数……！\
**37**: But you're a 0. You're not an irrational!

**维尔汀**：不，我就在这儿等你，哪也不会去。\
**Vertin**: No, I won't go far. I will wait for you here.

**维尔汀**：——只是，你应该自己去推开那扇门。这是你的问题，你的证明。\
**Vertin**: This is your gate to open. It is your question, your answer.

**维尔汀**：我会在这里见证。如果有危险，我也能第一时间提供帮助。\
**Vertin**: I will stay here and watch over you. If you encounter any danger in there, I will come to your aid at once.

**37**：——可是，你不向无限定者提问吗？\
**37**: But don't you also have a question to ask Apeiron?

**37**：你的疑问还没有得到解答，不是吗？\
**37**: Aren't your doubts unresolved?

**维尔汀**：不……我已经不需要问了。\
**Vertin**: No. I don't need to ask anymore.

**维尔汀**：你想问的那个问题，那个能够自“流溢”中帮助所有人的问题。\
**Vertin**: The question you're going to ask, the one that will free us all from the "Emanation,"

**维尔汀**：——就是我现在最想问的问题，37。\
**Vertin**: is exactly the question I want to ask, 37.

37歪着头，疑惑在她脸上稍纵即逝。\
37 tilts her head curiously, but her confusion soon fades.

她很快便理解了，一如既往。\
She quickly understands, as she does with most things in life.

**37**：——我明白了！你选择当置身事外的观察者，就像奥林匹克竞技场的第三种人。\
**37**: I see! So you're choosing to be the one who looks on, like the third kind of men in the Olympic Games!

**37**：智慧的选择，也符合数字的0的特性！\
**37**: A choice of insight, most appropriate for the number 0!

她不假思索地转过身去，进入了最终的试炼大门。\
Without further hesitation, she turns and steps into the final gate.

**37**：那，等会儿见，维尔汀!\
**37**: In that case, I will see you later then, Vertin!

**维尔汀**：……嗯，等会见，37。\
**Vertin**: See you soon, 37.

深呼吸，放下手中的箱子，在心里温习那道熟悉的咒语。\
Put the suitcase down, and breathe. Be ready for anything.

**维尔汀**：会发生那样的事情吗？如果……\
**Vertin**: Will this really be the collapse of her world as she knew it, like 6 said? If that happens ...

**维尔汀**：也许，我还能在这里撑起一把伞。\
**Vertin**: I'll be here to hold the umbrella for her.

## 7TH-09 不可超越物 / Outside the Limits

洞穴里映衬着祈祷用的烛光，为净化仪式而作的准备已经结束。\
The cave is basked in warm, flickering candlelight. Preparations for the cleansing ceremony are finally complete.

整数们正在等待着领袖的回归。\
The integers are waiting for their leader to return.

**888**：……你们认为37可以通过那个试炼吗？\
**888**: Do you think 37 is going to make it?

她压低了声音，将言语中的一丝担忧隐藏了起来。\
888 lowers her voice, concealing her worry.

**210**：谁知道呢？\
**210**: Who knows?

210斜靠在岩壁上，百无聊赖地整理着自己头上的葡萄。\
Leaning against the cavern wall, 210 absentmindedly adjusts the grapevine on his hair out of boredom.

**210**：6一定是最好过的一关，迷宫里的数字谜题也难不倒我们闪闪发亮的小天才。\
**210**: 6 should be the easiest one to pass. The math puzzles in the labyrinth shouldn't be a problem for our little star either.

**210**：最难的是无限定者的诘问——没有人知道问题会是什么。\
**210**: The only tricky question is from Apeiron, and no one knows what it will be.

**210**：游戏是公平的。在你提出问题之前，必须先回答无限定者的一个问题，这是规则。\
**210**: It is a fair game. Answer Apeiron's question, and It will answer yours.

**210**：倘若你没能回答出来——啊哦。\
**210**: But if you give the wrong answer, oops.

210随意地捏爆了手里的葡萄，紫色的汁水溅到了他的手上。\
He pinches a grape between his fingers and crushes it, its juice splattering onto his hand.

**210**：就会像这样。\
**210**: It'll hardly be a graceful end.

**888**：真恶心。\
**888**: You're gross.

888摇了摇头，毫不掩饰目光里的嫌弃。\
888 shakes her head, not even bothering to hide her disgust.

**教众Ⅱ**：我们对此所知甚少，毕竟，已经三个世纪没有人通过仪式了。\
**Believer II**: We know little about the test. The last person to pass the test was three hundred years ago.

**教众Ⅱ**：失败的代价太过惨痛，很长一段时间，历代的6都禁止教众们参与。\
**Believer II**: The price of failure was high. For the longest time, the 6s forbade people from risking their lives for it.

**888**：……不，6在这一点上说谎了。\
**888**: Well, 6 lied.

**888**：有人在四年前通过了仪式。\
**888**: Someone passed the test four years ago.

这是一个令人惊愕的消息，连210都不禁挺直了腰板。\
An unexpected piece of information. Even 210 straightens up in attention.

女妖抬起头，望向远处蜡烛映照在岩壁上的火光。\
The banshee gazes into the distance, watching the shadows cast by candles dance on walls.

**888**：……她们实在是太像了。天赋、思维，连遇到不可跨越的困难时，第一时间想到的解决方案都一样。\
**888**: The two of them are so much alike—their talents, their mindsets, even their first thoughts when facing an impossible challenge.

**888**：这的确也是一个难以抗拒的诱惑。\
**888**: It is an irresistible temptation indeed.

**888**：假如有一个近在眼前的渠道，通过它，便可以得知一切的真理……\
**888**: With a path to all Truths right in front of you, just within reach,

**888**：有什么理由不去试一试呢？\
**888**: who wouldn't want to give it a try?

光线影影绰绰，试炼已行至终点。\
Amid the swirling lights and shadows, the trial is reaching its conclusion.

这是迷宫的最深处，米诺陶的居所，最后的考验所在。\
She has reached the heart of the maze, the lair of Minotaur, where the final challenge awaits.

雾气之中，一道闪烁的轮廓逐渐鲜明起来。\
Through the mist, a form gradually takes shape.

先是一位智者，一个士兵。一个国王，一个农夫。一个孩子，一个老人。\
First it appears to be a scholar, then a soldier. But it continues to transform—into a king, a farmer, a child, an elder.

最后，它逐渐定型，化为一个笑容尖锐的年轻女人。\
Finally, it stops and solidifies into a young woman with a sharp and chilling smile.

**37**：……妈妈？\
**37**: Mama?

**37**：你为什么在这儿？\
**37**: How are you here?

幻影发出了一声轻笑。\
A soft chuckle slips out from the shadow.

**77？**：不，我的孩子，我不是你所想之人。\
**77?**: No, I'm not who you think I am, child.

**77？**：我只是一个影子，一抹火光，一个投射于你眼前的幻象。\
**77?**: I am but a shadow, a flicker of fire, a projection before you.

**77？**：因为有限无法度量无限。你可怜的感官无法想象出未曾见过之物，也无法理解从未聆听之声。\
**77?**: The finite cannot comprehend the infinite. Your limited senses cannot imagine what you've never seen, nor fathom what you've never heard.

**77？**：我是你惶然的祈求，你得见天光之前的狱卒，你的困惑投于水面的倒影。\
**77?**: I am the answer to your desperate prayers. I am the blindfold before you see daylight. I am the reflection of your confused, hollow faces in the water.

**77？**：——我是上一个发声者驻足的回音。\
**77?**: I am the lingering echo of the last visitor.

**37**：可你看起来就是妈妈！\
**37**: But you look just like Mama!

37惊异地呼喊着，不自觉地上前了一步。\
Eagerly, 37 steps forward.

**37**：我已经到了试炼的最后一关，我来到了真理的门前，对吗？\
**37**: This is the last obstacle of the test. The gate of Truth is just ahead, right?

**37**：而你在这儿，也就意味着，你真的抵达了超验的天国——！\
**37**: And here you are, standing in front of me. Does that mean that you finally reached the transcendental realm?

**37**：我的猜想没有错，我们的模型也没有输，是这样吗？\
**37**: So my conjecture was right, and our model did not fail, correct?

**77？**：……天国？\
**77?**: The transcendental realm?

女人突然奇异地笑了起来。\
The woman's laugh is strange and unsettling.

**77？**：我的女儿，你在说什么？难道你把我说的话都当了真不成？\
**77?**: You speak adorable nonsense, my dear daughter. Did you really believe what I said?

**77？**：傻孩子……多么可爱的傻孩子！\
**77?**: You silly little goose!

上前的脚步停止了，37错愕地抬起了头。\
37 stops in her tracks and lifts her head in disbelief.

那对碧色眼眸的神情不改，熟悉依旧。\
She locks eyes with those aquamarine orbs that are unmistakably her mother's eyes.

**77？**：可是，你真的从未怀疑过吗？\
**77?**: Have you not doubted, even for a moment?

**77？**：你不也动摇过一瞬吗？当你夜晚独自漫步在沙滩上，目光无可避免地触及那些几何体时……？\
**77?**: You did. You wavered when you strolled the shores at night, when you inevitably gazed at the geometric bodies.

**77？**：“如果它们真的是超验世界的象征，那我为何无法在这些碎块中分辨出妈妈的数字？”\
**77?**: "If they really are manifestations of the transcendental world, why can't I find Mama's number in the broken pieces?" You thought.

**77？**：“我为何听不到她的声音？我为何看不到这其中的规律？我的眼前一片漆黑！”\
**77?**: "Why can't I hear her voice? Why can't I see their patterns? The darkness blinds me!"

**77？**：“——妈妈，我很想你！”\
**77?**: "I miss you, Mama!"

**37**：——！\
**37**: ...!

**77？**：唉！我可怜的、可爱的女儿……\
**77?**: Oh, my poor, sweet daughter.

**77？**：你太年幼，太天真，太眷恋亲人的臂弯和脚下熟悉的土地。\
**77?**: You are too young and naive, too attached to what is familiar, and too trusting of your teachings.

**77？**：不然你本该继续怀疑下去，而非沿袭我架设的陈旧道路。\
**77?**: You should have continued doubting instead of following my outdated footsteps.

**77？**：那个猜想错了吗？那个模型对了吗？这并不重要，因为游戏规则已经改变。\
**77?**: Was the conjecture wrong? Was the model correct? It does not matter, child. The rules of the game have changed.

**77？**：制造混乱之人，扰乱局势之人，重塑规则之人，他们走在了前列。\
**77?**: The chaos-makers, the fear-mongers, and the rule-shapers—they have already outpaced us.

**77？**：我们并非错了，只是落后了。我们被名为天国的幻梦遮蔽，反而丧失了刺穿现实的能力。\
**77?**: We were not wrong. We simply fell behind. We were blinded by the dream of the transcendental realm and could not see through reality.

**77？**：但是没关系，我的女儿，因为你还是到这儿来了，这比任何事都重要。\
**77?**: But worry not, my daughter. You have made it here, and that is all that matters.

**77？**：我们又能一起计算，比任何一次都将做得更好。\
**77?**: We will do the calculations together. This time, the results will be more accurate than ever.

**37**：妈妈……\
**37**: Mama.

她微笑着拨拢额发，朝眼前的少女伸出手。\
With a gentle smile, the woman tucks her hair behind her ears and reaches out a hand to the girl.

**77？**：这世界是一个巨大的废墟，37。\
**77?**: This world is an enormous wasteland, 37.

**77？**：而占据其中的多数造物，那些沉默、拥塞、行色匆匆的芸芸众生。\
**77?**: Look at the creations in it. The congested, silent herds that scurry to and fro in their meaningless lives.

**77？**：他们此生从未抬头仰望过一次星空，从未俯身嗅闻过一次花香，从未聆听过那至高音律的一次鸣响，从未让心灵的琴弦为此颤栗过一秒。\
**77?**: Never have they looked at the stars above, nor bent to smell the flowers. The melodies of the patterns above go unheard by them, their souls unresonant to their wisdom.

**77？**：他们受困于躯体的坟墓，沉沦于感官的坟茔，却自以为能用暴力统治这颗星球。\
**77?**: They are the prisoners of their bodies, complacent in their dulled senses, and conceited over their success of ruling the planet through violence and bloodshed.

**77？**：他们嘲笑我们，背弃我们，屠杀我们，放逐我们至历史的边缘，视我们为胡言乱语的疯子，我们挚爱的一切为无价值的垃圾。\
**77?**: They mocked us, shunned us, and slaughtered us. They discriminated against us throughout the ages, branded us as lunatics, and spat on what we held dear.

**77？**：——可我们从未放弃，也从未真正被打垮。因为他们是错的，他们总有一天会知道。\
**77?**: But we never gave up once. We were never truly defeated. One day, they will be proven wrong, and they will be forced to admit it.

**77？**：我的女儿，我最珍贵的海贝里的珍珠。\
**77?**: My daughter, my precious little pearl.

**77？**：来吧，到妈妈这儿来，让我们回到争论和灾难之前，回到只有你、我与数字证明的海滩上。\
**77?**: Come to me, back in your mother's arms. Let us return to a time before disputes and disasters, when it was just you and me wandering the boundless beach.

**77？**：我将分享于你无穷无尽的奥秘，万事万物的本质，超越一切的真理。\
**77?**: I will share with you the infinite secrets of this world, the essence of all things, and the Truth that transcends everything.

**77？**：你正是为了它到这儿来的，不是吗？\
**77?**: That's what you came for, yes?

她的目光真诚而热烈。\
Her eyes are earnest and sincere.

37走上台阶，几乎就要握住那双温暖的手。\
37 slowly climbs the stairs, longing to reach out and grasp her mother's hands.

而后，她抬起头，困惑地问出了一个问题。\
She suddenly looks up, confused, and asks a question.

**37**：可是，妈妈。\
**37**: But, Mama.

**37**：我的数字是37，不是无穷大。\
**37**: I am 37, not infinity.

**37**：——我为什么要知道无穷无尽的奥秘呢？\
**37**: Why would I want an infinite number of secrets?

**77？**：——！\
**77?**: ...!

**维尔汀**：这股震动是……\
**Vertin**: The ground is shaking.

**维尔汀**：是37回答错误了吗？！\
**Vertin**: Did she give the wrong answer?

蜃景突然变得有所不同。\
The cavern's illusory landscape shifts again.

洞穴内壁无故卷起了飓风。\
A fierce wind abruptly rises around her.

在那风暴的中心，37仰起头，目光越过了母亲的幻影，径直望向空中。\
Amidst the howling gale, 37 looks defiantly up into the air, her eyes peering past her mother's silhouette.

**37**：——我不想知道无穷的奥秘，这不是我的数字！\
**37**: I don't long for the infinite secrets, for it is not within the scope of my number!

**37**：我知道，我是37，仅是37，一个有限的数字，沙滩上一粒微小的石头，海潮随时可以没过我，摧毁我，碾碎我。\
**37**: I know who I am. I am only 37, a finite number, a pebble in the sand. The tides could wash over me, engulf me, and crush me at any moment.

**37**：即便如此，我也为此骄傲！因为我知晓自己的有限——而所有伟大的存在都对此一无所知。\
**37**: Even so, I am glad to be 37, for I know my limits, I know my boundaries—a concept the supreme existences cannot even fathom.

母亲的幻影逐渐破裂，那些几何体的碎片闪烁着微弱的辉光，如同呼吸的起伏。\
Her mother's shadow shatters, the shards shimmering and pulsing in the air as if they were alive.

四周的风声愈发巨大，气流吹起长发，几乎让她睁不开眼睛。\
The wind picks up, whipping her hair around and forcing her to narrow her eyes against the current.

但她仍勉力挣扎着，不屈地站立着。\
But she stands her ground, refusing to yield.

**37**：无限定者，我来只是想询问一个简单的问题！！！\
**37**: Apeiron, the Boundless One! I am here for a simple question!

**37**：——我们如何才能不受现象世界的黑暗所绊，一劳永逸地自灵性的“流溢”中幸免！\
**37**: How can we escape the darkness of the phenomenal world, and be freed from the "Emanation" forever?

清脆的声音如同投掷入水潭的石子。\
Her voice disappears into the wind, like a pebble sinking into a pond.

然后，从古老的岩壁上传来了回音。\
But then, the ripples echo back.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**？？？**：智慧的回答。\
**???**: A worthy reply.

**？？？**：——尊重限度之人，汝展现了足够的谦卑。\
**???**: Thou hast heeded thy boundaries. Through humility shall thou ascend to higher wisdom.

**？？？**：作为报偿，汝将得到所求之物。\
**???**: Thou shalt be answered.

**？？？**：————\
**???**: ...

**37**：……呃！\
**37**: Ugh!

难以理解的异响，像是深海里的古老回音。\
Incomprehensible sounds assault her ears, like ancient echoes rising from the depths of the ocean.

那不能被称为是规律的音节，它更像是层叠的岩壁共振的应声。仅仅是听到一个震颤，身体便像是被利刃穿刺。\
They aren't recognizable syllables of any known language, but more like reverberations between layers of rock walls, each note stabbing through her like a dagger.

呼吸变得粘滞，血液也从鼻腔中涌出。\
Her breathing becomes labored and blood trickles from her nose.

致命的眩晕在颅骨内回荡，眼前的一切都变成了重影。\
Dizziness churns in her head, causing her vision to blur and double.

**37**：怎么会，无限定者明明同意了分享答案——\
**37**: How ...? It clearly promised me an answer.

**37**：难道这个问题的解答……这个超越的真理……\
**37**: Is it because ... the answer to my question ... the transcendental Truth ...

**37**：——是我们无法承受的吗？\
**37**: ... is outside of our limits, too?

**破译组长**：……快让开，让开！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Make way! Move!

**破译组长**：露西女士，这个读法是对的！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Madam Lucy, we have the right pronunciation!

**破译组长**：您拿给我的纸条是正确的，这就是这个术式使用的神秘学语言！您究竟是从哪里拿到了它——\
**Cryptography Lead**: The scrip you gave me was correct. This is the arcane language of the incantation! Where did you get it?

**露西**：很好，把它给我。\
**Lucy**: Very well. Give it to me.

**露西**：我们需要告诉科算中心全体，“暴雨”研究正式进入下一阶段。\
**Lucy**: Inform all research teams that we are moving on to the next phase of the project.

斩钉截铁的脚步穿过一排排透明的玻璃房间，抵达了“暴雨”研究与观测的主控室。\
Swift and sure footsteps stride past glass-walled rooms, stopping at the main control room of the "Storm" observation and research initiative.

联络员正在操作台前忙碌，新消息通过电信号与气动管道被传递到科算中心的各个科室。工作进程比血液更为流畅，一切都井然有序地进行着。\
The control station is bustling with activity as liaisons send messages through electrical signals and pneumatic tubes to various offices, all part of a well-oiled routine.

作为心脏中未被及时代谢掉的部分，一位擅离职守的前研究员也在这里。\
Enigma is here too.

**哑谜**：如果您是来询问进度的——那很遗憾，所有小组都没有进展。\
**Enigma**: If you're here to check on the progress, there is none.

**哑谜**：您恐怕是要白跑一趟了，露西女士。\
**Enigma**: I'm afraid you'll leave disappointed, Madam Lucy.

机器并不会为这种程度的讥讽所动。\
The robot hardly notices the mockery in his tone.

她走到临时的联络员前，递出了那枚鸽子带来的纸条。\
She approaches one of the liaisons and holds out her hand. In her palm is the scrip brought by the dove.

**露西**：将这个发送出去。\
**Lucy**: Send this to everyone.

**露西**：验证通过了，这就是免疫“暴雨”术式的正确读法。\
**Lucy**: It has been verified. This is the correct pronunciation of the immunity ritual.

**哑谜**：……？！你说这个就是——\
**Enigma**: ... ?! This is ...

掌心微微颤抖着。\
His hands tremble.

这张狭窄的纸条远比它看起来要沉重。\
Despite its size, the tiny slip of paper holds great importance.

纸条半摊着，借由上方标注的念法，他读出了第一个单词。\
Following the pronunciation guidelines, he carefully spells out the first word.

**哑谜**：La unua ...\
**Enigma**: La unua ...

纸条被拿走了。\
The scrip is taken from his grasp.

联络员走了过来，她的动作同样因为欣喜而颤抖。\
Standing next to him, the liaison holds the scrip in her hand, also trembling with excitement.

**联络员Ⅰ**：我们得赶快把它告诉所有人——\
**Liaison Staff I**: We must share this with everyone.

她几乎是一路小跑到机器前。\
She trots over to the control station.

纸条在屏幕上摊开，联络员紧张地核实着，确保自己不会遗漏这重要咒语的任何一个细节。\
The scrip is transposed onto the screen. The liaison meticulously checks every detail, ensuring that nothing is overlooked.

**联络员Ⅰ**：La unua ... cirklo ...\
**Liaison Staff I**: La unua ... cirklo ...

读写一致。她按下了发送键，欣悦地转过身。\
She reads into the microphone, her voice confident and clear. With a final press of the send button, she turns away with a satisfied smile on her face.

**联络员Ⅰ**：……唔……？！\
**Liaison Staff I**: Ahhh. Help!

毫无征兆，她的身体逐渐开裂。然后成片的碎屑落下。\
Without warning, her torso cracks apart and her entire form crumbles, shattering to the ground in pieces.

**哑谜**：什么——？\
**Enigma**: What was that?

**露西**：……！\
**Lucy**: ...!

地狱在这一刻降临了。\
All hell breaks loose.

慌乱后退的脚步和地板发出尖锐的摩擦声，有人惊慌地把咖啡打翻在了地上。\
Chairs scrape loudly against the floor, coffee cups clatter to the ground, and people scramble about in a frenzy.

总负责人伫立在原地，但条屏仍震惊地闪烁着。\
The director of Laplace remains still, her eyes fixed on the rapidly flashing lights on the screen.

**哑谜**：快终止传输！！这个术式有问题！！！\
**Enigma**: Stop the transmission! The ritual is wrong!!!

**露西**：——\
**Lucy**: ...

她停顿片刻。\
She pauses.

这一时刻，需要有人能基于现实运转。\
In the face of chaos and turmoil, it falls on someone to step up and take action.

**露西**：不，术式没有问题。\
**Lucy**: No.

**露西**：——它的确是正确的。\
**Lucy**: The incantation is indeed correct.

## 7TH-10 泥泞路 / Returned to the Earth

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-破译房间。

**破译员Ⅲ**：……发生什么事了？\
**Cryptographer III**: What is going on?

玻璃房间里的研究员们困惑地仰起头。\
In other glass-walled rooms, researchers look up from their work in confusion.

走廊里的气密门降了下来，电力设备正在疯狂地闪烁。\
The airlock doors have been sealed tight, and their electronic equipment is flashing erratically.

**广播**：警告，警告……\
**Broadcast**: Warning, warning.

同一时间，屏幕上亮起了新的讯息。\
At the same time, all of their screens light up simultaneously, indicating the arrival of a new message.

**破译员Ⅳ**：——嘿，道金斯，别管外面的事了，快来看这个！\
**Cryptographer IV**: Hey, Dawkins, forget the outside, come look at this!

**破译员Ⅳ**：有人完成了破译！他们找到了术式的正确读法！\
**Cryptographer IV**: Some guy's cracked it! They found the correct pronunciation!

**破译员Ⅲ**：什么？！老天爷，它最好是真的，而不是哪个精神崩溃的研究员的恶作剧……\
**Cryptographer III**: For real?! They better be serious. If this is some kind of prank ...

人们自然地簇拥到了屏幕前，激动地阅读着那则传输完毕的咒文。\
Despite the blaring alarms, the staff gathers around their screens, eagerly reading aloud the incantation that was just sent.

**破译员Ⅲ**：La unua ... cirklo ...?\
**Cryptographer III**: La unua ... cirklo ...?

**哑谜**：该死，该死，该死！！！\
**Enigma**: Damn it! Damn it! S**t!!!

研究员在走廊上奔跑着，气密门关闭前一秒，他勉强冲了进去。\
He runs down the corridor at full speed, gasping for air. Just as the airlock doors begin to close, he flings himself through.

距离最近的玻璃房子里烟雾萦绕，视野中只有一片白色。\
The closest room with glass walls is filled with thick white smoke.

他疯狂地拍打着那扇门。\
He sprints to the door and frantically pounds on it.

**哑谜**：乌尔里希！道金斯！维克托！理查德！你们在里面吗！！\
**Enigma**: Ulrich! Dawkins! Victor! Richard! Are you in there?!

**哑谜**：听着，如果你们收到了任何“咒文的正确读法”，千万不要诵读！不要抄写！不要传递！\
**Enigma**: Listen, if you receive the pronunciation of the incantation, do not recite it! Do not write it down! Do not pass it on!

**哑谜**：我知道我们之前闹得很不愉快。但你们得相信我，这事关所有人——\
**Enigma**: I know we've had our differences, but you have to trust me. I'm trying to save you!

门那端寂静无声。\
A chilling silence looms on the opposite side of the door.

只有露西女士的声音自走廊上方的扩音器传出。\
The only noise that can be heard is Lucy's emotionless voice coming through the speakers.

**广播**：警告，警告。\
**Broadcast**: Warning, warning.

**广播**：所有科算中心人员，立刻离开身边的通讯设备，不要读出屏幕上的任何文字。\
**Broadcast**: All personnel stay away from their communication terminals. Do not recite any messages on the screen.

**广播**：重复一次。不要读出咒文。不要读出咒文。不要读出咒文……\
**Broadcast**: Repeat. Do not recite the incantation. Do not recite the incantation. Do not recite ...

门突然打开了，气阀里喷出的烟雾呛得哑谜咳嗽了一声。\
The door suddenly opens. The smoke pouring out nearly chokes him.

**哑谜**：咳咳……！\
**Enigma**: *cough*

**哑谜**：……理查德？\
**Enigma**: Richard?

**破译员Ⅳ**：……\
**Cryptographer IV**: ...

破译员从烟雾中走出来，动作僵硬，表情诡异地平静。\
A cryptographer emerges from the thick smoke, his movements stiff and his face expressionless.

他试图开口，他也做到了。于是一道裂纹在他脸上扩散开来，就像一个在烧制过程中碎裂的泥俑。\
As he opens his mouth to speak, a small crack forms at the corner of his lips and quickly spreads across his entire face, as if he were made of clay.

**破译员Ⅳ**：道……\
**Cryptographer IV**: Daw—

男人倒了下来，他全身的皮肤都变得像干涸的土地结块。\
Suddenly he collapses, his skin splitting and cracking like parched earth.

**哑谜**：——理查德！\
**Enigma**: RICHARD!

哑谜及时地扶住了同僚，使他免于像文物一样碎裂的厄运。\
Enigma quickly moves to support him, preventing his colleague from breaking into pieces on the hard floor.

他迅速检查了一下对方的生命特征——还好，脉搏仍在有序地跳动。变异仅仅发生在皮肤表层，没有改变人体的根本性质。\
He checks his vitals—still alive; only his skin has been affected by the mutation. Underneath the cracked exterior, he can still see human flesh and blood.

**哑谜**：别再说话了，我送你去康复中心！\
**Enigma**: Don't speak. We're going to the rehab center!

**破译员Ⅳ**：不……你快去……道……金斯……\
**Cryptographer IV**: No ... You ... Go ... Daw ... kins ...

他伸出一根泥土覆盖的手指，艰难地指向玻璃房内。\
Lifting a muddy finger, he manages to point toward the room.

烟雾弥漫的门洞中，逐渐出现了一个巨大的轮廓。\
Slowly, a monumental figure emerges from the hazy entrance.

一个浑身流着泥浆的泥巴傀儡走了出来，就像一个烤糊的大号姜饼娃娃。\
It is a mud golem, with thick clumps of mud dripping off its body.

面目已经难以辨认，但属于研究员道金斯的工牌还挂在他的身上。\
The only remaining human element is Dawkins's nameplate, barely clinging to its chest.

**破译员Ⅲ**：呃，呃呃呃——\
**Cryptographer III**: Urh, urrrrrh.

**破译员Ⅲ**：我要——\
**Cryptographer III**: I'm ...

**哑谜**：道、道金斯……不……不，不——！\
**Enigma**: Dawkins! No, no. No!!

走廊那头的气密门被打开，全副武装的安全员带着催眠弹和拘束网冲了进来。\
The airlock door at the end of the hallway hisses open. A squad of security guards with hypno bullets and restraint nets barge their way in.

**拉普拉斯安全员**：——阿德勒研究员，请你带着其他人离开！\
**Laplace Safety Officer**: Researcher Adler, please evacuate immediately!

**拉普拉斯安全员**：这里先交给我们！\
**Laplace Safety Officer**: We will take over from here!

剧情场景-暴雨眼观测室（1.7的那个场景）

**哑谜**：我本以为，这个术式最多只是无用的。因为我们无法驾驭它，不能使用它……\
**Enigma**: I thought the worst case would be that the ritual is useless, since no one here can wield it.

**哑谜**：我错了。我错得离谱，真实的情况比那糟糕一万倍。\
**Enigma**: I was wrong, so terribly wrong. The reality is a million times worse.

**哑谜**：我们招致了诅咒——比重塑之手的面具更加可怕、更加随机、完全不可抵挡的诅咒。\
**Enigma**: We have invited a disaster. It is a curse—even more unpredictable, unstable, and uncontrollable than the mask!

哑谜用手抓着自己的头，声音接近控诉。\
He grips his hair tightly, his voice hoarse as he shouts.

**哑谜**：朵拉在我眼前化为了碎土，理查德全身的皮肤都覆盖了结块，道金斯变成了一个不会说话的泥巴娃娃……\
**Enigma**: Dora crumbled to dust. Richard cracked like dry land, and Dawkins turned into a statue of mud.

**哑谜**：还有维克托，他凭空消失了。我们用尽任何物理方式都没能在房间里探查出他，他本人却还能打字，发邮件，甚至给我开门。\
**Enigma**: And Victor, he vanished. We've tried everything, but he's nowhere to be found. Yet he's here, typing, sending e-mails, getting the door for me.

**哑谜**：而我们仅仅是念出了三个单词，三个。\
**Enigma**: All of these catastrophic events, and only three words were uttered. Three.

哑谜苦笑着摇头，接连发生的变故令他的精神濒临崩溃，甚至编不出太多讥诮话。\
He shakes his head and laughs bitterly, not even in the mood for mockery after all that's happened.

**哑谜**：——我们到底是在研究什么，露西女士？我们究竟是在从哪位愤怒的神灵手上窃取怎样超凡的力量？\
**Enigma**: What are we dealing with, Madam Lucy? Which deity are we provoking and stealing from?

没有人回答他的问题。\
No one can answer his question.

安全员们在清理地面，联络员们在发布关于咒文危险性的紧急通告，并确认事故的波及范围。\
The security guards are busy cleaning up the mess, while liaisons are frantically issuing warnings and confirming the extent of the casualties.

康复中心的员工匆匆赶来，带走了这场始料未及的传输事故里的所有伤者。\
The rehab center personnel have also arrived, and as they leave, their stretchers are filled with injured people.

他的上司则刚刚挂断一则内线通话。\
His supervisor finishes up a call and hangs up the phone on the wall.

**露西**：回去休息吧，阿德勒先生。\
**Lucy**: Get some rest, Mr. Adler.

**露西**：你的任务已经结束了，后续工作会交给其他人。\
**Lucy**: Your mission is complete. Other researchers will take it from here.

**哑谜**：什么……？\
**Enigma**: You what?

人类研究员错愕地问，愤怒之火在他胸膛中燃烧。\
He asks in disbelief, anger swelling in his chest.

**哑谜**：所以您并不打算中止研究，在发生了……这样的事后？\
**Enigma**: Are you not going to call it off? After all that's happened?

**露西**：研究必须进行下去。\
**Lucy**: The research must go on.

机器的回答非常简短。\
The robot's answer is concise and cold.

**露西**：咒语的有效性，甚至任何人都可以使用的潜在可能性，已在这场意外事故中得到了验证。\
**Lucy**: The authenticity of the incantation, and the fact that any arcanist can recite it, were revealed to us through this unexpected mishap.

**露西**：于是，当前最重要的课题出现了——寻找消除术式副作用的方法。\
**Lucy**: Now, a new question arises: how can we eliminate the side effects?

**露西**：我们不再需要人类研究员的援助了。\
**Lucy**: From now on, we no longer require the help of human researchers.

她径直下达了判决，声音平静、克制、温和。\
Her tone is calm and gentle, yet with authority. The decision has been made.

**露西**：——神秘学的诅咒只能用神秘学来消除。\
**Lucy**: Only arcanum can lift a curse of arcanum.

剧情场景-幻境2-中间的门轰然打开，里面传来巨大的气流。该场景做氛围图差分来出。

**维尔汀**：37——！\
**Vertin**: 37!

洞穴之内，那股奇异的响动仍在持续。\
The eerie sounds continue to reverberate in the cave.

37虚弱地跪倒在透明的台阶上，口鼻已经流出了血液。\
37 kneels on the transparent stairs, blood seeping from her mouth and nose.

**维尔汀**：坚持住，我带你离开——！\
**Vertin**: Stay with me! I'll get you out!

将箱子在地上摊开。\
The suitcase. The noises wouldn't reach her in there.

它应该能良好地隔绝异响和扰动。\
It could be her refuge.

**37**：——唔！\
**37**: Uhm!

37突然挣扎了一下。自她的怀中，那个镶着金边的卷轴缓缓升起。\
37 suddenly jerks. Slowly, an ornate scroll rises from her bosom.

**维尔汀**：这是……6的卷轴？\
**Vertin**: Is this 6's scroll?

动画-6的调和卷轴，一边摊开，一边升起，出现内部金色的几何图形。卷轴升到最高后，闪光转场，切到氛围图。

异响逐渐平息了。\
The strange noises begin to fade.

取而代之的是一串悠远的乐声。\
In its place is an ancient melody.

**37**：+1、-1、+2、-3、3、-3、+2、-1、+1……\
**37**: +1, -1, +2, -3, 3, -3, +2, -1, +1 …

**37**：……原来是这样，我明白了。\
**37**: I see. I understand now.

**维尔汀**：什么意思，37？你没事了吗？\
**Vertin**: What did you say? 37, are you feeling better now?

她点了点头，神智已经恢复清明。\
She nods, having regained her clarity.

**37**：是数字，维尔汀。\
**37**: They're numbers, Vertin.

**37**：6的卷轴调和了我们与伟大存在交感的灵性鸿沟，现在我可以听懂了。\
**37**: 6's scroll reconciled the gap between the supreme existence and me. I can now hear and understand.

**37**：那个问题的回答，从“流溢”中幸免的方式，无限定者给予的终极解答——\
**37**: The answer to my question, the solution to free us from the "Emanation," the response Apeiron promised me ...

**37**：是一串数字。\
**37**: ... is a string of numbers.

## 7TH-11 巨石滚落之刻 / The Rolling Boulder

剧情场景-幻境2-中间的门轰然打开，里面传来巨大的气流。该场景做氛围图差分来出。

风暴已经平息，洞穴的四壁重归宁静。\
The winds died down. The cave is quiet again.

试炼结束了，一如既往，赫尔墨斯之星得到了她所寻求的答案。\
The trial is over. As usual, the Star of Hermes has found her answer.

**37**：——我们拿到它了，这就是那串通往真理的数字密码！\
**37**: We got it! The key to the gate of Truth!

**37**：无限定者回答了我的提问，祂给了我一劳永逸的解法！\
**37**: Apeiron has answered me! This is the final solution!

她雀跃地说着。卷轴尽职地完成了翻译工作，落回了她手中。\
She chirps with delight as the scroll completes its task and lands back in her hand.

**37**：我们得赶快出去，把它告诉大家——！\
**37**: We must leave here at once. We have to tell everyone!

**维尔汀**：……嗯，我为你感到高兴，37。\
**Vertin**: I am so proud of you, 37.

**维尔汀**：这个答案一定可以帮助到大家的。\
**Vertin**: We will save everyone.

紧张的神经终于可以暂时放松下来，这无疑是最好的结果。\
There is finally room to breathe, if only for a brief moment.

可是，心中的不安感却并未消失。\
Yet, the feeling of unease remains.

**维尔汀**：……有一件事我不明白。\
**Vertin**: But there's one thing I don't understand.

**37**：嗯？\
**37**: And that is?

前进的脚步止住了。37歪了歪头，不解地转过身来。\
She pauses mid-step and looks back, tilting her head inquisitively.

**维尔汀**：——6给予的卷轴发挥了作用。\
**Vertin**: 6. His scroll saved your life.

**维尔汀**：或许他预想到了这里可能发生的情形，并帮你规避了危险。最终，你也顺利地从试炼地离开。\
**Vertin**: Maybe he foresaw the dangers and protected you from it, so you can leave there almost unharmed.

**维尔汀**：那么，为什么他要对你发出那样的告诫……\
**Vertin**: But what was he trying to tell you,

**维尔汀**：为什么他会说：“你所追求的真理，也许会摧毁你熟悉的世界……”？\
**Vertin**: when he warned you about "the collapse of your world as you know it"?

剧情场景-岛屿-洞穴中心。（旧场景复用，问下美术能不能把洞穴中心那张的石头去掉）

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

**888**：……\
**888**: ...

**210**：……\
**210**: ...

通往净化的道路十分漫长。\
The walk to the cleansing site is long.

甬道里只有滴水声和轻微的脚步声。\
Only the sounds of dripping water and soft footsteps can be heard in the tunnel.

**教众Ⅱ**：请小心脚下，我们正在经过真言之壁。\
**Believer II**: Mind your step, everyone. We are passing the Wall of Truth.

**教众Ⅱ**：任何不实或虚伪的话语都会导致岩壁坍塌。如无必要，不宜在此地贸然开口。\
**Believer II**: The wall will come crashing down if false words are spoken. Silence is advised here, unless circumstances dictate otherwise.

信仰者们谨慎地点点头。\
The followers nod with respect.

他们一路已经走过了缄默之壁、善良之壁、智慧之壁。\
They have walked past the Walls of Silence, Goodness, and Wisdom respectively as part of the ritual.

这是仪式必要的考验，唯有遵循所有美德之人，能完成最终的“净化”。\
Only those who embody these virtues can find safe passage to the final cleansing.

**教众Ⅱ**：……888女士？\
**Believer II**: 888?

身为协理人的888突然上前一步，挡在了领袖的前面。\
The Custodian suddenly steps up in front of the leader, blocking his path.

**888**：抱歉，但我想现在是一个适当的时机。\
**888**: Forgive me, but this seems to be the right moment,

**888**：适宜问出那些尚待厘清的问题。\
**888**: for some long-neglected questions to be answered.

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

人群之中，又有几名教众上前，将领袖围在了中央。\
As she speaks, a few others emerge from the crowd and surround 6.

狭窄的道路立刻变得无法通过。\
On the narrow pathway, there is no way to get around them.

**6**：这并非义举。\
**6**: Perhaps. But hardly appropriate or righteous.

**888**：欺瞒也并非义举，6。\
**888**: We will talk of righteousness after you've shared what you know, 6.

**888**：你已在这四年里沉默了太久。从你成为“6”的第一天起，你就在回避一些问题。\
**888**: You've been silent for too long. Four years have passed since you became 6, and for four years, you have been hiding things from us.

**888**：它们日积月累，已助长了学派内的不合倾向。如今，巨岩滚下，我们正在悬崖边缘。在这涉及存亡的时刻，我希望你能对我们坦诚相待。\
**888**: The long-neglected questions have created a cloud of doubt between us. And now, the boulder of fate is falling on us, and we are teetering on the brink of destruction. It's time to be honest and true to your people—while you still have them.

**888**：——我们是追求真理之人，不应对真理视而不见。\
**888**: We are the seekers of Truth. It is unjust to keep us from it.

888伸出一只手，指向四周沉默的岩壁。\
888 extends an arm, gesturing to the silent cavern walls that surround them.

**888**：请先贤所造的真言之壁为我见证！我的心中并未存有任何虚伪和欺瞒的念头，每字每句皆为真心。\
**888**: Let the Wall of Truth bear witness! I want nothing but an answer from you. I am not here to provoke untimely conflicts.

岩壁不动如山，她的真诚毋庸置疑。\
The wall stands firm. The genuineness of her words is not to be doubted.

**210**：回答她吧，你应该庆幸，在这里提问的不是我。否则这道岩壁马上就会坍塌。\
**210**: Answer her, 6. You should be glad that I am not the interrogator here, because the wall would have collapsed immediately.

岩壁依然沉默，显然，修辞学家的这句玩笑也是真意。\
The wall remains silent, seemingly confirming the rhetorician's mocking words as truth.

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

**210**：你可以说谎，那会使得岩壁坍塌。你可以沉默，那样，我会说谎来使得岩壁坍塌。\
**210**: You may lie, but the wall will fall. You may stay silent, then I will lie to break the silence and the wall.

**210**：当然，你可以求助于悖论。这一点我已经替你测试过了，“我现在说的这句话是谎话”对真言之壁无效。\
**210**: Or maybe you could outwit the wall with the liar's paradox. Only sadly, I have tested it for you—one cannot deceive it by stating "I'm lying."

**210**：毕竟这是一个道德试炼，不是逻辑考题——它只是想要确保你的真诚，此外无他。\
**210**: After all, it's a test of morality, not logic. It needs your honesty, not your wit or anything else.

货真价实的威胁，但领袖对此并无特别的反应。\
It's a delicate situation, one that requires precision. The leader remains composed.

**6**：你们想要知道什么？\
**6**: What do you wish to know?

**210**：——当然是那个最重要的问题，关于本质的问题。\
**210**: What else? The most important question, of course—the question about the essence.

210上前了一步，声音轻微颤抖，不复之前的平静。\
210 takes a step, his voice trembling, no longer as calm as he used to be.

这些疑问已经在他心里盘旋了太久。\
These questions have plagued his mind for too long.

**210**：这四年里，我们的研究为何止步不前？关于1929年和这一次“流溢”的预测，为何会完全失败？\
**210**: Why has our research stagnated for the past four years? Why did we fail to predict the "Emanation" in 1929 and again in this time?

**210**：是不是我们搞错了根本前提——“流溢”的本质，根本不是超验规律的显现？\
**210**: Have we misunderstood the premise? What if the "Emanation" is not a manifestation of the transcendental Law at all?

6平静地望向他，目光并无波澜。\
6 remains stoic, showing no signs of emotion.

**6**：你弄错了提问对象，210。崇奉者专事教务，论理者深究思辨，政事者体察外界，形而下学者感悟自然。\
**6**: Worshipers worship. Thinkers think. Governors govern, and researchers research. Your questions are not mine to answer, 210.

**6**：“流溢”研究并非6的领域，我的智慧不能为你解答本质的问题。\
**6**: A 6 has no expertise on the study of the "Emanation." I am not qualified to answer about its essence.

这是事实，岩壁的沉默印证了这一点。\
A truth is spoken, and the silent wall attests to its veracity.

**888**：你的问题太抽象了，210。\
**888**: Your question is too abstract, 210.

协理人摇了摇头，上前一步。\
The Custodian shakes her head and takes a step closer.

**888**：我要问的正是你所知道的，6。\
**888**: Don't dance around the subject, 6.

**888**：每一代的6在接受灵魂数字时，会同时继承上一代的智慧。这里面有知识、见闻，还有至关重要的记忆。\
**888**: The wisdom has been passed on to you, as it has to every other 6. You have inherited not only knowledge and insight, but also the memories of your predecessors.

**888**：那么，你应当知道这件事，它理应存在于你的传承之中。\
**888**: You must know the answer, for it is part of your inheritance.

**888**：上一任“流溢”研究的领航人——77。她在无限定者面前问了怎样一个问题，又得到了怎样的真理？\
**888**: Tell us this: the last leader of the study of the "Emanation," 77—what question did she bring to Apeiron, and what answer did she receive?

沉默。沉默预示了她切入的正确。\
There's no immediate response, confirming that she's hit the nail on the head.

**888**：我曾目睹她步入迷宫，也见证了她无恙返回。\
**888**: I watched her walk into the cave and come out unharmed.

**888**：那之后，上一代6和77驾船出海，去现象世界探寻。船只未能及时返航，“流溢”在我们眼前降临。\
**888**: I watched her and the previous 6 board the ship in search of answers in the phenomenal world. The ship didn't come back in time. The "Emanation" caught them.

**888**：——而这仅仅是接连不断挫折的开始。\
**888**: And that was only the beginning of our misfortunes.

**888**：模型为何失败？坐标为何外泄？癔症为何蔓延至此？旧有的规则为何突然失灵？\
**888**: The model failed. Our whereabouts were revealed. Hysteria now poisons the minds of our people, and the empirical knowledge accumulated over the years suddenly no longer applies to the current situation. Why?

**888**：是她发现了什么吗？是不是她从神谕里得知——\
**888**: What did she find out? Could it be ...

**888**：那至高的秩序，超验的规律，我们信仰的“真理”——发生了什么变故？\
**888**: ... that something's happened to the transcendental Law above? Has the Truth we believed in changed?

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

重重诘问之下，领袖突然笑了。\
Barraged with so many questions, he lets out a chuckle.

那笑容如释负重，就像一个等待多年的被告突然收到了法庭的判决。\
He smiles with relief, like a prisoner finally receiving his death sentence after years of waiting.

与此相反，教众们屏住了呼吸。\
It has the opposite effect on the crowd. They hold their breaths in suspense.

**6**：希帕索斯发现了根号2的奥秘，于是毕达哥拉斯学派覆灭了。\
**6**: Hippasus discovered the secrets of √2 and toppled Pythagoras's school of thought.

**6**：牛顿忽略了无穷小量的推导，令微积分的大厦险些轰塌。\
**6**: The controversy surrounding Newton and infinitesimals presented a challenge to the groundwork of calculus.

**6**：罗素发现集合的自指悖论，引发了第三次数学危机。他完善了集合论，却消除不了自指的幽灵。\
**6**: Russell's self-referential paradox sparked the third mathematical crisis. Though set theory was eventually perfected, the lessons on self-referentiality remained.

**6**：最终，哥德尔下达了判决，不完备性迎来了最终的胜利。\
**6**: In the end, Gödel's incompleteness theorems showed that proving or disproving everything is impossible, therefore absolute knowledge is unattainable.

领袖的感慨在空旷的洞穴里回荡。\
His profound sentiments echo throughout the cave.

**6**：命运的巨石总会自高山上滚落。即使不是37，也会有其他人来开启。\
**6**: The boulder of fate will tumble down its peak, whether 37 is the one pushing it or not.

**6**：俄狄浦斯违抗的努力，反而助长了命运的悲剧。\
**6**: However hard Oedipus tried to defy destiny, his path to tragedy remained unchanged.

**888**：……什么意思，6？\
**888**: You're talking in riddles again.

女妖皱起眉头，而领袖只是轻轻向她鞠了一躬。\
She furrows her brow. However, 6 gives her a small nod of respect.

**6**：谢谢你，888，我回答你的疑问。\
**6**: I should thank you for bringing the question here, 888, so I may finally speak the truth.

**6**：是的，77的确曾问出过这样一个问题，关于“流溢”本质的问题。\
**6**: 77 did ask about the essence of the "Emanation."

他抬起头，平静地注视着面前环绕他的教众。\
He stands tall and looks around at the people.

信仰者们亦是专注地聆听。\
They're listening intently.

**6**：她询问——“至高的存在究竟发生了什么，才让世界变得如此癫狂？”\
**6**: She asked, "What happened to the supreme existence? What plunged the world into madness?"

**6**：答案是，“紊乱。”\
**6**: The answer was "Disorder and chaos."

**888**：——！！！\
**888**: ...!

真言之壁并未坍塌，先贤铸下的考验认可了他的诚意。\
The Wall of Truth still stands. The trial left behind by the ancient sages confirms his words.

但是，一阵更深、更幽远、更磅礴的轰鸣声，从岛屿中心传来。\
A deep, ominous rumble comes from the center of the island.

那震动浩瀚无垠，势不可挡，好像海啸和火山在同一时间到来。\
The tremors are like the island is being shaken to its core, like a tsunami and a volcanic eruption combined.

**210**：——该死的！！！\
**210**: You blasted ...!

210第一个反应了过来。他一个箭步冲上去，抓住领袖的衣领。\
210 is the first to come to a realization. He lunges and grabs 6 by the collar.

**210**：你早就知道了？！从四年前的第一天，从你成为6的那一刻开始？？？\
**210**: You knew this all along? From the first day of your "Revelation," when you became 6???

**210**：知道“流溢”并不是超验规律的显现，而是超验规律的彻底紊乱？！\
**210**: You knew that the "Emanation" was not a manifestation of the transcendental Law and patterns above, but rather a symptom of its utter disorder and chaos?!

**210**：知道再也没有永恒超越的数学天国，我们所信仰的灵性本质，已经是一个不尽变动的无理数？！\
**210**: And you knew that the transcendental realm of numbers was no more, and that the essence of pneuma, the one true Form we believed in, had become an ever-changing existence like the irrational numbers?!

巨大的愤怒和荒谬冲昏了他的头脑，修辞学家注视着那位竟敢证实信仰已毁灭的领袖，几乎笑出声来。\
Rage threatens to consume him. The rhetorician glares at the leader, who has the audacity to confirm that their faith is shattered. He almost breaks into a bitter laugh.

**210**：四年！你隐瞒了这件事四年！为了什么？\
**210**: Four years! You kept this to yourself for four years. Why?!

**210**：为了虚假的和平？为了平静的表象？！为了欺瞒所有人——我们追求的一切还没有成为一片虚无？！\
**210**: Was it for a false sense of peace? To keep the island stable? Did you deceive us to prevent the realization that our research would be in vain?

6没有回答这个附加的问题，它不在义务范围内。\
6 does not answer the added inquiries, for they are not within his duty.

**888**：现在不是争辩的时候，立刻带所有人离开！\
**888**: It's time to halt the bickering. Get everyone out of here now!

协理人强硬地分开了他们，开始指挥惶恐不安的人群从狭窄的甬道撤离。\
The Custodian steps in and separates them with a stern look. She then turns and begins to lead the panicked crowd to safety.

在这一片混乱中，领袖垂下眼睛，念出了本该在净化仪式上诵读的经文。\
Amidst the chaos, the leader lowers his eyes and reads the verses prepared for the ceremony.

**6**：“……为你将做的事向神祈祷，祈求一切顺利。”\
**6**: "Pray to the gods for what you are about to do, and pray that all goes well."

“当你熟悉了这一切，你便会知晓永恒的诸神与有死的凡人之体系。”

屏幕震动的效果，模拟地震。\
"Once familiar with this practice, you will understandthe constitution of both eternal gods and mortal men."

**苏菲亚**：……唔！\
**Sophia**: Uhm!

**苏菲亚**：净化仪式……没有顺利进行吗？\
**Sophia**: What happened? Did they not carry out the cleansing ceremony?

“知晓世间万物为何者所包容，又如何联结为一。”

屏幕震动的效果，模拟地震。\
"You will know the extent of all things, the boundariesof their entirety, and what connects them together."

**星锑**：呜啊，站、站不住了……怎么回事？！这是地震了吗？\
**Regulus**: Whoa, what's going on?! An earthquake?

**十四行诗**：不……这是……\
**Sonetto**: No. This is ...

**十四行诗**：一直环绕在岛上的那个大型神秘术式的气息。它……似乎正在自行消解？！\
**Sonetto**: The large-scale ritual on this island is undoing itself!?

“你将懂得，正如你应当懂得，宇宙在任何地方都是齐一的。”

屏幕震动的效果，模拟地震。\
"You will see, as you should, that the natureof the universe flows in all things alike."

**37**：……为什么？\
**37**: Why?

**37**：我们的圆……消失了？\
**37**: Why is our circle gone?

剧情场景-岛屿-洞穴中心。（旧场景复用，问下美术能不能把洞穴中心那张的石头去掉）\
The leader stands quiet and resolute, like a rock by the sea.

混乱之中，他平静地伫立，如海边沉默的礁石。\
Watching the fall of the heavenly transcendental, feeling the tides of change wash over everything.

目击天国在眼前坍塌，海潮将一切倾覆。

**6**：“——如此，你便不会盼望不该盼望的，亦不会受到蒙蔽。”\
**6**: "Thus you will not hope for what is beyond your reach, and you will not be deceived."

领袖合上了卷轴，结束了诵读。\
He rolls up the scroll and ends his reading.

**6**：祈祷吧，我的朋友们。\
**6**: Pray, my friends.

**6**：为自己祈祷，为众人的命运祈祷，为周边的一切苦难祈祷。\
**6**: Pray for yourselves, and pray for everyone. Pray for all the suffering and misery around you.

**6**：对不可见的黑暗伸出手，向不可知的伟大者祈求。开口吧，言说一个有限者想要超越自身存在的希冀。\
**6**: Reach into the unseeable darkness and pray to the unknowable supreme. Speak your hopes, for you are a finite creature yearning to transcend its own existence.

**6**：这份意志曾令我们超越尘世的破碎和自身的渺小，触碰灵性初涌的辉光，如今也是一同。\
**6**: The determination that once helped us overcome our insignificance and touch the light of pneuma, should guide us once more.

黑暗中，他燃起了一道火炬。\
In the darkness, he lights up a torch.

**888**：……你要去哪？\
**888**: Where are you going?

**6**：向深处去。\
**6**: To the cave.

**6**：先贤的考验尚未结束，最终的净化还未抵达。我们的义务，亦未尽下。\
**6**: The trial is not over. The final cleansing is yet to come. There are still duties to fulfill.

然后，他不再驻足。\
He trudges forward.

背着惶然的人群，他独自朝着漫漫无尽的净化之路走去。\
With his back to the fearful crowd, he sets off again, onto the lonely road, into the long night.

## 7TH-12 豆子派对 / The Party of Beans

**维尔汀**：唔……\

剧情场景-学派公共区(1.4旧场景，叠我们那个有白边的滤镜）

广场上人声鼎沸，相比平日的肃穆和洁净，平添了许多分节庆的色彩。\
The square is alive with joy and activity. The usual silence and seriousness have been replaced by a symphony of giggles and cheers.

空气中盈满着烤兔子的香气。人们搬来装有葡萄酒的罐子，一边饮啜一边交谈。\
The aroma of roast rabbit is thick in the air. Barrels of wine are being rolled around, and people are gathered, drinking and chatting merrily.

**红弩箭**：哈！这酒还不错，是你们自己酿的？\
**Lilya**: Ah! Nice wine. Did you make it yourself?

**维尔汀**：……白色的……公鸡？\
**Vertin**: A white rooster?

人们喜悦着，欢笑着，互相道贺着。\
Cheers and shouts fill the air as people revel in jubilant euphoria.

一名基金会的职员拾起了地上掉落的证件。\
A Foundation employee picks up an ID from the ground.

一名教众于道路中央劈开了一节木柴。\
An Apeiron believer splits a log in half on the road, earning enthusiastic applause from the crowd.

他们吃着鹰嘴豆拌成的沙拉，将桌上的面包切成整齐的数片，用刀剑拨弄广场上的火炬，令它燃得更旺盛些。\
The tables are filled with chickpea salad and neatly sliced bread, while people use their swords to poke fires and keep them burning.

那火焰熊熊燃烧，却没有倒映出任何影子。\
The flames burn fiercely, casting no shadows on the ground.

**维尔汀**：不，这里的一切都不太对劲！\
**Vertin**: Something's not right. None of this is right!

**维尔汀**：小岛发生了某种变故，我并没有真正离开地底！\
**Vertin**: Something's happened on the island. I must still be in the cave!

焦急的心情在胸腔中蔓延，为一切眼前的乐景蒙上了阴霾。\
A churning anxiety fills the chest. The once-joyful scene now takes on a surreal quality.

**维尔汀**：我得立刻离开这儿——！\
**Vertin**: I have to get out of here!

画面-黑屏。

**77**: How ugly, how inelegant! How could this be the revelation from the patterns of the transcendental Law above? How could such a terrible answer fall on my ears?!

白屏-逐渐醒来的感觉

意识猛然惊醒。\
Consciousness is snapped back to reality.

**37**：星锑接管了6的职位，宣布这里以后就是无理数的摇滚王国。她狞笑着拿了一罐咖啡，逼迫我吃下豆子……\
**37**: Regulus claimed 6's throne and declared this the rock 'n' roll empire of irrational numbers. She took out a jar of coffee beans and stuffed one into my mouth.

37摇了摇头，似乎极力想把这荒唐的一幕从脑海里甩走。\
37 shakes her head hard, as if trying to rid her mind of the horrific scene.

**37**: I'm relieved that I woke up in time. And you as well!

**37**: Let's go, Vertin! We need to tell everyone the numbers.

她雀跃地说着，脸上洋溢着摆脱噩梦的真切喜悦。\
She chirps, her face lighting up with delight, finally free from the long nightmare.

洞穴的前方透出了狭窄的天光。\
A beam of daylight appears before them.

这趟漫长无比的试炼之旅终于迎来了应有的终点。\
The lengthy trial has finally come to an end.

**37**：听，维尔汀，外面听起来真热闹！\

**37**：一定是苏菲亚来接我了！我告诉她在外面等我的。\
**37**: Must be Sophia here to pick me up! I told her she can wait for me outside.

**37**：——苏菲亚！\
**37**: Sophia!

女孩欢欣地向光亮奔去。\
The girl runs happily towards the light.

像一只灵巧的雨燕，在视线中一晃而过。\
Like a young swallow swooping out of sight.

**Vertin**: Wait, 37!

得追上她。\
Got to catch up.

得离开这里。\
Got to leave this place at once.

得把地底的发现告诉其他人。\
Must share the findings here with the others.

——终于，那道刺眼的天光就在眼前了。\
Finally, the light of day comes into view.

气流毫无征兆地在眼前卷起，洞穴出口的几何石块在眼前飞出。\
A gust of wind suddenly rushes by, sending pebbles scattering across the ground.

一股似曾相识的味道刺激着鼻腔。\
The all too familiar stench of sulfur fills the air.

——那是属于战争的硝烟味。\
It is unmistakably the smoke of war.
