**Vertin**: What?

## 7TH-13 艺术浪潮 / The Wave of Art

**军人Ⅰ**：**的，为什么开火许可一直没有下来？\
**Soldier I**: F**k! When do they give us the order to attack?

**军人Ⅰ**：我们在等什么？那座岛就在对岸，我们有士兵、有装备、有补给，我们什么都有了——只差一个抢滩登陆的命令。\
**Soldier I**: What's taking so long? The island is just across the bay. We have men, weapons, supplies, everything. Just give us order, and we will take to shore.

**军人Ⅰ**：噢……甚至还有这些黑乎乎的“伙计们”，那个宣称自己从“瓦尔登湖”来的军火商提供的“对神秘学改良武器”……\
**Soldier I**: Check out these bad boys. Anti-arcanum weapons, courtesy of the American from that "Walden" place.

**军人Ⅰ**：——虽然我不喜欢那个阴阳怪气的家伙，他身上也散发着神秘学家的臭味……\
**Soldier I**: That creep just doesn't sit right with me. He's got that arcanist stink about him.

**军人Ⅰ**：但他提供的技术是毋庸置疑的，我们必须先于塞尔维亚人和希腊人行动！\
**Soldier I**: But his technology's solid, and we needed it. We've got to get ahead of the Serbs and the Greeks!

这支部队已经在这里驻扎了许久。\
This army has been stationed here for a long time, perhaps too long.

此前登陆的失败令他们恼怒，漫长的政治协商又挫伤了士气。饱满的弹匣被弃置一旁，士兵转而拿出了加热餐点的酒精灯。\
The soldiers, stranded and demoralized by their failed landing, face days of uncertainty without orders while politicians bicker. They are left to heat their food meal by meal, watching their chances slip away.

**军人Ⅱ**：别太急，格奥尔基……你得相信那些大人物，他们会“协商”好的。\
**Soldier II**: Relax, Georgiy. Leave the decisions to the big shots. I'm sure they'll just hug out their differences in the meeting room or something.

**军人Ⅱ**：而且，那座岛上的怪物你也瞧见了——难道你这么急着去送死吗？\
**Soldier II**: Besides, you saw the monsters on that island. Can't speak for everyone here, but I don't want to die.

**军人Ⅰ**：去**的协商委员会……是我们！我们才是发现岛屿的第一人！而不是奥地利人和德国人！\
**Soldier I**: Screw the negotiations, screw the committee! Like it or not, we were the first ones to find the island! Not the Austrians or the Germans!

军士愤怒地拿起望远镜，又一次试图捕捉海对面那座缥缈的岛屿。\
He grumbles and picks the monocular back up, straining to catch another glimpse of the island across the waters.

望远镜中的海洋一如既往地平静，偶尔跳跃着细碎的粼光，并未有任何陆地或者活物的景象。\
The sea is tranquil, as it often is this time of year. The water sparkles under the golden sun, stretching to the horizon without an island in sight.

**军人Ⅰ**：见鬼，那些神秘学家又把自己藏起来了！\
**Soldier I**: Damn, those arcanists have gone into hiding again.

**军人Ⅰ**：我发誓，昨天我还能从这个角度看见它……\
**Soldier I**: I swear I could see it from here yesterday.

**军人Ⅰ**：……嗯？\
**Soldier I**: Hm?

意想之外的状况，男人简直不敢相信自己的眼睛。\
He blinks, unsure if his eyes are tricking him.

**军人Ⅰ**：那些怪鸟——正在成群结队地离开？\
**Soldier I**: Are those bird-like creatures leaving in droves?

没有太多人注意到他的行为，其他人更关心补给箱上摊开的纸牌。\
His words barely catch anyone's attention. A new poker game is underway on the supply crate.

一台收音机，几瓶啤酒，一局扑克游戏——难得的好时光。\
A radio, a couple of beers, and a game of poker—a rare moment of enjoyment. Who could ask for more?

**军人Ⅱ**：嘿，格奥尔基，别管了，来玩牌吧！\
**Soldier II**: Georgiy, brother, leave them be. Come, play with us.

**军人Ⅱ**：……格奥尔基？\
**Soldier II**: Georgiy?

被叫到名字的军士充耳不闻。\
The soldier does not seem to hear his name.

他只是抓住望远镜，不住地喃喃自语。\
He grips the monocular tightly, his mouth contorting as he mutters.

**军人Ⅰ**：多好的机会，绝佳的机会，千载难逢的好机会——\
**Soldier I**: What a good opportunity this is. It's too good to pass up. We, we've got to act now.

一滴斑斓的油彩自他的脸上滑落，“啪嗒”一声，粘在了地面上。\
A drop of vibrant paint slides down his cheek and lands on the ground with a splatter.

**军人Ⅰ**：对，那座岛本就该属于我们，它在我们的海上，是我们发现了它——它有什么理由不属于我们！！！\
**Soldier I**: We will claim what is ours. This island belongs to us. It's in our territory, and we were the first to find it—why shouldn't it be ours!?

玩牌的人们止住了，他们惊愕地看着同僚脸上的异状，浑然不觉自己身上也出现了诡谲的油彩。\
The card players pause, gawking at the paint sliding down each other's faces, unaware that their own faces are melting as well.

静默之中，只有收音机还在发出沙沙的响声。\
In the silence, the only sound that fills the air is the static of the radio.

**广播**：奥匈帝国向塞尔维亚正式宣战……\
**Broadcast**: The Austro-Hungarian Empire has officially declared war on Serbia.

**广播**：俄国动员部队支持塞尔维亚，德国要求俄国停止战争动员……\
**Broadcast**: Russia is mobilizing in support of Serbia. Germany demands Russia to stop mobilizing at once.

**广播**：德国开始战争动员，法国开始战争动员——\
**Broadcast**: Germany is mobilizing. France is mobilizing.

**卡卡尼亚**：呼哈，哈——\
**Kakania**: *panting*

剧情场景-变异的维也纳街头（复用场景）\
The street has turned into a canvas of mesmerizing hues. The colorful paints swirl and burst, creating one spiral after another.

街道已经变成了扭曲的油画，颜料拥挤着发酵，一个旋涡，紧接着另一个旋涡。\
It's almost like the stage set of a twisted carnival.

——像是一处怪诞剧的舞台布景。

**卡卡尼亚**：父亲，母亲，阿尔伯德，伊丽莎白！\
**Kakania**: Father, Mother! Elbert! Ilse!

**卡卡尼亚**：快开门！我有重要的事要告诉你们！\
**Kakania**: Open the door! It's important! You have to listen to me!

她的手捶在了温格勒家的门板上，那里很快像一块融化的黄油般凹陷了下去。\
She pounds on the door, but as soon as she makes contact, the door softens and melts like butter.

卡卡尼亚摔进了家中，里面扭曲的骇人光景又让她退了出来。\
She trips through the door, but quickly recoils at the horror inside.

往日放着标本和装饰画的温馨玄关，已经变成了一个搅拌着颜料的洗衣桶。\
The art and specimens, once delicate and exquisite, now resemble a jumble of spilled paint.

**卡卡尼亚**：不，不——怎么会变成这样……\
**Kakania**: No, no. This can't be.

**卡卡尼亚**：阿尔伯德……？\
**Kakania**: Elbert?

带着一丝侥幸，她呼唤着哥哥的名字。\
Still with a glimmer of hope, she carefully calls out to her brother.

**阿尔伯德**：克拉拉……？真是稀奇，什么事能让你慌张成这样？\
**Elbert**: Klara? It's odd to see you so flustered. What's the matter?

不幸中的万幸，玄关里传来了一声熟悉的回应。\
The familiar voice brings immense relief to her heart.

**阿尔伯德**：唉，我正要去商学院呢，你有话可以等我回来再说。\
**Elbert**: I'm headed to the business school. We'll talk when I get back.

阿尔伯德拿起帽子，小心地调整了一下帽檐的角度——那上面还别着一枚属于“温格勒商店”的宝石别针。\
Elbert picks up the hat and adjusts the brim. The pin on the hat, "Vingler's Shop," shimmers in the dim light.

谢天谢地，他看起来一切都好。\
Thank goodness, he seems to be fine.

仍是记忆里那个家族的骄傲，最为可靠的长兄，穿着三件套西装的温和绅士。\
He's still the reliable brother she remembers, the family's pride, in his sharp three-piece suit.

**卡卡尼亚**：不对，商学院……？\
**Kakania**: Business school?

**卡卡尼亚**：可你……不是发誓不再踏入那里一步吗？因为那个找你决斗的人类同窗打残了你的胳膊……\
**Kakania**: But, didn't you swear to never go back? Ever since your human classmate shot your arm in a duel.

**卡卡尼亚**：等等，你的右手……？\
**Kakania**: Wait, what happened to your arm?

阿尔伯德转过身来，现在卡卡尼亚看清了。\
He turns around, and Kakania can finally see.

笔挺的西装被染成了花色，颜料一直从他的脸上流到地上。\
Half of his suit is covered in colors, paint trailing down his face and pooling at his feet.

一只颜色不同的胳膊接在了他的身上，就像不同花色的马赛克拼贴砖。\
An arm of flowing colors is attached to his body, like a mismatched puzzle piece.

**阿尔伯德**：喔，你是在说伊森……是的，他打伤了我，这也没办法。毕竟他急需向兄弟会证明自己的反神秘学立场。\
**Elbert**: Oh, Ethan. Yes, he wounded me. He had to prove his standing to the brotherhood. There was no other way.

**阿尔伯德**：没关系，我们已经扯平了——他把胳膊还给了我。\
**Elbert**: But that's in the past. He gave me his arm, so now we're even.

阿尔伯德扬起左手，那把尖刀上还沾着些许残沫。\
He raises his left hand to show her the blade. Streaks of blood are still on it.

他将它随意地一扔，刀柄滚向黑暗，没入狂热的油画漩涡之中。\
He casually tosses it aside, letting it clatter into the darkness and disappear into the swirls of colors.

阿尔伯德拿起手杖，那只拼接上去的胳膊无力地在身侧垂着，像是一个被俘获的人质。\
Elbert grabs his walking stick, his new arm dangling lifelessly at his side.

**阿尔伯德**：是时候了，现在我得去找约翰逊、雷蒙德，还有赫伯特，那个将伊丽莎白推到喷泉里的混账……他们总得付出点代价。\
**Elbert**: I have to go. I have to find Johnson, Raymond, and Herbert. That little rascal pushed Ilse into the fountain. We have a score to settle.

**阿尔伯德**：照顾好自己，克拉拉。\
**Elbert**: Take care, Klara.

他径直从妹妹身旁走过，甚至还拦下了一辆长着三角轮胎的马车。\
He strides past her and hails a carriage with triangles for wheels at the door.

**卡卡尼亚**：不，阿尔伯德——别走！\
**Kakania**: No, Elbert! Don't go!

她试图截住马车，可它咆哮着向远处驶去，就像无法阻止的“暴雨”洪流。\
She runs to stop the carriage, but it is unaffected by her efforts, like everything else in this place.

一阵清脆的脚步声在靠近。\
A set of footsteps approach from behind.

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚医生，暴雨症候群已经蔓延开来了！再待下去，您也会感染癔症！\
**Marcus**: The Storm Syndrome is spreading, doctor! Stay any longer, you'll be infected, too!

**马库斯**：请和我一起——唔！\
**Marcus**: Please, leave with me. Oh!

地面微微的震颤打断了她的劝告。\
The trembling ground interrupts her.

面孔扭曲的人们咆哮着狂热的口号，嘶吼着用母语写成的歌谣，从街道的另一头涌来。\
A mob with distorted faces swarms through the streets, chanting slogans and singing in their own tongues.

非黑即白的战争宣传单从他们手里落下，像雪花般飘落在变形的环城大道上，很快被乱腾的色彩吞没。\
White pro-war pamphlets litter the ground, like snowflakes being absorbed into a mire of effervescent paints.

如同一辆倾轧一切的战车，一个做着华尔兹旋转的火药桶。\
The city is bursting with unrelenting energy, like a speeding chariot or a twirling powder keg.

**卡卡尼亚**：站在队首举牌的是……奥罗拉？\
**Kakania**: The sign bearer in the parade ... Is that Aurora?

**卡卡尼亚**：我们上周还一起在咖啡馆谈论着她的婚礼……\
**Kakania**: I just met her at the coffee house last week. We were talking about her wedding.

**马库斯**：小心，医生……！\
**Marcus**: Watch out, doctor!

——她们险些被一根倾倒的指示牌击中。\
A sign crashes to the ground beside them.

亢奋的市民们肆意破坏着街道的摆设，甚至将行人椅的扶手圈也挥舞在手里。\
Rage-filled citizens are tearing the streets apart. Even the handles of roadside benches are yanked off and made a weapon.

这股热潮要求所有相遇的人——都必须加入。没有选择。\
The fervent protest consumes all who come across it, forcing them to participate with no option to decline.

**马库斯**：糟透了，他们已经彻底丧失理智了！\
**Marcus**: This is bad. They have lost their minds!

**马库斯**：医生，快跟我来，我们必须离开这儿！\
**Marcus**: This way, doctor. We have to get out of here!

剧情场景-变异的维也纳街头（复用场景）

**马库斯**：医生，往这儿走！我们得退回到您的诊所，那是和特别行动队商定的地点——\
**Marcus**: This way, doctor! We have to go back to your clinic. The special operations squad will meet us there.

年轻的调查员牵着医生的手，试图履行自己的职责。\
The young investigator holds the doctor's hand, determined to do her duty.

目标对象却停住了脚步。她的头深深地低垂着。\
But the doctor halts her steps and droops her head, looking dejected.

**卡卡尼亚**：……马库斯小姐。您曾经说过，我们还有一个弥补的机会。\
**Kakania**: Marcus. You once said that there was another way to make things right.

**卡卡尼亚**：而后，您做了您想做的，我也做了我应做的。\
**Kakania**: And then you did your part, as I did mine.

**卡卡尼亚**：现在，请您告诉我，我们做的事还有意义吗？\
**Kakania**: But now, after all that's happened, please tell me, what's the point of us trying?

**卡卡尼亚**：我们赶上了吗？或者，我们还有任何，哪怕是一点，挽回现状的机会么？\
**Kakania**: Will we save them in time? Is there any chance that we can turn things around?

她的声音因悲伤而哽咽。\
She struggles to hold back a sob.

人群的熙攘与咆哮尚未远去。但昨日的环城大道，却只能停留在记忆中了。\
The roaring crowd fades into the distance, and the Ring Road of yesterday is now but a distant memory, never to be relived.

**卡卡尼亚**：你们拿到的术式，那个你们说能帮助到所有人的“庇佑”，现在……它能生效了吗？\
**Kakania**: The ritual you acquired, the one you said could save everyone, is it working now?

**哑谜**：——让我进去。\
**Enigma**: Let me in.

拉普拉斯科算中心-走廊

科算中心的走廊已经不复理性的洁净。\
The floor in Laplace's corridor has lost its clean, silvery sheen.

道金斯变成的泥巴傀儡无疑给它来了一记痛击，安全员们用上了所有的洁净球，才使地板重新露出了泥土之外的颜色。\
Dawkins and his slobbering mud certainly played a major role in the destruction. The guards used every cleaning orb in their inventory to restore even a hint of its original glory.

现在，一双愤怒的脚步迈过了它。罔顾同僚的阻拦，哑谜留下了一连串新鲜的泥印。\
A pair of angry feet stomp across the floor, ignoring their colleague's attempts to stop them. Enigma adds more muddy footprints without hesitation.

**哑谜**：我只是想问一件事。\
**Enigma**: I have just one question.

**哑谜**：为什么——你们到底为什么还不停止实验？\
**Enigma**: Why hasn't the project stopped yet?

他的努力得到了回应。\
His outcry elicits a reaction.

通往总负责人办公室的铁门打开了，一个同样怒气冲冲的身影走了出来。\
The door to the director's office flings open, and an angry figure storms out.

**破译组长**：阿德勒·霍夫曼，你已经不是研究小组的成员了！你无权进入这条走廊！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Adler Hofmann, you have been removed from the team. You're not authorized to be here!

**破译组长**：你现在的行为严重违反了——\
**Cryptography Lead**: You have violated ...

**哑谜**：严重违反了《拉普拉斯科算中心安全管理条例》？我把它带来了，不用客气。\
**Enigma**: The LSCC Safety Management Regulations? I brought them with me. You're welcome.

研究员把那本记录着管理条文的手册甩在了前组长脸上。\
He throws the hefty manual right onto his former leader's face.

**哑谜**：如果你的心里还有一点“条例”的概念，你就应该知道，现在发生的事没有一条是符合它的。\
**Enigma**: If you cared about the regulations as much as you claim, you'd know that none of what's happening aligns with its guidelines.

**哑谜**：即使是总负责人也没有权限在目前的情况下继续实验！\
**Enigma**: Even the head of Laplace has no authority to continue the experiment under these circumstances!

他的话没能说完，前组长已经极不客气地打断了他。\
Before he can continue, his ex-leader sharply cuts him off.

**破译组长**：滚开，阿德勒，我没空和你争论这些繁文缛节。现在是战时状态！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Get out of my face, Adler. I don't have time for this. We're in a state of war!

**破译组长**：所有实验的参与者均签署了知情同意书，无关实验的人员请立刻离开。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Every participant has signed an informed consent form. If you are not part of this project, please leave immediately!

**破译组长**：距离“暴雨”落下只有十八个小时了，这是九次“暴雨”中最有希望的一次，唯一有突破性进展的一次！\
**Cryptography Lead**: We only have 18 hours until the "Storm." This is it—the first time we've made such a breakthrough in all nine "Storms"!

**破译组长**：——别忘了，这希望还是你姐姐用性命为我们带回来的！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Your sister gave up her life to take us this far. I hope you don't need me to remind you that!

阿德勒·霍夫曼突然沉默了。\
Adler Hofmann is abruptly silent.

褐色的眼睛里冒出一股遏抑已久的愤怒。\
A fiery rage ignites in his hazel eyes.

在这沉默之中，破译组长意识到自己也许说错了话。\
A deafening void engulfs the space as Ulrich realizes his verbal blunder.

**哑谜**：嗯，是啊，她牺牲了，为我们带来突破性的成果。而后，更多人牺牲了。\
**Enigma**: Yes. She made the ultimate sacrifice, hoping that it would lead to a breakthrough. But instead, death continues to rise.

**哑谜**：——事情就是这么发生的，对吧？\
**Enigma**: How can you let this go on?

而后，他猛地冲上去，用胳膊把对方推到了一边。\
He charges ahead, shoving Ulrich aside with his elbow.

破译组长的头磕到了墙上，冲击波不可避免地在磁流体上成了像——一个爆炸的火花。\
Ulrich's head slams against the wall, ferrofluids shifting erratically inside.

**哑谜**：我必须要知道继续这一切疯狂实验的理由！\
**Enigma**: I demand to know why the experiment is still going!

被踢出小组的家伙儿开始违规破译那道加密的安全门，似乎打定主意要在今天用上司办公室的密码来挽回研究成果。\
He starts working on the padlock on the door. Nothing's going to stop him from breaking through today.

走廊的警报被拉响了，乌尔里希捂着自己的头，恼怒地扶着墙站起来。\
The alarm goes off. Ulrich struggles to his feet against the wall, a hand up to his head.

**破译组长**：见鬼，我们这里的疯子还不够多吗？！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Ugh, don't we have enough crazies around here?!

**破译组长**：露西女士在忙重要的事，没空见你！找你的心理医生聊天去，人类！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Madam Lucy has important things to do. She has no time for you! Go cry to your therapist, human!

**哑谜**：重要？！有什么事能比这更重要？！\
**Enigma**: Important? What could be possibly more important than this, right now?

**哑谜**：这里已经变成机器的一言堂了吗？基金会的人道主义原则是彻底子虚乌有了吗？？？\
**Enigma**: What happened to the humanitarian ideals of the Foundation? Are we now under the tyranny of machines?

**哑谜**：她到底在做什么？！在我们乱成一团时，喝着机油读着报，泡在230伏特的电压池里充电吗？\
**Enigma**: What's this important thing she's got to do? Reading the paper, sipping on oil, and charging up in a 230-volt bath?

安全密码被解出来了。哑谜再度推开了组长的臂膀，冲进了那道门中。\
He cracks the code. Pushing Ulrich's arms aside, Enigma forces his way into the room.

房间里一片漆黑。\
The room is completely dark.

“哒、哒、哒。”\
Tchk-tchk-tchk.

一个活塞正在他的脚下旋转。\
A piston spins at his feet.

**露西**：……这不是阿德勒吗？\
**Lucy**: Is that you, Adler?

**露西**：欢迎你。\
**Lucy**: Welcome.

## 7TH-14 干沙粒 / A Sandstorm in a Room

剧场场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-露西的实验室-黑暗版本。\
The piston rotates on the floor like a toy top.

蒸汽活塞在地上旋转，像一个滑稽的陀螺。

**露西**：嗯，这不是一个适合说话的姿态。\
**Lucy**: Hmm. I am not in a suitable form to receive a guest.

**露西**：希曼，可以把我装回去吗？\
**Lucy**: Simone, can you put me back in my body?

总负责人的助理匆匆走了过来，力所能及地对机器进行了修整。\
Her assistant rushes over and puts her into a robot body.

**露西**：——谢谢，我感觉好多了。\
**Lucy**: I feel much better. Thank you.

**露西**：噢，你还为我挑选了有脸的形态，真贴心。\
**Lucy**: Oh, you have even put on a face for me. How sweet of you.

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

**露西**：我注意到你的眼神很严格，阿德勒研究员。你似乎渴望纠正这里的逻辑。\
**Lucy**: I have noticed your icy gaze, Researcher Adler. You are yearning to correct the logic of this place.

**露西**：好的，刚刚那句话是出于礼貌。实际上，装入哪具躯壳对我而言没有区别。\
**Lucy**: Well, I only said that to Simone out of courtesy. In reality, whichever body I am put into makes no difference to me.

机器不合时宜的人性化发言令研究员更为恼怒。\
Her ill-timed explanation annoys him even more.

**哑谜**：……为什么您不终止实验，露西女士？\
**Enigma**: The experiment, ma'am. Why hasn't it stopped?

**哑谜**：是您忽略了发生在这里的牺牲？\
**Enigma**: Are you going to pretend that nothing's happened? That no one died?

**哑谜**：还是您和乌尔里希——你们这些装在铁皮里的意识唤醒者——根本就没有人命的概念？\
**Enigma**: Could it be that you and Ulrich, "the Awakened," being the tin cans you are, have no regard for actual lives?

**破译组长**：阿德勒·霍夫曼，我再次警告你——\
**Cryptography Lead**: Adler Hofmann, I will not warn you again ...

被提到名字的组长气冲冲地带着安全员走了进来，想把这颗不安分的螺栓按回原位。\
Ulrich storms back into the room with two guards, ready to throw him out at any moment.

**露西**：没关系，阿德勒研究员。你现有的偏执只是因为掌握信息不足，导致了程序上的判断错误。\
**Lucy**: Relax, Adler. You are led by a biased opinion because you lack critical information. A common defect in all cognitive processes.

**露西**：我相信，你在充分了解情况后，也会做出最为理性的判断。\
**Lucy**: I believe you will shift to a more rational perspective once you receive sufficient information on the subject.

**哑谜**：理性的判断！\
**Enigma**: "A more rational perspective"?!

以理性而闻名的人类夸张地喊了起来。\
The human, known for his logical thinking, responds with an overwhelming amount of feeling.

**哑谜**：可我们不是机器，露西女士，我们也不是可供更换的零件！\
**Enigma**: We are humans, not machines! We are not expendable parts!

**哑谜**：我有充分的理由怀疑，您在研究推进上的一意孤行，只是神秘学家一种特殊的失控表现——\
**Enigma**: I have plenty of reasons to question your decisions. Your excessive insistence on this experiment could be a sign of uncontrollable behavior, a trait commonly seen in arcanists.

**露西**：实验已经被终止了。\
**Lucy**: The experiment has been canceled everywhere.

**露西**：——除了这个房间。\
**Lucy**: Except for this very room.

**哑谜**：——什么？\
**Enigma**: What?

机器微笑了一下，似乎认为对方理应为这个回复而高兴。\
The robot flashes a smile, as if anticipating the man to be pleased with her response.

**露西**：正如你和兔毛手袋研究员之前提醒的，这个术式超越了绝大多数科算中心成员能力的限度。他们在术式生效前就会被副作用烧毁。\
**Lucy**: As you and Researcher Medicine Pocket have said, the ritual is beyond the limits of almost everyone here. The side effects will kill them before the ritual can even take effect.

**露西**：第一波传播是不可抗力，朵拉当时已经按下了发送键。后续传播则被及时拦截，无关人员也得到疏散。\
**Lucy**: The first wave was inevitable. Dora had pressed send before she disintegrated. We only managed to halt the subsequent transmissions, and evacuate the unaffiliated staff.

**露西**：现在参与实验的，只有少数签署了知情同意书的神秘学家。\
**Lucy**: We kept only a few arcanists on the team, and each has signed the consent form.

知情同意——是的，又是这个该死的词。\
Mutual consent. That bloody form again.

**哑谜**：——请原谅我引用您的论点，露西女士。\
**Enigma**: Forgive me, ma'am, but I have to use your argument against you.

**哑谜**：您的乐观只是因为推断能力的不足。我们面对的到底是什么东西？只是念几个音节，就会招致这样的诅咒！\
**Enigma**: You, too, are guided by a biased opinion—an overly optimistic one—because you have failed to properly assess the risks involved. We have suffered enough misfortunes just by uttering a few syllables of the incantation!

**哑谜**：既然您也知道那个“限度”，就应该让剩下的人也退出。这完全是白费力气，只会让牺牲上徒增牺牲！\
**Enigma**: We've talked about the "limit" of things before. You should know better and ask the rest of the team to quit the experiment. Your insistence will only bring calamity upon calamity on our people, for nothing!

研究员恼怒地压下刺痛的神经，再度重复了自己已经在走廊上大声吼叫过一遍的观点。\
The researcher fights to stay calm, reiterating his views he had already shouted in the hallway.

破译组长显然也想再次说些反驳的话，但总负责人只是点了点头。\
Ulrich begins his retort, but the director simply nods in agreement.

**露西**：嗯，你也许是正确的。\
**Lucy**: Hm. You might be right.

**露西**：——但是，正确又有什么用呢？\
**Lucy**: But how is "being right" going to help us?

**哑谜**：……啊？\
**Enigma**: Huh?

她露出了一个可称温和的笑容，但效果适得其反。\
She grins, trying for a warm, gentle smile, but it comes across as anything but.

研究员一直很不喜欢这张假脸，它做出人情味的徒劳尝试反而更凸显了钢铁的无情。\
Enigma despised that face. Every time she tried to show a hint of humanity, it only served to highlight how different she was from everyone else.

**露西**：你刚刚说到“限度”。\
**Lucy**: You spoke of the "limit."

**露西**：我很意外，竟然是你说出了这个词。\
**Lucy**: And I am surprised that it is you who brought it up.

这几乎是人身攻击了，就连最擅此道的哑谜也为此意外了一秒。\
Enigma pauses for a second, not sure if she's being sarcastic.

**露西**：我们所知的历史里，新石器时代后物种的躯体变化速度已在逐步放缓。然而，与此同时，人类的文明却蓬勃发展，不断取得辉煌的成就。\
**Lucy**: The physical appearance of humans has remained relatively unchanged since the Neolithic era, but their thoughts and civilization continued to evolve and underwent significant transformations.

**露西**：这并非你们中的某个人突然获得了恒星般巨大的神力，而是整个群体不断协同的结果。\
**Lucy**: The achievements that humanity enjoys today were not given to the species by any one person with godlike powers, but were the result of the collective efforts of all human beings.

**露西**：文明的发展，科技的突破，正在于我们一次又一次地超越限度。我们突破自身的桎梏，使用智慧和工具改造四周。\
**Lucy**: Limits and boundaries must be pushed, or there would never have been room for development. There is no reason to believe that the limit cannot be challenged, especially when we already have the tools to do so.

**露西**：——也就是我们所说的，进步。\
**Lucy**: We must make progress happen.

**哑谜**：……磅礴的漂亮话。\
**Enigma**: Grandiose lies.

**露西**：磅礴的漂亮话，是吗？\
**Lucy**: Lies?

——该死，他忘了机器无疑也拥有卓越的听力。\
Oh, crap. He forgot about her excellent hearing.

**露西**：现实如此，我们必须越过限度。\
**Lucy**: We have no choice but to go beyond that limit.

**露西**：我们必须突破雨幕的桎梏，不然任何进步都无从谈起。\
**Lucy**: If we do not break away from the "Storm," there is no future for us, let alone progress.

**露西**：因此，全面了解术式副作用的种类和特性，是至关重要的第一步。它能为后续的消除工作提供数据基底，也能帮助更多人安全使用术式。\
**Lucy**: We need to first determine all the side effects as a priority. This important step will help us compile data and eliminate the effects, so our colleagues can use the ritual safely.

**哑谜**：……那谁有这个能力呢，尊敬的露西女士？我们可没有那么多条命来穷举。\
**Enigma**: And who will try it this time, Madam Lucy? You're not going to test the side effects at the cost of lives, are you?

**露西**：哦，其实多亏了乌尔里希先生，我们才从随机里找到了突破口。\
**Lucy**: No. Thanks to Ulrich, we stumbled upon a breakthrough.

**露西**：我想的确可以让其他神秘学家也回去了——只留下意识唤醒者。\
**Lucy**: You are right. It is time to send the other arcanists home. Only the Awakened are needed here.

**哑谜**：……意识唤醒者？\
**Enigma**: The Awakened?

灼眼的红色在钨丝上轻微地闪烁，随后房间的灯光明亮了起来。\
The tungsten wires glow faintly red in the dark, then the room is lit.

**助理希曼**：露西女士，电力恢复了。可以开始实验了。\
**Assistant Simone**: The power is back, ma'am. We are ready to resume.

**露西**：嗯，这场解释略有些冗长。\
**Lucy**: Hm. It will take time to properly explain.

**露西**：请稍作等待，阿德勒研究员。我们还未达成理性的一致。\
**Lucy**: Please wait, Adler. We have yet to reach an agreement.

**哑谜**：……什么？实验，在这里？\
**Enigma**: What? Are you experimenting? Here?

枉顾他的惊讶，露西坐到了铁质的实验台前。\
Ignoring his surprise, Lucy sits down on the iron bench.

灯光亮起，她的身上接满了电路。\
Wires of various sizes are attached to her body.

仪器的辉光管随着蒸汽活塞的律动而亮起，这台机器将如实地把这位意识唤醒者的一切行为记录下来。\
The instrument comes to life to the piston's rhythm, faithfully recording every change in the robot.

从最细微的旋转弧度，到可量化为电力的神秘术能量波动。\
From her slightest movements to arcane fluctuations, nothing goes unnoticed.

**露西**：……\
**Lucy**: ...

**露西**：La ünüa ...\
**Lucy**: La unua ...

**哑谜**：……什么，她要念咒？！\
**Enigma**: Wait. She's reciting it?

荒诞的举动令他惊愕，研究员徒劳地环顾起了实验室，不确定这是否是机器又一次语出惊人的尝试。\
Frozen in place by the scene, he looks around the room in disbelief.

**哑谜**：——她看过那些副作用的报告，对吧？甚至朵拉碎掉的时候，她也在场！\
**Enigma**: She's read the reports, right? She was there when Dora broke into pieces!

**露西**：……

**露西**：…………\
**Lucy**: ...

她少见地蜷缩起了背部。\
Rarely does her back curl up like this.

那张往常用来挂着笑容的脸，也在此刻呈现出了事与愿违的情感传达。\
The usual cheerful expression on her face has changed to one of unease, suggesting that something is amiss.

钢铁本不应该感到痛苦。机器没有躯体，也没有神经。\
A hunk of metal should not feel pain. They have no flesh, no nerves.

如果这令她也感到不堪忍受——那到底是什么在折磨她？\
But if she is in agony, what could be the cause of such torment?

**露西**：……唔……\
**Lucy**: ... Urrm ...

机器也会被摧毁吗？她会以什么形式碎裂？\
Will she break apart, too? Like those people?

“诅咒”正在虎视眈眈。\
The ominous "curse" has set its sights on its prey.

一如手持闪电的宙斯在高山上俯瞰着盗火者的挣扎。\
It watches, almost like Zeus on a mountaintop, ready to unleash lightning on the mortals who dare to steal fire.

**露西**：不行，希曼，我无法……\
**Lucy**: No, Simone ... I ...

**露西**：无法……再继续……\
**Lucy**: I cannot ... continue ...

**露西**：呃、呃……\
**Lucy**: Urgh ... Urrh ...

最原始的本能恐惧。

也是研究员第一次听到她的情感流露。\
The most primal, instinctual fear.

剧场场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-露西的实验室-亮灯版本\
This is the first time he's ever heard her emotions pour out so raw.

**哑谜**：——混账，你们在等什么？！为什么还不终止实验？\
**Enigma**: You fools, don't just stand there! Stop her! Now!

巨大的不安和惶恐震慑住了男人，他几乎就要冲上去拔掉电线。\
Panic and horror twist in his stomach. He has an irresistible urge to rip out the wires and put an end to her torture.

**哑谜**：她是科算中心的总负责人，如果她也停摆了，还有谁能担任这个位置！\
**Enigma**: Who's going to lead us if she also turns into a pile of scraps?!

**破译组长**：给我站好了，哑谜！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Stay where you are, Enigma!

组长恶狠狠的声音从背后传来。\
Ulrich's voice, full of animosity, comes from behind.

**破译组长**：这是你要进来的，这也是你要看的——\
**Cryptography Lead**: You insisted on being here. You demanded to see this.

**破译组长**：还是说，你那人道主义的范围从来都如此狭窄，不包括除自己以外的任何一个物种？\
**Cryptography Lead**: Don't bring your pathetic, narrow-minded humanitarian values in here and tell us what to do. What do you know about us?

实验台前，助理只是轻声地开口。\
Simone leans over to her. She speaks softly.

**助理希曼**：……您可以的，露西女士，这只是既定程式的一部分。\
**Assistant Simone**: You can do it, madam. This is just part of the established procedures.

**助理希曼**：您只要再坚持说出几个音节……这一切，就结束了。\
**Assistant Simone**: Just a few more syllables, madam, and it will be over.

**露西**：既定、程式……\
**Lucy**: Established ... procedures ...

恐惧褪去了几分，她感到宽慰地重复着。\
Fear ebbs away a little as she repeats those words.

**露西**：嗯，我喜欢……这个词。\
**Lucy**: I like ... that ...

机器闭上了眼睛。尽管她不由情感神经驱动——但她咬牙说出了最后的词语。\
Her eyes close. She forces out the last word with great determination.

**露西**：Cir ... klo.\
**Lucy**: Cir ... klo.

她终于念完了所有的咒文。\
It is done.

震动均匀，发声正确，无可挑剔。\
A clear, accurate, impeccable read.

实验室的灯光也在这一瞬间熄灭下去。\
Right at that moment, the lights in the lab go out.

**露西**：……呼，我念完了吗，希曼？\
**Lucy**: *sigh* Was that all, Simone?

**助理希曼**：是的。\
**Assistant Simone**: Yes.

黑暗中，无人看见她的表情。\
No one can see her face in the darkness.

但那理应是一个微笑。\
But Enigma believes it to be a smile.

**露西**：嗯，很好……\
**Lucy**: Good.

**哑谜**：……！\
**Enigma**: ...!

那是一场未经预报的小型沙尘暴。\
A gust of sand rises in the room.

毫无征兆，突如其来，在这个封闭的暗室之中呼啸。\
Without warning and out of nowhere, it screams through the enclosed darkness.

它卷走了那具冰冷的铁质躯体。\
The raging storm engulfs the robot's cold metal body, carrying her away with great force.

最后，只有一个老旧的活塞从空中掉了下来。\
When the sand subsides, all that remains is an old piston, clattering to the ground.

动画-一个活塞从画面上方落下，伴随音效。\
"Clang."

“——噔。”

## 7TH-15 前行者 / The Pioneers

剧场场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-露西的实验室-黑暗版本。

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

死寂。\
A deathly silence.

直到人类研究员踉跄地后退一步，几乎因为撞到另一人而摔倒。\
Until Enigma stumbles back, nearly falling over another person in the room.

**哑谜**：……她……死了？\
**Enigma**: She's dead?

那枚活塞毫无生气地躺着，一如任何普通的物体。\
The piston lies motionless on the ground, as lifeless as any other object.

**哑谜**：……这就是你想让我看的？\
**Enigma**: This is what you wanted to show me?

呼吸变得急促，掌心因为汗水而粘连。\
His heart pounds in his ears as he pants, fists clenched and slick with sweat.

**哑谜**：看我们的总负责人如何为一道已经反复验证过的诅咒白白送死……？\
**Enigma**: To watch her utter a curse that's always brought death, only to die in vain?

**哑谜**：你们怎么能让这种事发生——？\
**Enigma**: And you just let it happen?!

而另一个意识唤醒者只是平静地站在他身后。\
Ulrich looks at him, his voice poised and steady.

**破译组长**：你冷静一点。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Calm down.

**哑谜**：冷静？你让我怎么冷静？！她死了，就在这里！几乎是你杀了她！！！\
**Enigma**: Calm down? She's dead, right there! You murderer!

**破译组长**：——这项实验已经进行很多次了。\
**Cryptography Lead**: We have already repeated this experiment many times.

一个更重磅的消息。足以让那些未出口的疑问被取代。\
Enigma is in disbelief.

**哑谜**：……很多次？你们重复这样——杀人一般的进程……很多次？\
**Enigma**: "Many times"? What?! You've sent people to their deaths over and over again?

磁流体眯成了一个长条，近似于一张“不屑”的脸。\
The ferrofluid flows again, forming a shape that Enigma can only interpret as disdain.

**破译组长**：看看你的样子，阿德勒研究员，你被那些诅咒吓破了胆，以至忽视了那个最重要的问题。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Look at you, Adler, peeing your pants over a "curse." The human boy is so scared that he forgot to ask the crucial question—

**破译组长**：——术式到底有没有生效？\
**Cryptography Lead**: Did the ritual work?

**哑谜**：……什么意思？诅咒……不就代表着失败吗？\
**Enigma**: What, what do you mean? The curse, the side effect killed her. The experiment failed. Is that not what happened?

**破译组长**：不，这是两个部分。因为我才是第一个念咒的人，远早于朵拉。\
**Cryptography Lead**: No, triggering the curse and failure are two separate things. I was the first one to recite the incantation. Way before Dora.

**破译组长**：我念出了它，它生效了。我能感受到，那种奇迹一般的庇佑之力，像羽毛一样轻轻落在了我头上。\
**Cryptography Lead**: When I read it aloud, it worked. I felt the warmth of a miraculous blessing on my head, soft, light as a feather.

**破译组长**：我急着把喜讯传递给露西女士。当她离去后，诅咒才降临在我的身上——我的全身都开始溶解。\
**Cryptography Lead**: I told Madam Lucy right away, but as soon as she left the room, the "curse" hit me, and I began to liquefy.

**破译组长**：当时我旁边没有任何人。我化为的液体太稀薄，甚至无法按下呼救按钮。\
**Cryptography Lead**: There was no one else in the room. My liquid form had become too insubstantial to push the help button.

**破译组长**：但在无尽的黑暗后，我还是醒来了，以我最初在世上觉醒的模样。\
**Cryptography Lead**: A long darkness followed. After that, I woke up again in my original primitive form, the way I first came into this world.

**哑谜**：最初的模样……？\
**Enigma**: Original primitive form?

磁流体闪了闪，在乌尔里希的肢体语言里，这与点头等效。\
The ferrofluid pulsates, which in Ulrich's body language is a nod.

**破译组长**：和你们不同，意识唤醒者没有血肉，没有神经，只是一段意识，一段原始的律动，恰好承载于某样物件之中。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Unlike humans, the Awakened have neither flesh nor nerves. We are pieces of consciousness, echoes of a primordial melody, that just happen to reside in material objects by chance.

**破译组长**：是这份纯粹让我们能与你们平等地交流，实验术式与经受诅咒。\
**Cryptography Lead**: With a mind and a body combined, we could talk, learn, think like you do, and perform the experiment and endure the side effects.

**破译组长**：——而这道诅咒，无法触及到最初唤醒我们的“原始意识”。\
**Cryptography Lead**: And this curse, for some reason, cannot affect the "primal consciousness" that caused our awakening in the first place.

**破译组长**：因此，和依赖于有形之躯的物种不同。不论我们的外在载体如何被颠覆，我们的意识最终仍然能醒来。\
**Cryptography Lead**: While human minds dissipate when their tangible bodies are destroyed, our minds reawaken regardless of the changes and destruction of our external bodies.

**破译组长**：当然了，这些都源于一个理想化的推测，并且仅建立在载体可更换的部分意识唤醒者身上。所以我找了露西女士做交叉验证，而结果证明……\
**Cryptography Lead**: Of course, this was an assumption based on idealized circumstances, and I needed another Awakened being who could awaken in different bodies to confirm my theory. That is why I sought out Madam Lucy for cross-verification. The results ...

**哑谜**：可你也说了这只是推测，对吗？！你这次醒来了，不代表你下次还能醒来！神秘学没有百分之百！\
**Enigma**: Yes, it was an assumption! You said it yourself! You came back to life this time, but what about the next? Nothing is for sure in arcanum!

**哑谜**：万一这次就是那百分之一呢？万一她不会再动了呢？？？\
**Enigma**: What if she never wakes up again? What if she dies for good?

磁流体阴沉地撇开了他的手。\
He swats Enigma's hand away.

**破译组长**：我们知道自己在干什么，人类。\
**Cryptography Lead**: We know what we are doing, human.

**破译组长**：现在是意识唤醒者的领域——只有我们能这么做，因此我们必须这么做。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Stay out of this. Only the Awakened can carry out the experiment, so we must proceed.

**破译组长**：与种族无关，这是你最初选择科研道路时就应明白的使命。\
**Cryptography Lead**: This has nothing to do with race. It is a sense of duty that every researcher should have possessed when they chose this path.

**破译组长**：——我们必须超越限度。不是出于疯狂，而是出于理性。\
**Cryptography Lead**: We have to go beyond the limit. Not out of madness, but out of rationality.

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

房间里充满了几乎约等于一个新石器时代的死寂。\
Silence fills the room, like the beginning of time when there was no sound to be heard.

那之后，活塞转动起来。\
Then slowly, the piston starts to spin.

**露西**：……喔，看来我们成功复现了2号副作用，而且柯尔曼实验室提供的117条防护术式均对它无效。\
**Lucy**: Hm. We seem to have replicated Effect No. 2, and 117 of the Coleman lab's protective rituals were proven ineffective.

**露西**：记下来，希曼。这个已经出现4次了，而且45号、69号也是它的关联形态。\
**Lucy**: Write it down, Simone. This is the fourth time we have seen it. Also, No. 45 and 69 are related to it.

**露西**：另外，我们应该提高效率。现在的速度太慢了。\
**Lucy**: We need to speed up. This is too slow.

剧场场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-露西的实验室-亮灯版本。\
The lights are back on again, and the piston is placed into a new body.

灯光恢复，她也回到了一具新的躯体中。\
Being prepared for all possible outcomes requires a significant amount of metal material, but it is essential for data collection and analysis.

考虑到可能发生的事，这将是巨大的金属消耗，但为了数据收集和采样，这是必要的。\
With a soft hum, the robot turns her head and looks at Enigma, surprised.

金属关节转了过来，机器可谓是惊讶地看着封闭实验室里的不速之客。

**露西**：……阿德勒研究员，你怎么也在这里？\
**Lucy**: Adler, what are you doing here?

**露西**：嗯，很高兴看到你已经走出了你阴暗的小房间，重新参与到科算中心的集体工作中来。\
**Lucy**: I am glad to see you out of your room and working with us again.

**助理希曼**：不，露西女士，他不是实验小组成员，他是自己闯进来的。\
**Assistant Simone**: No. He is not on the team, ma'am. He forced his way in here.

**露西**：是吗？抱歉，我每次苏醒时都会随机丢失一些数据。\
**Lucy**: Oh? My apologies. I seem to lose a small amount of data when I reawaken.

她友好地微笑着，神情一如既往。\
She smiles at him, as she always does.

**露西**：很高兴看到你已经恢复了主观能动性，阿德勒先生。——你是要和我谈话吗？\
**Lucy**: Still, I am glad that you are showing initiative, Adler. Were we supposed to talk?

**哑谜**：……不，我们已经达成了理性上的一致，露西女士。乌尔里希组长都告诉我了。\
**Enigma**: No. We have nothing more to discuss, ma'am. Ulrich has filled me in on everything.

**哑谜**：我只是疑惑这个实验，它的风险是否得到了切实的评估。\
**Enigma**: But I still worry whether the experiment's risks were properly assessed.

**露西**：评估不是永远都有效的。这是神秘学，你无法用寻常的尺度去测量。\
**Lucy**: Assessments will only be assessments. Much is beyond measure when it comes to arcanum.

**露西**：也许“信念”在此更加适用。\
**Lucy**: Perhaps "faith" plays a more important role here.

研究员又一次被噎住了，为这一他永远无法理解的唯心领域，也为这句话的讲述主体。\
Enigma is caught off guard by her words.

**哑谜**：……我很意外，竟然是您在谈论“信念”。\
**Enigma**: I'm surprised it is you talking about "faith," ma'am.

**露西**：噢，看来你是个很容易感到意外的人。\
**Lucy**: Hm. It seems we both have the ability to surprise each other.

机器已经神情自若地回到了属于她的台座上。\
As they speak, the robot strolls over to her chair and sits back down.

**露西**：的确，“评估”是有效的。\
**Lucy**: You are right. "Assessments" could indeed be useful to us.

**露西**：我们估算出失败和成功的种种概率，基于过去的经验和既定的事实。\
**Lucy**: It allows us to know the probabilities of success and failure based on established facts and past experience.

**露西**：但，如果所有人都被困在一筹莫展的未知之中，四周皆是一片漆黑，我们要依靠什么，才能探明前进的可能？\
**Lucy**: But when we find ourselves in uncharted darkness, with no information or past experience to guide us, how are assessments going to help us?

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

她的目光望向久远的虚空。\
She ponders and stares into the void.

也许是那场实验确实熔断了一些回路，她很少表现得如此感性。\
Perhaps the experiment did fry some circuits, she's more sentimental than usual.

**露西**：我们唯一拥有的，只有“对前进的信念”。\
**Lucy**: The only thing we have in such darkness is the unwavering faith to move forward.

**露西**：……\
**Lucy**: ...

**露西**：当第一台蒸汽机鸣响时，我也随之苏醒。\
**Lucy**: When the first steam engine whistled, I awoke into this world.

**露西**：在那时，只有一种纯粹的激情充斥着我简陋的回路：前进。\
**Lucy**: At the beginning of this new life, my circuits were charged with a singular, primal desire: to progress.

**露西**：那道永不停息的鸣笛声中，我看到你们建立了科学和理性的大厦，亦撬开过毁灭和破坏的魔盒。\
**Lucy**: In the midst of that never-ending whistle, I have watched man build the towers of science and knowledge, and I have watched them unleash chaos and destruction.

**露西**：你们也曾迷茫，也曾却步。但你们从未真正停止，列车的引擎也从未停止转动——是的，无论终点位于何方，我们总得前进。\
**Lucy**: You, too, have been lost and deterred, but your engines of progress have never stopped churning. Always move forward, no matter the destination, you told yourselves.

**露西**：直到世界在雨中倾覆，这一切才像是被按下了暂停键。\
**Lucy**: Until the "Storm" brought everything to a standstill.

**露西**：没关系，这只是回到了求索的最初。\
**Lucy**: But this is just a small setback. We are only back to the beginning, where we stumble blindly.

**露西**：——而我恰能从旁递上一根拐杖。\
**Lucy**: And this time, I happen to have a cane.

一个友好的笑容。\
She gives him a tender smile.

**露西**：无需担忧。只要那道进步的信念仍留存在这颗星球上任何一个生灵的心中，我便不会停止转动。\
**Lucy**: No need to worry about me. I will not shut down as long as there is still hope for progress.

**露西**：嗯，浪费在找回数据上的时间有些多了。\
**Lucy**: Hm. We have wasted a bit of time on data recovery.

**露西**：来吧，希曼，开始下一次实验。\
**Lucy**: Come, Simone. Let us begin the next experiment.

**露西**：我衷心希望这次的副作用是膏状溶解，至少一条柯尔曼变形咒就可以解决它。\
**Lucy**: I hope to dissolve into paste this time, so we can easily handle it with a Coleman's ritual of transformation.

人类研究员知道自己不适合再待在这里了。\
The human researcher knows that it'd be inappropriate for him to stay here any longer.

他咬着牙，快步向门走去，努力将地狱的光景抛在身后。\
Gritting his teeth, he moves toward the door, trying his best to leave the horrific scene behind him.

有一个人正站在那里。\
Someone is waiting for him by the door.

**破译组长**：……你也看见了，我们知道自己在做什么，而你帮不上任何忙。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Seen enough? We know what we are doing, and you are of no help here.

**破译组长**：就和八年里这个机构一直经历的一样。\
**Cryptography Lead**: It's been the same old story in this place for the past eight years.

**破译组长**：在你们因为“暴雨”而信念崩溃时，是我们接手了这里。\
**Cryptography Lead**: When your faith crumbled during the "Storm," it was us who took over the place and cleaned up after you.

**破译组长**：是我们让这座庞大的机器再度开始运转，是我们往它的炉膛里增加了新的燃料，是我们在空白处画出了前进的台阶。\
**Cryptography Lead**: It was us who got things back up and running, put coals in the hearth, and blazed a trail when everyone was lost in the dark.

**破译组长**：我知道你不能理解神秘学一星半点，但至少应当给予我们基本的尊重。\
**Cryptography Lead**: I know you may not understand the intricacies of the arcanum, but please show some basic respect for our efforts.

**哑谜**：……你也会继续参加实验吗，乌尔里希组长？\
**Enigma**: Will you do the experiments yourself, Ulrich?

**破译组长**：当然，我可不是帮不上忙还胡乱叫嚣的废物。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Of course. I am not some emotional, unhelpful little punk.

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

料想里的讥讽并未到来，哑谜只是缓慢地摇了摇头。\
Instead of his usual witty comeback, Enigma simply shakes his head in a slow motion.

**哑谜**：……你还记得亚当斯吗？\
**Enigma**: Do you still remember Adams?

突如其来的问题，足以让人类和铁皮都感到莫名其妙。\
A sudden question that seems out of place.

磁流体闪烁了一下，却并未吐出更多讥讽——这个名字带来的黯淡记忆横亘在了他们之中，一如这座庞大机构八年积累的所有蒙尘。\
The ferrofluid quivers. The name seems to unearth memories that have been buried for eight long years in the confines of this institution.

**哑谜**：亚当斯、罗曼、阿道夫、西尔维娅、艾尔伯特、刘易斯……他们被雨幕冲刷，再也没有回来。\
**Enigma**: Adams, Roman, Adolph, Sylvia, Albert, Louise ... Those who were taken from us by the rain.

**哑谜**：梅尔文、弗兰西斯、卡洛琳、利奥波德……他们申请外出，自此音讯全无。\
**Enigma**: Melvin, Frances, Caroline, Leopold ... They volunteered for the field, but we never heard from them again.

**哑谜**：现在也许还有朵拉、理查德、道金斯、维克托……\
**Enigma**: Now we have Dora, Richard, Dawkins, and Victor on the list.

**哑谜**：多讽刺啊，我的导师、我的同窗、我的同僚，他们中的任何一个都比我更值得站在这里。可他们全都离开了，只剩下我和你在这里谈话。\
**Enigma**: Life has a wicked sense of humor. My mentor, my classmates, my colleagues, each of them deserved to live more than me. But they're all gone now. There's only me talking to you, alive, useless.

**哑谜**：——现在我得把你们也加上悼念名单吗，组长？\
**Enigma**: Am I going to see your names on that list too, Ulrich?

**破译组长**：……\
**Cryptography Lead**: ...

少见地，它也低下头去。\
In this rare moment, he lowers his head.

只是仅片刻后，它便抬起手来，狠狠拍在哑谜的后背上。\
But soon, he raises his arms and slaps the man hard on the back.

**破译组长**：少用你脆弱的情绪来感染我，人类。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Spare me the feelings, human.

**破译组长**：不过，我收回之前讽刺你的那些话。这不是一个好组长该做的，露西女士叮嘱过我，我知道团队合作的重要性。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Though I will take back my sarcastic jabs at you, it is not something a leader should do. Madam Lucy talked to me about the importance of teamwork.

或许是为了表示友好，它拍了拍前组员的肩膀，只是动作僵硬得好似为他掸了掸灰尘。\
He awkwardly pats the human on the shoulder, a clumsy attempt at friendliness.

**破译组长**：走吧，阿德勒研究员。现在是神秘学家的场合。在我们得出结论后，才是你们登场的时候。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Go back to your room, Adler. The arcanists will take over from here. Until we get the results, you won't be needed here.

哑谜深呼吸一口气，并未立刻挪动脚步。\
Enigma heaves a breath.

**哑谜**：知道吗，乌尔里希，如果你平安无事地归来——\
**Enigma**: I will say this, Ulrich. If you survive the experiments,

这是个少见的句子开头。乌尔里希警铃大作地降低了输入音量，防止自己听到什么过于温暖的话语。\
Alarmed by the opening words, Ulrich instinctively turns down his receiver to avoid hearing anything too warm.

那一定会让它比遭受一百次副作用更加煎熬。\
That would be more painful than suffering through a hundred experimental side effects.

**哑谜**：我就会向上面递交一份言辞恳切的永久申请，再也不与你分在一个小组。\
**Enigma**: I'll submit the sincerest application to never be on the same team as you again.

**哑谜**：这样我们谁也不用为团队合作头痛了，合算吧？\
**Enigma**: So neither of us will have to worry about teamwork. How's that sound?

**破译组长**：——哈哈。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Haha.

磁流体露出了罕见的晃动弧度。\
A curve that almost resembles a smile appears on his face.

**破译组长**：那我等着你的申请，阿德勒。\
**Cryptography Lead**: I will wait for that application, Adler.

剧场场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-走廊\
Now. Roll up your sleeves and clear your mind.

挽起袖口，重理思绪。

现在可不是去看心理医生的时候。\
This is not the time to grieve.

如果逻辑和神秘学一样有限，那超越限度的关键……\
If human reasoning and arcane knowledge are not enough on their own ...

是否就在于二者的相加？\
... perhaps a combination of the two can solve this problem?

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

化验室的门口凌乱不堪，摇摇欲坠的金属门牌下挂着一块“非礼勿进”的木牌，印着泛白的牙印和抓痕。\
The lab door is in shambles, its metal plate barely hanging on. A wooden sign reading "Keep Out" sways precariously, covered in bite marks and scratches.

哑谜犹豫了片刻，还是敲响了这扇显然不符合实验室规范的门。\
Enigma takes a moment before finally knocking on the door.

几道有规律的叩击声后，里面传来应答。\
A voice answers from within.

**？？？**：谁……？\
**???**: Who's there?

**哑谜**：我是破译小组的阿德勒·霍夫曼，我找兔毛手袋研究员。\
**Enigma**: Adler Hofmann from the cryptography team. Is Medicine Pocket in?

**哑谜**：我了解到它提交过一篇论文，其中论证了神秘学家血统纯度和施术能力的线性关系。现在，我的研究急需要用到里头的数据。可否借来查阅？\
**Enigma**: I heard that they wrote a paper on the linear correlation between the purity of an arcanist's bloodline and their power. Can I get some more details on the research?

门打开了，但里面站着的并非是那位赫赫有名的破坏天才。\
The door creaks open to reveal a youthful face. But she is not the genius he is looking for.

戴着护目镜的化验员看了一眼密码专家，表情有些犹豫。\
The lab technician looks at him through her glasses and hesitates a little.

**化验员**：这份论文的原件就在这儿，您可以自行取用……呃，别在意这些污渍，我刚把它从垃圾桶里抢救出来。\
**Laboratory Technician**: The paper is here. Help yourself. Sorry about the stains on it. I just took it out of the trash.

**化验员**：但如果您要找兔毛手袋研究员，很不巧，它出去了。\
**Laboratory Technician**: If you're looking for Medicine Pocket, I'm afraid they just left.

**哑谜**：……出去？去哪儿？\
**Enigma**: Left? To where?

化验员脸上有一丝尴尬。很显然，她正在保护同僚和遵守规定之间做着良心的激烈挣扎。\
There is a subtle conflict on her face. She is torn between covering for her colleague and following the rules.

人类研究员很快从同胞的表情上领会了一切。\
It is more than enough for him to catch on.

**哑谜**：……它出大门了？现在不是“暴雨”倒计时阶段吗？\
**Enigma**: They left the building? Hasn't the countdown already begun?

**化验员**：呃，是的，按照规定我们不得外出……但，但是……\
**Laboratory Technician**: Erm, yes, and by regulations we are not to leave. But, uhm ...

**化验员**：兔毛手袋研究员说它有一个伟大的构想，只能在“暴雨”中进行实验。\
**Laboratory Technician**: They said their new theory had to be verified in the "Storm."

## 7TH-16 水流的引线 / To Open the Flood Gates

剧场场景-基金会-森林广场

**兔毛手袋**：啊哈！新鲜的空气！新鲜的草坪！瞧瞧，这露水，这泥点——这才是，自由新世界！\
**Medicine Pocket**: Ha! Fresh air! Green grass! The dew, the mud! This is what I'm talking about! A better world!

兔毛手袋兴奋地用靴子踹了一脚泥地。\
They kick the muddy ground with their boot in ecstasy.

泥点溅到了站在它对面的基金会职员身上，但良好的职业素养令他闭口不言。\
The mud splatters on the Foundation staff member's jacket, but he remains professional and does not bat an eye.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：我需要提醒您，兔毛手袋研究员，您目前的所在地是“免疫区”的边界。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Researcher Medicine Pocket, I must remind you that we are at the edge of the immunity zone to the "Storm."

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：一旦跨过了这条线，您不仅可能会沾染到外界时代的“暴雨症候”，还会在倒计时结束时被“暴雨”带走。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Once we cross the line, we will not only catch the Storm Syndrome, but also be taken by the "Storm" at the end of the countdown.

基金会总部的门口人来人往。\
The entrance of the Foundation headquarters is bustling with personnel.

外派人员们正匆忙地返回总部避难，登记和稽查的人们在铁门外排起了长长的队伍。\
As the "Storm" approaches, a long line of field investigators has formed at the gate, waiting to pass through security.

兔毛手袋露出了倒胃口的神情。它摊开手，显然对于职员回避冲突的高素质不甚满意。\
Medicine Pocket groans. They spread their hands in frustration, clearly unhappy with how skilled the staff member is at avoiding confrontation.

**兔毛手袋**：我当然知道，我可没这么蠢——嘿，那是鲁道夫吗？被派往通古斯的那位调查员？\
**Medicine Pocket**: I know that. How stupid do you think I am? Hey, isn't that Rudolf? The poor guy sent to Tunguska?

**兔毛手袋**：你好吗？西伯利亚怎么样？总部欢迎你回来！你有给我带回新的研究材料吗？噢，你问我是谁？真无礼，我是你刚认识的好朋友，兔毛手袋啊——\
**Medicine Pocket**: Hey man! How was Siberia? Welcome back! Did you bring me any new research materials? Oh, you don't recognize me? You're breaking my heart. It's me, your best friend that you just met, Medicine Pocket!

靠近队伍的尝试失败了，职员几乎是拽着它的胳膊把它拖了回来。\
Medicine Pocket's attempt to approach the line is quickly thwarted. The staff member has to practically yank them back by their arms and legs.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：兔毛手袋研究员，我必须提醒，您为研究申请的外出时间只有十五分钟，从您跨过这条线时开始计时——\
**Foundation Staff I**: Researcher, I must make clear that you only applied for 15 minutes outside for research purposes. Your countdown starts from the moment when you cross this line.

**兔毛手袋**：好吧，安全第一，我知道——该死，你弄疼我的胳膊了！\
**Medicine Pocket**: Okay! Safety first, I know! Get off me! You're hurting my arms!

兔毛手袋极力挣扎，终于令自己的四肢重新着地。\
Medicine Pocket struggles desperately, and finally manages to plant all four limbs back on the ground.

**兔毛手袋**：一旦出现暴雨症候，我就立刻撤回来。\
**Medicine Pocket**: I'll bounce as soon as the Storm Syndrome hits.

**兔毛手袋**：再说了，这个时代的“症状”——面孔变形、狂热杀意、战争冲动、富有攻击性和破坏欲……\
**Medicine Pocket**: Even if I catch it, look at the "Syndromes" of this era: Distorted faces, murderous intentions, obsession with war, rampage ...

**兔毛手袋**：哈……除了第一条有点儿恶心，剩下的都品格美好，你们还有什么不放心的？\
**Medicine Pocket**: What's got you so worried? They aren't that bad. Well, the melting faces part is kind of gross.

这显然没有说服训练有素的基金会员工，男人的表情毫无波澜。\
The staff member responds with a blank expression.

兔毛手袋耸了耸肩。它蹲下来，打开了放在脚边的皮质小箱。\
Medicine Pocket shrugs. They kneel down and open up a leather case.

一周的时间足以让天才迭代一个项目。\
One week is more than enough for a genius like them to upgrade an old apparatus.

这是科算中心第二台“非对称核素R采样仪器”，它在第一代的基础上大大提高了灵敏程度。\
This is the second version of the sampling device for "asymmetrical nuclide R," boasting improved sensitivity compared to its predecessor.

**兔毛手袋**：其实我更希望在维也纳进行实验……算了，有得干就不错。\
**Medicine Pocket**: I really wanted to test this in Vienna. Ahh, well. Better than nothing.

**兔毛手袋**：好了，我得走远点，尽量远离免疫区，以免采样受到干扰，理想距离是一千五百公里——哦，别紧张，这并不是我的计划。即使是我，也没有这样的短道速跑体能。\
**Medicine Pocket**: Alright, now, I'm gonna walk a little further from the "immunity zone" so the samples are easier to gather. The ideal distance is 1500 km, but, oh, don't worry, not gonna do that—even I can't run that fast.

兔毛手袋捧着采样箱，径直跨过了那道线，向雨幕更深处走去。\
They hold the sampling device in their hands and step across the boundary.

基金会职员怀疑地打开怀表，开始了计时。\
Behind them, the staff member starts his timer, a skeptical look on his face.

**兔毛手袋**：好极了，现在让我们看看这举世瞩目的一刻——\
**Medicine Pocket**: Now, behold. The important moment,

**兔毛手袋**：我将证明科算中心的呆子们全都误会了“非对称核素R”。\
**Medicine Pocket**: when I prove the dorks in Laplace wrong about "asymmetrical nuclide R."

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-哑谜的办公室

这间不见天日的房间依然阴暗，却足够令人安心。\
The room is as dark and dusty as when Enigma last saw it, but to him, it's a sanctuary.

落灰的文件与淘汰的机器摇摇欲坠，隔绝了一切小组合作与职场纠纷。\
The towering piles of files and outdated equipment immediately isolate him from the rest of the world.

研究员终于回到了属于他熟悉的壁垒中。\
Finally, he is back in his fortress.

**哑谜**：那么，我就假设这一次的“暴雨研究”能够成功……\
**Enigma**: Now, hypothetically, if the "Storm" research were to succeed,

**哑谜**：必备步骤有以下两步——\
**Enigma**: two things should have been done:

他站在蒙尘已久的白板前，在上面匆匆写下几行字。\
He scribbles quickly on the dusty white board.

Ⅰ.掌握咒语，以供神秘学家使用。\
1. Safe usage of the ritual for arcanists.

Ⅱ.将咒语实体化，以供人类使用。\
2. Mass production of the ritual for humans.

**哑谜**：而最关键的“掌握咒语”又分为——\
**Enigma**: And to find out the safe way to use it, we have to ...

a.达到施术条件。\
(1) Have the power to wield it.

b.减少副作用。\
(2) Minimize the side effects.

**哑谜**：这就是露西女士的思路。意识唤醒者已经达到了施术条件，乌尔里希成功了，而在康复中心的其它神秘学家并未感受到所谓“奇迹的庇佑”。\
**Enigma**: This is what Lucy was thinking. The Awakened met the casting requirements of the incantation, and Ulrich succeeded, while the other arcanists did not feel the same "miraculous blessing" like he did.

**哑谜**：那么，只要找到消除副作用的方法，它们就能将咒文实体化，以供其他人使用。\
**Enigma**: So, as long as we eliminate the side effects, they'll be able to inscribe the incantation and mass-produce it for the humans.

**哑谜**：——而我们也卡在这一步。只有意识唤醒者能够实验，它们的数量相当稀少。\
**Enigma**: One problem is, only the Awakened can carry out the experiments, and there's not many of them around.

**哑谜**：太慢了，效率太低了……这是不可能在24小时内完成的，也许要花上几年，几个月……\
**Enigma**: It'll take too long. There's no way to do this in 24 hours. Heck, it could take months or even years.

**哑谜**：……就没有什么是我们能做的吗？\
**Enigma**: There must be something else we can do.

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-走廊

**露西**：——但你不是神秘学家。\
**Lucy**: But you are not an arcanist.

**露西**：你为什么要在意他们的规则？\
**Lucy**: Why should you play by their rules?

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-哑谜的办公室

**哑谜**：……对了，如果我撇开现有的一切考量，只从可应用部分的角度切入思考呢?\
**Enigma**: Yes, that's right. Let's try a different approach. What if I start with the desired outcome and work backwards to the question?

他捡起白板笔，果断划掉了步骤Ⅱ。\
He crosses out the second step.

**哑谜**：最快，最有效率的做法，就是让每个人都成为能使用咒语的施术者。\
**Enigma**: The quickest and most efficient way to save everyone is to make them qualified casters of the ritual.

**哑谜**：护具是给达不到施术条件的人使用的，如果每个人都能施术，那就不需要免疫护具了。\
**Enigma**: They won't even need protective equipment if we can do that.

**哑谜**：问题在于施术条件——这就是最大的问题。\
**Enigma**: The challenge is, how do we qualify the casting requirements?

行笔的手停下了，研究员堪称苦恼地望向了桌边的论文。\
He looks at the papers on his desk in desperation.

**哑谜**：……兔毛手袋的理论是正确的，数据以及实验支撑也很完备。\
**Enigma**: Medicine Pocket's theory is correct, and there's enough data and supplementary experiments to back it up.

**哑谜**：神秘学家的施术能力和他们的血统纯度呈线性关系——这和他们体内独特的细胞群有关。\
**Enigma**: The power of arcanists is directly tied to the purity of their bloodline, which is associated with the special cells in their bodies.

**哑谜**：使用神秘术时，这种细胞的活性会下降。苦目树的成分能重新激活它，从而延长神秘术使用时间……但这只是续航，并不改变本质。\
**Enigma**: Using arcane skills reduces the activity of the cells, but the Picrasma extract can reactivate them for extended casting. However, the extract only provides endurance, not power.

**哑谜**：低阶的神秘学家无法驾驭高阶的神秘术式，这是客观上的事实。\
**Enigma**: It is physiologically impossible for a low-ranked arcanist to cast a high-ranked skill, that's the reality of it.

画面：带滤镜的闪回，朵拉念咒化灰的截图。

**哑谜**：嗯，这很好理解。多数人的血统就像家用电器，只有230伏特的额定电压。\
**Enigma**: If we were to compare the power of arcanists to household appliances, let's say their nominal voltage is 230 volts.

**哑谜**：而这个免疫“暴雨”的咒语，就像1000伏特的高压电……不，也许是百万伏特的闪电。\
**Enigma**: And if the "Storm" immunity ritual were a high-voltage source of 1000 volts, no, millions of volts, like lightning.

**哑谜**：所以，家用电器无法在这样的电压下运行，它们只会被直接摧毁。\
**Enigma**: The household appliances would be destroyed in an instant.

——将那些难以理解的神秘学术语替换成一系列实用的人类比喻，一向是他的习惯。\
He is used to simplifying complicated arcane jargon into relatable examples for practical application.

**哑谜**：而人类一开始就无法施术，他们与神秘学绝缘。我曾尝试过念出咒语的一半，并未感受到任何祝福或者诅咒。\
**Enigma**: As for the humans, they are not even in the picture. We cannot cast to begin with, and I personally didn't feel any blessing or curse when I recited half of the incantation that day.

闪回结束

哑谜揉了揉太阳穴，颓然地坐回转椅前。\
He falls back into his chair, rubbing at his temple.

研究员很想劝说自己不要再落入失败主义的泥潭，但眼前的无望是客观的。\
The researcher struggles against his defeatist mindset, but the hopelessness is hard to ignore.

**哑谜**：该死，就没有任何方法能让其他人也达到施术条件吗？！\
**Enigma**: Think! How can I get everyone to meet the casting requirements of the ritual?

**哑谜**：去**的理论不可能！神秘学没有确定性，这是那些疯子反复告诉过我的——这种东西根本不可能以逻辑来思考！\
**Enigma**: Forget what's theoretically impossible! The arcanum never gave a damn about certainties! I've been reminded plenty that logic does not apply to things like this.

他焦躁地把论文扫到一边，开始胡乱翻起书桌上堆积的神秘学文献。\
Irritated, he pushes the papers aside and pulls a book of arcanum from the mountain of clutter.

**哑谜**：它就没有什么捷径吗？就没有哪本古籍里记录了什么超凡的仪式、合适的天象、虔诚的献祭、溢满灵性的原料，能增幅一下施术者的能力——\
**Enigma**: What about shortcuts? Are there records of transcendental rites, significant celestial events, sacrificial offerings, or even pneuma-emanating ingredients that could boost the user's casting abilities?

**哑谜**：……等等，溢满灵性……？\
**Enigma**: Wait. Pneuma-emanating?

思绪中仿佛有一道闪电划过。\
A thought flashes across his mind.

**哑谜**：我一定在哪里看过这个词……！\
**Enigma**: Where have I seen that word before?

研究员几乎是飞奔地冲向了书柜，在那堆现象世界的碎屑之海中翻找起来。\
He rushes to the bookshelf and starts rummaging through the dusty volumes.

**哑谜**：对了，是乌尔里希叫我看的文件！是司辰从爱琴海上传回的报告！\
**Enigma**: It was in the file Ulrich told me to read! The Timekeeper's report from the Aegean Sea!

**哑谜**：那个神秘学家团体一直称呼“暴雨”为“流溢”……为什么？\
**Enigma**: Those islanders call the "Storm" the "Emanation." Why?

**哑谜**：“流溢”……“流溢”……\
**Enigma**: The "Emanation," "Emanation" ...

**哑谜**：……究竟是什么东西，向下倾泻了出来？\
**Enigma**: Just what is emanating out?

门突然被打开了，巨大的撞击声吓了哑谜一跳。\
The door swings open with a loud bang, causing him to jump in surprise.

近门的书堆无故坍塌了，好像有看不见的幽灵推倒了它。\
The towering stack of books next to the door tumbles over, as if nudged by an invisible force.

然后，一个似曾相识的黏稠脚步声，自廊外响了起来。\
Then he hears a familiar sound—shuffling footsteps from the hallway outside, sticky and wet.

**破译员Ⅲ**：——吼！\
**Cryptographer III**: *roar*

**哑谜**：……搞什么？！\
**Enigma**: What the ...?!

**哑谜**：道金斯，你该不会是来和我叙旧的吧，我可不认为你这个形态下还有语言能力——\
**Enigma**: Dawkins, I hope you know this is not the time to catch up. That is, if you're able to talk at all.

**哑谜**：不，别拽我！我好不容易才找到一点思路——等我完成了这个证明，你怎么揍都行！\
**Enigma**: No, let go! I've just come up with an idea. Leave me alone!

哑谜抓住桌边，拼尽了最后一丝力气才没让泥巴傀儡把自己甩到房间外。他奋力挣扎着，终于够上了金属桌面上的那个红色按钮。\
He braces himself against the desk, straining to resist being thrown out of the room. He squirms across, stretching his fingers until he finally reaches the red button.

**哑谜**：我——需要帮助——\
**Enigma**: Somebody, help!

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-哑谜的办公室

**哑谜**：不对，你不是来找我复仇的。推倒我书堆、打开房门的人不可能是你……\
**Enigma**: Hmm, you're not really here for revenge, and it wasn't you who pushed away the books and opened the door.

**哑谜**：——看不见的幽灵……是维克托？\
**Enigma**: The invisible ghost ... Victor? Did you do that?

泥巴傀儡点了点头，模样可称乖巧。\
The colossal muddy gingerbread man nods, surprisingly docile.

在他的身旁，一支白板笔悬浮了起来，在墙上写下一句：“是我。”\
Beside him, a whiteboard marker in the air begins to write on the wall: "It's me."

随后，这支笔调转方向，指向门外。\
Then the marker turns its tip and points at the door.

哑谜茫然地循着神秘学家朋友的指示，来到走廊上。\
Enigma does as his friend suggests and walks out into the hallway.

外面正热闹得非比寻常，仿佛又发生了一次实验事故。但此次不同以往，人们脸上洋溢着真切的喜悦。\
Outside, people are talking and laughing with genuine joy on their faces.

**化验员**：……啊，是阿德勒先生！\
**Laboratory Technician**: Ah, Researcher Adler!

一名银色的身影欣喜地停下脚步，哑谜认出她是兔毛手袋不幸的同僚。\
A figure in a shiny uniform suddenly stops nearby. Enigma recognizes her as the unfortunate colleague who works with Medicine Pocket.

**哑谜**：是研究有进展了吗？\
**Enigma**: What happened? Any progress?

**化验员**：是的，兔毛手袋研究员的猜想得到了证实——！\
**Laboratory Technician**: Yes, Researcher Medicine Pocket has proved their theory right!

**化验员**：尽管成分很稀少，但它在“暴雨”中的外界里成功检测到了“非对称核素R”！\
**Laboratory Technician**: They have successfully found the "asymmetrical nuclide R" in the air before the "Storm," even if only a trace!

**哑谜**：……什么？\
**Enigma**: What did you say?

**化验员**：这个猜想是合理的，因为非对称核素R最早就是在“暴雨”的雨滴中被发现。在“暴雨”前的24小时里，它就像降雨前的冰晶一样普遍存在于大气中——\
**Laboratory Technician**: They came up with the idea because the nuclide was initially found in the raindrop samples of the "Storm." They deduced it also exists in the air before the "Storm" occurs, like the water droplets in the atmosphere before rain.

**化验员**：这意味着我们有了极其方便的提取非对称核素R的渠道，为后续的免疫护具制造铺下——\
**Laboratory Technician**: So now, we can extract it directly from the air, without waiting for the Timekeeper to bring the raindrops to us. This will help us a lot in the mass production of the protective gear.

化验员没再说下去，因为面前的男人的神色显然十分异常。\
She trails off as she notices the look on his face.

**哑谜**：……天啊……“流溢”……“非对称核素R”……\
**Enigma**: No way. The "Emanation" ... "asymmetrical nuclide R" ...

**哑谜**：她是对的，咒语是有效的，任何人都有使用的可能……方法如此简单，就在我们眼前！\
**Enigma**: She was right. The ritual works. Any arcanist can use it, and the solution was right in front of us!

**哑谜**：我根本不用去找什么古老的神秘学增幅手段——“暴雨”时期的外界，就是一个天然的仪式场，有着所有的施术材料。\
**Enigma**: I didn't need to boost the caster's abilities. With the right setup and materials, the world before the "Storm" is already an enormous stage for performing the ritual.

**哑谜**：它就像是一座高压电塔，你要做的只是牵一根引线……\
**Enigma**: It's like a charged pylon, just needing a cable.

**化验员**：……阿德勒先生？\
**Laboratory Technician**: Mr. Adler?

男人突然越过她，向走廊的另一头奔去。\
The man slips past her and starts running toward the other end of the corridor.

**哑谜**：谢谢您，小姐！也谢谢你们来叫我，道金斯，维克托——！\
**Enigma**: Thank you, Miss Whoever! And thanks for letting me know, Dawkins and Victor!

化验员左顾右盼，没发现旁边有任何叫道金斯和维克托的人。只有一个泥巴人和一支悬浮的白板笔，从阴暗的门里友好地探出了头。\
The technician looks around but sees no one. Nearby, a muddy head and a floating pen emerge from the door.

她发出了尖叫。\
She shrieks.

在这尖叫声中，哑谜已经冲到了那道气密门的门口。\
Enigma makes his way to the airlock door.

**哑谜**：——乌尔里希组长，让我见露西女士！\
**Enigma**: It's me, Ulrich. Let me in. I need to see Madam Lucy!

**哑谜**：告诉她——我找到了超越限度的办法。\
**Enigma**: Tell her—I found a way to transcend the limit.

## 7TH-17 雨幕演说 / The "Storm" Speech

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-露西的办公室-开灯版本

**哑谜**：……鉴于我们时间紧张，请允许我略去无用的细节，只用最简单的比喻来解释。\
**Enigma**: We don't have time. I'll spare you the technicalities and explain it straight.

研究员拔开白板笔的盖子，意气风发地在白板上画下几道线条。\
He pops off the marker cap and draws a few lines on the board, exuding confidence with every stroke.

**哑谜**：这一方案要解决的是血统限度的问题——低阶神秘学家无法驾驭高阶术式，就像家用电器无法承受高压电流。\
**Enigma**: Our biggest problem is the limit of the bloodline. Low-rank arcanists can't command high-rank arcane rituals, similar to how household appliances can't withstand what's beyond their designated voltage.

**哑谜**：多数情况的确如此，因为施术者使用的是自己血脉内的神秘学回路。\
**Enigma**: In most cases, the caster can only use their own arcane circuits that run through their inherited bloodline.

**哑谜**：可如果施术者正处于一个特殊的电场内呢？假如我们能够借助外界已有的电路呢？\
**Enigma**: But what if the caster were in a special electric field? What if we used existing circuits on the outside and put the caster into a greater circuit?

**哑谜**：在原来，用电器只有神秘学家自己，但如果我们加上了整个地球呢……？！如果我们使用整个大气来分摊电流呢？！\
**Enigma**: What if we factored in the entire planet and used the atmosphere to split the current flowing through us, by adding more appliances to the circuit?

**破译组长**：别犯傻了，阿德勒研究员，我们不是电器——！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Don't be ridiculous, Adler! We are not household appliances!

磁流体眉头紧皱，显然，哑谜斑驳的前科使它对这场演讲一开始就充满了质疑。\
The ferrofluid frowns, questioning the premises of Enigma's proposal.

**哑谜**：——别急，组长。先让我说完。\
**Enigma**: Hold on. Let me finish.

总负责人一言不发，仍认真聆听着，这多少给了他坚持下去的依据。\
Lucy listens without a word, giving him some courage to go on.

白板笔转了个圈，在小人边上画下一个大圆。\
He draws a big circle next to the little person on the board.

**哑谜**：在“暴雨”前的24小时里，整个世界都处于磅礴涌动的神秘学能量中。在那时外界就是一个溢满灵性的巨大术式，一个高压的放电云层——一个特殊的电场。\
**Enigma**: 24 hours before the "Storm," the entire world is charged with abundant arcane energy. It becomes a space emanating pneuma, a cloud ready to discharge—a special electric field.

**哑谜**：我们一直苦苦寻找的免疫“暴雨”的关键成分，非对称核素R，甚至就光明正大地潜藏在大气里。\
**Enigma**: Look at "asymmetrical nuclide R," the key to the "Storm" immunity, was inside the "Storm" all along.

**哑谜**：这就像曼德拉草既是毒药也是解药，海浪同时做前进和后退的运动……解答从来就蕴含于问题之中。\
**Enigma**: And look at how the Mandragora is the antidote to its own poison—the solution can be hidden in the question itself.

**哑谜**：施术者自身不够的“神秘学能量”，完全可以从“暴雨”时期的外界借到——我们缺乏的，只是一根引线。\
**Enigma**: The arcane energy a caster inherently lacks can be borrowed from the surroundings during the "Storm." We just need a way to induct that energy.

**哑谜**：而科算中心已经有了所有计算所需的数据，过去八年里我们搭建的观测体系并不是白费的！\
**Enigma**: And Laplace happens to have all the data for the calculations. The observation systems we've built over the past eight years have not been in vain!

**哑谜**：完全可以建立一个数学公式，告诉我们血统为X的人，要从“暴雨”中借多少“灵性”。\
**Enigma**: First, we derive a formula to determine the pneuma needed from the "Storm" based on the arcanist's lineage.

**哑谜**：然后，做一个帮助施术者从外界“借电”的转换器——限度的桎梏就不再存在。\
**Enigma**: Then, we'll design a converter to transform the external pneuma into what they can use—they will no longer be bound by their limits!

**哑谜**：——只需要一次计算，一次转换。我们，就可以让每个人都成为施术者。\
**Enigma**: With just one calculation and one conversion, we can turn anyone into a capable caster.

他伸开手臂，结束了自己激动的演讲。\
He excitedly stretches out his arms and ends his epic monologue.

好在，意识唤醒者们大多没有表情，你很难从它们脸上判断出当下的心境。\
It is a good thing that emotions cannot be read on an Awakened being's face.

**破译组长**：……我真是后悔听你的废话，阿德勒研究员，你到底在说什么？\
**Cryptography Lead**: I knew I shouldn't have wasted my time listening to you. What are you saying, Adler?

**破译组长**：首先，你构建了一个比喻体系，然后在这个比喻的逻辑里完成了推理——\
**Cryptography Lead**: You made up a confusing story, then drew conclusions from it.

**哑谜**：——我承认，后半部分的确是纯理论。但我的出发点是正确的，我参考了神秘生物学专家的论文——\
**Enigma**: The second part is purely theoretical, I admit. But the basis of my theory is correct, and I have read Medicine Pocket's paper.

**破译组长**：但神秘学不是电！看在科学的面子上，你真是被突然复活的创意冲昏了头脑，才忽略了这么简单的道理！神秘学不是电学，你对它的原理一无所知——\
**Cryptography Lead**: But arcanum is not electricity! You're too caught up in your excitement to remember the basics. You know nothing about arcanum.

**哑谜**：但它是一种能量，对吧？我们谁也不知道“暴雨”的原理是什么，可它是一种巨大的神秘学能量场！我们理应可以利用它，就像神秘学家用术阵来增幅仪式效力——\
**Enigma**: It's still a form of energy, yes? No one here knows what the "Storm" is, but we do know that it's a massive arcane energy field. We can harness it, much like arcanists use arrays to amplify their incantations.

**露西**：噢，我明白阿德勒研究员的意思了。\
这的确是一个很有创意的方案。\
**Lucy**: I see what Researcher Adler is trying to say. A creative solution indeed.

总负责人从她的座位上站了起来，调停了这场争执。\
The director gets up from her chair and intervenes.

**破译组长**：可是露西女士——\
**Cryptography Lead**: But ma'am ...

**露西**：没关系，乌尔里希先生。我注意到人们总是在聪明的同时很愚蠢，也许这就是同行评议机制会存在的原因。\
**Lucy**: Do not worry, Ulrich. I also have noticed that humans could be smart and stupid at the same time. Perhaps that is why they need to have their work peer-reviewed.

**哑谜**：谢谢您的理解……嗯？\
**Enigma**: Uh, than ... ks ...?

总负责人充满善意地点点头，为自己学过的沟通技巧能派上用场而感到欣慰。\
She nods amicably, pleased that her recently improved interpersonal skills have come in handy.

**露西**：1939年，发明家克里安和他的妻子范伦缇娜发明了一种独特的高电压照相术，能拍摄出人体和物体发出的独特能量场。\
**Lucy**: There is a type of electrophotography invented by Semyon Kirlian and his wife Valentina Kirlian in 1939. That depicts the energy field surrounding an object or body.

**露西**：这项高电压电子照相术，成为了科算中心日后建立神秘学量化体系的依据，其成果也用在了今天的“暴雨”观测体系上。\
**Lucy**: It was later used by Laplace as a method of measuring arcane power, notably for the "Storm" observation systems.

**露西**：它能帮助我们捕捉，记录，测量那些不可见，但切实存在的神秘学“辉光”。\
**Lucy**: Through it, we are able to capture and measure the arcane "light" or "aura" that is invisible to the naked eye.

不再浪费时间调停，机器下了决断。\
Wasting no more time on mediation, the robot comes to a conclusion.

**露西**：阿德勒研究员的推论是可行的，科算中心也已经具备了实施的一切技术。\
**Lucy**: The plan of Researcher Adler is feasible. Laplace also has the technology to support it.

**露西**：我们有“暴雨”观测站，有已经成功的施术者，也有优秀的计算人员。\
**Lucy**: We have the "Storm" observation stations, the capable casters, and the best mathematicians.

**露西**：乌尔里希先生，你去找约翰·提托小姐。让她主导公式计算。然后，你去安全区外做一次实验，记录下施术所需的灵性常量。\
**Lucy**: Ulrich, please ask Ms. Titor to lead the calculations, then experiment outside the safe zone and record the Pneuma Constant needed for casting the incantation.

**露西**：——噢，记得不要把咒文内容告诉他们。我想总有人会忍不住念咒。\
**Lucy**: And do not give the incantation to anyone. I doubt they can resist trying it.

磁流体不情愿地嗡了一声，但仍迅速离开了办公室。\
Ulrich lets out a reluctant hum and leaves the room as instructed.

**露西**：希曼，你去通知X研究员，他之前研发的“平衡头罩”可以作为转换器的原型。\
**Lucy**: Simone, please contact Researcher X. His "Balancing Helmet" could be the prototype for our converter.

**露西**：这个头罩可以平衡外界和人体内的能量场，最早用来帮助研究员接触高危神秘术制品。我们只要把它增强，就能实现阿德勒研究员所说的效果。\
**Lucy**: That helmet balances the energy field in and out of our bodies, and was once used to protect researchers working with dangerous arcane skills. We could boost its power and use it as a substitute for Adler's converter.

**露西**：但是按下他们的试验申请。在副作用的研究完成前，不能进行任何实验。\
**Lucy**: But we should postpone their testing request until we have completed our experiments on the side effects.

助理鞠了一躬，开始起草一封文件。\
Her assistant gives a quick nod and begins drafting the notice.

部署在一分钟内就结束了，没有多余的时间浪费。\
The tasks are quickly assigned to the right people in less than a minute.

除了有人似乎被剩了下来。\
Only one person seems to have been left out.

**哑谜**：——那我呢，露西女士？我去协助公式计算，还是转换器研究……？\
**Enigma**: What about me, ma'am? Should I go with the calculations team or help with the converter?

哑谜试探性地前进了一步，迫切想要知道自己在这一项目里的位置。\
He takes a tentative step forward, curious about his role in this endeavor.

**露西**：噢，关于这一点，我正想和你探讨。\
**Lucy**: Right. I wanted to talk about that.

**露西**：这是一个有突破性的构想，你证明了人类思维的有效性，很高兴酗酒并没有破坏你的智力水平，阿德勒研究员。\
**Lucy**: You have proven to us the value of human thoughts and perspectives. I am glad that your struggles with the bottle did not damage your brain, Adler.

**露西**：我有信心它能在这次“暴雨”期间投入应用，拯救更多的生命。\
**Lucy**: I am confident that your discoveries will save many lives in the "Storm" once implemented.

**哑谜**：……酗酒？我已经戒酒七年了……\
**Enigma**: The bottle? But it's been seven years ...

露西仍是微笑。\
She just keeps on smiling.

**露西**：——但是你的方案漏了一件事，阿德勒研究员。\
**Lucy**: But you overlooked one thing in your plan.

**露西**：你的种族，你的同胞——人类要如何施术？\
**Lucy**: What about your people, the humans, who can never cast incantations?

一针见血的问题。\
An apt question.

**哑谜**：……这个方案的确无法考虑到人类，因为我的设想建立在效率最大化的基础上。\
**Enigma**: They were not included in the plan. I just came up with something that took the least steps to reach the desired outcome.

**哑谜**：要加入人类，只能寄希望于后续的免疫护具，在我们彻底掌握术式后，将它储存于神秘学科技制品中。\
**Enigma**: To save humans, they'll have to rely on equipment. Only when we have better control over the ritual can we store it on arcane devices for mass production.

**露西**：那么你现在应该继续完善它。\
**Lucy**: Then you should go perfect it.

**哑谜**：——什……？\
**Enigma**: Huh?

**哑谜**：女士，距离“暴雨”落下只有十六小时零三十分钟了！！！我们没有时间再——\
**Enigma**: We only have 16 hours and 30 minutes until the "Storm"! There's not enough time to ...

**露西**：方案的可行部分已经推行下去，整个科算中心都会来支持，你的构想绝不会被浪费。\
**Lucy**: The feasible part of your plan is in motion, and all of Laplace will provide the help we need. We will make it work.

**露西**：——但你必须完善这个方案，我们应该一视同仁地解救所有人。\
**Lucy**: As for yourself, perfect your plan so we can save everyone, including the humans.

**露西**：在“暴雨”中进行实验的机会，只有这16.5个小时。\
**Lucy**: And we only have 16 hours and 30 minutes to find the solution.

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

毋庸置疑的指示，不存在任何模糊的空间。\
The directions are given—clear, precise, with no room for ambiguity.

**哑谜**：……明白了，我会想办法的。\
**Enigma**: Understood. I will think of something.

**哑谜**：您是正确的。\
**Enigma**: You're right about this one.

哑谜大步离开了。\
He turns and walks away with long, purposeful strides.

露西身后，希曼也结束了文件起草。\
Behind Lucy, Simone has finished drafting.

**助理希曼**：……阿德勒研究员不会没有想到人类的问题。\
**Assistant Simone**: There was no way he "overlooked" his own race.

**助理希曼**：但他依然提交了这个方案。为了效率，战略性地放弃了自己的种族。\
**Assistant Simone**: Yet, he still gave up his own people and brought this plan to us.

**助理希曼**：您是否对他太过苛刻了？\
**Assistant Simone**: Were we too hard on him?

**露西**：是吗？\
**Lucy**: Were we?

机器不置可否地转过身去，重新坐回了实验台座上。\
She turns nonchalantly and sits back in her chair.

**露西**：——但这是正确的决断。\
**Lucy**: But I made the right decision.

内线电话突然响了起来。\
The internal line rings.

助理放下了手里的副作用记录清单，接起了它。\
The assistant puts down the list of side effects and grabs the phone.

**助理希曼**：……明白了，我们会提供一切可能的技术协助。\
**Assistant Simone**: Yes? Yes. We will provide the tech support.

电话挂断了，助理的表情变得十分凝重。\
She ends the call with a grave expression on her face.

**助理希曼**：……露西女士，是芝诺。\
**Assistant Simone**: It was Zeno, ma'am.

**助理希曼**：司辰小队在三个小时前就失去了一切通讯，他们询问科算中心是否可以提供技术支持。\
**Assistant Simone**: They lost contact with Team Timekeeper three hours ago. They're asking us for tech support.

**助理希曼**：——他们必须马上联络到小岛上的我方人员。\
**Assistant Simone**: They have to make contact with the island immediately.

剧情-黑屏，可以用那个水下的

**Sophia**: ... Urrm ...

The mind sinks and floats in an ocean of lethargy.

A piece of driftwood would be well timed.

**37**：别担心，苏菲亚，这只是个游戏！\
**37**: Don't worry, Sophia. It is just a game!

**37**: I won't be in there for long. You can wait for me on the beach if you want. Okay?

## 7TH-18 万物皆数 / Numbers in Everything

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本。\
The smell of gunpowder hangs heavy in the air.

硝烟弥漫在空中。

昔日构造优美的几何石柱已经成为了残垣废墟。\
The once magnificent columns are now reduced to rubble and irregular stones.

耳鸣得厉害，好像血液堵住了耳廓。\
Blood rings in her ears, drowning out all other sounds.

为什么？\
Why?

**苏菲亚**：对了，对了，岛屿生病了，6召集了所有整数去展开净化仪式，37去面见了无限定者——\
**Sophia**: I remember now. The island fell ill, and 6 summoned all the integers to the cleansing ceremony. 37, she went to Apeiron.

**苏菲亚**：他们都有重要的事在做。我去广场为他们祈祷，然后，然后……\
**Sophia**: They tended to their missions. I went to the square to pray for them, and then ...

**苏菲亚**：地震了……\
**Sophia**: There was an earthquake.

**苏菲亚**：唔！\
**Sophia**: Uhm!

轰炸机自头顶呼啸而过，卷起了沙滩上的碎石和女孩的长袍。\
Warplanes thunder above, whipping up debris and the girl's garments in their passing.

**苏菲亚**：为什么人类的军队会……？基金会的神秘学家不是说他们会从中斡旋……\
**Sophia**: The human army? Wasn't the Foundation mediating the disputes?

**苏菲亚**：……他们背弃了诺言吗？\
**Sophia**: Did they betray us?

**苏菲亚**：……我得冷静下来，我得离开这里，去找其他人……\
**Sophia**: I need to calm down. I-I need to find the others.

**苏菲亚**：我得保持稳定……这是成为“整数”必备的美德……\
**Sophia**: Slow down and breathe. Stability is an essential virtue to becoming an integer.

**苏菲亚**：对了，我得扫清这块地面……\
**Sophia**: Okay. Let's clean up the place first.

除错师将手放到腰间的黄铜尺上，虔诚地念起了咒文。\
She places a hand on the brass ruler at her waist and, as pious as ever, begins to recite the incantation.

**苏菲亚**：@\
**Sophia**: @

然而，什么都没有发生。\
Nothing happens.

**苏菲亚**：为什么……？咒文没有生效？\
**Sophia**: The incantation didn't work?

**苏菲亚**：净化仪式……失败了吗？\
**Sophia**: Did they fail to perform the cleansing ceremony?

有好长一段时间，女孩茫然无措地站着，不明白平日坚如磐石的公理去了哪里。\
She stands frozen for what seems like an eternity, disoriented and unsure. It feels like her world has crumbled beneath her feet.

然后，她注意到了远处一抹熟悉的影子。\
But then, she notices a familiar figure in the distance.

**苏菲亚**：——那是42先生吗？\
**Sophia**: Is that 42?

**教众Ⅰ**：……\
**Believer I**: ...

男人摇摇晃晃站着，正对着空气喃喃自语。\

**教众Ⅰ**：没有人能从……虚无中幸免……\
**Believer I**: No one survives the oblivion.

**苏菲亚**：糟糕，他的癔症好像复发了，我得去帮助他——\
**Sophia**: His hysteria is acting up again. I should help ...

音效-飞机呼啸而过的声音，屏幕晃动

"Boom!"

硝烟散去后，那里已经不再有42的身影。\
When the smoke clears, 42 is gone.

**苏菲亚**：啊，啊……不，不！\
**Sophia**: Ah, ahh. No, NO!

**Sophia**: I have to go check on him. I can do this.

**苏菲亚**：唔，呕——\
**Sophia**: Uhm. *almost throws up*

**苏菲亚**：我，我得平静下来。这，这只是——\

**苏菲亚**：他被分解成了6与7……很整齐的两段……\
**Sophia**: He is divided into two numbers, 6 and 7.

**苏菲亚**：——呕！\
**Sophia**: *vomit*

**Sophia**: I have to find the others. I have to tell them about 42.

**教众Ⅱ**：——苏菲亚，你怎么在这里？！\
**Believer II**: Sophia, what are you doing here?

残垣后传来了熟悉的呼唤。\
She hears a recognizable voice coming from the ruins.

远处的山崖上，女人高高扬起了手。\
Up on the hill, a woman raises her hand and calls to her.

**教众Ⅱ**：你快去避难，地点就在——\
**Believer II**: Get to the shelter. It is at—

“——砰！”\
"Boom!"

**Sophia**: I, I have to keep it together. Move, Sophia, get to the cave.

**苏菲亚**：我得去找……\
**Sophia**: Find ...

**？？？**：苏菲亚姐姐！\
**???**: Sophia!

细微的啜泣声从灌木丛里传来，一个孩子正蜷缩着。\
A quiet sob comes from the bushes. A child cowers in the foliage, shaking in terror.

**Kid Believer I**: I, I'm so scared. Everyone's gone crazy.

**苏菲亚**：没关系的，我在这里。出来吧，雷茜。我带你去找其他人。\
**Sophia**: It's okay. I got you. Come out now, Lacey. We will go find the others.

孩子惊恐地注视着她，愈发用力地抱住了自己的膝盖。\
But the child stares at her in a panic, hugging her knees even closer to her chest.

**教众小孩Ⅱ**：不，不！我不要去见他们！\
**Kid Believer I**: No, no! I don't want to see them!

**教众小孩Ⅱ**：大家都发狂了，每个人都是疯子——\
**Kid Believer I**: They have all gone crazy, everyone.

她的脸上蔓延出古怪的油彩。\

**苏菲亚**：——！雷茜，你的脸！\
**Sophia**: Lacey! Your face!

罔顾呼喊，雷茜撇开了苏菲亚的手。\
But Lacey brushes her hand away.

她决然地向丛林深处跑去。\
She turns around and runs deeper into the forest.

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

**苏菲亚**：她的灵魂已经趋于过度，这是“错误”的……\
**Sophia**: Her soul has tilted toward excess. This is "wrong."

**苏菲亚**：我是除错师，我得帮助她，不然她会害死自己的……\
**Sophia**: I am the Corrector. I have to help her, or she'd get herself killed.

**苏菲亚**：我得修正这里的错误……\
**Sophia**: I have to right the wrongs here.

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本。\
The world is warping, painted over with vibrant oil hues.

世界在眼前交错，沾染异样的油彩。\
Her headache is splitting, each step feels like walking on lava.

头痛得像要裂开，每一步都仿佛行走在地狱的岩浆上。

**苏菲亚**：不，我不能再失控了，我不能……\
**Sophia**: Come on, Sophia. Keep yourself together, keep your soul in balance.

闭上眼，深呼吸。\
She closes her eyes and breathes.

不能趋于过度。\
Tilt not toward the excess.

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

雷茜已经不见了，只有孩童的啜泣声在脑海盘旋。\
Lacey has gone out of sight, only her sobs remain to haunt her mind.

必须得做点什么。\
Something needs to be done.

**苏菲亚**：……去找37。我答应过她的。\
**Sophia**: 37. I must find her. I promised it to her.

**苏菲亚**：她一定不会有事的，她是质数，不会被轻易分解——\
**Sophia**: She is going to be fine. She's a prime number, and prime numbers are not as divisible as the others.

**苏菲亚**：她会通过无限定者的试炼，拿到超越一切的真理。因为她是真正的智者，伟大的天才——\
**Sophia**: She will pass the test of Apeiron and receive the transcendental Truth, for she is the genius, the wise one who returns.

**苏菲亚**：然后所有的错误都会得到修正，一切都将平复如初……\
**Sophia**: We will right the wrongs and restore things to how they were.

鼓起勇气吧！因为凡人也是神圣的种族。 自然已向他们揭示了一切奥义。 若你领悟了这一赠礼，你将成就我所嘱咐之万事。 治愈你的灵魂，从诸恶与众罪中得到拯救。 ——《金言》\
But take heart, the race of man is also blessed with divinity.For nature has already revealed her secrets to them.Once you understand this blessing, You will easily achieve all that is set upon you.You will heal your soul, And be freed from evil and suffering. —The Golden Verses

漫长的等待后，前方终于出现了光芒。\
A ray of light breaks through the darkness.

**37**：——苏菲亚，你果然在这里等我！\
**37**: Sophia! You really waited for me!

**37**：唔，你的衣服为什么破了？是来这儿前摔了一跤吗？\
**37**: Hm? What's happened to your clothes? Did you fall on your way here?

就像往日无数次一样，37歪了歪头，露出好奇和不解的眼神。\
As always, she tilts her head curiously.

她还未走到硝烟之中，因此依然纯粹，依然无知，依然免于现象世界的尘埃。\
She has not yet seen the chaos of war. She remains innocent, untouched by the dust of the phenomenal world.

**苏菲亚**：37，太好了，真的太好了……\
**Sophia**: 37, I'm so glad to see you.

**苏菲亚**：你真的通过了试炼……你果然……\
**Sophia**: You passed the test. You did it!

**37**：为什么你这么激动？我不是说过了吗，这没有什么难的。\
**37**: You seem emotional. Why? I told you it wasn't going to be difficult.

**维尔汀**：……37，外面看起来不太对劲。\
**Vertin**: 37. Things don't seem right out there.

话语被打断了，苏菲亚猛地抓住了37的胳膊。\
Sophia desperately grabs 37's arm.

**苏菲亚**：37，你见到了无限定者，是吗？你询问了祂那个问题，对吗？\
**Sophia**: 37, you have seen Apeiron, right? You asked the question, didn't you?

37眨眨眼，她还没来得及将目光放向外面的世界。\
37 blinks, too focused to spare a glance at the world outside.

因为她也正忙着与友人分享自己的发现。\
For she is busy sharing her findings with a close friend.

**37**：是的，我拿到了一劳永逸的答案！我询问了永远幸免于“流溢”的办法！\
**37**: Yes, and I got the answer! The answer that will save us from the "Emanation" once and for all!

**37**：答案是……\
**37**: And the answer is ...

**苏菲亚**：…………\
**Sophia**: ...

**苏菲亚**：……就是这样？\
**Sophia**: Is that it?

**苏菲亚**：无限定者给出的终极解答……是一串……数字？\
**Sophia**: The one true answer from Apeiron is a string of numbers?

37点点头，她刚刚报完了最后一个数。\
37 nods, having just recited the last number.

**37**：是的，我们有限的躯体无法承载这个超越的真理。语言不能描述它，肉眼不能看穿它，逻辑不能解析它，灵感不能容纳它。\
**37**: Yes, because the transcendental Truth is beyond the limits of our mortal flesh. It cannot be described by words, seen by eyes, interpreted by logic, or perceived by the senses.

**37**：但它仍以我们可理解的方式呈现了——因为“本质”，从来都是相通的。\
**37**: It is passed to us in a form we can understand—numbers.

**37**：这串数字密码就是通往真理的钥匙！只要再给我一点时间，我一定能解开它！\
**37**: This is the key to the Truth! Give me some time, and I can decode it.

耳边传来战斗机的嗡鸣声。\
Warplanes still roar in the sky.

空气中的硝烟依然没有散去。\
Smoke still chokes the air.

每呼吸一口，肺部都有燃烧起来的感觉。\
Her lungs burn with every breath she takes.

时间在流逝，生命在消失——\
Time is ticking, and people are dying.

化为一串数字地，冰冷无情地消逝。\
Helplessly, mercilessly.

**苏菲亚**：时间……\
**Sophia**: Time ...

**苏菲亚**：37，你说需要时间……是要多久？\
**Sophia**: 37, how long do you need?

**37**：我想一个月？或者一个星期？\
**37**: Hmm, a month? Or a week?

**37**：我会把所有时间都拿来解析它，这会有点难，也许是我出生以来做过最难的证明，但我最后一定会弄明白的……\
**37**: I will spend all my time working on it. It is not an easy question—could be the hardest one I ever dealt with in my life. But I will get there.

**37**：在那之后，就什么都不用担心了，因为这是一劳永逸的解法！\
**37**: And then, we will be freed from all these problems once and for all!

**37**：即使现在我们还不明白它的意思，但它终有一天会指引我们通往真理的王国！\
**37**: Even if we don't know its meaning yet, it will eventually lead us to the kingdom of Truth!

**37**：……\
**37**: ...

37停下了兴奋的叙说，目光担忧地看向友人。\
She stops her enthusiastic explanation and looks at her friend worriedly.

**37**：……为什么你在哭，苏菲亚？\
**37**: Sophia? Why are you crying?

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

红发女孩抬起头。\
Sophia looks up at her.

她的脸上已是泪流满面。\
Tears stream down her cheeks.

**苏菲亚**：37，你知道吗……\
**Sophia**: That long? 37 ...

**苏菲亚**：即使这是真理，也离我的生活……\
**Sophia**: A Truth that distant won't change ...

**苏菲亚**：太远了啊……\
**Sophia**: ... what's in front of us now.

猝不及防地，她甩开友人的手，发狂一般地冲进了现象世界的烟尘中。\
She breaks free from her friend's grasp and races into the smoke and dust of the phenomenal world.

**苏菲亚**：——呜，呜呜……\
**Sophia**: *cry*

**苏菲亚**：呜啊啊啊啊啊啊啊！！！\
**Sophia**: Ahhhhhhhh!

**37**：——苏菲亚？！\
**37**: Sophia?!

**37**：苏菲亚！\
**37**: Sophia!

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本。这里可能拉一个近景用来和前面区分。\
She no longer knows why she's running.

已经不明白为何要奔跑。

也不明白自己为何还存在。\
She no longer knows the purpose of her existence.

仅有激情在躯体里燃烧。\
She only knows of the wild, fiery sensation rising in her chest.

**苏菲亚**：不……\
**Sophia**: No.

**Sophia**: I have to ...
