**Arcana**: You seem astray, child.

**苏菲亚**：——！\
**Sophia**: ...!

于沙滩的疮痍之上，伫立着一抹置身事外的身影。\
A detached figure looks on from the ruins of the beach, unperturbed by the chaos.

**阿尔卡纳**：你为何如此悲伤？\
**Arcana**: And sad. What pains you so?

**阿尔卡纳**：你们的“真理”没有眷顾你吗？\
**Arcana**: Has the "Truth" not graced thee with its miracles?

**苏菲亚**：……！\
**Sophia**: ...!

## 7TH-19 双行道 / The Fork in the Road

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本。\
37 stands dazed on the beach.

沙滩上，一个女孩呆然地站着。\
She looks around at the familiar island.

她望着熟悉的岛屿。

往日洁净的沙滩上，已经布满了人类武器的残骸。\
The once pristine shores are now cluttered with the debris of human weapons.

**37**：……为什么会这样？\
**37**: How did this happen?

**37**：我通过了试炼，我拿到了真理，我找到了答案……\
**37**: I passed the test. I was granted the Truth. I have the answer with me.

**37**：——是我做错什么了吗？\
**37**: What did I do wrong?

**维尔汀**：……不，37，与你无关。只是外部世界的癔症蔓延到了这里。\
**Vertin**: No, 37. None of this was your fault. Hysteria has come to this island, and people are caught up in it.

**维尔汀**：——名为“战争”的暴雨症候。\
**Vertin**: It is the Storm Syndrome taking the form of "war."

脑海中的弦紧紧地绷着，直觉强烈地报着警，眼前的一切都超出了预期。\
The mind is growing increasingly tense, the situation has gone far beyond expectations.

**维尔汀**：——距离我们进入洞穴已经过去了六个小时？！\
**Vertin**: Has it been six hours since we entered the cave?

**维尔汀**：那个怪诞的梦境……竟然持续了这么长的时间吗？\
**Vertin**: That strange dream, it lasted longer than I thought.

6提出的撤离时间是两个小时，现在已经超过了整整两倍。\
6 gave two hours to leave, and now six hours have gone by.

不过，眼下无论是岛民还是外来者，都已无暇顾及这一约定了。\
But the islanders and the visitors are all too wrapped up in their own misery to notice.

**维尔汀**：糟了，和芝诺学院的计划——\
**Vertin**: This is bad. The plan we have with Zeno ...

这才是最紧急的事态。\
This objective is of the utmost importance.

——同伴们目前在哪里？\
But where is the team now?

**维尔汀**：37，我得去……\
**Vertin**: 37, I have to go.

**37**：我必须去找苏菲亚！\
**37**: I have to find Sophia!

她急切地冲进树林，试图找寻那名红发的除错师。\
She dashes into the forest, desperately searching for any sign of her redheaded friend.

又在听到微弱的呼喊声后止住脚步。\
Just as she goes further, a faint call stops her.

**6**：……37。\
**6**: 37.

**37**：——？！\
**37**: ...?!

**37**：6？！你的身上……\
**37**: 6?! You seem ...

**6**：……咳。\
**6**: *cough*

领袖的脸颊相较平时更无血色。\
The leader looks even paler than usual.

瓦砾划破了他的袍子，那顶金色的头冠也沾上了泥点。\
His robe is in tatters, and his crown is covered with dirt.

6勉力靠着身后的石柱，望向面前的少女。\
He rests his back against a broken pillar, gazing up at her.

**6**：——你通过了试炼吗？你询问了什么问题，又得到了什么答案？\
**6**: Have you passed the test? On what question did you seek Its knowledge, and what answer did It give you?

一连串的变故使37愕然。她第三次说出那串来之不易的数字。\
Stunned by everything she's just been through, 37 recites the numbers for the third time, still a little dazed.

领袖听完了那个答案，短暂陷入了沉默。\
He listens intently and falls into a silence.

**37**：6，你们不是去举办净化仪式了吗？还有苏菲亚，她——\
**37**: 6, weren't you going to perform the cleansing ceremony? And Sophia, she ...

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

6仍是沉默。37注意到了对方袍子一角渗出的深色液体，及时止住了话头。\
37 trails off as she notices the dark fluid seeping from his robe.

**6**：——维尔汀小姐，请到这来，我有话要对您说。\
**6**: Please come up to me, Ms. Vertin. I wish to have a word with you.

他的声音很轻，但语调空前严肃。\
His voice is gentle, but his expression is grave.

一道伤口横亘在他的腹部，那里已被鲜血晕染。\
A gash runs across his stomach, his robe is soaked in crimson.

**6**：从这里往上五十步，学派的半圆广场上，您的朋友与学派的其他成员都在那里。\
**6**: Fifty strides from here, on the semicircle square, you will find your friends and the rest of our people.

**6**：我已完成了力所能及的“净化”。如果情况理想，受到影响的人马上就会醒来。\
**6**: I have done as much cleansing as I could. If nothing goes wrong, they will regain consciousness soon.

**维尔汀**：……您能否告诉我，净化仪式上到底发生了什么？\
**Vertin**: May I know what happened during the cleansing ceremony?

**维尔汀**：在那场地震后，我和37都做了一个离奇的怪梦。在那时，小岛上的所有人都陷入沉睡了吗？\
**Vertin**: 37 and I each had a bizarre dream after the earthquake. Did everyone on the island fall asleep, too?

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

**6**：我们的信仰铸就了此地的秩序。\
**6**: The island's order is forged by our faith.

**6**：——现在，信仰破灭了，仅此而已。\
**6**: And now, that faith has been broken. That is all there is to it.

**37**：……什么？\
**37**: What did you say?

**维尔汀**：我曾在初登岛时做出推断，整座岛都萦绕在一个巨大的术式之中。\
**Vertin**: Upon our arrival, I sensed a large-scale ritual surrounding the island.

**维尔汀**：那就是你们提到的圆？是它……在仪式上被颠覆了吗？\
**Vertin**: Is that the circle you kept talking about? Was it broken during the ceremony?

**6**：不，仪式只是仪式，它并非信仰的来源。\
**6**: No. The ceremony was just a ceremony, was never the source of our faith.

**6**：毁灭我们的正是我们一直不倦追求的东西，维尔汀小姐。\
**6**: Our journey was ended by the same thing that began it, Ms. Vertin,

他并没有看向37，只是轻轻对着空气说出了答案。\
He whispers softly, without looking at 37.

**6**：——是真理。\
**6**: which is the Truth.

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本-可以是一个拉近用的版本，因为这里她所在位置和37在的不一样。

海浪冲刷着沙滩。\
The waves crash onto the shore,

还有正浸润其中的飞机残骸。\
bringing debris from the planes with them.

**阿尔卡纳**：我并不惊讶。\
**Arcana**: It doth not surprise me.

**阿尔卡纳**：耽于思辨而怠惰现实，从来是智者的特征。\
**Arcana**: The wise, so blinded by their pursuit of knowledge, they oft neglect the harshness of reality. A common downfall of the contemplative.

**阿尔卡纳**：只是，在眼前如此的苦难之下……他们高明的智慧又在何处呢？\
**Arcana**: Pray tell, in the midst of such overwhelming destruction, where has their vaunted wisdom gone, and what good does it bring in this final hour?

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

**阿尔卡纳**：我听得见你心中的悲鸣和绝望，苏菲亚小姐。\
**Arcana**: I can hear thy weeping and bellowing within, Ms. Sophia.

**阿尔卡纳**：你匍匐在真理的殿前，数年如一日。你奉献，祈祷，苦修，仅仅为了他人的利益，全然无我。无人能够质疑你高尚的忠诚。\
**Arcana**: Many a time you have knelt at the temple of Truth, devoted yourself, prayed for your people, and withstood the tribulations set upon you, all for the betterment of others. Thy character is without reproach.

她微笑着抬起手。空中，轰炸机的呼啸仍未停止。\
She lifts her hand, smiling. Above, the roar of warplanes persists.

**阿尔卡纳**：——但“真理”并没有选择你，不是吗？\
**Arcana**: Yet the Truth has never deemed you worthy, has It?

**苏菲亚**：不，这是——\
**Sophia**: No, that's not ...

想要离开，脚却仿佛被钉在了沙滩上。\
She wants to leave, but her feet are rooted in sand.

直觉不愿依从，但身体却迟迟没有行动。\
She wishes to defy, but her body refuses to budge.

……离开，又能去往何处？\
And where would she possibly go, after all this?

**阿尔卡纳**：我给你另一个选择。\
**Arcana**: You shall be granted a greater opportunity.

**阿尔卡纳**：一个致虔诚者的祝福。\
**Arcana**: A blessing that befits thy devotion.

女人嗓音暗哑地开口，语句中的内容令红发女孩立刻后退了半步。\
Her unsettling tone causes the girl to instinctively step back.

**苏菲亚**：不，不，这是违背教义的！\
**Sophia**: No. That's a violation of the Scripture!

**苏菲亚**：我们不应——\
**Sophia**: We shouldn't ...

**阿尔卡纳**：……教义？\
**Arcana**: The Scripture?

**阿尔卡纳**：可你从来都不是他们中的一员，不是吗？\
**Arcana**: Yet you were never truly counted as one of them, do you not agree?

**阿尔卡纳**：真理证明了这一点。\
**Arcana**: As evidenced by the decision that Truth hath made.

**苏菲亚**：……！\
**Sophia**: ...!

**阿尔卡纳**：呵呵……\
**Arcana**: Heh-heh.

**阿尔卡纳**：无人可以逃避命运，从来如此。\
**Arcana**: No one escapes their fate as ever.

剧场场景-黑屏

**37**：不，我不明白——\
**37**: I, I don't understand.

剧场场景-轰炸后的海滩-在原来的基础上做差分\
She looks at 6, eyes wide in disbelief.

她瞪大眼睛，不可思议地看向虚弱的领袖。\
He has just effectively declared that their faith is dead.

后者在刚刚下达了信仰已死的判决。

**37**：我知道妈妈得到的回答应当是正确的。超验的规律不存在了，至高存在发生了紊乱。所以我们的模型失效了，现象世界的纷扰也足以干扰“本质”……\
**37**: I know the answer given to Mama was right. The transcendental Law is gone, and the supreme existence is in chaos. This caused our model to fail and allowed the discord in the phenomenal world to affect the "essence" of things.

**37**：可紊乱也是一种真理，不是吗……？就像无理数也只是一类数字。即使你不喜欢，它也只是存在于那儿。\
**37**: But did the "Truth" really fall apart? Chaos is also a form of Truth, is it not? Just like how irrational numbers are numbers. Despite our dislike of them, they still exist and cannot be denied.

她喃喃地上前一步，试图从那尊沉默的礁岩里得到回答。\
She steps forward, hoping for an answer.

**37**：为什么……为什么大家的信仰会因此而覆灭？\
**37**: But how, how did this become the destruction of our people's faith?

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

6依然没有看向她。\
6 still does not look at her.

**6**：我不会回答你，37，因为这并不是你的问题，答案也对你全无帮助。\
**6**: You will hear no answer from me, 37, for that is not the question worthy of your attention.

**6**：——你还记得你在试炼地回答我的话吗？\
**6**: Do you still remember what you answered to me in the cave?

37点了点头，强行压下心中的疑惑。\
She nods, holding back the whirlwind of questions in her mind.

她半蹲着，握住领袖的手。目光真诚，神情专注——这从来是一双很难回避的眼睛。\
She kneels beside him and takes his hand in hers, gazing at him with intense focus.

在一切因海潮而颠覆时，仍有星星悬在夜空中。\
Her eyes are still glittering like the stars above, unaffected by the tumultuous waves below.

**6**：那么，这便够了。\
**6**: That would be enough then.

他的声音有一丝难以察觉的欣慰。\
There's a hint of relief in his tone.

**6**：你不需要理解这些，也不必要因为与他人不同而怀疑自己。你只需要沿着自己的道路前行。\
**6**: Don't waste your time on the collapse of the faith. Don't question yourself because others think differently. Walk on, onto the path you have chosen.

**6**：因为你并没有做错什么。\
**6**: You have done nothing wrong.

这是需要漫长证明的题目，而她没有在第一时间读懂。\
This is a lesson that takes time to understand, one that can't be grasped so quickly.

她只是茫然地眨了眨眼，把题目记了下来。\
She blinks softly, holding the lesson close to her heart.

**6**：——维尔汀小姐，我有一件事想请求您。\
**6**: Ms. Vertin, I'm afraid I must trouble you for a favor.

他虚弱地捂住了腹部的伤口，试图凝聚神秘术的辉光。\
He weakly places his hand over the wound, and a faint glow of his arcane power coalesces in his palm.

那光芒仅亮起了一瞬，便石沉大海，如消逝的生命烛火。\
But the glow lasts only a moment, like a shooting star disappearing into the night.

**6**：如您所见，此后的事，我很难再参与了。\
**6**: As you can see, I can hardly take part in this matter for any longer.

**6**：如果事态到了最坏的地步，请您带37离开，协助她解开那串数字密码。\
**6**: Should the situation turn for the worse, please take 37 to safety and assist her in decoding the numbers.

**37**：——？！\
**37**: ...?!

**维尔汀**：……我会的。\
**Vertin**: You have my word.

这是一个严肃的请求，它的潜台词也足够冷酷。\
It is a weighty request with unspoken implications.

领袖点了点头，望向远处布满瓦砾的残垣断壁。\
The leader nods, looking on to the distant ruins.

他无神的蓝色眼睛越发暗淡。\
His empty blue eyes are getting dimmer by the minute.

**6**：我们生而面临着两种抉择。\
**6**: We are born facing a choice.

**6**：要么在调和与节律中克制己身，要么在激情和癫狂中走向毁灭。前者是一条狭窄的林间小道，后者是无止境的茫茫黑暗。\
**6**: Either we restrain ourselves and strive for harmony and discipline, or succumb to destruction fueled by passion and madness. Though the former may be challenging, the latter will only plunge us into eternal darkness.

**6**：1—10的每个数字都有特殊的道德含义。然而，却是6担任了学派领袖的位置。\
**6**: From 1 to 10, each number has its moral purpose and mission. Among them, only 6 was chosen to be the leader.

**维尔汀**：……因为6代表着平衡。\
**Vertin**: Because 6 stands for balance.

**6**：是的，我们必须时刻注意激情和理智的调和，才能穿行于这片幽微的古老森林，摆脱来源于血脉深处的召唤。\
**6**: Yes. We must pay heed to the balance between passion and reason, so as to stay on the right path and not be led astray by the calling of our blood.

**6**：我们恪守戒律，谨守誓言，抛却现象世界的纷扰和纠纷，向至高的存在献出知识的崇奉。\
**6**: For generations, we committed ourselves to the Scripture and stayed true to what we pledged. We left the trivialities and troubles of the phenomenal world behind, and served the supreme existence with the fruits of our knowledge.

**6**：这种信仰造就了小岛的繁荣，也是我们得以救赎的来源。\
**6**: This kind of faith was how the island prospered, and it was the source of our salvation.

**6**：在求索和苦行的辉光下，我们得以保持自身，遗世独立。\
**6**: Through diligent practice and contemplation, we managed to remain secluded and independent from the rest of the world.

**维尔汀**：而你们所厌恶的“无理数”……对应的是另一条激情和疯狂的道路？\
**Vertin**: The "irrational numbers" that your people rarely appreciate—are they faced with a different path, a path of passion and madness?

领袖微微颔首，似乎默认了这种说法的合理性。\
The leader nods slightly, acknowledging her speculation.

**6**：接连不断的“流溢”，阻断了我们与外界的联通。\
**6**: We have been long isolated from the outside world by one "Emanation" after another.

**6**：四年前的求索，被证明为一次徒劳的尝试，亦让我们损失了一批最精锐的学者。\
**6**: Four years ago, we tried to seek proof in the outside world, but failed. We regrettably lost some of our best scholars and friends in the process.

**6**：但真正让我们失败的，是信仰内部的危机。\
**6**: However, it was not the failed attempt that led to this upsetting situation, but a crisis from within.

**6**：如今，船只已经倾覆，天平已被打翻。我亦无力再调和人心的倾斜。\
**6**: Now, with our ship capsized and our scale fallen, I am no longer able to reconcile the tilt of people's hearts and souls.

**6**：学派将分裂。那些来自异乡的狂热者，也终于能在虚无中传播他们最热衷的仇恨。\
**6**: We will be divided. The fanatics from the foreign lands can finally spread their hatred amongst the ruins of our shattered beliefs.

**维尔汀**：……我会阻止重塑之手的。\
**Vertin**: I will stop Manus Vindictae.

6闭上眼睛，他的脸色和石柱一样苍白了。\
6 closes his eyes. His face is now as pale as the pillar behind him.

**6**：请记住您此前的承诺，维尔汀小姐。\
**6**: Forget not your promise, Ms. Vertin.

不远处传来脚步声。\
Footsteps approach from the distance.

一些理应熟悉的身影走了过来。领袖认得他们，他们是未去参加净化仪式的分数和无数字的学徒。\
6 recognizes them—they are the fractions who weren't taken to the cleansing ceremony, and the apprentices still seeking their numbers.

但现在，他们的穿着已经和往日截然不同。\
But they're dressed completely different now.

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：6，我们是来向你告别的。\
**Manus Believer I**: 6. We came to bid you farewell.

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：这里发生的一切，已经证明了你并没有领导学派的能力。你坚守的调和与中立，只是懦夫和逃避的托词。\
**Manus Believer I**: Everything happened here proves you to be an incapable leader. Your preachings of moderation and reconciliation were nothing but excuses for cowardice.

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：人类用炮火轰炸我们时，你在哪里？！你提倡的净化，又帮助了我们什么？！如果这就是“整数”的美德，我宁可永远做一个分数。\
**Manus Believer I**: Where were you when the humans dropped bombs on us? What did your "cleansing" do to help us? If those virtues are meant to be the virtues of an integer, then I would prefer to be a fraction.

**37**：不是的，整数们只是没能及时醒来，因为净化仪式出现了变故——\
**37**: Please listen, the integers were unconscious during the attack, because the ceremony was ...

**重塑教众Ⅱ**：让开，37！你对发生的事一无所知，因为你当时也正忙着做美妙的数字游戏！\
**Manus Believer II**: Out of my way, 37! You knew nothing about what happened. You were in that cave having fun with your little games!

**重塑教众Ⅱ**：重塑之手的使者没有说错，我们已经在假想的安逸圈中龟缩了太久——我们遗忘了爪牙与利齿，误以为只要远离灾难的源头，就能迎来永恒的和平。\
**Manus Believer II**: The envoy from Manus Vindictae was right. We have grown too complacent on the island and have forgotten how to fight. We foolishly believed that staying out of conflicts would guarantee us everlasting peace.

**重塑教众Ⅱ**：睁开你的眼睛看看，人类在此地犯下了何等可怖的暴行！难道你要我们咽下这股仇恨？！\
**Manus Believer II**: Now, open your eyes to the humans' atrocities against us! How can we not seek revenge for our spilled blood?

**重塑教众Ⅱ**：——用行动夺回本该属于我们的一切，这才是真正的“拯救”。\
**Manus Believer II**: We must act and reclaim what was taken from ours. That is the true meaning of "salvation."

人群的怒火越发活跃。\
Their anger continues to escalate.

37固执地摇摇头，仍不肯移开半分脚步。\
37 shakes her head firmly, refusing to back down.

**37**：我的确错过了一些状况，但是请听我说，一切都会好起来的，因为我已经得到了“真理”！\
**37**: It is true that I was absent earlier, but please listen to me. Everything will get better, because I already have the "Truth" with me!

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：真理？事到如今，它有什么用？\
**Manus Believer I**: The "Truth"? What good will it do right now?

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：它能帮助我们对抗人类吗？它能帮助我们夺回家园吗？它能让我们被炸死的同伴复活吗？\
**Manus Believer I**: Will it drive out the humans? Will it reclaim our home? Will it bring back our deceased friends?

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：Πάσας τὰς ὀρθὰς γωνίας ἴσας ἀλλήλαις εἶναι!\
**Manus Believer I**: Πάσας τὰς ὀρθὰς γωνίας ἴσας ἀλλήλαις εἶναι!

男人念出了那属于真理的咒文，那是任何一个立下誓言的学派成员都能使用的基本术法。\
The man recites an incantation, a simple spell derived from the Truth that anyone in Apeiron could cast on their first day.

——而在信仰倾覆的如今，没有任何辉光亮起。\
But now that their faith has crumbled, the radiance is no longer there.

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：当仇人将尖刀穿过我们的身体时，你的真理又拯救了什么呢？\
**Manus Believer I**: What salvation did your "Truth" bring when steel pierced our chests?

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：重塑之手予以了我们反击的力量，而基金会的这些人，她们当时又在哪里呢？！\
**Manus Believer I**: Manus Vindictae granted us the power to fight back. What did the Foundation do?

愤怒的声浪一波接着一波，黏稠的液体自他们的面具下流出。\
One angry question after another. Sticky, slimy fluids seep through their masks.

**重塑教众Ⅱ**：不用再和整数争辩了！基金会的使者在这里，就说明了他们的选择——他们选择了人类！！！\
**Manus Believer II**: Don't waste your time with these integers! The Foundation's envoy is here. It is clear they have taken the side of the humans!

**重塑教众Ⅱ**：杀了基金会的使者，把她的头割下来，献给伟大的“母亲”！\
**Manus Believer II**: Kill the envoy, cut off her head, and bring it to our "Mother"!

**37**：什、什么？你们……\
**37**: What? Y-You ...

**维尔汀**：面具影响了他们的神智，对话已经不再有意义了。\
**Vertin**: The mask has robbed them of reason. There's no point in talking further.

**维尔汀**：37，你把6带去安全的地方。他们的目标是我。\
**Vertin**: Take 6 to safety, 37. I'm the one they are after.

**37**：那你……\
**37**: Then how are you going to ...

**维尔汀**：我会去广场找十四行诗他们，能够和外界通讯的无线电小姐在那里。\
**Vertin**: I will meet with Sonetto at the square. Ms. Radio is with them, and we will contact our people from there.

**维尔汀**：别担心，我们此前有一个针对重塑之手的计划，现在实施也不算太晚。\
**Vertin**: Don't worry. We had a plan against the Manus, and we can still carry it out.

**维尔汀**：现在，三、二、一——\
**Vertin**: Now, on my mark ...

**维尔汀**：跑。\
**Vertin**: Run.

## 7TH-20 古希腊悲剧 / A Greek Tragedy

这个世界是一扇门， 通往寂寥与苦寒的荒原。 迷失的人们啊， 你所迷失的已立于乌有之乡。 ——弗里德里希·威廉·尼采《孤独之歌》\
The world is a door,To a thousand ruins, desolate and cold.For those who have lost,What you have lost are long in the void. —Vereinsamt by Friedrich Nietzsche

剧场场景-轰炸后的海滩-在原来的基础上做差分\
The flames of war rage along the shore.

火焰在沙滩上蔓延。

人类、重塑之手、教众混作一团，暴雨症候的变异流彩将海洋染成了异色。\
Humans, Manus Vindictae, and Apeiron believers, all consumed by madness. The paints from their storm syndrome have bled into the sea, creating a disordered mixture of colors.

炮火的闪光和神秘术的辉光交相辉映，海洋生物的尸体平摊在沙滩之上，如同一幅抽象派画作。\
The flash of artillery and the glow of arcanum collide. Dead, infected sea creatures litter the shore, like a tableau of an abstract painting.

**玛尔塔**：37，你要出去……？\
**Marta**: Where are you going, 37?

盲眼的女人忧心地抬头，领袖已经在她的悉心照料下及时止住了血。\
The sightless woman inquires with concern. Under her care, the leader's bleeding has finally ceased.

**37**：6就拜托你了，玛尔塔女士——\
**37**: Please take care of 6 for me, Madam Marta.

**37**：我得去找苏菲亚！\
**37**: I have to go find Sophia!

她奋不顾身地冲进那抹烟尘中，如同一颗被掷出去探路的石子儿。\
Not caring about anything else, she runs into the smoke.

轰鸣声掠过头顶，炮火在身旁坠落，披上重塑之手衣装的教众正在怒吼，声音犹在耳畔。\
Gunfire and explosions fill the air. The angry battle cries of former Apeiron believers, now in Manus attire, echo in all directions.

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：去死吧，人类！！！\
**Manus Believer I**: Die, humans!!!

**37**：唔——！\
**37**: Uhm!

巨大的震动和气流让她跌了一跤，摔倒在满是碎石的泥地里。\
The explosion knocks her off balance. She stumbles onto the gravel.

**37**：好痛……\
**37**: *winces in pain*

一双手伸到了她的面前。\
A pair of hands reaches out to her.

**？？？**：没事吧，37？你能自己站起来吗？\
**???**: Are you alright, 37? Can you get on your feet?

**37**：苏菲亚……！\
**37**: Ah! Sophia!

终于找到的熟悉声音令她心安。\
Finally. The voice she's been searching for fills her with relief.

37高兴地伸出手去，又犹豫地止住了手。\
She happily reaches for her hands, but stops abruptly, uncertain.

**37**：你……也换了一身衣服吗？\
**37**: Did you change your clothes?

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

压抑下心中涌起的复杂情绪。\
She pushes down the cacophony of emotions swelling inside her.

该用什么作为开场白呢？\
Where to begin?

**苏菲亚**：37，我知道自己的灵魂数字了。\
**Sophia**: I have found my number, 37.

**苏菲亚**：果然，你的计算一直都是正确的，从来没有出错过。\
**Sophia**: Your calculation was correct. As always.

**37**：……真的吗？太好了！\
**37**: You found it? That's good!

她不假思索地接受了这个消息，衷心表达了自己的祝福。\
She accepts the news without hesitation, her face lighting up with a genuine smile.

**37**：我一直都想告诉你。这是一个很好的数字，一个属于伟大先知的数字。\
**37**: I always wanted to tell you. It is a great number, the number of a herald, prophet, and pioneer.

**37**：它的发现引发了第一次数学危机，但也造就了数学的进步。\
**37**: When it was first discovered, mathematics was nearly destroyed. But luckily, it also spurred advancements in the field.

她顿了顿，没有再抛出更多关于数字的话题，而是真诚地望向了友人的绿眼睛。\
She stops, no longer rambling on about numbers, and sincerely gazes into her friend's emerald eyes.

**37**：——我们还是朋友吗，苏菲亚？\
**37**: Are we still friends, Sophia?

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

她笑了，笑她依然如此。\
Sophia smiles. Smiling that she's still the same, even now.

懂得如此之多，却又什么都不懂。\
She knows so much, yet she knows so little.

**苏菲亚**：是的，37。我们还是朋友。\
**Sophia**: Yes, 37. We still are.

**苏菲亚**：但是，有比那更重要的事。\
**Sophia**: But there are more important matters I must tend to.

呼啸声从头顶传来，伴随着人类飞行员狂热的大笑。\
A bomber howls over their heads, the pilot laughing hysterically.

他的飞机已经沾满了时代的油彩，机翼在蜷缩中不断地抽搐，如同舞台布景上坏掉的装置。\
The plane is covered in thick layers of paint, its wings curled and twisted.

**军人Ⅰ**：这是我们——我们发现的土地——！\
**Soldier I**: Hahahahaha! This is ours! The land we discovered!

飞行员显然发现了伫立在礁石之上的两道人影——两枚炮弹于机体之下整装待发。\
The pilot has spotted the two targets on the barren rocks below, with two explosives prepared for release.

苏菲亚没有避让，只是握紧了手中的小小圣像。\
Sophia does not flinch or retreat, instead her fingers wrap gently around the tiny idol.

**苏菲亚**：Διορθωθεί το σφάλμα!\
**Sophia**: Διορθωθεί το σφάλμα!

爆炸声，震荡声。

那辆飞机在空中炸开了，干净利落，连同一个年轻人类的生命。\
The bomber detonates in the sky, taking the young pilot with it.

**37**：苏菲亚，你的神秘术，你的样子……\
**37**: Sophia, your power, and your look ...

**苏菲亚**：……我要走了，37。\
**Sophia**: I must leave now, 37.

**苏菲亚**：阿尔卡纳女士向我指明了另一条道路。\
**Sophia**: Lady Arcana has shown me another path.

**37**：不，不……！\
**37**: No. NO!

**37**：为什么你要离开……？是因为我们的圆消失了吗……？\
**37**: Why are you leaving, too? Is it because our circle has been broken?

**37**：可是，我已经找到了真理……！\
**37**: But I found the Truth!

**37**：我从无限定者那里获得了一劳永逸的解法！只要给我一点时间，一切都能好起来的，我保证……！\
**37**: I have the final solution! Just give me a little more time, and everything will be fine again, I promise!

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

闭上眼，箴言上的训导还历历在目。\
She closes her eyes, the scripture still lingers in her mind.

“来到奥林匹克竞技场的有三种人。” “最低等是那些到场行商者，其次是参赛者。” “而其中境界最高的，是那些置身事外的观察者。”\
"There are three kinds of people who come to the Olympic Games." "The lowest class is made up of those who come to buy and sell, and the next above them are those who come to compete." "But the most esteemed, however, are those who come to look on."

“唯有这些智者，真正的贤人——”\
"Only these wise pursuers of knowledge ..."

“能将自己从‘生之巨轮’中彻底解救出来。”\
"... may release themselves from the 'wheel of birth.'"

**苏菲亚**：……并不是每个人都像你一样的，37。\
**Sophia**: You and I are different, 37.

**苏菲亚**：并不是每个人都有置身事外的资格。\
**Sophia**: Not all of us have the privilege to look on from the sidelines.

重塑之手的追随者握紧了手中的圣像。\
She clenches the tiny idol.

漆黑的黏稠液体弥漫开来。几乎是瞬间，天空中的飞机被驱散了，露出了铬黄色的天空。\
A thick, tar-like substance seeps out from her body. In an instant, the bombers are wiped out completely.

**37**：……苏菲亚，你……\
**37**: Sophia, you ...

不能再拖延下去了，她知道。\
She can't prolong the inevitable any longer, she knows that.

这是最后的抉择。\
This is the last thing she wants.

**苏菲亚**：……我会加入重塑之手，我会带领其他人一起离开。\
**Sophia**: I will join Manus Vindictae, take others with me, and leave.

**苏菲亚**：我会抛却一切教义，前往现象世界，投身复仇的漩涡……\
**Sophia**: I will renounce the Scripture and seek vengeance in the phenomenal world.

**苏菲亚**：来吧，37。\
**Sophia**: Make your move, 37.

一滴泪水从她的眼角滴落。\
Tears roll down her eyes.

**苏菲亚**：如果你真的是能战胜一切，跨越一切的天才……\
**Sophia**: If you really are the genius who can overcome anything ...

**苏菲亚**：那就向我做出你的证明。\
**Sophia**: Prove it to me.

**苏菲亚**：阻止我，超越我，击败我——\
**Sophia**: Stop me, transcend me, defeat me …

**苏菲亚**：……碾碎我。\
**Sophia**: Crush me to dust.

剧场场景-轰炸后的海滩-在原来的基础上做差分\
The explosions have finally ceased.

轰炸声早已停息。\
The planes rest alongside the geometric bodies in the sea, sinking into an everlasting sleep.

飞机沉入了海湾，和那里的几何体一起步入了安宁的永眠。\
The roars of battle are no more.

一切狂热的怒吼都远去了。

只有海潮仍在孤独地拍打岸边。\
All that remains is the crashing of the waves against the shore.

**苏菲亚**：……为什么？\
**Sophia**: Why?

**苏菲亚**：为什么你要手下留情，37？你的神秘术并没有失效，你不应该——\
**Sophia**: Why did you spare me, 37? Why did you show mercy? You weren't supposed to—

争斗迅速地结束了，几何辉光仅仅是割破了友人的袍角。\
The battle ended quickly. 37's geometric brilliance has left only a tear on her friend's robe.

**37**：我不想和你战斗，苏菲亚！\
**37**: Because I don't want to fight you, Sophia!

**37**：为什么……为什么我们非得这样不可？！\
**37**: Why? Why do we have to do this?!

她的声音近乎崩溃。\
Her voice is filled with anguish.

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

苏菲亚低下头，良久未置一词。\
Sophia looks down in a long silence.

而后，她轻轻地摇了摇头。\
Then, she gently shakes her head.

**苏菲亚**：……对不起，37。我真是昏了头，或者无药可救到了一定程度。\
**Sophia**: I'm sorry, 37. I have gone beyond reason, beyond cure.

**苏菲亚**：我竟然让你和我战斗。你的双手……并不是为了争斗而诞生的，它只应为托举真理而存在。\
**Sophia**: I must've been out of my mind to make you fight me. Your hands were never meant for violence. They were meant for upholding the Truth.

**37**：……？\
**37**: ...?

**苏菲亚**：而我——扫清道前的尘埃，才是我的使命。\
**Sophia**: As for me—I'm the one who clears the dust off the path, as fate foretold.

**苏菲亚**：再见了，我的朋友。\
**Sophia**: Goodbye, my beloved friend.

她不再犹豫，也不再回头。\
She no longer wavers or looks back.

她的背影微微摇晃着，但依然迈着坚定的步子，向重塑之手的信徒们走去。\
Her shoulders tremble, but she strides toward the Manus with determination.

**苏菲亚**：……到时间了。\
**Sophia**: It is time.

**苏菲亚**：诸位，请尽快完成沙滩的“清洁”工作。我们需要遵循阿尔卡纳女士的引导，一同离开岛屿。\
**Sophia**: Please "clean up" the beach as quickly as possible. We will depart soon, as Lady Arcana has instructed.

**37**：——苏——\
**37**: Soph- ...

**十四行诗**：——苏菲亚小姐！\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Sophia!

同伴们终于完成了汇合。\
The team is finally reunited.

为和平而生的姑娘在最后一刻赶到战场，她的胸口因剧烈运动而微微起伏。\
Sonetto arrives last, heaving from trying to catch up to the scene.

那场狂乱的梦境消耗了她太多精神，在别处的战斗也并不比这里更加容易。\
She had her own battles elsewhere on the island. That strange dream has taken its toll on her.

现在，她握着玻璃笔，沉默，坚定，绝不退让地挡在了道前，用目光无声地传达出疑问。\
And now she is holding her pen, silently questioning Sophia with a piercing stare.

——为什么？\
Why?

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

**苏菲亚**：我们都有自己的使命，十四行诗小姐。\
**Sophia**: We all have our own purpose to fulfill, Ms. Sonetto.

她径直越过了她。\
She walks right past her.

**苏菲亚**：这次我不会和你战斗。但下次见面时，我们就是敌人了。\
**Sophia**: I will not fight you this time. But I will draw steel the next we meet.

重塑之手的新成员们离开了。\
The new members of the Manus Vindictae have left.

他们的确完成了沙滩的清洁工作——视野里已经再无人类的身影。\
They did clean up the beach—every trace of humanity has been wiped clean.

沙滩上只剩下了碎石和金属的残骸。\
Only rock and metal debris remain on the beach.

**37**：……我不明白……\
**37**: I don't understand any of this.

她颓然地跌坐在地，目光空洞地望向前方。\
She slumps to the ground and stares blankly into the distance.

**37**：真理……理应超越一切，凌驾于现象世界的一切尘埃……\
**37**: The Truth transcends all and is above all trivial matters of the phenomenal world.

**37**：它会指引我们走向光辉的殿堂，摆脱诸恶和不幸，给予每个人幸福……不是吗？\
**37**: It guides us to enlightenment and protects us from evil and misfortune, does it not?

**37**：我相信着，我也拿到了它，可是……可是……\
**37**: This is what I have always believed, so I went seeking for it. It is finally in my hands. But now, but now ...

37将头埋在膝盖里，声音近乎哽咽。\
37 buries her face between her knees, on the verge of sobbing.

**37**：是哪里出错了……？是我做错了吗？是因为我们没能正确地运用真理吗……？\
**37**: What went wrong? Was it my fault? Isn't this how the Truth is supposed to work?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

这是一个岛外来客很难回答的问题。\
It is not an easy question for an off-island visitor to answer.

但有一点是确定无疑的。\
However, one thing is for certain.

**维尔汀**：不，37。你的真理并没有背弃你。\
**Vertin**: The Truth has not abandoned you, 37.

**维尔汀**：——你甚至还没开始运用它，不是吗？我们还没有解开那串密码。\
**Vertin**: You haven't used the key yet, have you? It is still coded.

**37**：——！\
**37**: ...!

**37**：密码……\
**37**: The key ...

伸出手，将37从地上拉起来。\
37 is helped up from the ground.

**维尔汀**：红弩箭核实了阿尔卡纳的位置，她还没有离开岛屿。\
**Vertin**: Lilya has verified Arcana's location. She is still on this island.

**维尔汀**：也许我们还有机会阻止重塑之手，在一切真正结束前。\
**Vertin**: We still have a chance to stop her before it's truly too late.

**维尔汀**：走吧，十四行诗。\
**Vertin**: We should go now, Sonetto.

**维尔汀**：——在“暴雨”落下前，我们还有十五个小时。\
**Vertin**: We have 15 more hours until the "Storm."

## 7TH-21 手影戏 / A Homage Paid

剧情场景-暴雨眼观测室（1.7的那个场景）

**联络员Ⅱ**：……和小岛的通讯已经恢复，芝诺已和司辰小队取得联系。\
**Liaison Staff II**: We've got signal. Zeno has restored communications with Team Timekeeper.

**助理希曼**：很好，科算中心的援助到此为止。\
**Assistant Simone**: Very well. We will leave you to it.

一贯冷静的助理松了口气。\
She sighs with relief.

随后，她并未第一时间切断与对方的联络，而是反常地停顿了一下。\
But before she hangs up, she has one more question.

**助理希曼**：……再次确认，你们的行动取得了人类和平安全理事会的授意，是吗？\
**Assistant Simone**: Just to confirm before we go—the operation Zeno is currently undertaking has been approved by the Pax Security Council, right?

内线电话的那端沉默了片刻，似乎并不想回答这个荒谬的问题。\
The internal call falls silent, as if the question is too absurd to answer.

**？？？**：当然，小姐。\
**???**: Certainly, Miss.

**？？？**：我们是军人，我们执行命令。\
**???**: We are soldiers. Soldiers act on orders.

剧场场景-岛屿-高地-阿尔卡纳剧情战专属场景\
This is the only part of the island untouched by war.

这是唯一一处未受侵袭的海角。\
Where the foliage is thriving and the view is stunning.

草木繁盛，风景独好。

**阿尔卡纳**：很高兴见到你。\
**Arcana**: I am most pleased to see you.

**阿尔卡纳**：——你的观光之旅还顺利吗，维尔汀小姐？\
**Arcana**: Had you a pleasant stay on this island, Ms. Vertin?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

她转过身来，笑容称得上优雅。\
She turns around, a smile gracing her face.

**阿尔卡纳**：这是个很有趣的小岛，不是吗？\
**Arcana**: Are they not an intriguing flock of people?

**阿尔卡纳**：智者们在脚下画上一个圈，然后宣扬自己站在世界之外。\
**Arcana**: Their wise ones drew a circle at their feet and declared themselves apart from this realm.

**阿尔卡纳**：一代又一代，他们兢兢业业，像劳碌的工蚁一般维护它，敬畏它，崇奉它。使自己免于召唤，也免于疯狂。\
**Arcana**: For generations untold, they toiled as diligent ants in service of the circle, adoring and venerating it while shielding themselves from insanity's call.

**阿尔卡纳**：我很喜欢这个图形，这个静止、古典、完美的圆。\
**Arcana**: I take immense pleasure in admiring this wondrous figure—the primordial, eternal, immaculate circle.

**阿尔卡纳**：可惜，它终究是画在沙地上的。\
**Arcana**: The more pity that it was etched upon sand.

海角之下，那片被炮火轰炸的沙滩已是满目疮痍。\
Below, the bombed-out beach is in a state of disarray.

**维尔汀**：我不这么认为。\
**Vertin**: I disagree.

**维尔汀**：正因为沙地脆弱易朽，人们才追寻永恒。信仰完满，本身并无过错。\
**Vertin**: The fragility and impermanence of sand is precisely why people strive for something eternal. Believing in perfection is not a flaw.

**维尔汀**：……攻击这座岛的人类飞机上装载了绝不属于这个时代的武器。\
**Vertin**: I noticed the human aircraft were loaded with weapons not from this era.

**维尔汀**：是你们——重塑之手，提供了技术吗？\
**Vertin**: Did Manus Vindictae provide them with the technology?

女人微笑着。她的沉默更证实了猜想的可怕。\
Arcana smiles, the silence confirming the disturbing revelation.

**维尔汀**：……我不明白。\
**Vertin**: I can't fathom your motives.

**维尔汀**：如果重塑之手是想教唆仇恨，自岛上招募纯血神秘学家成员，那你的目的已经达成。\
**Vertin**: If you came here to incite hatred and recruit the pure-blood arcanists on this island, you may now walk away with satisfaction.

**维尔汀**：如果你们是要占领这里作为据点，那在净化仪式失败时，你也早就可以动手。\
**Vertin**: If you wanted to take the island as one of your bases, you could have done so after the cleansing ceremony failed.

**维尔汀**：可是你什么都没做，只是站在这里……为什么？\
**Vertin**: But you did nothing. You just stood there. Why?

**阿尔卡纳**：呵呵，呵呵呵呵……\
**Arcana**: *chuckle*

毫无缘由地，她笑了起来。\
Without rhyme or reason, she laughs.

**阿尔卡纳**：很难理解吗，维尔汀小姐？\
**Arcana**: Do you struggle to comprehend, sweet Vertin?

**阿尔卡纳**：——我在等你。\
**Arcana**: I was waiting for you.

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

十四行诗和红弩箭同时上前了一步。\
Sonetto and Lilya take a step forward.

**红弩箭**：不用和她废话了，维尔汀，动手吧。\
**Lilya**: Enough talk, Vertin. It's time for action.

**十四行诗**：请小心距离，阿尔卡纳的神秘术会在近距离下影响人的神智。\
**Sonetto**: Mind your distance. Arcana has power over people's minds at a close range.

**阿尔卡纳**：真是可惜。\
**Arcana**: A pity.

她抬起手臂，亮出了手上的石环。\
She raises her arm, the stone bangle still intact on her wrist.

它自手腕上滑落，迅速没入草地，化为了微不可寻的齑粉。\
The next moment, it slides off and falls to the grass, dissolving into thin air.

**阿尔卡纳**：这是对精巧的“戒指”……我本想留着它。\
**Arcana**: I didst wish to keep this bangle. Mine and yours, a pair in perfect match.

**阿尔卡纳**：只是——你能这么轻易地摘下它吗，维尔汀小姐？\
**Arcana**: How will you remove yours, Vertin?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

是的，正如仍有信徒在坚守信仰，仍有智者在维系学派，仍有整数走完了净化仪式的漫漫长路——\
The bangle burns, a reminder of those who still believe in the teachings of Truth and Apeiron, and those who remained until the end of the cleansing ceremony.

这枚石环也固守着自己的职责。\
The symbol of faith remains true to its purpose.

不可交战的协定依然有效。\
The peace agreement is still in effect.

**星锑**：——什么？这座岛都被炸成这样了，这玩意还没失效？\
**Regulus**: What? The island's been blasted to smithereens. How come the bangle still has its power?

**星锑**：这究竟是什么材质……\
**Regulus**: What is it made of?

**十四行诗**：别担心，星锑，这和最初计划的一样。\
**Sonetto**: Don't worry, Regulus. We have foreseen this.

第一助手并未因此却步。\
The chief assistant shows no signs of worry.

**十四行诗**：最初，我一直对岛上的规则感到疑惑。但在教典的学习中，我逐渐理解了。\
**Sonetto**: When we first arrived, I was bewildered by the rules on this island. But as I learned more about their Scriptures, things began to make sense.

**十四行诗**：基于自然语言传递的知识是脆弱的。它模糊、矛盾，永远会存在大量的漏洞。因此岛上的神秘学家们尊崇更加精确的数学，视它为真理的语言。\
**Sonetto**: Language is an unreliable means of communication. Information can become muddled, and vague wording can lead to mistakes and contradictions. That's why the island values math as a more precise and truthful language.

**十四行诗**：对于语言，他们嘲笑它的模糊，讥讽它的漏洞，揭示它的矛盾，就像那场辩论。\
**Sonetto**: They mock language for its ambiguity, scorn its flaws, and ruthlessly expose its inconsistencies, like they did during that debate.

**十四行诗**：——也如这个石环的规则。\
**Sonetto**: The pact on this bangle is of a similar nature.

**红弩箭**：不错，不可主动攻击——但什么是攻击？\
**Lilya**: I see. It forbids us from actively attacking, but what is considered an attack?

**红弩箭**：制定试卷的长官可没把这个写在卷面上啊。\
**Lilya**: The rule-maker did not specify that.

**十四行诗**：没有攻击意图，就不会被判定为攻击。\
**Sonetto**: An act without the intent to attack will not be seen as an attack.

**十四行诗**：——这就是石环隐藏的规则。\
**Sonetto**: That is the unspoken rule of the peace agreement.

**阿尔卡纳**：呵呵，很有趣的钻空子尝试。\
**Arcana**: Heh-heh. An adorable attempt.

**阿尔卡纳**：那你准备好牺牲你给予忠诚的那位同伴了吗，基金会的小狗儿？\
**Arcana**: Are you truly prepared to gamble the life of thy sworn companion, little pup of the Foundation?

她的身后出现了混沌不明的造物影像。\
Behind her, an unidentifiable form materializes into existence.

十四行诗摇了摇头，握着玻璃笔的指尖并未动摇分毫。\
Sonetto shakes her head, her wand remains steady.

**十四行诗**：我不会再犯同样的错误了，阿尔卡纳小姐。\
**Sonetto**: I will not make the same mistake again, Ms. Arcana.

**十四行诗**：我很清楚自己在做什么，你的暗示是无用的。\
**Sonetto**: I know perfectly well what I'm doing. Your provocations will not work on me.

**十四行诗**：——为了所有人的和平……\
**Sonetto**: For the peace of this world,

**十四行诗**：我会阻止你。\
**Sonetto**: I will stop you.

神秘术的辉光自术杖尖端流出。\
The wand radiates an intense brilliance.

**十四行诗**：Regna sereno intenso ed infinito!\
**Sonetto**: Regna sereno intenso ed infinito!

剧场场景-游轮。

浪花击打着船舷。\
The ship sways gently in the waves.

这是一艘前往新世界的船，也是一艘注定不会返航的船。\
It is set for a new world, and there's no turning back.

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

红发女孩自上船后，一言未发。\
She hasn't spoken a word since they sailed.

一切都已成定局的现在，她唯有沉默。\
The situation is final and the board is set, there's nothing for her to do but to stay silent.

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：……苏菲亚小姐。\
**Manus Believer I**: Ms. Sophia.

**重塑教众Ⅰ**：引导之人真的不和我们一起离开吗？她……\
**Manus Believer I**: Is the Guiding One really not coming with us? She ...

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

传令人没有应答，只是不断摩挲着手中小小的圣像。\
She doesn't answer, absentmindedly caressing the tiny idol.

获得它的一幕依然清晰。

剧场场景-岛屿-炮火轰炸的沙滩-闪回滤镜\
She still remembers the moment she received it.

**苏菲亚**：您是说，您……\
**Sophia**: Are you saying ...

**阿尔卡纳**：不用慌张，我的孩子。\
**Arcana**: Fret not, my child.

**阿尔卡纳**：你没有听错。\
**Arcana**: You heard me true.

**阿尔卡纳**：——我将于今日死去。\
**Arcana**: I shall die today.

剧场场景-黑屏-闪回结束

**十四行诗**：司辰，术式α点位准备完毕！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, location α is ready for the ritual!

**红弩箭**：β点位就位！\
**Lilya**: Location β, ready!

**星锑**：我和APPLe先生这边也好了！\
**Regulus**: Mr. APPLe and I are ready!

**维尔汀**：很好！\
**Vertin**: Good!

这场战斗的目的，自一开始就并非攻击。或者说，至少不是一场在此地发生的攻击。\
This is not a preparation for an attack. At least not for an attack here.

**维尔汀**：我申请使用大型神秘术收录号000262603100008，“心向往之”——\
**Vertin**: Requesting to use the advanced arcane skill "Aferoj Around," No. 000262603100008,

**维尔汀**：传送一名极其危险的犯罪者前往巴门尼德基地！\
**Vertin**: to teleport a top priority threat to the Parmenides Base!

巨大术式的辉光亮起，笼罩了居于中心的阿尔卡纳。\
The glow of the ritual envelops Arcana.

**阿尔卡纳**：……噢？\
**Arcana**: Oh?

**红弩箭**：别慌张，这只是个长距离旅途邀请。\
**Lilya**: Loosen up and enjoy the ride.

**红弩箭**：——一路顺风，伙计。\
**Lilya**: Goodbye.

芝诺的军事基地观察室内，伊戈尔将军（原索姆将军）以及一行人正在紧张的注视着屏幕。在云爆弹发射的倒计时里，阿尔卡纳被传送到了指定地点，云爆弹落下，白光照在伊戈尔将军的脸上。芝诺报告生命反应消失，作战计划成功，阿尔卡纳死亡，以室内一片最后的狂欢结束。

**操作员Ⅰ**：引爆器准备就绪。发射倒计时，30、29、28……\
**Operator I**: Launch sequence initiated. Starting countdown. 30, 29, 28 ...

**观察员Ⅰ**：目标尚未抵达指定地点。警告，目标尚未抵达——\
**Observer I**: The target has not reached the designated location. I repeat, the target has ...

**操作员Ⅰ**：15、14、13……\
**Operator I**: 15, 14, 13 ...

**观察员Ⅰ**：检测到大型神秘术式能量，校验通过，“心向往之”。生命信号出现，目标已监测就位，启动引爆器——\
**Observer I**: Large-scale arcane ritual detected. "Aferoj Around," verified. Life signal detected. Target is in position. Initiating detonation ...

**操作员Ⅰ**：6、5、4、3、2……\
**Operator I**: 6, 5, 4, 3, 2 ...

**操作员Ⅰ**：1——\
**Operator I**: 1!

画面3-爆炸特效。一个持续的白光。

**操作员Ⅰ**：真空弹引爆成功。\
**Operator I**: Vacuum bomb detonated.

**观察员Ⅰ**：无法监听到任何神秘学能量信号，无生命反应迹象。\
**Observer I**: No arcane energy detected. No life signal detected.

**观察员Ⅰ**：目标，阿尔卡纳女士，已被剿灭……\
**Observer I**: Target eliminated. I repeat. The target has been eliminated.

画面4-画面1的差分，操作员兴奋地转头，伊戈尔将军摘下护目镜，观察员望向他们。

**操作员Ⅰ**：太好了，我们做到了？我们做到了！\
**Operator I**: We did it? We actually did it!

**操作员Ⅰ**：上将，汉斯……我们九九年没有做到的事情……\
**Operator I**: Admiral, Hans, we made up for what we didn't do in '99.

**观察员Ⅰ**：这是，这是胜利……？\
**Observer I**: Did we win?

**伊戈尔将军**：不要放松警惕。\
**Admiral Igor**: It's too early to celebrate.

**伊戈尔将军**：……但为了那场战役所失去的一切，这一刻将永远铭记在世界历史上。\
**Admiral Igor**: But history will remember this moment and honor all that was lost in this long battle.

**操作员Ⅰ**：稍等，汉斯！\
**Operator I**: Wait. Hans!

**操作员Ⅰ**：……那是什么声音？你的监听耳机里……\
**Operator I**: You hear that? In your headphones.

所有人都听到了它。\
Everyone can hear it.

一阵刺耳的沙沙声，毫无缘由地在理应隔音的室内再次响起。\
A grating static.

**观察员Ⅰ**：……\
**Observer I**: ...

**观察员Ⅰ**：报、报告，我好像听到了一些生命信号，但是音质受到干扰，我不确定那是……\
**Observer I**: A-Admiral, we might have a life signal, but there's too much interference.

**伊戈尔将军**：耳机给我。\
**Admiral Igor**: Give me that.

画面6-伊戈尔将军凝重地、紧张地监听着耳机，但情绪没有特别外露。其他的员工紧张地望着他。

这次的作战计划是临时提出的，观察室的选址也并不完备。\
The plan was made with little time to spare, and the location chosen for the observation room is far from ideal.

至少室内古怪的杂音已经消失了。\
But soon enough, the strange sound in the room subsides.

**伊戈尔将军**：……

**伊戈尔将军**：…………\
**Admiral Igor**: ...

**伊戈尔将军**：不，并不是。那不是生命的声音。\
**Admiral Igor**: No, it's nothing. There is no sign of life.

**伊戈尔将军**：那是……风在呼啸。\
**Admiral Igor**: It was the wind.

**众**：…………\
**Crowd**: ...

**操作员Ⅰ**：……！也就是说……\
**Operator I**: So, that means ...

同志们，我们做到了。\
We did it, everyone.

**操作员Ⅰ**：——祝贺伟大的胜利日！向您致敬，向司辰小队致敬——！\
**Operator I**: A triumphant victory! A salute to you, admiral, and to the Timekeeper!

**观察员Ⅰ**：上将，今日，我们终于捍卫了和平。荣耀归于这英勇的一日！\
**Observer I**: Our efforts for peace have prevailed, and we have emerged victorious. Let us forever remember this day for its greatness!

**众**：荣耀归于为这一刻奋战的所有人！\
**Crowd**: Glory to all who fought for this moment!

**众**：我们做到了！\
**Crowd**: We did it!

缓慢的淡出，黑屏。

观察室内迎来了最终胜利的欢呼。\
The observation room erupts in triumph.

阿尔卡纳，死亡。\
Arcana, deceased.

## 7TH-22 致传道者 / The Ones Who Pray

在这平坦的沙滩上，在这海面与陆地之间，我能建造或创作什么，以抵挡暗夜的降临？告诉我，该刻下何种符咒，以抵御袭来的波涛，告诉我，该建筑何样堡垒，以庇护比我更长久的岁月。 ——阿尔弗雷德·豪斯曼\
Here, on the level sand,Between the sea and land,What shall I build or writeAgainst the fall of night?Tell me of runes to graveThat hold the bursting wave,Or bastions to designFor longer date than mine.—Alfred Housman

**210**：把这个喝了，能让你忘掉腿部的疼痛……对，这酒并不是用我头上的葡萄酿造的，你大可放心。\
**210**: Drink this. It will help relieve your pain. Worry not, it's not made from the grapes on my head.

剧情场景-传道者之厅-被炸毁版本\
The war may have ended, but its scars remain in this place.

战火已经停息，此地却永久地留下了创伤的烙印。\
The Hall of Truth, once the palace of knowledge, now stands in ruins.

真理的殿堂已经是一地废墟。

210观察了一会儿伤员的情形，确定他的痛苦已经得以缓解。而后，他站起来，望向刚刚进入厅堂的人。\
210 examines the injured man's face closely, making sure his pain is eased. Then he stands and watches as more people are brought through the gate.

**888**：29，再坚持一下。\
**888**: Hang in there, 29.

888背着丧失了行动能力的同胞，小心地让他在尚算开阔的平地上躺下。\
888 makes her way into the hall, carrying an incapacitated believer on her back. She carefully lowers the person to the floor.

她的胳膊也在炮火轰炸中挂彩，所幸伤势并不致命。\
Her own arms are wounded from the attack, but fortunately they're not fatal.

自整数们醒来后，便一直在重复这样的过程。\
Since the integers awakened, this has been the only thing they've been doing.

**210**：还有尚未发现的伤员吗？\
**210**: Are there any other injured that have not been found yet?

**888**：不，我走遍了整座岛屿，所有数字应当都在这里了。\
**888**: I've scouted the island. Every remaining member should be here.

**210**：是吗。\
**210**: So you have.

一声轻微的叹息，关于一个无可奈何的事实。\
He sighs, the ramifications of the situation weighing down on them.

**210**：——所以，其他人都加入了重塑之手。\
**210**: It means the members not here have joined Manus Vindictae.

厅堂沉默着。\
The hall is dead silent.

仅在数小时前，人们还在这里争辩、议论、进行思想的交锋和学派事务的探讨。\
Just a few hours ago, it was alive with debates, ideas, and passion.

如今，厅堂空了一半。被炸成碎石的穹顶自高处落下，占据了缺席者的位置。\
But now one half of the hall is gone, its seats buried under the shattered dome and crumbling walls.

**888**：玛尔塔女士，6仍未醒来吗？\
**888**: Is 6 still in a coma, Ms. Marta?

盲眼的信众摇了摇头，脸上的忧虑越发凝重。\
The blind woman nods, concern etched on her face.

女妖不再言语，她身上的伤口也急需清理。\
The banshee doesn't say anything else. She needs to clean out her own wounds.

接连发生的变故摧毁了这里的一切：信仰的崩溃、人类的轰炸、重塑之手的离间……\
The last few hours have been a whirlwind. Their faith has crumbled, the humans have invaded their island, and Manus Vindictae has turned them against each other.

好在，它们已经全都离开了——真理、仇敌、同伴。\
But now, everything's gone—enemies, friends, and even the Truth.

仅剩下往昔的碎片和伤员的低吟。\
All that's left are the moans and groans that fill the hall.

在这空旷的寂静之中，有人开始微弱的祈祷。\
In the midst of the hushed void, some begin to pray.

**教众Ⅴ**：……唯一的无限，唯一的自在者，伟大的不可言喻者。请允许我的祈求。\
**Believer V**: To you, O the alone infinite, the non-subsistent, the ineffable, I call;

**教众Ⅴ**：让我不要丧失于本性的灵光，让真理指引魂灵以自由……\
**Believer V**: Grant me inspiration of nature, guide my soul with Truth.

哀悼与希冀由同一个声音说出。\
These are the words of both sorrow and hope.

这是一个庄严的时刻，它予以生者沉思的空间，也予以逝者片刻的尊重。\
Words of contemplation and honor for the dead.

也让人们从悲伤和悔恨中短暂地移开目光。\
A brief respite where they can find solace to ease their pain.

**教众Ⅴ**：请赐予我启明的力量，让我得以冲破盲目与无知之网。\
**Believer V**: Give me power of enlightenment, tear off from the web of ignorance.

低声的跟读加入了祈祷，和声循环往复。\
More people join in. Their prayers reverberate through the hall.

**教众Ⅴ**：……由此，得以解除萦绕在我身上的沉沦、仇恨和恶。\
**Believer V**: Redeem me from the evil, hatred, and what throttles me down.

**教众Ⅴ**：得以冲破罪恶的根源、堕落的镣铐、阴郁的高墙、逼真的死亡、感觉的尸首、包围我们的坟墓。\
**Believer V**: Break through the ground of bad, corruption's chain, the carapace of darkness, the living death, sensation's corpse, the tomb I carry.

**教众Ⅴ**：认识到真理的美和善，领悟到万物的平衡和限度。\
**Believer V**: Learn the beauty of Truth, the balance and limitations of all.

**教众Ⅳ**：——够了！\
**Believer IV**: ENOUGH!

有人突然发出了呵斥。是29，协理人刚刚放下的伤员。\
It's 29, the injured believer just carried in by 888.

他的腿被炸断了，但依然强忍着痛苦，背靠石柱，使自己能够坐起来一点。\
A leg is missing, but he manages to get up and sit down against the wall.

**教众Ⅳ**：事到如今，祈祷又有什么用？！真理已经不存在了！！！\
**Believer IV**: Why are you still praying? The Truth is gone!

**教众Ⅳ**：我们向谁祈祷？又有谁会回应？\
**Believer IV**: Who are we praying to? Who will answer us?

怒吼没能持续，男人的声音逐渐哽咽，化为不甘的啜泣。\
His outburst falters, turning into a bitter sob.

**教众Ⅳ**：我们在漫长时光里所追求的一切……究竟有什么意义？我们这些侥幸存活的人……又是为了什么而活下来？\
**Believer IV**: For generations, we have searched for purpose and meaning. But now that the Truth is lost, what is left for us to live for?

**37**：——不，真理还存在着！！\
**37**: No, the Truth is still there!

清亮的答音。像一粒石子落在冬日冰冻的湖面上。\
A crisp voice echoes through the hall.

37气喘吁吁地出现在厅堂内，旁边站着司辰小队的成员。\
37 arrives panting at the door, accompanied by members of the Timekeeper's team.

**37**：我通过了无限定者的试炼，我拿到了它，这个一劳永逸免于生之巨轮流转的方法。\
**37**: I passed Apeiron's test, and It showed me the answer. It will free us from the wheel of birth, once and for all.

**37**：只要给我一些时间解开——！\
**37**: I just need some time to decode it!

厅堂的所有人都转向了她。\
She feels their stares weigh heavily on her—

尚在祈祷的人、缺失了腿脚的人、丢失了魂灵和信仰的人。\
—the wounded, the desperate, those who have lost their faith and their souls in the last few hours.

协理人迎了上来，她的声音依然沉静。\
The Custodian walks up to her, still composed and steady.

**888**：我们会全力协助你，37。\
**888**: We will do our best to help.

**888**：问题是，你需要多少时间……？\
**888**: But, how much time do you need?

一针见血的疑问，女孩移开了双眼。\
A crucial question. The girl averts her eyes.

上次回答这个问题时的失败，令她丧失了脱口而出的信心。\
Her confidence has waned since the last time she answered this question.

**维尔汀**：……关于这一点，我想，有一个办法可以提高破译密码的速度。\
**Vertin**: I have someone in mind that can help us decode faster.

是的，在世界的另一个角落，正有人在雨幕之下做着同样的研究。\
Elsewhere in this world, some people are also making the same efforts at all costs.

免疫“暴雨”的研究。\
They, too, are studying the immunity to the "Storm."

**维尔汀**：但在获得他们的帮助前，我需要征求你的同意，37。\
**Vertin**: But I need your approval before I ask them for help.

抬起帽檐，礼貌地注视她的眼睛。\
This will require some finesse.

这事关学派的原则，理应严肃地对待。\
What's about to be asked might rattle the founding principles of their belief system.

**维尔汀**：——你愿意我将你得到的真理分享出去吗？\
**Vertin**: May I share the Truth with the others, 37?

剧情场景-露西女士的办公室-开灯版本\
The experiments on the side effects of the ritual are ongoing.

关于术式副作用的研究正紧锣密鼓地进行着。\
The list of conditions they've encountered stretches down the pages like a long, winding snake.

出现的诅咒种类在纸上蜿蜒如一条无首的长蛇。

**露西**：嗯，它的确是完全随机的。在目前的统计样本里，有0.52%的概率不会触发任何副作用。\
**Lucy**: The side effects are completely random. Among the current samples, the probability of no side effects occurring is 0.52%.

**露西**：而在登记的81种副作用中，39种会对生物躯体造成不可逆转的破坏作用，24种会永久改变躯体存在的性质……\
**Lucy**: And of the 81 recorded side effects, 39 of them will cause irreversible damage to the biological body; 24 will permanently alter the composition of the caster's body functioning;

**露西**：还有18种较为轻微，仅在体表造成轻微损害，不会影响施术者正常生活。\
**Lucy**: and 18 minor effects will cause only minor, superficial injuries that do not affect daily functioning.

**露西**：科算中心储备的术式库可以有效防御最后一种情况，但前两类诅咒依然是几乎致死的。\
**Lucy**: Laplace's Archives has enough rituals to protect casters from the minor effects, but the other two categories are highly lethal.

这是张用生命写成的统计表，她也的确同拆解机器般去推演它。\
The list was made at the cost of lives, and she meticulously analyzes each item as if taking apart an intricate machine.

**露西**：实验进行72次后，副作用多样性明显减少。但不确定这是因为在同一对象上实验次数过多，还是因为副作用的类型有极限。\
**Lucy**: After 72 experiments, the diversity of side effects has decreased significantly. It is unclear if this is due to repeated testing on a single subject, or due to a limited range of possible side effects.

**露西**：……而这些副作用90%以上，都和“泥土”、“尘埃”有关。\
**Lucy**: More than 90% of these effects are related to concepts such as "dirt" and "dust."

**露西**：它和这个术式的力量来源有关吗？\
**Lucy**: Is it because of the origins of this ritual's power?

**露西**：……嗯？\
**Lucy**: Hm?

拿着列表的手短暂地顿了一下。\
She stops briefly, scanning through the list again.

**露西**：这里登记的副作用共有86种，不是81种。\
**Lucy**: The number of recorded side effects is 86, not 81.

**露西**：……这5条是我什么时候写上去的？\
**Lucy**: When did I write these five down?

敲门声中断了她的思绪，助理礼貌地走了进来。\
A knock at the door interrupts her thoughts. Simone walks in.

**助理希曼**：露西女士，芝诺军备学院的计划成功了。\
**Assistant Simone**: Madam Lucy, Zeno's plan was a success.

**助理希曼**：他们联合司辰小队，将重塑之手的领袖传送到了一处废弃的军事基地上，随后关闭传送阵，朝那里发射了一枚燃料空气弹。\
**Assistant Simone**: With the help of Team Timekeeper, the leader of Manus Vindictae was teleported to a deserted military base and targeted with a thermobaric weapon.

**助理希曼**：……炸弹击中了目标，生命反应切实消失了，观察室的摄像头记录下了那历史性的一幕。\
**Assistant Simone**: It was a direct hit with no signs of life detected. The momentous event was captured on camera in the observation room.

总负责人在纸张和文件间点了点头。这是个震撼人心的好消息，但在研究的紧要关头，她分不出太多回路去表现喜悦。\
The director nods in approval. It is good news, but she can't devote much of her processing power to expressing joy while she's focused on research.

**露西**：这是十分伟大的荣耀，请替我向上将传达祝贺之词。\
**Lucy**: A tremendous victory. Please extend my congratulations to the admiral for this remarkable feat.

**助理希曼**：另外，有两个人想要和您通话。\
**Assistant Simone**: Also, you have two call requests.

**助理希曼**：一位是司辰，在对重塑之手的作战成功后，她立刻向科算中心提出了通话请求。\
**Assistant Simone**: One is from the Timekeeper, which Laplace received shortly after the battle with Manus Vindictae.

**助理希曼**：她希望我们能远程协助阿派朗学派的成员解开一串数字密码，这事关免疫“暴雨”的研究。\
**Assistant Simone**: She is requesting remote assistance to help the Apeiron decode a numerical code related to the "Storm" immunity.

这是一个不可忽视的情报，总负责人迅速地抬起头。\
This information demands attention. The director's head snaps up.

**露西**：请立刻帮我接通。\
**Lucy**: Put her through immediately.

助理点了点头，但绷紧的肩膀并未松懈。显然，她此行并不只为了传递好消息。\
Simone nods, but her shoulders remain tense. There's more.

**露西**：……另一个人呢？\
**Lucy**: And the other call?

**助理希曼**：是帮助马库斯调查员传回这个术式的维也纳神秘学家，卡卡尼亚。\
**Assistant Simone**: It's Kakania, the Viennese arcanist who helped Investigator Marcus in acquiring the ritual.

助理的眼神有一些犹豫。\
A hint of hesitation appears in her eyes.

**助理希曼**：……我们已将目前研究的进度和副作用告知于她。\
**Assistant Simone**: We have updated her the progress of the study and the potential side effects of the incantation.

**助理希曼**：但她仍然希望获得术式的正确读法。\
**Assistant Simone**: But she insists on knowing the right pronunciation.

## 7TH-23 碑文辞书 / The Rosetta Stone

剧情场景-洞穴研究室-1.9差分版本，进行一些改装\
在这里刷一个无线电小姐的spine，同时配一下那个通讯特效，表示在用收音机通讯。

**维尔汀**：是的，我们并不知悉这一情况。维也纳调查员传回术式时，我和37刚刚进入试炼地。\
**Vertin**: No, we are not aware of that. 37 and I had just entered the cave when the investigator sent back the ritual.

收音机那头的声音暗了下去，无线电小姐强打精神，尽力捕捉那飘忽不定的信号。\
The transmission is weakening. Ms. Radio musters all her strength, struggling to hold on to the fleeting signal in the air.

**维尔汀**：……我明白了，感谢您对研究现状不吝解释，露西女士。我会将这一情况告知阿派朗学派的成员。\
**Vertin**: I see. Thank you for the thorough explanation, Madam Lucy. I'll make sure to inform the members of Apeiron.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

真的能够记住这么多技术和数字细节吗？\
Is it really possible to remember all those numbers and technical details?

**维尔汀**：……如果您方便的话，可否等我们架设通讯设备后，请您再次为她们说明这些情况？\
**Vertin**: If possible, could you kindly explain this to them again after we set up the communication device?

这势必是洞穴研究室开凿以来最为热闹的一天。\
The lab has never been busier since the day it was built.

之前散落的文件已经被全部收拢，幸存的整数们也参与到了研究室的整理中。\
The scattered files are neatly gathered, and more integers have come to help sort through the years of documents.

无线电小姐被庄重地放在IDM旁边，仿佛是神庙前的贡品。\
Ms. Radio is placed next to the IDM with a sense of reverence.

计算机的屏幕亮了起来，一个熟悉的声音正从里面传出。\
The computer screen lights up, a familiar voice comes out of the speakers.

**X**：那么接下来你们需要装置感声元件。当然了，你们手边没有也很正常～星锑，你去找……\
**X**: The next thing's the acoustic components. Totally understandable if you don't have any on hand. Regulus, can you help me find some ...

**星锑**：你在说什么？伟大的唱片骑师怎么可能没有这种东西！\
**Regulus**: What are you saying, mate? Of course, this great Disk Jockey would have the acoustic components!

**星锑**：我可是一有空就去和海豚打好关系，指望它们把APPLeⅡ号上的电台设备叼回来……\
**Regulus**: I'll have you know, I made friends with the dolphins as soon as I had the chance, hoping they'd retrieve some of the radio components from APPLe II.

**星锑**：——还真让我回收了不少！\
**Regulus**: And guess what? They actually found some!

星锑兴致勃勃地说着，将感声元件装到了IDM上。\
She attaches the acoustic component onto the IDM, beaming with excitement.

**星锑**：喂，喂喂——\
**Regulus**: Hello? Testing, testing, one, two, three.

巨大的杂音令众人立刻捂住了耳朵。\
The screeching feedback forces everyone to cover their ears.

**X**：好的，我想你们现在就多了一个含扩音器的通讯线路。毕竟你们不能所有人都把耳朵贴在收音机上……\
**X**: Perfect. You finally have a communicator equipped with a speaker. Before, there were too many ears for one tiny radio.

**X**：——噢！\
**X**: Ah?!

椅子、桌子撞到的声音（比格拆家的声音）

**教众Ⅴ**：天啊，发生什么事了？轰炸机又打过来了吗？\
**Believer V**: Wh-what now? Another attack?

**X**：不不，这只是我们的同僚兔毛手袋在工作。\
**X**: Not quite. That's the sound of our colleague, Medicine Pocket, hard at work.

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-破译房间。\
Finally, a real communicator for Team Timekeeper.

帮助司辰小队架设通讯设备的任务已经完成了。\
X gets up, skirts around Medicine Pocket's mess on the floor, and casually makes himself a cappuccino.

X站起来，小心地绕开同僚制造的一地混乱，悠哉地给自己泡了一杯卡布奇诺。

**X**：维尔汀，你们那边的情况还好吗？\
**X**: How goes it on your end, Vertin?

**X**：距离“暴雨”落下只有8个小时了，小岛的“免疫区”停止缩小了吗？\
**X**: The "Storm" is only eight hours away. Has the "immunity zone" on the island stopped shrinking?

**维尔汀**：我想是的，免疫区的衰减已经停止了，“暴雨”症候没有侵入传道者之厅以内的岛上区域。\
**Vertin**: I think so. No one in the Hall of Apeiron's affected by the Storm Syndrome so far.

**维尔汀**：它似乎进入了一个暂时的稳定态。\
**Vertin**: The "immunity zone" seems stable for now.

**维尔汀**：……毕竟，重塑之手和人类都已经离开，这座岛也不会再承受更多破坏了。\
**Vertin**: Manus Vindictae and the humans have left. There should be no further destruction on the island.

**X**：唔，这么说来，它的衰减不是线性的，受到岛民对真理的态度影响，而且达到一定程度就会停止。\
**X**: Hmm, so the decay of the immunity zone is not linear. It seems to be influenced by the islanders' mindset toward the Truth, and it eventually reaches a stopping point.

X放下了咖啡杯，思索起自己在这段闲聊中获取的新信息来。\
He puts down the cup and thinks about everything he heard from the call.

**X**：难道岛民信仰所构成的巨大术式，仅仅是对岛屿免疫“暴雨”范围的增幅？嗯，这很有趣……\
**X**: Could it be that the ritual on this island, rooted in the power of faith and belief, serves to amplify only the radius of the "Storm" immunity? Fascinating.

**破译组长**：——那个等会再说，X研究员。\
**Cryptography Lead**: That can wait, Researcher X.

性情急躁的磁流体带着更重要的课题插了进来，打断了X的侃侃而谈。\
Ulrich, impatient as ever, interrupts his musings with a more important concern.

眼下，有太多十万火急的研究讨论正等待着接入聊天线。\
There are still pressing matters to discuss with the Timekeeper through the device.

**破译组长**：我想确认一件事，司辰。\
**Cryptography Lead**: There's one thing I'd like to confirm, Timekeeper.

**破译组长**：有关37小姐在地下洞穴询问的问题——“如何才能不受现象世界的黑暗所绊，一劳永逸地自灵性的‘流溢’中幸免。”\
**Cryptography Lead**: About the question Ms. 37 asked in the cave, "How can we escape the darkness of the phenomenal world, and be freed from the 'Emanation' forever?"

**破译组长**：如果我没有理解错，这个问题几乎等价于询问免疫“暴雨”的办法。\
**Cryptography Lead**: To my understanding, that is almost the same as asking how we can be immune to the "Storm."

闪回-回忆画面-37问天的复刻

**维尔汀**：是的。据37所说，她有限的躯体无法承受这个真理。无限定者回答了一串异响，光是听到就足以让人心智失常。\
**Vertin**: Yes, and 37 also said the transcendental Truth was beyond the limits of her mortal flesh. Apeiron answered her with an eerie sound, one that could drive anyone mad just by hearing it.

**维尔汀**：随后，6给予的卷轴摊开，将其转译为一串数字，我们的答案由此得来。\
**Vertin**: It was then that the scroll 6 gave her unfurled and transcribed the sound into a string of numbers, providing us with the code.

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-露西的办公室。

**破译组长**：对，这正是问题的关键！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Yes, that's the key to our problem!

**破译组长**：我们双方在同一时间，获得了同一个问题的答案，免疫“暴雨”。\
**Cryptography Lead**: We both received a solution to the same question simultaneously—immunity against the "Storm."

**破译组长**：如果我没有想错，这就是罗塞塔石碑，司辰！——我们得到了一个罗塞塔石碑！！！\
**Cryptography Lead**: This could be our Rosetta Stone, Timekeeper! We've found our own Rosetta Stone!

磁流体的声音越发激动，它已经完全沉浸在了玻璃缸脑内的小小世界中。\
His voice rises in excitement as he becomes fully immersed in his thoughts.

与之对应的，它听众的注意力正逐渐流失，变为一个发自内心的问号。\
Meanwhile, his listener's mind is starting to wander with a big question mark in the air.

**维尔汀**：罗塞塔……石碑？\
**Vertin**: Rosetta Stone?

**露西**：嗯，我来为诸位解释吧。\
**Lucy**: Allow me to explain.

总负责人的声音适时地出现，为这跨越性的理解鸿沟递上了一块木板。\
The director interjects with a well-timed explanation.

**露西**：在罗塞塔石碑上刻着同一段诏书的三种语言版本，分别是圣书体、世俗体、古希腊文。\
**Lucy**: The Rosetta Stone is a stone tablet inscribed with a decree in three different languages: Hieroglyphs, Demotic, and Ancient Greek.

**露西**：圣书体是献给神明的语言，世俗体是平民使用的文字，这二者都是古埃及象形文字，在石碑发掘时已彻底失传。\
**Lucy**: Hieroglyphs were the sacred writing for the divine, while Demotic script was known as "the language of the people." Both scripts were ancient Egyptian, lost to time when the tablet was discovered.

**露西**：而古希腊文则是今人可阅读的，于是，借由三段文字的对照，人们最终破译了这些古埃及文。\
**Lucy**: However, because scholars were still able to read Ancient Greek, and through comparing the three inscriptions that all said the same thing, they were finally able to understand the Hieroglyphs.

**露西**：——现在我们也有三种语言。\
**Lucy**: And now, we too have our own set of "inscriptions" to decode.

**露西**：第一段圣书体，是37小姐在洞穴中聆听的真理。仅仅听到，就会让人心智失常，完全不可解析。\
**Lucy**: The first is similar to Hieroglyphs, as the Truth Ms. 37 heard in the cave is completely unintelligible and can drive people insane just by listening to it.

**露西**：第二段世俗体，是我们目前截获的原始术式。一旦念出，就会招致诅咒，常人无法掌握。\
**Lucy**: The second is like Demotic script, a ritual we obtained from Arcana that can place a "curse" upon those who read it aloud. It cannot be handled by ordinary people.

**露西**：第三段古希腊文，是您分享的数字密码，我们可以掌握。它本身不具备神力，却可以帮我们解开前二者的奥秘。\
**Lucy**: Finally, the numerical code you shared with us is like the readable Ancient Greek—without any divine powers, but crucial in deciphering the other two inscriptions.

**37**：——太有趣了！\
**37**: How intriguing!

罗塞塔石碑收起

37的声音兴奋地插入了通讯线路里，这个比喻无疑勾起了她的兴趣。\
37's voice chimed in over the line, clearly excited by the analogy.

**37**：你是说，我们双方的研究合并起来，就可能触及更深层的秘辛，获得只属于神明的知识……？\
**37**: That is to say, if we work together and combine our research, we may unlock even deeper knowledge that only belongs to the divine?

**破译组长**：正是！我们探寻的是同一个问题的答案，就像罗塞塔石碑上刻印的是同一段诏书。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Exactly! We're looking for the same answer to the same question, like how the same decree is inscribed onto the tablet in different forms.

**破译组长**：而我们也获得了内容不同的有效回答，就像罗塞塔石碑上的三种语言！\
**Cryptography Lead**: And just like the inscriptions on the tablet, we have three versions of the ritual!

**破译组长**：如果我们能借此加深对它的本质理解，掌握术式深层的奥秘。\
**Cryptography Lead**: If we can delve into the essence of the ritual and master its inner workings,

**破译组长**：那么最终，我们就有可能把它转译成一个无副作用的、所有人都能使用的、一劳永逸的有效版本！\
**Cryptography Lead**: we may eventually transcribe it into a side-effect-free ritual that can be used by everyone!

**37**：唔噢——！\
**37**: Yes!

**37**：一定是这样的，因为宇宙在任何地方都是齐一的！\
**37**: It should work! Because the nature of the universe flows in all things alike!

**破译组长**：很高兴您能这么想，37小姐！\
**Cryptography Lead**: I'm glad you think so, Ms. 37!

通讯那头的女孩也被这样伟大的创想打动了。这无疑是一场成功的电波相会，磁流体感动地在玻璃缸内打起了旋。\
The girl on the other end of the phone is equally ecstatic. There's no question that they're in sync on this incredible idea. The ferrofluid happily swirls around in its fishbowl.

可惜，它的上司是一个实用主义者。\
Regrettably, his boss is a practical thinker.

**露西**：你的假说里有太多的“如果”了，乌尔里希组长。它缺乏进一步的完善和验证。\
**Lucy**: Your hypothesis is based on too many assumptions, Ulrich. It requires further refinement and confirmation.

**露西**：我们已经得到了切实有效的咒文，眼下应该沿着这条道路继续前行。\
**Lucy**: We now have valid incantations. We should continue in this direction.

总负责人无情中断了破译组长的滔滔不绝。\
Her words are like a bucket of ice water dumped over their heads.

对机器而言，现在有更具现实意义和可行性的课题。\
As always, the robot steers them to a more practical path.

**露西**：但您刚刚说到转译——这的确是术式改良的关键，司辰的描述中也有这至关重要的一步。\
**Lucy**: You mentioned the word "transcribe," just like the Timekeeper did. It holds the answer to improving the ritual.

**维尔汀**：您是说……\
**Vertin**: You mean ...

**露西**：是的，您描述里的卷轴，“能助人跨越与伟大存在交感时的灵性鸿沟。”\
**Lucy**: The scroll you mentioned that can "bridge the gap between you and the supreme existence during communion."

**露西**：是它将不可知的异响翻译为了数字，规避了致死的副作用。\
**Lucy**: It is the scroll that transcribed the eerie sound and saved 37 from the lethal side effects.

**露西**：这是否意味着……它也能够有效降低免疫咒文的副作用？\
**Lucy**: Does this mean it could potentially lessen the negative effects of the immunity incantation?

**破译组长**：……！\
**Cryptography Lead**: ...!

实验室内的所有成员意识到了事情的关键。\
Everyone in the lab realizes it at once.

不论从哪个方向攻克课题，副作用都是最需解决的问题。\
Reducing the side effects is faster than trying to come up with a perfect, side-effect-free incantation from scratch.

现在，它出现了——神秘学的诅咒理应能通过神秘学的方式消除。\
Now, the solution is right in front of them—the scroll that can solve arcanum with arcanum.

**破译组长**：等一下，露西女士，这里让我来——\
**Cryptography Lead**: Wait, Madam Lucy, let me take it from here—

**露西**：——我们想要调查这个卷轴。\
**Lucy**: We would like to borrow this scroll for research.

**露西**：如果贵方愿意将这个卷轴临时出借，研究将会有突飞猛进的进展，我们也会为学派提供一切后续所需的支持。\
**Lucy**: If you lend us this scroll, we will make significant advancements on the research, and we promise to provide every assistance you require in the future.

——破译组长的热心没能赶上，机器直截了当的电磁音已经先一步抵达。\
The ferrofluid flinches into the shape of a droplet of sweat. It was too late to stop her.

磁流体变成了一滴汗水的形状，通讯设备另一头的神秘学家们的神情也因此而变色。\
The atmosphere on the other end of the call changes dramatically.

剧情场景-洞穴研究室-1.9差分版本，进行一些改装

**888**：分享卷轴——？\
**888**: Lend you the scroll?

正在整理资料的协理人从研究室的一角站了起来，神情多少有些不可思议。\
The Custodian leaps up from her corner in disbelief.

**888**：您是说，要我们将学派宝贵的遗产、不传的缄默之秘——授予你们，一个主要服务于人类的科研组织？\
**888**: Are you asking us to give the legacy of Apeiron, our most cherished possession, to YOU, a scientific research organization that serves humans?

研究室内陷入了沉默，沉默预示着问题的严重。\
The lab falls silent, reflecting the seriousness of the request.

对一个以守秘为原则的教派而言，这无异于触及它们誓言的核心、信仰的咽喉。\
For a school of thought that has always kept its knowledge hidden, this is a major threat to its core beliefs and sacred vows.

而回答她的依然是那道清脆的声音。\
But the silence is broken again by that cheery voice.

——那道永不缺席的质疑之声。\
The voice that always questions and doubts.

**37**：——为什么不能？\
**37**: Why not?

**37**：这也是为了真理，不是吗？\
**37**: We are seekers of Truth, are we not?

## 7TH-24 历史的回环 / The Cycle of History

剧情场景-传道者之厅-被炸毁版本

**888**：……37，请你听取我的意见。\
**888**: Heed my words, 37.

**888**：你手上的卷轴是学派先贤传下的珍贵遗产，它由每一代的6保管，只会被授与那些勇于挑战无限定者试炼的信仰者。\
**888**: That scroll is a sacred relic passed down from the wise sages of Apeiron, safeguarded by the 6s and entrusted only to believers who brave Apeiron's test.

**888**：它有着调和与节制的力量，在你参悟无限定者分享的奥秘之前，你可以一直保有它。\
**888**: It has the power of harmonization and reconciliation. You may keep it until you've fully grasped the secrets shared with you by Apeiron.

**888**：——但你不应将它分享给一个附属于人类的外部组织。\
**888**: But you will not share it with some organization affiliated with humans, and certainly do not allow them to study it.

不可避免的分歧终究还是发生了。\
The inevitable disagreement is finally upon them.

888几乎是将37拉离了洞穴研究室。\
888 grabs 37 by the arm and drags her out of the lab.

**37**：——为什么呢？\
**37**: Why?

**37**：我们开设传道会，接待岛外的访客，正是为了分享知识和智慧，让真理的光辉为世人所见，不是吗？\
**37**: Sharing the scroll is sharing wisdom and knowledge with others, like what we have done through our doctrinal meetings and receiving visitors from the outside world. It is for the sake of spreading the light of Truth, is it not?

**37**：人类的研究者……他们也发明过很多优美的数学定理。\
**37**: The human researchers, they have also discovered many brilliant theorems.

**37**：在“流溢”把这儿和外界隔开前，我们也有过这样的交流。那很有趣，比后来发生的事有趣得多。\
**37**: Before the "Emanation" cut us off, we had these types of communications with the outside world. It was fun, unlike what came after.

**37**：我笃定这次分享，能够帮助我们解明无限定者的数字密码。\
**37**: I'm sure by sharing this scroll, the code from Apeiron will be deciphered.

**37**：我必须证明真理的辉光仍是存在的——！\
**37**: I must prove that the light of Truth still glimmers!

女孩摇了摇头，固执地不肯却步。\
She stands her ground.

她的提议是正确的。经历了信仰的崩溃后，人们亟需新的希望和道标。\
She is right. With their faith shattered, people need something new to keep them going.

甚至在向来被忽略的实用性上，她的坚持也无可厚非。\
And this time, her suggestion makes sense in a practical way—a quality often missing from her previous ideas.

既有的庇佑不再稳定，其他越过“流溢”的手段能够稳固人心，虚弱的学派也正需要一个盟友。\
With the island no longer shielding them, the school must find another way to survive the "Emanation." In their moment of weakness, they need a powerful ally more than ever.

**888**：——可你能确定，这个卷轴只是被用于交流和学习吗？\
**888**: But how can you be sure the scroll will only be used for researching the ritual?

**888**：你能保证，它不会被人类用于武器设计和制造吗？\
**888**: How can you ensure that the humans won't exploit it to create weapons of destruction?

**37**：……？！\
**37**: ...?!

协理人抬起头，望向穹顶上那个炮弹所致的巨大缺口。\
The Custodian looks up at the fractured dome.

斑斓的阴影覆盖在报丧女妖的脸上。\
The speckled daylight illuminates her cool complexion.

**888**：在加入阿派朗学派前，我和我的族人已在世上流浪了许久。我的族群比一般人更加长寿，也因而更加不容于世俗。\
**888**: Before joining the School of Apeiron, my people and I had wandered the world for ages. Our long lives made it difficult for us to truly fit in with the world.

**888**：真理的女儿，请你聆听我作为一个老人的意见。\
**888**: Daughter of Truth, I implore you to hear the words of this old soul.

**888**：人类确实创造过美好的成果，那份启蒙的辉光也曾将我打动。\
**888**: Humans have indeed achieved incredible feats, and their enlightenment has even touched my soul.

**888**：但遗憾的是，并非人人都如此。更多的人类缺失了对知识与限度的敬畏，只会盲从于力量的追求。\
**888**: But unfortunately, most humans do not have an inherent respect for knowledge or its boundaries. They only chase after power blindly.

**888**：我经历过、劝说过、厌倦过，因此，我来到这里。\
**888**: I have experienced it firsthand. I tried to guide and persuade them, but ultimately, I failed. That is why I am here now.

**37**：……\
**37**: ...

**888**：你分享的不仅仅是知识，它是一个仪式，是一份力量。\
**888**: What you're deciding to share is not only knowledge, but it is a ritual, a piece of power.

**888**：它为调和而生，为那些心怀虔诚的崇敬者而生，为了那些在神庙前匍匐祈求的贤者而生。\
**888**: A ritual designed for harmonization, created for the devout believers, and created for the sages seeking the Truth.

**888**：可它也能被反过来利用，成为手枪上的消声器、机枪上的制退器、氢弹里的反应公式，服务于更残酷的暴行。\
**888**: Yet, on the other hand, it can also be used for unspeakable horrors, such as silencers on guns, suppressors on rifles, or even on nuclear bombs.

**维尔汀**：……不！\
**Vertin**: It won't!

**维尔汀**：888女士，我不会让那种事发生的。我向您保证。\
**Vertin**: 888, I won't let this happen. I promise.

**888**：您不能保证，维尔汀小姐，因为您也只是一个孩子。\
**888**: You can't promise anything, Ms. Vertin. You are too young.

**888**：你对历史的恶性一无所知。\
**888**: Too inexperienced to comprehend the dark nature of history.

掷地有声的指责。\
A valid and powerful observation.

在这个刚被炮火焚毁的殿堂中，任何辩驳都显得苍白无力。\
The hall itself, ravaged by war, now stands as a testament to the banshee's claim.

就连37也沉默了。\
Even 37 is speechless.

**210**：——可是，那是真理啊。还有什么比这更重要呢？\
**210**: But it's the Truth we're talking about. What could possibly outweigh the Truth?

一个意外的声音响了起来。\
An unexpected voice speaks up.

极为罕见的，修辞学家这次并未提出反对。\
To everyone's surprise, the rhetorician does not raise any objections this time.

**210**：假如借出一个卷轴，就能帮助我们触及到那不可说的隐秘——那为什么不这样做呢？\
**210**: If all it takes is lending someone a scroll to unlock unspeakable secrets, why not do it?

**210**：过去四年的失败，难道还不足以证明，真理的辉光并不会存在于固步自封之中？\
**210**: Haven't the failures of the past four years proven that a stagnant mindset does not bring forth the light of Truth?

**210**：对于将毕生奉献予沉思的人来说，对真理的热爱永远是第一位的，因为这是我们在这个世界上唯一值得过的生活。\
**210**: As individuals devoted to critical thinking, should the pursuit of Truth not be our primary goal in life?

**210**：不要为仇恨而丧失前进的勇气，我的兄弟姐妹们。不要让现象世界的尘埃蒙蔽你们的心智。\
**210**: My brothers and sisters, do not let hatred stop you, and don't let the dust of the phenomenal world blind you.

**37**：210……\
**37**: 210.

210摆摆手，从残垣上站起。\
He waves his hand and gets up from his seat.

**210**：而且，那是她通过的试炼，那是她获得的卷轴。她有权处置。这是她的天赋，也是她的责任。\
**210**: And remember, it was 37 who passed the test and earned the scroll. It is her rightful responsibility to handle this situation.

他看向别处，神态比起真心支持，更像是漫不经心。\
He looks elsewhere, his demeanor suggesting a lack of interest rather than genuine support for the argument.

**210**：——我们又有什么更好的选择吗？\
**210**: Otherwise, what other choice do we have?

他挥了挥手，走出了满目疮痍的庇护所。\
He shrugs and walks out of the hall.

而赫尔墨斯之星坚定了自己的决心。\
Behind him, the Star of Hermes clenches her fist with resolve.

迎着信仰者们态度各异的目光，她声音清亮地开口了。\
To the murmuring, doubting crowd, she speaks again, loud and clear.

**37**：……我不会改变我之前的想法。\
**37**: I have made up my mind.

**37**：我会分享这个卷轴，和科算中心合作，解开无限定者留下的数字密码。\
**37**: I will share this scroll with Laplace. We will decipher the code together.

**37**：真理就是真理，它不应当为其它而转移。\
**37**: The Truth is the Truth. It should not be swayed by anything else.

**37**：诸位，如果你们也同意，便投下手中的卵石吧！如果是6来主持，他也会做出民主的决断。\
**37**: Please, everyone, cast your pebble if you agree with me! If 6 were here, he too would have called for a vote.

一些人径直离去了，但更多幸存者们投下了手里的卵石。\
Some of them decide to leave the hall instead, but most stay and use the pebbles in their hands to speak for them.

她赢下了这场政事表决，还有一声叹息。\
Her victory arrives with a gentle sigh from the corner.

**888**：……唉。\
**888**: *sigh*

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本-轰炸后\
War and smoke have long left this place.

战火和硝烟已经远去了。\
An area has been cleared for takeoff.

留下一片正适合起飞的空地。

**十四行诗**：……红弩箭小姐，你确定没有问题吗？\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Lilya, are you certain about this?

**红弩箭**：哈，能有什么问题？现在的天气可比我们登岛那天好多了。\
**Lilya**: Absolutely. See the nice weather today? Much better than the day we landed.

**红弩箭**：无风，晴朗，一览无余——天空中甚至还有一个巨大的月亮！\
**Lilya**: No wind, no cloud, the clear sky, and that giant moon!

红弩箭跨坐在Su-01ве上，拍了拍腰间的卷轴。\
Sitting tight on her Su-01ве, she gives a quick pat to the scroll secured on her belt.

那是学派奉献的核心。\
This is the essence of Apeiron's goodwill, in their newfound alliance with Laplace.

**红弩箭**：不过是向总部配送一个包裹，甚至还没出欧洲，三个小时绰绰有余。\
**Lilya**: Can't find a better day to deliver the package. It's just to the headquarters, not even going outside of Europe. Three hours is more than enough.

**红弩箭**：自从上了岛，各种憋屈的事情就没停过，我可是等这个兜风机会很久了！\
**Lilya**: I'm done being stuck on this suffocating island. Nobody can stop me from taking this flight!

**十四行诗**：但是这里离总部至少有768海里！而且，在无防护的情况下长距离飞行是很危险的。\
**Sonetto**: The headquarters are at least 768 nautical miles away, and you have no protection during the long flight. It's dangerous!

**十四行诗**：——距离“暴雨”落下只有7个小时了。\
**Sonetto**: And we have only seven hours until the "Storm."

**红弩箭**：嗯，不错，是很危险。但这可是在“暴雨”中飞行768海里啊，十四行诗。这绝对是让他们修订《飞行手册》的大好时机！\
**Lilya**: Dangerous? Maybe. But this is an exhilarating flight in the "Storm," Sonetto! What better chance than now to push Zeno into updating their Flying Manual?

红弩箭掏出军用水壶，猛地朝嘴里灌了几口，接着，兴致勃勃地启动了扫帚——仿佛要去参加一场狂欢。\
She takes a few long gulps from her canteen and warms up her broomstick, brimming with anticipation as if she were going to a carnival.

**红弩箭**：再说，沾染一小块油画也不算太坏——省去了买纪念章的工夫。\
**Lilya**: Besides, what's wrong with a bit of oil painting on me? Should be a nice badge of honor.

**星锑**：老天，你可别一头栽进地中海里啊！\
**Regulus**: Mate, that's quite a distance. Just be sure not to go toppling into the Mediterranean Sea!

**红弩箭**：哈，红色38可不是APPLeⅡ号！\
**Lilya**: Heheheh, Red 38 is no way an APPLe II!

扫帚急促升空，星锑变得愈来愈小，很快便缩减为一个简略的红色符号。\
She soars higher and higher until Regulus shrinks to a tiny red dot on the beach.

飞行女巫同时也注意到了附近袭来的黑影。\
From the corner of her eye, she notices shadows slowly creeping toward her.

**红弩箭**：噢哦，这是重塑之手的奥利图欧……？看来先前的清扫工作不太彻底。\
**Lilya**: Uh-oh, Manus Olitiaus? We didn't kill them all off?

**红弩箭**：——可怜的小傻瓜，可别指望我会把时间浪费在你们身上。\
**Lilya**: I don't have time for you, little stingray rats.

扫帚调转了方向，猛地提高了速度。\
The Olitiaus trail close behind her.

奥利图欧群也不倦地紧随其后。

**红弩箭**：速度不错。看来老板的死亡对你们没太大影响，是吗？\
**Lilya**: Still got your speed, huh? I guess the death of your boss didn't faze you much.

**红弩箭**：噢……？\
**Lilya**: Oh?

浸润紫色液体的充气式飞空艇缓缓出现在了前方，鼓动的气囊如同一颗跃动的心脏。\
A swollen blimp comes into view, filled with a dark substance and throbbing like a beating heart.

然后，它柔软的炮口自动调转，像生物的触角一样锁定了飞行女巫。\
The creature's soft, tentacle-like turrets slowly rise and lock onto Lilya.

**红弩箭**：重塑之手的“飞艇”？这倒是个有意思的对手。\
**Lilya**: A Manus aircraft? Worth a fight.

再次加速。

**红弩箭**：哈哈……来试试看吧。正好能用你的爆炸在地中海上奏响一发二十一响礼花！\
**Lilya**: Haha, bring it on! Your downfall will be an explosive orchestra over the waters!

要安全地使用免疫术式，一共需要两步。\
To safely cast the immunity ritual, two conditions must be met.

a.达到施术条件。\
(1) have the power to wield it

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-破译房间。

**X**: This is an unprecedented chance to rob the "Storm" of its energy. I wouldn't miss this for anything.

b.减少副作用。\
(2) minimize the side effects

剧情场景-露西女士的办公室-开灯版本

**露西**：阿派朗学派的卷轴在这一点上已经表现出了非凡的潜力，它应当能发挥比柯尔曼防护术式更良好的防护效果。\
**Lucy**: The scroll of Apeiron has shown great potential in protecting casters from the ritual. It is expected to outperform the Coleman protection rituals.

**露西**：副作用种类的繁多是一个问题——不过我们已经有了一张记录122种诅咒特性的列表。一旦卷轴送到，我们只需逐一拟合它对每个条目的应对效果。\
**Lucy**: The sheer variety of side effects is concerning, but we already have a list of 122 curses and their effects. Once the scroll arrives, we will test and record its reactions to each of the effects.

**露西**：这将大大加快我们的解析进程。\
**Lucy**: This should speed up our analysis considerably.

但理应还有第三步。\
But this isn't enough.

剧情场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-哑谜的办公室

**哑谜**：……怎样让人类也能使用这个术式？\
**Enigma**: How can we get humans to make use of this ritual?

哑谜站了起来，在拥挤的书柜与杂物之间来回踱步。\
He stands up and paces around the cluttered room.

**Enigma**: Ideally, the incantation is made into a tool like the Manus mask, or Laplace's incantation soft disk.Enigma: However, this would require a thorough analysis and mastery of the ritual! The side effects are extremely deadly.The chief assistant explains to her reassuringly.Finally, someone speaks again.Cryptography Lead: Apologies. There's no time for details.Annoyed, he interrupts his rambling and gets straight to the point.Cryptography Lead: Anyway, Timekeeper, we'll need the help of that lady—Ms. Radio, right?Ms. Radio: Huh?!Flattered, the blue flower on Ms. Radio perks up.No ordinary signal could reach this island. Since their arrival, she's been diligently managing their communications.As a result, she was somewhat reduced to being just a radio.Cryptography Lead: Yes, somebody, please find her a metal square plate, fix it on a sturdy base, and pour sand on it. Sonetto and Regulus get to work immediately.Fortunately, there's no shortage of metals and sand on the island. A makeshift receiving station is quickly built.Cryptography Lead: Now, a special recording will be sent to you. Please stay by the edge of the plate, embrace the sound and, um, uh, groove along.Ms. Radio: I assume you mean "vibrate"?Cryptography Lead: No no no no no, that's just rude ... but uh, yes, exactly.He stammers.Cryptography Lead: If all goes well, the vibrations will move the sand and visualize the text in a pattern.Cryptography Lead: We have 12 recordings ready, each representing a letter in the incantation. We'll play the first one when you're ready.Ms. Radio: O-of course, my pleasure!She trembles with excitement, ready to give her all for this important task.As she grooves with the signal, a pattern begins to form on the plate.Vertin: First one's done, Mr. Ulrich.Cryptography Lead: Alright, 11 to go.The transmission continues as planned, each letter falling into place like pieces of a puzzle.Until finally, the last letter is recorded on the page.Vertin: ...!Vertin: This incantation ...The sight is hard to believe.How can this be?Regulus: W-what? Are you reading it in your head?Regulus: Ah! Mother?A myriad of thoughts flood the mind.Vertin: 37, I think I know what it says.Vertin: It means "the first circle."

**哑谜**：但它的前提是对咒语的彻底解析和掌握！重塑之手可以，因为阿尔卡纳就是那样卓越的施术者。

剧情场景-洞穴研究室-1.9差分版本，进行一些改装

**37**：喔，所以这就是虚数们的计划。

洞穴研究室内，37饶有兴致地思索着。

与科算中心的合作顺利进行着——双方刚刚完成了研究进度的交换。

**维尔汀**：是的，37，你有什么想法吗？

**37**：一点也不优美，充满了生搬硬凑和投机取巧。纯粹只是为了应用，没有任何理论的优美性，就像虚数。

**星锑**：什么？我觉得这计划还挺酷的！

37摇摇头，不动声色地把自己的坐垫往星锑的反方向挪了挪。

37期盼地望向通讯设备，电波那头，破译组长已经沉寂了好一阵。

**十四行诗**：科算中心正在寻找安全传递咒文的方法，鉴于之前的传播事故，审批也需要一点时间。

第一助手尽心地为此刻的等待解释着。

终于，电波那头传来了回音。

**破译组长**：抱歉，我们花了一些时间来测试传递方法。

**破译组长**：另外，为了保障诸位的安全，我们本次只会传输咒语的文本。具体的念法，我们会在稍后单独传递给司辰。

**星锑**：——呼，真是多谢你了，伙计。

**破译组长**：考虑到小岛缺乏可视化的通讯手段，我们决定用克拉尼共振法来单独传递每个字母。那是科算中心之前研发的一种将简单图形转换为声波的技术——

**破译组长**：见鬼，跳过这部分吧，现在可没有介绍技术原理的工夫。

磁流体暴躁地打断了自己，它那边听起来也是一片混乱。

**破译组长**：总之，司辰，我们需要借助您身边那位女士的帮助——无线电小姐，是吗？

**无线电小姐**：唔？！

无线电小姐受宠若惊地抬起了蓝色小花。

这座岛屿隔绝了除她之外的一切电波信号，因而这位意识唤醒者自登岛以来，便一直担任着沟通内外的桥梁工作。

——也让她在极大程度上沦为了一台真正的收音机。

**破译组长**：是的，请您先找一块方形的金属薄片，将它固定在坚实的底座上，并在上面撒上薄薄的细沙。

十四行诗和星锑立刻行动了起来。

好消息是，岛上四处都是几何状的金属和沙子。一个临时的实验台很快搭了起来。

**破译组长**：随后，我们会发送给您一段特殊的录音。您需要感受它的声波，并随它在薄板边缘——呃，起舞。

**无线电小姐**：我猜您想说的是，振动？

**破译组长**：不不，这太失礼了，我怎么能对一位女士说“振动”——但好吧，就是这个意思。

磁流体的声音听起来有一丝自暴自弃。

**破译组长**：如果顺利的话，驻波将在沙子上形成一个图形，那即是我们要传递的咒文。

**破译组长**：我们总共会发送12段录音，每段录音对应着咒文的一个字母。等您准备好，我们就先尝试第一个。

**无线电小姐**：当，当然，我很荣幸——！

蓝色小花因激动而震颤着，她已准备为这神圣的使命全力以赴。

伴随着她悬浮的舞步，金属板上出现了第一个图形。

**维尔汀**：……我记录下来了，乌尔里希先生。

**破译组长**：好的，接下来还有11段——

传输有序进行，免疫“暴雨”的咒文通过这种方式来到了电波彼端。

最终，最后一个字母也付诸纸上。

**维尔汀**：——！

**维尔汀**：这个咒文……！

难以相信眼前所见。

怎么会这样？

**星锑**：怎、怎么了，维尔汀，你不会在心里默念了吧？

**星锑**：你不会要告诉我，默念也会招致诅咒吧……？

**维尔汀**：不，只是……

**维尔汀**：我认识这种语言。

La unua cirklo.

是的，它并不陌生，开启箱子的咒文也是用这种语言写就。

唯一的问题是，是谁、在何时教授了它？

是在那个一片空白的千禧年夜晚吗？

是……母亲吗？

摇摇头，令心绪平复。

**维尔汀**：……37，我想我现在理解它了。

**维尔汀**：——这条咒语的意思是“最初的圆”。

## 7TH-25 最初的圆 / The First Circle

剧场场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-露西的实验室-开灯版本\
The researchers on the receiving end quickly grasp the message.

电流那头的研究员们也在第一时间听到了这个惊愕的信息。

**破译组长**：最初的圆……？您是说，这句咒语……是这个意思？\
**Cryptography Lead**: "The first circle"? That's what the incantation says?

磁流体立刻意识到了，有一个一直被遗漏的信息。\
He suddenly remembers a detail that has eluded him all along.

**破译组长**：天啊，维也纳调查员的确汇报过相关的内容！“一个古老的奇迹，一个拯救的魔圈。”\
**Cryptography Lead**: That's it! The investigator in Vienna reported a similar thing! "An ancient miracle, a circle of salvation."

**破译组长**：——阿尔卡纳当时在空气中画的正是一个圆！如此随意，好像只是闲谈中一个随手而为的手势。\
**Cryptography Lead**: Arcana even drew a circle in the air while saying it. She did it so nonchalantly, as if it were a meaningless gesture.

**破译组长**：而我们被咒文和诅咒吸引了全部注意力，在确认这个手势并不对施术产生影响后，就没有再追究这一点。\
**Cryptography Lead**: We didn't think much of it at the time. Once we confirmed that it did not affect the casting of the incantation, we forgot about it and moved on.

**破译组长**：……我竟然忽略了这么重要的信息！\
**Cryptography Lead**: I can't believe I overlooked it!

急性子的组长给了桌子重重一拳，又用双手悲痛地捂住了自己的脸。\
The hot-tempered cryptography lead slams the table and buries his face into his hands, clearly exasperated.

**露西**：这并不是你的责任，乌尔里希组长。\
**Lucy**: This is not your fault, Ulrich.

**露西**：这条信息在先前被忽略，是因为它对研究没有实际帮助。我们所有应用导向的研究，都不涉及对咒文的理解。\
**Lucy**: The gesture was overlooked because it did not really help the research. Our focus was on practical application rather than understanding the incantation itself.

**露西**：如果这条咒文的原意是“最初的圆”……\
**Lucy**: If the incantation means "the first circle" ...

实用主义者的声音依然冷静。\
The pragmatist's voice is still serene.

**露西**：——那它对研究又意味着什么？\
**Lucy**: How will this be helpful to the research?

**37**：……我明白了，原来是这样！\
**37**: I see! I understand now!

剧情场景-洞穴研究室-1.9差分版本，进行一些改装\
A moment of epiphany.

赫尔墨斯之星发出了惊呼。

她快速地抓过了几张演算纸，全神贯注趴在地上写画起来。\
She snatches a handful of papers, sprawls out on the floor, and scribbles frantically.

**星锑**：唔，维尔汀，我不知道你是怎么看懂的这份咒文，但我知道，你这句话一定会让这家伙十分得意……\
**Regulus**: Well, Vertin, I don't know why you can read it, but I do know that gal is thrilled by your interpretation.

**星锑**：因为这是她最喜欢的圆。\
**Regulus**: Because you mentioned her favorite shape, the circle.

无理数的判断颇具道理，质数已经完全沉浸在了畅想之中。\
The irrational number is spot on. 37 has drifted into a world of her own.

**37**：对了，是这样，这份咒文的本质就是一个圆……！\
**37**: Yes, yes! The essence of the incantation is a circle!

**37**：可是，它是哪一种圆呢？在拓扑上，只要是封闭的平面曲线，都算得上是一个圆……\
**37**: But what kind of circle is it? In topology, any closed curve on a plane can be classified as a circle.

**星锑**：——啊哈，我说什么来着？\
**Regulus**: Aha. Told you!

星锑摊开了手，无言地给37腾出了一些地面的空间。\
Regulus spreads her hands, speechless. She takes a step back, giving 37 more room to calculate.

没有人再打扰她，无线电小姐甚至贴心将自己的音量也调低了些。\
Everyone is talking quietly so as not to disturb her, even Ms. Radio has lowered her volume.

在研究室的地面将被演算纸摊满前，她终于站了起来。\
Just as her sheets are about to engulf the entire floor, she finally stands up.

**37**：看，维尔汀，回到我们最开始的罗塞塔石碑假说。\
**37**: Look, Vertin, let's go back to the Rosetta Stone hypothesis.

**37**：这个假说的基本内容是，这个咒文和数字密码指向的本质是相通的，都是免疫“流溢”的办法。\
**37**: Based on the hypothesis, if the incantation and the numerical code share a common essence, which is the key to the "Storm" immunity,

**37**：而现在我们知道，咒文的本质是一个圆。\
**37**: and we now know the incantation refers to a circle ...

**维尔汀**：……那么，这串数字密码的本质，也是一个“圆”？\
**Vertin**: Then, the essence of this numerical code should also be a "circle," right?

37点了点头。\
37 nods.

**37**：在和你们交流之前，我对数字密码并没有方向判断，它可能是一段咒语，也可能是一个优美的几何术阵……\
**37**: Yes. Before this conversation, I had no idea which direction to take. The numerical code could be a snippet of an incantation, or it could be a geometrical ritual array.

**37**：我可以构想出很多假说，但一一验证它们需要大量的时间，我估计是几个星期或者几个月。万一我的假设全是错误的，那就会白白浪费数十年……\
