**37**: I had a lot of theories to go on, but testing them could take weeks or even months. Worse yet, if my line of thinking was completely wrong, we could waste decades of time and effort.

**37**：可你们的石碑假说却是很好印证的，我们现在就可以用假设法来验证这一点！\
**37**: But the Rosetta Stone hypothesis is easy to verify!

**37**：我们的假设是，咒文和数字密码的本质相通。\
**37**: Let us suppose that the incantation and numerical code share a similar essence.

**37**：我们的已知条件是，咒文是有效的，意识唤醒者们已经切实印证了这一点。\
**37**: We know that the incantation does work, as proven by the Awakened.

**37**：那么，如果咒文是一个圆，数字密码也理应是一个圆，且这个圆的作用和咒文等同。\
**37**: If the incantation is a circle, then the numerical code should also be circular in nature, and has the same effect as the incantation,

**37**：它应当是一个拥有免疫“流溢”效用的圆，可以同样被意识唤醒者们用实验印证。\
**37**: which is, a circle that saves people from the "Emanation," and can also be experimented with by the Awakened.

**维尔汀**：……如果实验成功，则假说成立。如果实验失败，则假说推翻。\
**Vertin**: If the experiment works, then the hypothesis is true. And vice versa.

**维尔汀**：我明白你的意思了，37，这的确是一个可被快速印证的假说。\
**Vertin**: I see what you mean here. It really is an easily provable hypothesis.

**星锑**：而我明白的是，你只是想要证明那串数字密码也是圆，因为你喜欢它！\
**Regulus**: To my ears, you're just trying to prove that the code means a circle, because you're really into circles!

**37**：唔！我并没有特别喜欢圆，只是因为它是一个很好的图形……\
**37**: Umm, not specifically. I simply like it because it's a great shape.

**十四行诗**：可是，我不明白。\
**Sonetto**: But, I don't understand.

十四行诗拿起那张写着数字密码的纸张，认真思忖了起来。\
She picks up the numerical code and studies it carefully.

**十四行诗**：+1、-1、+2、-3、3、-3、+2、-1、+1……\
**Sonetto**: +1, -1, +2, -3, 3, -3, +2, -1, +1 …

**十四行诗**：这串数字和“圆”又有什么联系呢？\
**Sonetto**: How do these numbers relate to the "circle"?

**哑谜**：——“最初的圆”？\
**Enigma**: "The first circle"?

剧场场景-拉普拉斯科算中心-破译房间\
Enigma narrows his brows, spinning a pen between his fingers.

哑谜皱着眉头，在书山背后转着笔。\
His drafts are scattered across his desk, each of them a dead end.

他那无望的研究草案铺满了整个桌面。

**破译员Ⅴ**：是的，司辰对咒文的语义给予了这样的回答。\
**Cryptographer V**: Yes, it was the Timekeeper who translated the incantation.

**破译员Ⅴ**：据维也纳调查员传回的情报，阿尔卡纳施术时的手势也是一个圆。\
**Cryptographer V**: And according to the investigator in Vienna, Arcana also drew a circle when she cast the ritual.

**破译员Ⅴ**：但根据实验，手势的添加对于术式使用毫无影响，这一发现疑似只是象征上的表达……\
**Cryptographer V**: But experiments have shown that the gesture has no effect on the ritual. We thought, maybe it was a symbolic gesture.

**哑谜**：不不不，这绝对不是简单的象征！\
**Enigma**: No no no! It is no way just symbolic!

哑谜猛地站了起来，扬起的灰尘令对面的破译员也打了个喷嚏。\
He jumps to his feet. The cryptographer sneezes at the cloud of dust he just stirred up.

**哑谜**：就思维习惯而言，神秘学家正是自动将经验转换为象征的种族。\
**Enigma**: Arcanists excel at condensing their experiences into symbolic representations.

**哑谜**：元素、符号、图腾，这些正是最初的象征，也是神秘术的力量来源之一——如果基金会撰写的通识教材没有骗我！\
**Enigma**: Signs, totems, elements, these are primitive symbols, and some are sources of power for arcanum. At least that's what the Foundation's textbooks tell me!

**哑谜**：这就是为什么象征符合的媒介物才能增幅神秘术的效用，我们甚至得使用不同材质的软盘去储存实体化的咒文……\
**Enigma**: That's why arcane skills can only be enhanced by mediums that align with their symbolic nature. Precise materials are required when creating soft disks for each incantation.

转笔的手突然停了下来。\
He stops spinning his pen.

**哑谜**：如果这个咒文象征的正是“最初的圆”……\
**Enigma**: If the incantation symbolizes "the first circle,"

**哑谜**：那么，假如我们要将它实体化，以供所有人使用……\
**Enigma**: and if we were to create a physical form that could be mass-produced for everyone,

**哑谜**：……它也会是一个圆形吗？\
**Enigma**: will that form have to be a circle, too?

剧情场景-洞穴研究室-1.9差分版本，进行一些改装

关于圆的研究如火如荼地进行着。\
In the cave, discussions and theories about the circle are also in full swing.

洞穴实验室的地板上已经铺满了纸张。\
Every inch of the floor is now covered with paper.

每一张上都画着一个不同形态的圆。立体的、交叠的、扭曲的……\
On each sheet is a differently drawn circle. Some are spheres, some have crossings, some are in distorted forms ...

就在这片汪洋大海将所有人淹没之前，她终于站了起来。\
Just as the sea of papers is about to drown everyone in the room, she finally stands up.

**37**：——噢，我应该早点想到的！\
**37**: Oh! I should have thought of this!

**37**：在最简单的事物中蕴含了最深刻的道理，从来如此。它已经介绍过自己了，“最初的圆”。\
**37**: The simplest things often hold the deepest meaning, as always. So, "the first circle" ...

**37**：那么，它是什么？是轮子？是绳子？是钟摆？\
**37**: What could it be? A wheel? A piece of rope? A pendulum?

37摇了摇头，踢翻了几张圆形之海的碎屑。\
37 shakes her head and kicks away some paper balls at her feet.

**37**：我在轮子和轴承那里耽误了太多时间，忽略了更有潜力的那个选择——圆也是一种绳结，它是交叉点为0的平凡结【unknot】。\
**37**: I spent too long on the wheel and the bearing, not realizing there was something more promising: a circle can also be seen as a knot with no crossings—an unknot.

**37**：这很可能是一个封闭曲线的变形，一个扭结【knot】。人们自古以来就用这种方式记录信息，就像印加人和中国人在绳子上打结。\
**37**: This could be a variation of a closed curve, a knot. Knots were how the ancients of the Incas and Chinese collected data and kept records.

**37**：但它又是哪一种结呢？\
**37**: But which knot is it exactly?

37伸出手，伴随着神秘术的辉光，优美的几何图形自她的指尖迸发。\
37 extends her hand, intricate geometric shapes take form in the radiance of her arcane light.

**37**：三叶结的琼斯多项式是t+t3-t4。\
**37**: The Jones polynomial of the trefoil knot is t+t3-t4.

**37**：八字结是t-2-t-1+1-t+t2……\
**37**: The figure-eight knot is t-2-t-1+1-t+t2 …

**37**：梅花结是t2+t4-t5+t6-t7……\
**37**: While the Cinquefoil knot, t2+t4-t5+t6-t7 …

**37**：这样的绳结，多少我都可以数出来。在交叉点达到10时，可能的扭结组合已经高达165种，交叉点达到13时，更是多达9988种……\
**37**: I could go on all day. There are 165 different knots with 10 crossings, 9988 knots with 13 crossings ...

**37**：——可是数字密码对应的又是哪一个呢？\
**37**: But which knot is the code referring to?

**37**：+1-1+2-3+3-3+2-1+1……\
**37**: +1-1+2-3+3-3+2-1+1 …

喃喃自语的脚步突然止住了。\
She stops.

**37**：这就是为什么我听到的是这串数字，不是吗？\
**37**: Of course. Of course, I would hear these digits instead of anything else.

**37**：6的卷轴将这个真理以我可以理解的形式转译了，因此它一定是对应着我知晓的数学体系。\
**37**: The scroll transcribes the Truth into a format I can understand, so it must be based on a mathematical system I already know.

**37**：我已经预先拥有了解开密码的一切知识，只需遵循直觉将它们挑选出来。\
**37**: I have all the knowledge needed to break the code, just need to follow my instincts and pick a system.

**37**：——而我在第一时间想到正是琼斯多项式！\
**37**: And the Jones polynomial is the first thing I could think of!

不可见的灵光在脑中划过，女孩迅速趴在地上写画起来。\
Struck by an idea, she drops to her knees and starts calculating again on the floor.

**37**：对了，我在洞穴听到的第二个3，与另外两个3的发音并不一样……它是中央区的常数项！\
**37**: Right. The second 3 I heard sounded different from the other 3s. That 3 must be the constant term of the polynomial!

**37**：那么，和数轴一样，它的右边是正方幂各项的系数，左边是负方幂各项的系数……\
**37**: Then, if we use this 3 as the origin, like a number axis, the left side is the coefficients for the negative exponents, and the right side is the coefficients for the positive exponents.

**37**：这就对了！这串数字是琼斯多项式的缩写，它可以被展开为t-4-t-3+2t-2-3t-1+3-3t+2t2-t3+t4……一个交叉点为8的扭结！\
**37**: Eureka! This string of coefficients is the shorthand of a Jones polynomial! If we assign the 8 coefficients to the 8 corresponding exponents in a Jones polynomial, we get its true form: t-4-t-3+2t-2-3t-1+3-3t+2t2-t3+t4 … A knot with 8 crossings!

她抬起头来，碧色的眼睛里盈满了笑意。\
She looks up, her bright aquamarine eyes shine with delight.

一个金色的绳圈从她的指尖溢出。\
A golden knot projects from her fingertips.

**37**：看，维尔汀，无限定者确实给了我们答案。\
**37**: See, Vertin, Apeiron did give us the answer.

**37**：这就是我们找寻的东西，最深层的隐秘，献给神明的语言。\
**37**: The key we've been looking for, the most profound secret, the language of the divine.

**37**：不需要任何声音，不需要任何文字，最纯粹的构造，最本质的形式。\
**37**: No sound or text is needed, just pure structure. The very form of the essence itself.

**37**：——一个优美的图形，一个简易的绳结！\
**37**: It is a beautiful shape, a simple knot!

**维尔汀**：扭结……\
**Vertin**: A knot ...

**维尔汀**：很好，那接下来就只剩验证环节了。\
**Vertin**: Great. Now there is only one step left: the verification.

点点头，目光望向通讯设备的彼端。\
She nods and looks at the communicator.

**维尔汀**：——您还在那边吗，露西女士？能请您帮忙验证扭结作为术式的有效性吗？\
**Vertin**: Did you hear that, Madam Lucy? Can you help us verify the authenticity of this knot?

紧张的沉寂后，无线电小姐终于想起来这是因为自己调低了音量旋钮。\
After an unsettling silence, Ms. Radio finally remembers that she has turned down the volume.

她连忙放大了音量，于是总负责人平静的声音从电波那头传了过来。\
When she turns it back on, Lucy's voice comes through clearly over the channel.

**露西**：当然，我一直在聆听诸位的研究进展。\
**Lucy**: Of course. I have paid close attention to the discussion.

**露西**：这个公式对应的扭结是唯一的，现在即可进行它作为术式的实验。\
**Lucy**: This polynomial produces a single, unique knot. We can now tie a knot to test it.

通讯那头再次沉寂了下去。\
The call goes silent again.

研究室内亦没有人说话，似乎任何声响都会打断空气中思维的交锋，就连唱片骑师也关闭了自己的随身音响。\
The cave is silent too, as if any noise would alter the outcome. Even Regulus has turned off her personal speakers.

无线电小姐再度放大了通讯线路的音量，但里面传出的只有微末的电流声。\
In the quiet hush, Ms. Radio cranks up her volume once more, but all they hear is a sharp hiss of static.

以及极其细微的沙沙声。\
And a soft, strange rustling.

指针示意已经过去了二十分钟。\
Twenty minutes have passed.

**维尔汀**：……露西女士？\
**Vertin**: Madam Lucy?

传来的只有窸窸窣窣的回应，夹杂着某些像颤栗的砂砾般的回音。\
The only sound is a constant static, accompanied by a faint, scratchy reverberation.

**维尔汀**：难道是无线电波出现了问题……\
**Vertin**: Is the signal dropping?

**维尔汀**：——露西女士，请问您还能收到我们这里的信号吗？\
**Vertin**: Madam Lucy, can you hear us?

**露西**：……\
**Lucy**: ...

**露西**：是……的……\
**Lucy**: I ... can ...

电波彼端，机器正吃力而平静地组织着语言。\
The robot utters with effort.

绳结从她的手中轻轻滑落到实验桌上。它在微小的生命历程里完成了最伟大的使命。\
The knot slips from her grip and falls. It has completed its great mission.

而后，金属开始粉碎，溶解。\
Then the robot starts to fall apart and melt.

在诅咒蔓延到核心前，盗火者露出了一个微笑。\
Before the curse could get to her core, the fire thief flashes a smile.

接下来这句话，她无论如何也要清晰地传达给无线电的另一端。\
She needs to ensure the next message is clear on the radio.

**露西**：——我们成功了。\
**Lucy**: It ... worked.

## 7TH-26 银镜与纱幕 / Mirror and Curtains

**哑谜**：……没想到，最终是司辰和阿派朗学派的神秘学家，找到了让人类参与施术的方法。\
**Enigma**: I never thought it would be the Timekeeper and the Apeiron arcanists who'd solve the problem. But now, even humans can cast this ritual.

科算中心陷入了难得的静谧，研究员们已经尽了自己能尽的义务。\
Laplace is now in a rare state of tranquility, for the researchers have done all they can; there's nothing left for them to do.

距离“暴雨”落下还有约4个小时，这是风暴前的短暂宁静。\
With only 4 hours to go, this is the final calm before the "Storm."

**露西**：噢，是的，扭结正是我们要寻找的实体化术式，学派的数字密码带来了意想不到的应用收获。\
**Lucy**: Indeed. The knot is the physical form of the ritual we were looking for. Surprisingly, the numerical code yielded practical results.

**露西**：我认为有必要向司辰所属的机构汇报她们取得的这一重大突破，这是她的功绩。\
**Lucy**: I thought it was necessary to report this to the Timekeeper's organization. It was her contribution.

**露西**：可惜，结果似乎不甚理想。\
**Lucy**: But it did not go well.

**参会人**：对不起，请允许我打断。但扭结是什么——？\
**Attendee**: Forgive the interruption. What's a knot?

**露西**：噢，我很乐意为您回答这个问题。\
**Lucy**: I will be glad to answer your question.

**露西**：扭结是代数拓扑的一个分支，在数学上，它指代的是三维欧氏空间中不与自己相交的连通封闭曲线，或者说，三维空间中的与圆周同胚的图形。\
**Lucy**: Knot theory is a branch of algebraic topology. In mathematics, a knot refers to a connected closed curve in three-dimensional Euclidean space that does not intersect itself. They can also be described as shapes in three-dimensional space that are homeomorphic to circles.

**露西**：扭结研究的是闭曲线在三维空间中的打结和链锁形态，而非曲线本身。因为所有的闭曲线都与圆周同胚，在拓扑上它们都属于圆。\
**Lucy**: Knot theory focuses on the entanglement and configurations of closed curves in three-dimensional space, rather than the curves themselves. Since all closed curves are homeomorphic to circles, they can all be topologically categorized as circles.

**露西**：与平面上的圆周等价的扭结被称为平凡结【unknot】，也就是一个“未打结”的圆圈。而——\
**Lucy**: A knot equivalent to a two-dimensional circle is called an unknot. And ...

**参会人**：……我无意质疑科算中心的判断，但这项成果也许并不适合推广。\
**Attendee**: I don't mean to question Laplace's expertise, but this approach may not be the best solution for widespread implementation.

**参会人**：这些概念，即使对于我们也晦涩难懂。我们更不可能让每个选区的成员站在一起，现场讲授高等数学原理。\
**Attendee**: The concepts are complex even for us, let alone others. We can't expect to give an advanced math lesson to every individual under these circumstances.

**参会人**：“暴雨”之下，我们没有时间去学习数学！\
**Attendee**: Doing math before the "Storm"—nobody's got time for that!

**露西**：结论是，现在进行技术汇报的确过早了。我们应当先将免疫护具生产出来，再进行一次正式汇报。\
**Lucy**: As it turned out, presenting a technical report was much too premature. We should have a complete and official report once the immunity gear is produced.

**哑谜**：……也许，您下次应该调整一下与基金会汇报时的策略。\
**Enigma**: Maybe you can change your approach the next time you report to the Foundation.

机器摇了摇头，不知是遗憾这场汇报的失败，还是遗憾提问者的数学能力。\
The robot shakes her head, disappointed by the failure of her report and the listener's math level.

**露西**：我只是如实回答了他们的问题。\
**Lucy**: I simply gave them honest answers.

她转过头，若有所思望向楼栋外的风景。\
She turns her head and looks thoughtfully out the window.

**露西**：但这的确是一个值得推广的结论。\
**Lucy**: But, this solution is deserving of widespread implementation.

**露西**：我们只需要找到一根绳子，将它两头闭合。\
**Lucy**: All we need is a piece of rope, and tie it end to end.

**露西**：然后，再花3-5分钟，将它按照指定的步骤交叉，就可以复制出这个术式。\
**Lucy**: And spend three to five minutes to make this knot.

**露西**：任何一个人类或者神秘学家，在任何一个地点，只要知道了打结的方式，就可以拿手边的条状物体准备仪式。\
**Lucy**: This can be done anywhere, at any time, by anyone using any type of cordage.

**露西**：这是最古老、最便捷、最简易的术式，也是越过“暴雨”的关键。\
**Lucy**: The oldest, fastest, and most basic ritual, the key to braving the "Storm" ...

**露西**：一个绳结。\
**Lucy**: ... is a knot.

**哑谜**：……您为何不把这些话告诉共融院的议员们呢？他们一定会大方地拨出预算的。\
**Enigma**: Why didn't you tell the House of Integratus? I'm sure they would've funded us generously.

**露西**：……之后我会把这些写在跨部门合作报告里的。\
**Lucy**: I will make sure to put it in my interdepartmental report.

机器的模样罕见地有些挫败。\
A rare hint of frustration flickers across her face.

好在她立刻找到了更值得关注的课题。\
But she quickly moves on to a subject that deserves her attention.

**露西**：不过，扭结目前的功效只是等同于咒语。\
**Lucy**: But at this point in time, the knot only functions like an incantation.

**露西**：在转换器和副作用的研究完成之前，它的确不适合向基金会汇报和推广。\
**Lucy**: It is not suitable for widespread use until the research on the side effects and the converter are complete.

**哑谜**：——不论如何，您指派我做的工作已经结束了。\
**Enigma**: In any case, I've completed all the tasks you assigned me.

**哑谜**：这是我最后的请求，请您下次不要再将我和乌尔里希放在一个小组。\
**Enigma**: My last plea is, please never put Ulrich and I on the same team again.

人类研究员打了个哈欠，他已经不眠不休了许久。\
The researcher lets out a deep yawn, feeling as if he hasn't slept in ages.

在实验阶段开始前，他也许还来得及打一个不长不短的盹。\
Maybe he can catch a quick nap before the final battle begins.

**哑谜**：……不过，我感到意外的是，您竟然没有在实验室里。是有什么进程在让您忧心吗？\
**Enigma**: Hm. I'm surprised that you're not in the lab. Something bothering you?

**哑谜**：等等，这该不会是在充电吧？\
**Enigma**: Wait, don't tell me you're charging here?

机器转过头来，脸庞上的表情可谓赞许。\
The robot turns to him, an approving smile on her face.

**露西**：很好，阿德勒研究员，看来你已经逐渐记住科算中心公共电源插头的位置了。\
**Lucy**: Excellent job, Researcher Adler. You have proven that you are keeping the locations of public outlets in Laplace in mind,

**露西**：这有助于你的再社会化。\
**Lucy**: which is a positive sign for your resocialization.

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

**露西**：但我的确是想用最好的状态迎接它。\
**Lucy**: But I am powering up to reach my optimal condition, preparing for what is to come—

**露西**：“暴雨”研究的最后一块拼图——阿派朗学派分享给我们的、能降低副作用的卷轴。\
**Lucy**: The scroll of Apeiron, the final piece of the puzzle, the key to minimizing any negative effects caused by the incantation.

剧情场景-空中

**红弩箭**：要我说，基金会的人工梦游还是太缺乏想象力了——\
**Lilya**: Whoa! The designers on Artificial Somnambulism could use some of this inspiration.

**红弩箭**：真该让他们看看这些沾染了暴雨症候的云层和环地平弧有多壮阔。\
**Lilya**: Look at the clouds, painted with a syndrome of colors and interrupted by a glorious streak of rainbow. It's truly a masterpiece!

绛红色的闪电一闪而过，但其后的奥利图欧群依然紧追不舍。\
The red blur streaks forward at lightning speed, but the Olitiaus are still in hot pursuit.

暴雨症候让它们的色泽愈发鲜艳。\
Their skins are becoming increasingly vibrant due to the Storm Syndrome.

**红弩箭**：有意思，它们好像会本能地飞向总部的方向……难道它们知道哪里有免疫“暴雨”的区域？\
**Lilya**: Funny. They're flying towards the headquarters out of instinct. Maybe they can sense immunity zones?

**红弩箭**：哈，还真是了不起的神秘动物啊——\
**Lilya**: These little beasts would make for a good study.

**红弩箭**：但我对押带俘虏回营可没什么兴趣。\
**Lilya**: But I'm not in the mood to take any prisoners.

红弩箭再次提升了速度，企图甩开那团“黑雾”构成的漩涡。\
Lilya speeds up again, trying to lose the pursuers that are swarming behind her like a dark vortex.

云层之下，基金会的灰白建筑已经清晰可见。\
In front of her, under the clouds, the gray buildings of the Foundation are now clearly visible.

**红弩箭**：啧，推进剂不足了！弹药储备也不够——\
**Lilya**: Fuel and ammunition are running out.

飞行高度已经很低了，红弩箭几乎可以看见委员会议室外的长廊。\
Her altitude is low enough. She can almost see the hallway outside the committee room.

**红弩箭**：带它们冲进副会长的办公室倒是个好主意，但其他人多少也会没命……算了。\
**Lilya**: Heh. Maybe I should storm the vice president's office with them? But other people might get hurt there. Never mind.

她转了个弯，思绪飞快运转。\
She makes an abrupt turn, her mind racing with ideas.

**红弩箭**：让它们冲进湖里？不，溅起的水花可能会沾湿卷轴。\
**Lilya**: Dive into the lake? But the splash might wet the scroll.

**红弩箭**：噢，那是……\
**Lilya**: Wait, isn't that ...

她看见了一簇舒展的新芽，那是返航的信号。\
Sprouts from the forest. That looks like a signal to land.

**槲寄生**：红弩箭小姐，请朝这儿来！\
**Druvis III**: Ms. Lilya, this way!

**红弩箭**：哈，好极了！\
**Lilya**: Ha. Good timing!

同伴的接应为她指明了方向。\
Her friend's presence has given her a clear sense of direction.

没有丝毫的犹豫，她带着“群鸟”向那片新生的森林俯冲去。\
Without a second thought, she charges into the new forest with the huge herd in hot pursuit.

就在飞行女巫的靴子尖与乔木相撞之前，红色38灵巧地转了个弯，如同火箭垂直向上射出。\
Just before crashing into the trees, Red 38 changes course and rockets upward in a perfectly straight line.

她纵身离去，那些遵循本能的神秘生物却并不具备这样的机动性。\
But the creatures behind her have no such finesse.

它们结实地撞上了乔木和藤蔓编制而成的巨网。\
One by one, they slam into the mesh woven by the dense tangle of trees and vines.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：拦截成功，接应对象已成功脱离。\
**Foundation Staff II**: Enemies intercepted. Ally landed successfully.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：奥利图欧全部撞上树网了，槲寄生小姐！\
**Foundation Staff II**: Ms. Druvis, the Olitiaus are all ensnared in vines!

德鲁伊闭上眼睛，这是久违的新鲜空气。\
The druid closes her eyes, savoring the fresh air.

**槲寄生**：——林间吹起了凯旋的风声。做得好，红弩箭小姐。\
**Druvis III**: The winds of triumph sweep through the woods. An excellent flight, Ms. Lilya.

**槲寄生**：那么，接下来便是我们的事宜了。诸位，请随我来，大地已向我们展开了丰获之路。\
**Druvis III**: We will take it from here. Come, everyone, we shall vanquish our foes with the aid of the woods.

**马库斯**：……特别行动队准备启程了。\
**Marcus**: The special operations squad is ready to go.

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚医生，您真的不和我们一起离开吗？\
**Marcus**: Dr. Kakania, are you really going to stay here?

剧情场景-变异的维也纳街头（复用场景）

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

她摇了摇头，手里还紧紧攥着马库斯的通讯器。\
She shakes her head, her fingers tight on Marcus's communicator.

在过去的十几个小时里，她一直在等待着科算中心的答复。\
For more than ten hours, she has been waiting for Laplace to respond.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

马库斯低下头，将眼眶的泪水和通红的鼻尖全都埋在围巾里。\
Marcus lowers her eyes, burying her face in her scarf to hide the tears.

医生及时注意到了她的异常，忙换了副轻松的口吻。\
The doctor quickly notices it, her voice softens and changes to a lighter tone.

**卡卡尼亚**：别太担心，小助理，这不会是永别的。\
**Kakania**: Don't worry about me, young missy. This won't be goodbye forever.

**卡卡尼亚**：而且，我能帮的忙已经结束了，不是吗？\
**Kakania**: Besides, I have already provided all the help I can, right?

**卡卡尼亚**：我告诉了你们镜中所见，也帮你们抓住了伊索尔德，你们也已经解出了这个术式……\
**Kakania**: I made Isolde show us the ritual and kept her under control. And now you've figured out how the ritual works.

**卡卡尼亚**：您也知道，实验总是需要那么一两个自愿报名的志愿者的。\
**Kakania**: To test its results, you will need a couple of volunteers.

这些语气轻快的话没能安慰到马库斯，年轻的调查员只是摇了摇头。\
But Marcus doesn't seem to find comfort in her words.

**马库斯**：可您也听到了科算中心的报告，没有转换器和调和卷轴，施术成功并存活的概率近乎于0——\
**Marcus**: But you heard the report from Laplace: the possibility of surviving the ritual is nearly zero without a converter and the scroll ...

**卡卡尼亚**：——可它不是0，不是吗？\
**Kakania**: Nearly, they said, but not surely.

医生语气轻快地打断了她。\
The doctor interjects briskly.

**卡卡尼亚**：……而且，我能去哪呢？\
**Kakania**: Plus, where else can I go?

**卡卡尼亚**：我出生在这座城市，也生长在这里。这里是我的故乡、我的居所、我的归处、我一整个世界的全部。\
**Kakania**: I was born and raised in this city. This is where I came from, where I lived, and where I belong. This is my whole world.

**卡卡尼亚**：我曾经为它的不公而痛心，为它金箔下的腐败而呼吁奔走，可我也爱着这里，爱着剧院石柱上的每寸雕花和码头工人们踩过的每寸泥土。\
**Kakania**: I despised the maggots under its golden surface, and fought for the justice and fairness in our society. But I also cherish every detail of this city, from the intricate carvings on the theater columns, to the dirt trodden by dock workers.

**卡卡尼亚**：这里有我的家人、我的朋友、我的同胞，我热爱的艺术、歌剧、文化，造就我的所有的一切。\
**Kakania**: All of these things made me me—my family, my friends, my people, and my operas and culture, are all here.

**卡卡尼亚**：我从没有想过离开它，我能去到哪里生活。\
**Kakania**: I never once thought about leaving this place.

**卡卡尼亚**：……我也从来没有想过要毁灭它。\
**Kakania**: I have never thought about destroying it, either.

她望向天空，释然地叹出一口气。\
She looks up and sighs sentimentally.

**卡卡尼亚**：能够和它一起消逝，已经是对我罪行最好的判决结果。\
**Kakania**: Being washed away with it would be a just punishment for all my sins.

她的眼中并无任何幽微。\
Yet her eyes are free of darkness and despair.

于是学徒也知道了，这是阻拦不住的。\
Marcus can clearly see her determination.

**马库斯**：……我真希望我是一个和您一样勇敢的人……\
**Marcus**: I wish I could be as brave as you are.

**马库斯**：再见，克拉拉小姐。\
**Marcus**: See you, Ms. Klara.

她轻轻地伸出手去。\
She gently reaches out to her.

远处，特别行动队的成员也做好了撤离的最后准备。\
Not far away, the special operations squad is ready to go.

直升飞机的螺旋桨打着摆子，执行今天最后一趟接送服务。\
The helicopter begins to whirl. Its last errand of the day.

伊索尔德垂着眼，一动不动地坐在舱内。她被套上了拘束衣，“剃刀”小队的成员正严密看守着她。\
Inside the cabin, Isolde sits between two "Razor" operatives, her wrists bound in cuffs.

**“剃刀”**：来吧，姑娘们，脚步快些！趁着我们还没有人成为享誉世界的“名画”。\
**"Razor"**: Hurry, ladies! Before any of us turns into one of those exquisite paintings.

**“剃刀”**：这儿到总部远远超过了传送软盘的距离，只能劳烦你们稍作忍耐，与我们这些粗野的家伙再待一会儿了。\
**"Razor"**: Sorry, but the headquarters is too far for the teleportation disk from here. You'll have to bear with us smelly old grunts for a little longer.

是时候要分别了。\
It is time to part ways.

**卡卡尼亚**：再见，马库斯小姐。\
**Kakania**: Goodbye, Ms. Marcus.

**卡卡尼亚**：很荣幸和您一同见证过时代的一角。\
**Kakania**: Sharing this era with you has been an honor.

温暖的手有力地交握在一起。\
Their warm hands clasp in a powerful handshake.

然后，她挥别了那不舍的女孩，义无反顾地走向世界的疯狂之中。\
With a wave to the teary-eyed girl, Kakania turns around and heads toward the city of madness.

**伊索尔德**：……您的生日就要到了，是吗，医生？\
**Isolde**: Is your birthday approaching, doctor?

女人恍惚的声音让她猛地回过头来。\
She twirls sharply around at the entranced voice.

伊索尔德向虚空中伸出了手。她并未醒来，仍深陷在催眠中，做着一个不愿醒来的梦。\
Isolde reaches out into the air, still in a dream she's unwilling to wake up from.

梦里，昨日的世界依旧，一切仍是美好的模样。\
There, the world is unchanged, and each day is filled with bliss.

对一位将在基金会的地下收容所中度过大多时日的人而言，这也许是一种好事。\
For a prisoner in the Foundation's facility, perhaps dreams will provide the solace she needs.

**伊索尔德**：我得把这个给您。医生，这是我为您而做的。\
**Isolde**: I made this for you.

贵族小姐递出了一枚胸针。它自由自在地在她甜美的声音中漂浮，仿佛它也是白日梦中不可碰触的一隅。\
She holds out a brooch. A piece so exquisite that it, too, seems to be an intangible figment of a wistful dream.

金属的花纹托举着闪闪发光的宝石，这无疑是件精心的礼物。\
The golden setting nestles the sparkling gem in place, a gift undoubtedly made with great affection.

**伊索尔德**：绿松石和托帕石，就像您和您的眼睛……\
**Isolde**: Turquoise and Topaz, just like you and your eyes.

**伊索尔德**：祝福您，医生，祝您幸福和顺利，祝您的勇气能够跨越一切障碍。\
**Isolde**: Please accept my blessings, doctor. May your life be filled with joy and contentment, and may your courage guide you through all that comes your way.

**伊索尔德**：您值得一切的奇迹和好运，我也会去教堂为您祈祷……\
**Isolde**: You are worthy of all the beauty and goodness this world has to offer, and I will hold you in my heart and in my prayers, forever.

今天不是卡卡尼亚的生日，她的身影也没有映照在那抹无神的目光中。\
Today isn't Kakania's birthday, nor can she see her reflection in Isolde's lusterless eyes.

歌剧演员只是含笑地，渴盼地，向一无所有的空气托举着。\
The Star of Vienna holds up the brooch, yearning at the emptiness before her.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

假如一个人今日就要死去……\
If one were to die today ...

她又能对昔日的友人说些什么呢？\
What would she say to her long-time friend?

**卡卡尼亚**：祝您好梦，伊索尔德小姐。\
**Kakania**: Sweet dreams, Ms. Dittarsdorf.

她还是接过了那枚胸针，将它别在西装上。\
She takes the brooch and pins it to her jacket.

腰间的通讯器传来了沙沙声，这是马库斯留给她的最后帮助。\
The communicator at her waist crackles.

一道指向希望的电波。\
A ray of hope shines through the static.

**卡卡尼亚**：——！\
**Kakania**: ...!

**卡卡尼亚**：露西女士……！你们的研究，有进展了吗？\
**Kakania**: Madam Lucy! Any progress on the research?

## 7TH-27 酒神颂 / Hymnus Ad Bacchum

**37**：……你是说，6醒来了？\
**37**: 6 is awake?

传道者之厅-洞穴研究室-1.9差分版本，进行一些改装

盲眼的女士微笑着点了点头。\
The blind woman nods, smiling.

37从地上站起来，目光难掩真切的喜悦。\
37 scrambles up from the floor, her eyes sparkling with joy.

**37**：太好了，现在我们得到了一个10——完美中的完美！\
**37**: Fabulous! Now everything is perfect, like the number 10!

**37**：他一定会很高兴听到我已经解开了数字密码的奥秘！\
**37**: He will be happy to hear that I've cracked the code!

她蹦蹦跳跳地转过头来，手里仍拿着那张画着扭结的纸张。\
She skips across the room, the paper with the knot on it still in her hand.

**37**：我做到了，维尔汀！\
**37**: I did it, Vertin!

**37**：我证明了真理的辉光仍是存在的，只是需要一些时间、交流和灵光，我们就能把它从不可触及的天空带回大地，让它的光泽普照每一个人。\
**37**: I have proven the light of Truth still shines. With some time, communication, and a flash of inspiration, we can bring it down from the unattainable skies and let its radiance illuminate all.

**37**：它离我们并不遥远，也不难以触及，我证明了这一点。\
**37**: And I've also proven that the Truth is not out of reach or too distant to grasp.

**37**：——所以，苏菲亚一定也会马上回来的，对吗？\
**37**: So, once Sophia knows about this, she'll come back to us, right?

她近乎期盼地仰起头来，渴望一个肯定的回答。\
She opens her eyes wide, eager for the affirmation she yearns to hear.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：我想她也一定会为你的成果感到高兴的，37。\
**Vertin**: I'm sure she will be happy with what you've accomplished, 37.

37点了点头，再度沉浸在了对成果的完善中。\
37 nods with satisfaction and quickly dives back into her work, further perfecting the solution.

飞跃的进展和领袖的归来助长了人们的喜悦，研究室里的教众们互相道贺着。\
The leaps in progress and the news of 6's return have filled the lab with smiles and lively conversations.

但往日最活跃的成员，却没有第一时间出现在庆祝现场。\
Yet the most active members of the past are not here for the celebration.

**37**：……唔？\
**37**: Hmm?

**37**：210和888是去迎接6了吗？\
**37**: Did 210 and 888 go to get 6?

剧情场景-岛屿-传道者之厅外-天色差分（是一个比较独特的光线，比如玫瑰紫）

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

**210**：你似乎并没有特别高兴。\
**210**: You don't seem that happy.

领袖止住了脚步，望向石阶上的来人。\
The leader stops, looking at the speaker coming down the steps.

**210**：我们的赫尔墨斯之星解开了无限定者的数字密码，找到了越过“流溢”的一个办法。\
**210**: The Star of Hermes deciphered the code of Apeiron. She found a way to cross the "Emanation."

**210**：我们应当为她感到高兴。\
**210**: We should all feel happy for her.

领袖没有应答，一如他多年来最为擅长的沉默。\
The leader does not answer, having mastered the art of silence over the years.

修辞学家不以为意，他向来能与任何人谈笑风生，无论对方是否是一块石头。\
The rhetorician doesn't care. He can effortlessly engage in dialogue and is at ease in any conversation, even with a rock.

**210**：——而你，如此平静。\
**210**: Yet here you are, so indifferent.

**210**：是因为你也知道，无论她是否成功，都已经无济于事？\
**210**: It is because you, too, know that what has happened will not change, regardless of whether she figures it out or not?

**210**：能够在“流溢”中幸免的术式，和至高规律的紊乱相比，只是最细枝末节的应用问题，并不触及本源的矛盾，也无法改变信仰已死的事实。\
**210**: A meager ritual to save people from the "Emanation" is nothing compared to the disruption of the Law above. It also cannot change the fact that our faith is dead.

**210**：海啸已经摧毁了这座岛屿。一次微末的奇迹、一道短促的火光，并不足以挽救一艘在大海中注定沉没的船。\
**210**: We're talking about how the island has sunk, and we're now sailing in a tsunami. A tiny miracle, a spark of inspiration won't save the ship from the wrath of the tides.

他讥讽地说着，目光却少了往日的戏谑。\
His tone is sarcastic, but the mockery is missing in his eyes.

**210**：不过，我也很意外她竟然问了这样一个实际的问题——看来现象世界的碎屑多少还是改变了她。\
**210**: To be honest, I was surprised that she asked such a practical question. I guess the trivialities of the phenomenal world did eventually affect her.

**210**：只可惜其他人并不像她那样，有目空一切虚无的意志和决心。\
**210**: It's a shame that many others lack her determined will to see beyond the void of our broken reality.

**6**：你想说什么呢？\
**6**: What's your point?

**210**：显然，我在挖苦你。\
**210**: Can't you see? I'm getting a rise out of you.

修辞学家露出了一个灿烂的笑容。\
He beams a huge grin.

**210**：谁能想到，我们伟大的、完美的、值得尊敬的、阿派朗学派的领袖，竟然是一个彻头彻尾的虚无主义者！\
**210**: Who would've thought that our great, perfect, honorable leader of the School of Apeiron has been a nihilist all along!

**210**：你从来没有一天敬畏过真理，对吗？所以你才会隐瞒了四年。你从来没有一天尊敬过我们所有人的信仰。\
**210**: You never revered the Truth, did you? That's why you kept us in the dark for four years. You never respected our beliefs for a second in your life!

石阶下的男人只是摇了摇头。\
The man down the steps shakes his head.

**6**：真理并没有追逐真理的人重要。\
**6**: The people who seek the Truth are more important than the Truth itself.

**6**：也许我无法解析那个永恒变动的数字，但我了解这里的人们。\
**6**: I may not understand that ever-shifting number, but I do understand and respect the people here.

他继续了这个话题，这是罕见的。\
He's continuing the conversation, a rarity to behold.

在成为那个代表调和的数字之后，他便少有语出讥讽的时刻。\
Ever since becoming 6, he's rarely had a chance to unleash his sarcastic wit.

**6**：那么，您又要做什么？\
**6**: So you know the secret, what now?

**6**：既然真理只是虚无，便索性放弃我们所有的教义、智慧、传承，报复性地步入幽微之中？\
**6**: Now that you know the Truth could lead to a nihilistic void, I wonder if you would abandon our doctrines, our wisdom, and our inheritance, and step into the darkness in a fit of rage?

**6**：“假如没有真理，一切都是修辞”——是吗？\
**6**: When Truth fails, sophistry prevails. Correct?

**210**：……哈。\
**210**: Ha.

**210**：我们必须承认，命运这位不可说者是智慧的。\
**210**: We cannot deny that fate, the unspeakable, holds wisdom beyond our understanding.

**210**：也许只有一个无药可救的怀疑论者、一个并无立场的虚无者……才能在这艘来回颠簸的船里保持他的观众席位。\
**210**: Perhaps it does take a resolute skeptic, an impartial nihilist, to steady this ship and remain detached enough to look on from the sidelines.

210抬起头，望向了远处葡萄紫色的天空。\
210 looks up at the distant grape-colored sky.

**210**：多遗憾啊，现在本该是酿制葡萄酒的时节。\
**210**: It's a pity. This was supposed to be the best time of year to make wine.

修辞学家径直离开了。

领袖沉默地沿着既定的路线前行。\
He leaves without looking back.

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本。这里可能拉一个近景用来和前面区分。\
The silent leader continues on the familiar path.

在视线的前方，37敏捷地从沙地上滑了下来。\
A short distance away, 37 slides gracefully down the sand and runs toward him.

**37**：——6，太好了，你果然在这里！\
**37**: 6! You're here!

**37**：888告诉我，他们要在“流溢”到来前举办一个庆典，纪念所有的死者和生者。你也会来参加吗，6？\
**37**: 888 said they're holding a celebration before the arrival of the "Emanation," in honor of the living and the dead. Will you join us, 6?

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

**6**：37，你还记得苏格拉底的故事吗？\
**6**: 37, do you remember the story of Socrates?

**37**：嗯？是你在试炼地说起的那个吗？\
**37**: Hmm? The one you told me in the cave?

**37**：试炼早就结束了，不是吗？你应该先回答我的邀请……\
**37**: The trial is over. Why mention it? You should answer my question first.

谈话没能继续，37突然惊恐地瞪大了双眼。\
Her words trail off as her eyes suddenly widen in fear.

发生在远处的状况牵引了她的全部心神。\
She's completely fixated on what's in the distance.

她曾重新计算过免疫“流溢”的区域，让信仰者们在安全的开阔地举办庆典。\
She knows the feast is underway, and she's recalculated the safe zone for them to hold it in.

而如今，人们正在满目疮痍的近海沙滩上架设桌椅，准备餐食，紧挨着那些破碎的战争遗迹。\
But now, people are laying out food and wine on the ruined beach, among the rubble and wreckage, right next to the remains of the battlefield.

**37**：不，他们举办庆典的地点——在免疫“流溢”的安全区之外！\
**37**: Wait, are they holding the ceremony outside the immunity zone!?

**37**：我告诉过他们，要在更靠近山顶的草地上举办的！那里是绝对安全的，我反复验算过，没有疏漏任何一个小数点……！\
**37**: I told them to go to the meadow near the top of the mountain, where they will be completely safe! I've checked my calculations over and over, leaving no room for error!

**37**：一定是888弄错了，我得去告诉她——\
**37**: 888 must've made a mistake. I need to warn them!

纤细的胳膊被拉住了。\
Her tiny arms are held back.

垂下的金发遮住了6的眼睛，37几乎是错愕地回过头来，望向这位一反常态的寡言领袖。\
Blonde hair droops over 6's eyes. 37 looks back in confusion at the leader's unusual behavior.

**6**：37……\
**6**: 37 ...

**6**：置身事外的智慧，和亲临其中的痛苦，你只能选择一个。\
**6**: Either be wise, uninvolved, and look on; or be practical, involved, and suffer.

**6**：——你想好选择哪个了吗？\
**6**: Which one will you end up choosing?

**卡卡尼亚**：……您是说，只需要一根绳子？\
**Kakania**: You mean, all we need is a piece of rope?

剧情场景-露西女士的办公室-开灯版本\
The voice on the phone sounds unsure.

通讯器那头的声音听起来十分不可思议。

**露西**：是的，为感谢您在研究历程中所提供的帮助，科算中心将破例向您分享这则成果。这是我们最新，也是术式破译的最终所得。\
**Lucy**: Yes. In recognition of your extraordinary contributions, Laplace is honored to present you with the fruits of our labor. This knot is the result of our research.

**露西**：在其他神秘学家的协助下，我们也已成功找到了规避副作用的方式，进行了小规模实验。扭结作为术式的有效性已经在普通神秘学家和人类身上验证过。\
**Lucy**: The knot has been validated as a working ritual on both humans and arcanists. With the help of other arcanists, we found methods to avoid side effects, and conducted small-scale experiments with success.

**卡卡尼亚**：也就是说，我们能——\
**Kakania**: So are you saying we can—

**露西**：但很遗憾，副作用研究完成的时间太过短暂，它的准备材料和术式构造太过复杂，目前尚无远程传输的可能。\
**Lucy**: However, since the experiment is still in its early stages, it involves a variety of materials and complicated rituals that are not yet possible for transmission.

**露西**：“暴雨”就要落下，我们也无法给您分发任何实验仪器。\
**Lucy**: Nor can we deliver you any experimental equipment, as the "Storm" is about to make landfall.

**露西**：扭结本身只是等效于咒文，要使用它，您依然需要承受达不到施术条件的风险，和很大可能存在的副作用。\
**Lucy**: The knot acts as an equivalent to the incantation, but it does not guarantee that we will meet the casting requirements or avoid the likely side effects.

对于一个在火灾中心等待水源的人来说，这些消息太过残酷。\
This is devastating news for anyone in need of rescue in the midst of a disaster.

机器也顿了顿，开始在数据库里寻找稍微柔软一些的说辞。\
The robot pauses briefly, searching its database for kinder phrasings.

**露西**：很抱歉，卡卡尼亚小姐。对您而言，我们最终的结果也许与最开始没有区别。\
**Lucy**: I apologize, Ms. Kakania. Perhaps the result of our work will not really help your situation.

**卡卡尼亚**：……您说，和只有神秘学家能使用的咒文不同，绳结是对所有人都生效的，是吗？\
**Kakania**: You said the knot works on both humans and arcanists, right?

意外的反馈，卡卡尼亚的声音并没有悲伤。\
Surprisingly, there's no despair in her voice.

**露西**：是的。\
**Lucy**: Yes.

**卡卡尼亚**：那么，这就够了，这就是我听到的最好的消息。\
**Kakania**: That is more than enough. This is the best news I've heard so far.

**卡卡尼亚**：……不是让一群人从一处分离出去，而是让大家能够一起活下来。\
**Kakania**: There's a chance for everyone.

机器并没有听懂这句喃喃自语，但她已经从数据库中找到了有利的信息。\
The robot did not understand her mumbling, but she found something in her database that might help.

**露西**：我能告诉您的还有两个好消息。\
**Lucy**: I have two more pieces of good news.

**露西**：其一是，诅咒并非百灵百验，在过往的实验中，有0.49%概率不会触发任何诅咒。\
**Lucy**: First, the curse is not inevitable. Our experiments showed a 0.49% likelihood of no side effects occurring at all.

**露西**：其二是，随着“暴雨”的逼近，流溢的灵性会越来越多，施术成功的几率也会越来越大。\
**Lucy**: Second, the closer the "Storm" gets, the more pneuma fills the air, leading to a greater success rate of the ritual.

**露西**：但他们组合起来的成功概率依然是难以估计的微小。\
**Lucy**: Yet, even with these factors combined, the rate of success is still extremely low.

**卡卡尼亚**：没关系，多么微小的概率乘以数以万计的基数，也有可能得到大于1的结果。\
**Kakania**: It's alright. With millions of people trying, there's hope that at least one person will succeed against the odds.

**卡卡尼亚**：谢谢您给我的机会，女士，我会竭尽所能地在维也纳传播这个绳结。\
**Kakania**: Thank you for sharing this with me, madam. I will do everything I can to spread this knot in Vienna,

**卡卡尼亚**：无论是神秘学家还是人类，无论是马扎尔人还是德意志人，无论是贩夫走卒还是贵族绅士，他们都是我的同胞。\
**Kakania**: to the arcanists, humans, Magyars, and Germans. They are all my people, regardless of their social status, profession, or race.

**卡卡尼亚**：——他们都理应享有活下去的机会。\
**Kakania**: They all deserve the right to survive.

露西关掉通讯仪器，转过身来。\
Lucy ends the call and turns around.

迎接她的是身后面色凝重的基金会职员。他被派遣来与露西女士接洽实验相关工作，却没想到会撞见眼前这一幕。\
There stands a Foundation employee, sent here to inquire about the experiment, with a stern expression after overhearing the conversation.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：露西女士，您刚才的行为似乎……忘了向基金会提请决策申请流程。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Madam Lucy, I can only assume you acted impulsively and overlooked the proper application process.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：“扭结”刚刚诞生，不具备大规模实验的基础。在维也纳进行免疫术式的公开传播，有可能造成新的伤亡案例，同时也有泄密给敌方的风险。\
**Foundation Staff I**: The knot is new and not ready for widespread testing. Distributing it in Vienna could lead to more casualties or even fall into the hands of our enemies.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：抱歉，我不得不提醒您，您的行为已经严重违反了人类和平安全理事会、圣洛夫基金会和拉普拉斯科算中心的规定。\
**Foundation Staff I**: I must remind you that this is a clear violation of the regulations set by Pax Security Council, the St. Pavlov Foundation, and Laplace.

**露西**：嗯，确实有些莽撞。\
**Lucy**: Ah, yes. How careless of me.

机器点了点头，深以为然。\
The robot nods.

**露西**：但是我答应过她，要告知她最终的研究结果。\
**Lucy**: But I did tell her I would share the results of the research.

**露西**：——这是一个“承诺”。\
**Lucy**: And this is what you call a "promise."

**露西**：数据库告诉我，“承诺”，就是要“兑现”的“诺言”。\
**Lucy**: And the database says, a promise made is a promise kept.

“暴雨”就要落下了，这是最后的时刻。

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本-轰炸后\
The "Storm" is imminent. The final moment has arrived.

**888**：敬爱的诸姐妹们、兄弟们，请你们暂时放下手中的酒杯，聆听我的话语！\
**888**: My brothers and sisters, put down your cups for a moment and lend ear to me!

**888**：我们是生而非凡之人，也是生而异己之人。漫长的时光里，我们漂泊，流浪，如同海上浮舟。\
**888**: We were born extraordinary, yet estranged from the world around us. Throughout the ages, we wandered the world like a ship lost at sea.

**888**：最终，我们从无定与混乱中脱颖而出，共同追求那启明一切的真理。\
**888**: Despite the instability and chaos, we persevered, and together, we sought after the Truth that would illuminate us all.

**888**：在沉思的净化之中，我们摆脱仇恨、疯狂和谵妄，寻得美与和谐的尺度。\
**888**: Through introspection and contemplation, we cleansed ourselves of hatred, madness, and delusion, and embraced the value of beauty and harmony.

**210**：而如今，我们的信仰已与现象世界的碎屑一同，变为错误历史的一道扬尘、海潮退去的一地废墟。\
**210**: Yet now, our shattered faith mingles with the rubble of this phenomenal world, as specks in an unjust timeline, as remnants of a tide long receded.

**210**：超验王国的幻梦已经破碎，至高规律已是一片虚无。\
**210**: The dream of the transcendental world is broken, and the order of the transcendental Law is no more.

**888**：遗世独立的基底已不复存在，我们注定生活在一个充满纷争的破碎世界。\
**888**: Our sanctuary has crumbled, exposing us to live in a world filled with conflict and turmoil,

**888**：陷入生之巨轮的无限流转，重复漫漫历史的无尽错误。\
**888**: where we will be trapped in the wheel of birth, doomed to repeat the mistakes of history for eternity.

**210**：——好在，我们还有另一条接近真理的进路！\
**210**: But do not despair, for there is another way to the Truth!

**210**：属于狂野和激情的那条坦途，被适度和节制所掩盖的那条路。超越一切个体，打破一切界限，向世界本质壮烈回归的那条路。\
**210**: It is a path fueled by unbridled passion, one that was stifled by moderation and restraint. A path that transcends the individual, breaks all boundaries and limitations, and leads us back to the essence in a fiery blaze of glory.

**888**：——步入“流溢”，以身证道。\
**888**: This path is the "Emanation," which we stride into for the ultimate Truth of our journey.

剧情场景-变异的维也纳街头（复用场景）

**小贩Ⅰ**：——医生？！\
**Vendor I**: Doctor?!

小贩惊讶地停下脚步，他看见了面前奔跑的故人。\
The boy eases his pace as he sees Kakania rushing his way.

**卡卡尼亚**：呼，太好了，总算遇到一个熟人……\
**Kakania**: Finally, someone I know.

医生喘着气，怀中抱着一堆刚刚印刷出来的传单。\
She cradles a thick stack of pamphlets in her arms, a little out of breath.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊里奇，去找所有你认识的还能行动的人，让他们拿着这张纸上广场去，照着上面的步骤念！\
**Kakania**: Illich, gather everyone you can, and have them read out these steps in the plaza for all to hear!

**卡卡尼亚**：如果他们能去电报局，去杂志社和报社使用印刷机，那就更好了！把它传播出去，越多人知道越好！！！\
**Kakania**: If possible, go to the telegraph office or use a printing machine to copy flyers. Distribute as many copies as you can!

**卡卡尼亚**：我现在得去利奥波德区找卖古董的格拉古兄弟，他们知道哪里有军方废弃的热气球——\
**Kakania**: I'll go to Leopoldstadt and find the Gracchus brothers. They know where to find abandoned military hot-air balloons.

**小贩Ⅰ**：你在说什么啊，医生。大家正忙着逃命呢，我可一点也不想再沾上那些疯子。\
**Vendor I**: What are you talking about, doctor? People are too busy trying to escape. I want nothing to do with those crazies.

**小贩Ⅰ**：这是……打结教程？世界都要毁灭了，您可真有闲心……还有这么一长串警告，谁会读完这么多字？\
**Vendor I**: This? A guide for tying knots? Don't you know the world is about to end? So many warnings. Who'd want to read this?

**卡卡尼亚**：——他们会读完的，因为这是可以活下来的办法！\
**Kakania**: The people who want to survive will read it!

**卡卡尼亚**：这不是百试百灵的解法，只是一次豪赌，但人们应该知道它！在世界消逝前，他们应当有选择站上那张赌桌的权利！\
**Kakania**: I can't guarantee anything. It's a gamble for our lives, but people have a right to try before doomsday arrives.

**卡卡尼亚**：求求你，伊里奇，再相信我一次！就这一次！！！\
**Kakania**: Illich, please trust me one more time! PLEASE!

男孩注意到了她话语里的哀求，他没有再说什么。\
The boy recognizes the plea in her voice.

**小贩Ⅰ**：……好吧，如果这是真的，以后你的咖啡我都买单了，克拉拉医生！\
**Vendor I**: Fine, Dr. Klara. If this works, your coffee for the rest of your life is on me!

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-炮火轰炸版本-轰炸后

**37**：为什么……？\
**37**: Why?

女孩抓着自己的头发，爆发出一声难以置信的哀鸣。\
Clutching at her own hair, she lets out a heart-wrenching wail.

**37**：为什么……？！为什么你们还是要离开——？\
**37**: Why?! Why are you still leaving?

**37**：我明明得到了真理，我明明完成了证明，我明明解出了无限定者的密码——\
**37**: I found the Truth, I completed the test, I deciphered the code of Apeiron.

不顾那阻拦的手，她近乎崩溃地想朝那片海滩冲去。\
She struggles, trying to break free from the arm holding her back, her eyes fixed on the beach before her.

**37**：——为什么你不阻止他们，6……？\
**37**: Why aren't you stopping them, 6?

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

一个熟悉且友好的身影出现在眼前。\
A friendly figure comes up to them.

**玛尔塔**：您好。\
**Marta**: Hello.

**维尔汀**：……玛尔塔女士，您也要加入他们吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you joining them, Ms. Marta?

她微笑着摇了摇头，并不存在的视线望向领袖的方向。\
She smiles and shakes her head, turning her face toward the leader.

**玛尔塔**：我也不知道我该去往何处。因此，我想请您为我解答疑惑。\
**Marta**: I find myself uncertain of which way to go. Would you kindly give me some guidance?

**6**：……玛尔塔女士，我能回答您的并不多。\
**6**: The guidance I can offer you is limited, Ms. Marta.

**6**：但我想——命运比我们更清楚自己的命运。\
**6**: I think fate knows its own fate better than anyone.

**玛尔塔**：……感谢您的解答。\
**Marta**: Thank you for your advice.

**玛尔塔**：如此，我明白了。\
**Marta**: I think I understand.

于是，她迈向了那条坦途。\
She steps into the path of no return.

**37**：不——！\
**37**: NO!

在遥远的山崖间我看见了巴克斯\
When I saw Bacchus on the distant hilltop

相信我 后世的朋友 他正在教授酒神赞歌\
Teaching his songs, and believe me, for posterity,

水神宁芙与半羊人的萨蒂尔都竖着耳朵 专注地谛听\
Nymphs and goat-legged satyrs surround him, listening intently with their ears pointing.

欧呵 将近的恐惧仍使我的心颤栗\
Euhoe! How this sight fills me with trembling awe,

灵魂被巴克斯充斥 狂喜而迷乱\
And the influence of Bacchus intoxicates me with delight.

欧呵 饶恕我吧 酒神 饶恕我\
Oh, Euhoe! Spare me, Liber,

你致命的权杖令人畏惧\
Spare me from the power of your mighty thyrsus,

由此我可以歌吟不知疲倦的祭司\
So that I may sing of your endlessly revelrous followers

歌吟流淌着酒与乳的 清泉与河溪\
Of your fountains of wine and rivers of milk,

并再次描绘

自空心树干中盈满而溢出的蜂蜜\
And tell again of your streams

歌咏你的伴侣如何在\
Of ever flowing honey;

星辰之间增添了荣耀\
And so that I may praise of your beloved, who is added

歌咏彭罗斯的家族 如何在灾难中轰然瓦解\
And honored among the constellations,

色雷斯人 吕库古如何毁灭\
And sing of how the house of Pentheus came to ruins,

你改变河的流向与异域的海洋\
Along with the fall of the Thracian Lycurgus.

你在孤峰上饮醉了酒\
You, the bender of rivers and barbaric seas,

用蝰蛇为色雷斯的信徒盘好头发\
You, so flushed with wine on your distant hilltop

她们却并未受到咬啮\
Tie the hair of Bistonian women

视频结束。\
With harmless knots made of serpents.

## 7TH-28 数轴的两端 / The Two Numbers

剧情场景-岛屿-沙滩-黄昏版本

**37**：我不明白……\
**37**: I, I don't understand.

**37**：我应该祝福勇敢回归本质的人们……但我不住地感到悲伤。\
**37**: I should be giving them my blessings. They're brave enough to return to the essence. But instead, sadness washes over me.

**37**：我应该为苏菲亚看清她的数字而高兴……可我只是感到难过。\
**37**: I should feel happy for Sophia, now that she knows her soul number. Yet, I am filled with sorrow.

沙滩恢复了昔日的洁净。\
The beach is quiet, clean, and perfect again.

“暴雨”冲刷走了其上的一切——战争的残骸、欢呼的人群、交错的酒杯。\
The "Storm" has washed away everything that's happened—the war, the crowds, and the clinking cups, all gone.

它被还原回了往昔某个美好时光的模样，未留下任何碎屑。\
It's restored to the likeness of a better time, with no remnants left behind.

一个时代在刚刚带走了最后的尾声。\
The last echoes of an era have faded into the distance.

**37**：为什么……你们都要离开？\
**37**: Why? Why did you all leave?

**37**：是因为我算得不够快吗？是我算得还不够好吗？\
**37**: Is it because I wasn't fast enough? Is it because I didn't do well enough?

**37**：我……\
**37**: I ...

她细小的身杆在空气中轻微摇晃，最终，像失去了无形的风般扑落在沙滩上。\
Her petite frame sways in the breeze, until finally, she crumples to the sand.

**37**：呜……\
**37**: *sob*

**37**：呜呜呜……

**37**：呜呜哇啊啊啊啊啊啊啊————！\
**37**: *crying out loud*

泪水不住地从她的脸上滑落，和地上的泥水混在一起。\
Rivulets of tears stream down her cheeks, mixing with the mud on the ground.

弄脏了她的脸颊、她的头发、她鎏金的长袍。\
Her face, hair, and gilded robe are marred with stains.

但她只是不顾一切地、撕心裂肺地发出幼兽的哭喊。\
But she shows no concern as she bawls her eyes out, her grief tearing at the core of her being.

——属于现象世界的第一次泣哭。\
... Like the first cries of a newborn entering the phenomenal world.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

于是领袖也知道了，这就是那个问题的答案。\
Thus the leader knows; the question is answered.

置身事外的智慧，和亲临其中的痛苦。她选择了“痛苦”。\
Rather than looking on, she has chosen to be practical, involved, and suffer.

那么，是分别的时刻了。\
And now, the moment of parting has come.

**6**：去岛外的世界吧，37。你应该去那里看看。\
**6**: Go, 37. Leave the island. To the world outside.

**37**：……？！\
**37**: ...?!

**6**：维尔汀小姐，你们摸索出了一条在现象世界的泥泞中求索的道路。\
**6**: Ms. Vertin, you're clearing a path out of the mires of the phenomenal world.

**6**：希望你们永远不会将它导向战争。\
**6**: I sincerely hope you will steer it away from the horrors of war.

**维尔汀**：……这是我们的使命。\
**Vertin**: It's our duty to do so.

领袖点了点头，他们都知道那个卷轴的份量。\
6 nods approvingly. The importance of the scroll needs no further proclamation.

**6**：对了，关于您要来此地找寻的人……我并不认识任何名为“兀尔德”的传记作家。\
**6**: Also, the person you were looking for ... I am not familiar with a biographer named "Urd."

**6**：但在上一代6的记忆中，曾有过一位女士，她和您有着一样特殊的数字。\
**6**: However, in my recollections from the previous 6, there was a lady with a soul number just as unique as yours.

**维尔汀**：……！您的意思是……\
**Vertin**: ...! Are you saying ...

**6**：很遗憾，我继承的“传承”中只有这些模糊的信息。希望这对您有帮助。\
**6**: Sadly, these vague scraps of information were all that I inherited. I hope they will be useful to you.

然后，他转过身去，不再望向那处已成空地的沙滩。\
He turns around. Without another look at the empty beach, he starts walking back.

有三三两两的教众跟上了他的脚步。\
Some believers trail after him without hesitation.

察觉到他的动作，女孩擦干眼泪，慌忙地从地上站起。\
Seeing this, the girl wipes off her tears and scrambles to her feet.

**37**：等一下，6，你要去哪里——？\
**37**: No. No, no, no. No! Wait, 6, where are you going?

**37**：每个人都走了，苏菲亚、210、888……现在，连你——也要离开吗？\
**37**: Everyone is gone. Sophia, 210, 888, and now you too?

**6**：我要回到洞穴中去，37。\
**6**: I'm returning to the cave, 37.

**6**：仍有人既不愿被仇恨的巨链裹挟，也未选择狂野和激情的道路。\
**6**: There are still people who refuse to be caught in the cycle of hatred, or give in to unrestrained passion.

**6**：通往圣地的路已在地震中被损毁，但人们的信念并未绝迹。\
**6**: The entrance to the sacred place may be destroyed, but the people's faith is yet to be extinguished.

**6**：我们会诵读典籍、抄写经文、修缮厅堂，在苦修和沉思中继续对古老者的崇奉，重拾破碎的信仰辉光。\
**6**: We will persist in studying the scrolls, copying the scriptures, and restoring our halls. We will worship the ancient one in penance and work to rekindle the flame of our broken beliefs.

**6**：是我们的选择塑就了这座岛屿，一个远离现象世界纠纷的沉思净土，一个古典的秩序王国。而我们的坚守，亦会让它常在。\
**6**: The island is a manifestation of our choices, a haven removed from the phenomenal world, a place of order and harmony. And it is our determination that will sustain its tranquil existence.

**37**：我和你一起去！\
**37**: I will go with you!

**6**：不，你已经做出了选择，37。你不应该再回到这儿了。\
**6**: No. Your choice has already been made, 37. You should not go back.

**6**：你的痛苦和疑惑，只能在亲历外部世界的过程中获得解答。\
**6**: The sorrows and doubts you have can only be alleviated by experiencing the outside world.

37的脸色在瞬间变得无比苍白。\
37's face turns completely pale.

6轻轻摇了摇头，看向海面上的夕阳。\
6 shakes his head, looking toward the setting sun.

**6**：数千年前，最初的信仰者们逃避罗马帝国的战火，来到这里建立教派。\
**6**: Thousands of years ago, the first faithful ones fled from the Roman Empire and journeyed to this island, where they founded the School of Apeiron.

**6**：五百年前，一支逃难的阿拉伯难民来到此处，用他们的抄本填满了洞穴中的书籍。\
**6**: Five hundred years ago, refugees from Arabia found shelter here. They filled the cavern's shelves with copies of their writings and texts.

**6**：半个世纪前，痛恨自己的研究被战争滥用的学者来到此处，补充了现代数学的智慧。\
**6**: Half a century ago, scholars who had their research exploited for warfare came and expanded our knowledge on modern mathematics.

**6**：他们中也曾有37，也有过许多6。\
**6**: There were many 37s and 6s among them.

**6**：——我们和他们又有什么本质的不同？\
**6**: Yet, are we any different from them in essence?

**37**：……！\
**37**: ...!

**6**：即使你和我都不在了，37和6也不会消失。即使这座岛在今天没入大海，也会有新的数字诞生于别处。\
**6**: Even if we are no longer here, the numbers 37 and 6 will still exist. Even if the island sank, these numbers would reappear elsewhere.

**6**：我们都知道整数的序列是无穷的，37。不要执着于数轴上的个别数字，你应当书写你自己的算式。\
**6**: The integer sequence is infinite, 37. Rather than clinging to a set of specific numbers, you should go and work out your own calculations and conclusions.

**维尔汀**：……所以您选择的是置身事外的智慧。\
**Vertin**: So now you're choosing to be wise and look on.

**维尔汀**：——但我不明白，智慧为何蕴含在置身之外中？\
**Vertin**: But I don't understand. How could one be wise by being uninvolved and looking on from the sidelines?

领袖笑了笑。\
6 lets out a sound, almost a chuckle.

**6**：您高估了智慧的效用，维尔汀小姐。智慧并不是万能的，它能使人免于无知，也会将人导向虚无。\
**6**: You overestimate wisdom, Ms. Vertin. It can't do everything. Wisdom can free people from ignorance, but it can also lead them to a nihilistic void.

**6**：但总有人需要这份虚无的智慧，让他们从尘世的痛苦中获得短暂的超脱。\
**6**: Yet someone will always seek this wisdom, even if nihilistic, to briefly rise above their worldly troubles and find some relief.

**6**：总有人需要留下，给现象之海上而来的漂泊者们提供一个无关政治的庇护所。\
**6**: And someone will have to stay here, and provide a neutral haven for the drifters of the phenomenal world,

**6**：——也给迷途的人们一个返航的归处。\
**6**: and give the lost souls a harbor to return to.

他转身离开了，不顾身后的呼喊。\
He turns again, ignoring the calling behind him this time.

**37**：等一下，6，等一下——！\
**37**: Wait, 6, wait—

37仓促地抹了一把脸，提着袍子在沙滩上奔跑起来。\
She rubs her face with her palms and pulls up her robe, running down the beach.

不合规则的凸起砂砾让她摔了一跤。但她枉顾疼痛，只是继续用尽全力追赶着。\
She stumbles over a pebble and falls, but she pushes through the pain and rises to her feet, still running as fast as she can.

**37**：请等等我，6——\
**37**: Wait, 6!

**37**：——亚齐！\
**37**: ATTICUS!

**6**：——！\
**6**: ...!

男人止住了脚步。\
The man stops.

这是一个他没有想过的名字。\
He had not expected to hear that name.

数字不是名字，数字是一个人灵魂的本质，而名字只是现象世界的短促气音。\
Numbers are the essence of one's soul, and names are but echoes of the phenomenal world.

他的数字自出生以来就已经决定，早于他获得命名之前。\
He was born into his number, long before he was given the name Atticus.

他也从未听到37用他的名字称呼他，因为她历来是最善分辨本质的。\
37 never once called him by that name, for she had always valued the essence above all else.

而现在，她站在他面前。头发因泥水而打结，膝盖流着血，狼狈不堪，但仍坚定着。\
Now here she stands, hair tangled with mud, knees bleeding, all battered and bruised. Yet, her gaze remains resolute.

**37**：……你会在闭关处为我留一扇小门吗，像我们小时候那样？\
**37**: Will you leave a door open for me in your cave, like when we were kids?

**37**：我知道至高规律紊乱了，但这并不意味着真理消失了。\
**37**: I know the transcendental Law is in disorder, but that doesn't mean the Truth is gone.

**37**：我会在紊乱中找到一条新的道路，我会算出更好的答案，我会前往现象世界一探究竟……\
**37**: I will carve a new path through the chaos, calculate better solutions than ever before, and delve into the phenomenal world to discover all it has to offer.

**37**：在那时，如果我遇到了难以解决的瓶颈，我还能像以前那样，去找你讨论问题、探究真理吗……？\
**37**: By then, if I run into problems that I can't solve, can we talk about them together, like we used to?

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

在德尔斐神庙的石柱上刻着三句箴言。\
Three maxims were carved on the pillars of the Temple of Apollo.

“认识你自己”，“凡事勿过度”，以及……\
"Know thyself," "Nothing in excess," and ...

“妄立誓则祸近”。\
"Give a pledge and trouble is at hand."

**6**：……\
**6**: ...

他能说什么呢？\
What can he say?

为众人解答疑惑，是领袖的义务。\
Alleviating doubts is a leader's duty.

**6**：——我会为你留一扇小门，37。\
**6**: Yes. A door will be left open for you, 37.

**6**：你和你的同伴都可以进来。\
**6**: Both you and your friends can come in.

**37**：——一言为定，6！\
**37**: It's a promise, 6!

她擦掉了眼中的泪花，伸手挥别自己的领袖。\
She brushes away her tears and waves to him.

这一次的离别终于不再那么残酷。\
It's still a goodbye, but it's no longer as devastating.

教众们全都离开了，沙滩上只剩下了来时的身影。\
The last of the Apeiron followers have left, leaving only the Timekeeper's team on the beach.

**维尔汀**：……芝诺的船只来接我们了。\
**Vertin**: Zeno's sent a ship to pick us up.

**维尔汀**：走吧，37，拉普拉斯的研究员们会很想见到你的。\
**Vertin**: Let's go, 37. The researchers of Laplace would love to meet you.

质数的肩膀正轻轻颤抖着。\
The girl's shoulders are trembling.

**维尔汀**：……你感到害怕吗，对那个未知的世界？\
**Vertin**: Are you nervous? Afraid of the unknown world?

**37**：……有一点。\
**37**: Maybe a little.

**37**：但我会努力习惯的！\
**37**: But I will get used to it!

她深深呼出一口气，将心中的繁杂思绪压下。\
She lets out a breath, clearing the tangle of emotions from her mind.

像平时一样露出笑容。\
A familiar smile lights up on her face.

**37**：——因为宇宙在任何地方都是齐一的，我知道。\
**37**: Because the nature of the universe flows in all things alike.

## 7TH-29 伞与结 / The Umbrella and the Knot

我们都是洞穴的囚徒，握着火光映射的一隅碎屑。但最终，人们交握双手，晃动镣铐，聋子挽着盲人，哑巴扶着瘸子，共同拼凑出了，真实世界的小小一角。\
We are prisoners within these cavern walls,Our gazes held captive by the shadows' thrall.Until our hands clasped and our chains rattled,We united to break free from our shackles. The sightless joined forces with the soundless, And the voiceless uplifted the helpless, Together, we assembled a sliver of truth, A piece of the world hidden since youth.

**小梅斯梅尔**：……\
**Mesmer Jr.**: ...

**维尔汀**：……你有什么东西要交给我吗，小梅斯梅尔？\
**Vertin**: Have you got something for me, Mesmer?

她的精神状态很差，但态度还算友好。\
Mesmer Jr. looks worn and tired, but her demeanor is still somewhat friendly.

两个黑眼圈显著地悬在小梅斯梅尔的眼睛下方，一如今天看见的科算中心所有职员。\
Dark circles are clearly visible under Mesmer Jr.'s eyes, just like every Laplace member encountered today.

**小梅斯梅尔**：是的，他们让我把这个给你。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: Yes. They asked me to give this to you.

**小梅斯梅尔**：这次研究的最后成果，所有人智慧的结晶，免疫“暴雨”的护具。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: The culmination of our research, the crystallization of man and all its wisdom—The protective gear against the "Storm."

**小梅斯梅尔**：——一把你用不上的东西。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: An umbrella, something you personally don't really need.

小梅斯梅尔语带讥讽地撑开了那把缎面纯白的伞。\
She takes a sarcastic jab as she opens the white satin umbrella.

**小梅斯梅尔**：第一代“平衡伞”，它由一个转换器、一个调和仪和一个术式核心组成。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: It's called the Equilibrium Umbrella. This is the first model, consisting of a converter, a harmonizer, and a ritual core.

**小梅斯梅尔**：转换器能够根据施术者的实际情况，架设一个在“暴雨”中进行施术的平衡场。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: The converter generates a balancing field that can cast rituals in the "Storm," taking account of the wielder's capabilities.

**小梅斯梅尔**：调和仪的图案则来自阿派朗学派的卷轴——露西女士模拟了它适配已知的162种副作用的情形，均取得了良好成果。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: The harmonizer's markings are inspired by the scroll of Apeiron. Madam Lucy tested it against 162 known side effects and found it to be highly effective.

**小梅斯梅尔**：卷轴的原件已经归还学派，这是它的简化和复制版本。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: The original scroll has been returned to the island. This is only a simplified and duplicated rendition.

**维尔汀**：……但这162种诅咒并不是全部，对吗？\
**Vertin**: The 162 curses aren't all of them, right?

**小梅斯梅尔**：是的，很可能还有未知的副作用等待发掘，所以平衡伞还在测试阶段。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: Correct. There may be other unknown side effects, so the umbrella is only a prototype in the testing phase.

**小梅斯梅尔**：最后是这个术式核心。一开始，它被命名为“37-露西结”，以纪念为此次研究做出巨大贡献的两位发现者。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: And, the ritual core. At first, it was called the "37-Lucy Knot" in honor of the two main contributors.

**小梅斯梅尔**：但两位当事人均表示了反对。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: However, both of them turned it down.

**维尔汀**：……是的，我还记得37当时的说法。\
**Vertin**: Yes. I still remember what 37 said at the time.

**维尔汀**：她更希望用这个结的数学性质去命名它，尽管这会让人们叫不出来。\
**Vertin**: She would rather name it after the mathematical properties of the knot, even if it's too much of a mouthful.

**37**：不，不！数字不是名字，我们也不需要用任何人的名义去给真理冠名！\
**37**: No, no! 37 is not a name, and the Truth should not be dressed up with anyone's name!

**37**：我只是发现了它，并不是发明了它。我不需要这种修辞手段来证明我的存在……\
**37**: I only found it. I didn't invent it. I don't need something named after me to prove my sense of existence.

**37**：……但这里不是岛上了，我知道。虚数们只是想要一个纪念。\
**37**: Hmm, but I'm not on the island anymore. I can understand that the imaginary numbers need to honor the discovery.

**37**：你们可以用其他贡献者的名字去命名它，我接受。\
**37**: You may use another contributor's name for it. I'm willing to accept that.

**小梅斯梅尔**：露西女士对术式核心的冠名也毫无兴趣，因此选择权便来到了研究的第三贡献者，阿德勒·霍夫曼先生身上。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: Madam Lucy showed no interest in the naming rights, so it was transferred to the third major contributor, Adler Hofmann.

**小梅斯梅尔**：很不巧，阿德勒研究员一开始也表明了拒绝，所以我们险些用上了日期。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: Sadly, Researcher Adler also rejected the offer, at first. We nearly ended up using the date of that day as the name.

**小梅斯梅尔**：不过在确认可以使用姓氏来冠名后，他的想法就改变了。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: But he changed his mind after confirming he could use his family name instead.

**马库斯**：……霍夫曼结？\
**Marcus**: The Hofmann Knot?

**马库斯**：你们用霍夫曼老师的姓氏命名了它？\
**Marcus**: You named it after Madam Hofmann?

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：是的，这是阿德勒·霍夫曼研究员的意愿，他希望大家能记住格蕾塔·霍夫曼调查员为此做出的牺牲。\
**Foundation Staff II**: Yes. Researcher Adler Hofmann wanted to make sure that Greta Hofmann would never be forgotten for her selfless sacrifice.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：请收好，四级调查员马库斯小姐，这是属于你的那把伞。\
**Foundation Staff II**: Level Four Investigator Marcus, please accept this umbrella. It is rightfully yours.

一把崭新的平衡伞被交到了马库斯的手上，明亮的光泽一度让她眼前一片空白。\
She receives an Equilibrium Umbrella. Its pearly sheen creates an illusion of pure whiteness in front of her.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：鉴于你做出的卓越贡献，你可以申请长期休假。\
**Foundation Staff II**: Given the incredible contributions you have made, you are welcome to apply for a well-deserved and extended vacation.

**马库斯**：……不，我要申请外出。\
**Marcus**: No. I will request for permission to go out.

**马库斯**：我的时代已经过去了，但我会带着它，去新世界，去未来看一看。\
**Marcus**: My era has gone. But with this umbrella in hand, I will venture into the new world and marvel at what's to come.

短暂地止住了话头，她的目光望向回忆的天空。\
Marcus looks up at the sky.

**马库斯**：……不知道萨赫蛋糕是否还是原来的味道呢？\
**Marcus**: Will the Sachertorte taste the same?

马库斯珍重地抱着伞，深深鞠了一躬。\
With the umbrella in her arms, she bows to the Foundation staff member.

然后，她向光明处小步跑去。\
Then she turns and walks toward the light.

**小梅斯梅尔**：最后，伞柄里注入的非对称核素R能使携带者免于暴雨症候的感染——不过这尚未得到实验。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: And lastly, the asymmetrical nuclide R in the handle of the umbrella is supposed to protect against the Storm Syndrome, but this still needs to be confirmed through testing.

**维尔汀**：没关系。\
**Vertin**: It's okay.

**维尔汀**：它正是我们最需要的东西。\
**Vertin**: This is the one thing we need the most.

**小梅斯梅尔**：……如果你对它的使用方式没有疑问，我就回康复中心了。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: If you have no further questions about its usage, I'm heading back to the rehab center.

**小梅斯梅尔**：那里还塞满了因公嘶吼、流脓、爬行的研究员们，急需一些磁疗的照料。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: The afflicted researchers there are in dire need of my magnet therapy.

**维尔汀**：……一把伞是不是太少了？\
**Vertin**: Don't you think one is not enough for my needs?

**维尔汀**：我想五把——不，十五把，也许会更合适我。\
**Vertin**: I think five, no, 15 might be more helpful.

这是个超乎意料的问题，小梅斯梅尔错愕地止住了脚步。\
An unexpected question. Mesmer Jr. stops with a surprised look on her face.

**维尔汀**：我的手提箱无法保护人类，他们需要借助平衡伞来越过“暴雨”。\
**Vertin**: My suitcase can't protect humans from the "Storm." They'll need the umbrella to survive.

**维尔汀**：在今后的行动中，也许我会遇到许多——\
**Vertin**: In the future missions, I may encounter lots of—

小梅斯梅尔的神情可称无言。\
Mesmer Jr. interrupts.

**小梅斯梅尔**：……这只是样品，司辰。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: Just a reminder, Timekeeper: this is only a prototype.

**小梅斯梅尔**：基金会大堂有“平衡伞”的领用申请表格——你要多少把伞，慢慢填写吧。\
**Mesmer Jr.**: The application forms for the umbrella are available in the Foundation lobby. Feel free to apply for as many as you need.

她快步离开了，似乎一秒也不愿多待。\
She turns and leaves, not staying for another second.

**维尔汀**：……谢谢你，小梅斯梅尔。\
**Vertin**: Thank you, Mesmer.

阳光正好。\
The amount of sunlight is just right.

撑开伞，在手中缓缓转着。\
The umbrella pops open, rotating with a touch of grace.

金色的几何线条印在白色的伞面内，洋溢着绚烂夺目的光芒。\
Against the white fabric, the golden knot gleams with brilliance.

**维尔汀**：……37没有说错。\
**Vertin**: 37 was right.

**维尔汀**：这是一个优美的证明。\
**Vertin**: It is a beautiful shape indeed.

广场已经恢复了往日的整洁。\
The Foundation Square has been restored to its former glory.

有一个人已经在这里等待了很久。\
A recognizable figure stands there, having waited for a long time.

**星锑**：嘿，维尔汀，交涉成功了吗？\
**Regulus**: Hey Vertin! Did you get it done?

**维尔汀**：很顺利。平衡伞的领取比我想象中更加便捷，只需要填写表格……\
**Vertin**: Yes, it went smoothly. I was expecting something more complicated. So to get the umbrella, you only need to fill out forms.

**星锑**：唔？那把伞是很重要，但我之前委托你的是其它事啊！\
**Regulus**: Huh? That's not what I was talking about!

**星锑**：是我们英勇的、无畏的、壮烈牺牲的、因公殉职的APPLeⅡ号！天啊，难道基金会不应该给我补偿一艘新的船吗？\
**Regulus**: I'm talking about the brave and glorious sacrifice of my APPLe II! Don't you think the Foundation should compensate me with a shiny new ship?

**维尔汀**：唔。\
**Vertin**: Oh.

**星锑**：——啊？“唔”是什么意思，维尔汀？\
**Regulus**: "Oh"? What do you mean "Oh"?

**星锑**：难道说，你忘得一干二净了吗……？\
**Regulus**: Are you saying you totally forgot about it!?

星锑愤慨地逼近，而后，一双手搭在了她的肩膀上。\
Regulus closes in, offended, putting her hands on both her shoulders.

**红弩箭**：别太心急，星锑。眼下那帮人要善后的文书工作可有一大堆，你就慢慢等着通知吧。\
**Lilya**: Easy, Regulus. Those people are likely buried in paperwork right now. Just be patient and wait.

她的手上把玩着一枚金色的勋章。\
She twirls a golden medal between her fingers.

**维尔汀**：红弩箭，你从表彰仪式上回来了吗？\
**Vertin**: Lilya. How was your commendation ceremony?

**红弩箭**：是啊，他们非得把这个给我，为了表彰我在“暴雨”中护送重要文件的卓越贡献。\
**Lilya**: Heh. They rewarded me for escorting the important item during the "Storm."

**红弩箭**：——请问，送卷轴算什么功勋？倒是有人切实该为我没有选择冲进委员会大楼而感谢我……\
**Lilya**: How is delivering a scroll worthy of a reward? I'll say someone should be grateful I didn't crash into the committee building.

红弩箭随手一扔，把勋章给了星锑。\
She tosses the medal to Regulus.

**红弩箭**：拿去吧，没准能成为炼金术的原料。\
**Lilya**: Take it. Might be useful for your alchemy.

**星锑**：噢，我看看——\
**Regulus**: Oh! Let me see.

星锑把勋章放到嘴边，不假思索地咬了一口。\
Regulus brings the medal to her mouth and takes a small bite.

**星锑**：多谢了，朋友，这好像是真的金子！\
**Regulus**: Thanks mate! It's made of pure gold!

**星锑**：海盗公国也会感谢你为炼金术事业做出的卓越贡献！\
**Regulus**: On behalf of the pirate community, I thank you for your remarkable contribution to alchemy!

**槲寄生**：我这里也有一枚。\
**Druvis III**: I have one, too.

槲寄生走来，将另一枚勋章放在了星锑的手里。\
Druvis III walks over and places another medal in Regulus's hand.

她和红弩箭一起参加了那场关于护送卷轴的表彰仪式。\
Like Lilya, she was rewarded for helping to deliver the scroll.

**槲寄生**：很遗憾我没有帮上太多忙，司辰。\
**Druvis III**: Please forgive my lack of contribution, Timekeeper.

久别重逢的故人摇了摇头，她因此前抗议活动的那片森林而错过了全部的海岛冒险。\
She missed the island trip because of the forest they planted in the Foundation Square.

好在，如今的广场已恢复如新。\
Fortunately, the square has been restored to its original condition.

**槲寄生**：不过，那些被唤醒的林木终于重获静谧，于我们而言，或许也是一份好消息。\
**Druvis III**: It seems the awakened woods have embraced tranquility once more. Perhaps a sign of good things to come.

**维尔汀**：我也很高兴看到你恢复了状态，槲寄生小姐。\
**Vertin**: I'm glad to see you back on your feet, Ms. Druvis.

**维尔汀**：实际上，我也正想为你介绍一处海角——那儿曾经草木丰茂，经逢“暴雨”与战争后，正需要一位品味良好的德鲁伊。\
**Vertin**: In fact, there's a place I'd like to introduce you to, a flourishing island that survived both war and the "Storm." I think a talented druid like you would be of great help to them.

**槲寄生**：嗯，听起来是个值得期待的地方。\
**Druvis III**: Sounds like a place to look forward to.

这场重逢被摇滚海盗的高呼打断了。\
The reunion is cut short by the pirate's cheering.

**星锑**：天啊，槲寄生，你真是棒呆了！虽然这块勋章小了一点，但它的金属更稀有——\
**Regulus**: Nice job, Druvis! It's not as big as Lilya's, but it is made of a rare kind of metal!

**APPLe**：这是个很好的方向，船长。APPLe某认为，只要再来三百块勋章，我们就能凑齐一艘船了。\
**APPLe**: This is a good start, Captain. This APPLe thinks we only need 300 more medals to afford a new ship.

**星锑**：正是这样，大副先生！不知道芝诺那边的作战表彰仪式什么时候召开？\
**Regulus**: You read my mind, Mr. Chief Mate! When will Zeno's ceremony be held?

**星锑**：虽然，本船长之前是不会接受这种官方授勋的……但是，咳……他们可以直接把勋章寄给我吗？\
**Regulus**: This Captain is not a fan of these ceremonies, so, um, could they just mail me my medal?

摇滚海盗欲盖弥彰地咳嗽了两声，墨镜后的眼神望向了别处。\
The rockin' pirate coughs awkwardly, her eyes darting away behind the cover of her shades.

**苏芙比**：——嗯？苏芙比错过了什么？\
**Sotheby**: Hmm? Did I miss something?

**苏芙比**：这是一个交换勋章的派对吗？\
**Sotheby**: Are we holding a medal-exchanging party?

**星锑**：苏芙比！\
**Regulus**: Sotheby!

星锑望着久别重逢的小淑女，热泪几乎在眼眶里打转。\
Regulus rejoices at the sight of the little lady, tears welling up in her eyes.

几乎本能地，她伸出手去，而苏芙比也正确理解了她的意思。\
She stretches out a hand, and Sotheby immediately gets the message.

**苏芙比**：苏芙比没有勋章……但我有这个，大的、圆的、金色的……\
**Sotheby**: But I don't have a medal. All I have is this big, round, golden ...

一串沉甸甸的珠宝放在了星锑手中。\
A handful of weighty jewelry is placed in Regulus's hands.

**APPLe**：船长，APPLe某认为我们已经攒够一艘船了。\
**APPLe**: Captain, I think we can buy a new ship with this.

无需提醒，星锑已经感激涕零地抱住了对方。\
Regulus wraps her in a ginormous bear hug, moved to tears.

这位有史以来最为慷慨的富家小姐、海盗公国的再造恩人、天才炼金术师的御用赞助人、行走的金库——苏芙比小姐。\
Praise Sotheby—the most charitable woman in history, the revitalizer of the pirate community, the prime sponsor of the ingenious alchemist, and the bank vault on legs.

**十四行诗**：星锑……星锑！\
**Sonetto**: Regulus, Regulus!

十四行诗气喘吁吁地跑了过来，手里扬着一叠盖着章的文件。\
Sonetto runs over panting, waving a stack of stamped papers in her hand.

**十四行诗**：司辰委托我将你的请求递交了上去，他们批准了！\
**Sonetto**: The Timekeeper asked me to request a new ship for you, and we have the approval!

**十四行诗**：APPLeⅡ将获得重建，基金会将支付它的日常保养费用——嗯？\
**Sonetto**: The Foundation will rebuild APPLe II and pay for its maintenance—hmm?

**维尔汀**：你来得正好，十四行诗。\
**Vertin**: Funny you say that, Sonetto.

树影在阳光下闪着细碎的光。\
The trees sway in the breeze and the sunlight streams through the leaves.

一个正适合前往新世界的好天气。\
It is a fine weather to set sail again.

**维尔汀**：——现在我们有两艘新船了。\
**Vertin**: Now we have two new ships.

## 7TH-30 谢幕词 / And Now, the Curtain Call

年轻的朋友们正欲扬帆起航。\
The youth are sailing for a new world.

而年长些的人们正在挥别过去。\
While the old are saying goodbye to the world they knew.

**露西**：嗯，我想这十五个插头已经涵盖了目的地一切可能的电源形制。\
**Lucy**: Fifteen plugs. This should be enough to cover all socket types at our destination.

**露西**：希曼，请把之前的实验记录也递给我。\
**Lucy**: Simone, pass me the experiment log, please.

拂去桌面上的灰尘，最后一次清点实验室内的设备。\
She brushes the dust off the desk and takes a final inventory of the lab's equipment.

房间内没有开灯，已经不再有这个必要了。\
She leaves the lights off, not needing them any longer.

门口传来了一阵急促的敲门声。\
An urgent knock sounds from the door.

**露西**：请——\
**Lucy**: Come—

她没能走完符合人类社会礼仪的流程，因为来人已经急切地推开了门。\
Before she finishes her protocol for human social customs, the door barges open.

**哑谜**：这是真的吗，露西女士？！您要离开拉普拉斯科算中心——？\
**Enigma**: Madam Lucy, is it true? Are you leaving Laplace?

**露西**：是的，问询会已经结束了。\
**Lucy**: Yes. The inquiry is over.

**露西**：这是所有人商议的结果。\
**Lucy**: This is the decision of all parties involved.

**哑谜**：他们在开什么国际玩笑！？\
**Enigma**: You have got to be kidding me!

哑谜重重地拍了一下桌子，实验遗留的灰尘从上面震了下来。\
Enigma pounds the table, sending the dust from the experiments into the air.

**哑谜**：您做出了如此卓越的贡献，他们——却要停您的职？！\
**Enigma**: After all the incredible contributions you've made, they're suspending you?!

**哑谜**：没有比这更荒谬的事了！没有您，我们根本不可能做出平衡伞，光副作用就会杀死每一个人！\
**Enigma**: This is absolutely ridiculous! Without you, there would be no umbrella, and everyone would've died from the side effects!

**露西**：噢，实际上还是有不少人因此牺牲。因为我低估了咒文的危害，造成了不可控的传播事故。\
**Lucy**: Hm, but many did perish because of me. I had underestimated the danger of the ritual, and it ended up spreading uncontrollably.

**露西**：你之前不是也为此深切抗议吗，阿德勒·霍夫曼研究员？\
**Lucy**: Did you not once have the same opinion, Researcher Adler Hofmann?

**哑谜**：那是……\
**Enigma**: I ...

机器友好地朝他点了点头。\
The robot gives him a friendly nod.

**露西**：很意外，你态度转变得如此之快。\
**Lucy**: It is surprising to see you change your mind so quickly.

**露西**：不过这正是我们需要的精神——理性的自我革新精神。\
**Lucy**: But that is just what Laplace needs: the spirit of rationality and self-evolution.

文件被有序归档。\
The documents have been filed away.

助理希曼走到露西女士旁边，接过了她手里沉重的实验仪器。\
Simone walks up to Lucy and takes the heavy experimental apparatus from her hands.

扬起的灰尘让哑谜咳嗽了几声。\
As the dust rises from their movements, Enigma lets out a cough.

**露西**：实际上，这次决策是合理的。他们必须照顾总部来自各阶层种族背景的工作人员。\
**Lucy**: I can imagine how they came to this decision. They must have considered the backgrounds of all the employees, including their social status and race.

**露西**：我们花了八年，才在雨幕中撑开第一把伞。但即使是这样的速度，对一些人而言也太快了。\
**Lucy**: After eight years, we finally created an umbrella to withstand the "Storm." However, our methods for achieving such progress and breakthroughs were too much for some to handle.

**露西**：人们的情绪需要一个出口，需要有人为这些事故和牺牲负责。\
**Lucy**: People needed an outlet for their frustrations, so someone had to be held responsible for the accidents and casualties.

**露西**：已经有许多研究员寄来投诉信，指责我冷酷、无人性、无感情、践踏生命、反人道主义。\
**Lucy**: Numerous complaints have been filed against me, accusing me of being a cold, heartless opponent of humanity.

**露西**：在基金会、芝诺和这里，也有许多人质疑能否让一个觉醒的蒸汽活塞就任科算中心的负责人。\
**Lucy**: Within the Foundation, Zeno, and even here, some are starting to question the idea of having an Awakened piston as the leader of Laplace.

**露西**：他们对我的神秘学能力是否在可控范围存有不同意见，并怀疑我正因能力失控而逐渐失去理性的决策能力。\
**Lucy**: They argued about my arcane abilities, unsure if I had them under control or if they were becoming unstable and affecting my ability to make rational decisions.

机器顿了顿，像是突然想起了一处疏漏。\
The robot realizes an overlooked detail.

**露西**：嗯，毕竟我违反保密协定在维也纳传播了扭结。\
**Lucy**: Hm. I did give the knot to Ms. Kakania in violation of the confidentiality agreement.

**露西**：不过，的确有人因此活下来。——这就够了。\
**Lucy**: But ultimately, it helped people survive, and that is all that matters.

人类研究员没有关注到这一补充。\
But Enigma does not pick up on this realization.

他已经出于愤怒地握紧了拳头。\
He's already enraged, fists clenched in a ball.

**哑谜**：所以，他们……质疑您的立场？就因为您是意识唤醒者，是神秘学家？\
**Enigma**: So they're questioning your standing because you're an Awakened, an arcanist?

**哑谜**：质疑一台比任何人都信奉科技和进步的机器，不够“理性”？\
**Enigma**: They're doubting the rationality of a machine that values technology and progress above all else?

**哑谜**：这真是我有生以来听过最可笑的事——在我自己都放弃的时候，是您提出来必须考虑人类！！！\
**Enigma**: Could anything be more absurd? Even I, a human, was on the verge of giving up! It was you who convinced me to save our species!

**露西**：——我疑惑的是，你为什么这么激动呢？\
**Lucy**: My question is, why are you so upset?

**露西**：这无关你的处境，你还得到了一个升职的机会。\
科算中心会成立一个专门的部门，你和乌尔里希应该都接到了负责人的邀请。\
**Lucy**: This does not affect you. In fact, you may be promoted. Laplace is setting up a new department, and you and Ulrich should have been invited to head it.

**哑谜**：因为这**的该死的不公平！\
**Enigma**: Because this is damn unjust!

**哑谜**：他们从来没有和你共事过一天，甚至不曾听过你的一句发言。他们享用你的成果，却蔑视你的存在——\
**Enigma**: These people don't know you. They haven't worked with you or even listened to you, yet they happily reap the fruits of your labor while showing you no respect.

**哑谜**：你会接到处分的唯一原因，就是因为你们——意识唤醒者，不像其他人一样只能牺牲一次！不然他们就该在墓碑前授予你一块勋章了！\
**Enigma**: The only reason you're getting suspended is because you, an Awakened, can't really die! Or they'd be honoring you with a medal on your grave right now!

**露西**：喔，那你就应该接受那个职位。\
**Lucy**: Hmm. Maybe you should take up that offer.

**露西**：——这对你来说是公平的。\
**Lucy**: At least you will get a promotion as a just reward.

哑谜的所有话都卡在了嗓子眼里。\
Enigma opens his mouth, but no sound comes out.

他张开嘴，想要反驳这天大的羞辱。但愤怒熔断了他的大脑回路，竟让他半天没想出讥讽的话。\
He wants to tell her she's wrong about him wanting the promotion, but he's too flustered and angry to speak.

机器的条屏闪了闪，继续它无情的理性陈词。\
The robotic eye slit pulses, and she continues in her unemotional tone.

**露西**：另外，乌尔里希的确得到了勋章。不过和你一样——它也不太高兴。\
**Lucy**: By the way, Ulrich ended up receiving a medal, but like you, he was not exactly thrilled either.

**露西**：此刻它正在委员会大楼前绝食抗议，但鉴于所有人都知道了意识唤醒者的生命有多顽强，它的抗议收效甚微。\
**Lucy**: He is outside the committee building, refusing to eat in protest. But everyone knows how resilient the Awakened can be. It is going poorly.

露西摇了摇头，似乎在为下属的情绪化行为深表遗憾。\
She shakes and sighs, deeply remorseful for her subordinate's behavior.

**露西**：在我看来，你和乌尔里希中应该有一个去接受这个职位，你们是最熟悉这项研究的人。\
**Lucy**: I will suggest that one of you take this position. No one knows this research better than the two of you.

**哑谜**：我不会去的！\
**Enigma**: Not a chance!

**露西**：这既是为了保障研究的进展，更是为了确保它不被滥用。\
**Lucy**: The research must progress, and you also need to ensure that the results will not be abused.

中肯的劝诫。\
A valid concern.

**哑谜**：该死，你是对的……\
**Enigma**: S**t! You're right.

哑谜陷入了沉默，显然，他的大脑正在原则和责任间做着疯狂的斗争。\
Enigma is caught in a fierce battle between his principles and his duty.

机器没有注意到这些不重要的细节。\
But the robot doesn't notice these unimportant details.

她不以为意地走到了实验椅前，开始进行最后的电量检查。\
She nonchalantly walks over to the chair and runs a final battery check.

**露西**：我并不介意这一处分，霍夫曼研究员。我从不奢求权力，那是你们生物的概念。\
**Lucy**: The punishment does not bother me, Researcher Hofmann. Power exists only in your dictionary, not mine.

**露西**：从我意识觉醒的那一刻起，我便不理解你们。时至今日，仍然如此。\
**Lucy**: From the moment of my awakening, I have been unable to comprehend you creatures. And even now, that remains unchanged.

冷静的陈述，并未掺杂任何情绪。\
She states, with no emotion added to embellish her delivery.

研究员有些惊愕地张开了嘴，但机器只是普通地叙说着。\
Enigma's mouth falls open in shock. Meanwhile, the robot just keeps on talking.

**露西**：我们运转的方式并不相同，内驱的燃料也相去甚远。好在，我们有一个共同的方向。\
**Lucy**: We operate in different ways, just like how our fuels differ. But the bright side is, our paths align.

**露西**：不论是生物还是机器，人类还是神秘学家，多数的有形之物总是希冀着更好的生活。这股原初的热情，正是所谓的“进步”。\
**Lucy**: Whether we are creatures or machines, humans or arcanists, most of us strive for a better life. It is this primal desire that drives "progress."

**露西**：因此我装上类人的身躯，佩戴上仿制的面孔，不断调整发声的语调和质感，为了便于与你们交流。\
**Lucy**: That is why I put on the mask of a human and work on improving my appearance and speech, all for the sake of better communication with you.

**露西**：我的努力不总是有效的，人们经常告诉我，“表面的一致只是彰显了本质的不同。”\
**Lucy**: Unfortunately, my efforts do not always pay off. Some say that the more human-like I appear, the more different I seem.

机器遗憾地摇了摇头。\
She shakes her head with regret.

**露西**：——但我依然如此，因为我并不在乎得到认同。\
**Lucy**: But I am who I am, and my motivation is not to gain recognition from others.

**露西**：我们的相交点只是在于进步，从来如此。\
**Lucy**: Our aligned path leads us to "progress," and that is all there is to it.

**露西**：在平衡伞发明后，科算中心中断八年的研究也将踏上正轨。倘若他们有更合适的舵手，我很乐意在这座轰鸣的引擎里当一个小小的活塞。\
**Lucy**: Thanks to the invention of the umbrella, Laplace can now resume its research unhindered. And if there is someone better qualified to lead, I am more than willing to remain a humble cog in their machine.

**露西**：而且，Z女士为我介绍了一个很好的疗养处。那里有一处弥漫着神秘学气息的湖景庭院，正适合我这样的意识唤醒者去休假散心。\
**Lucy**: Besides, Ms. Z introduced me to a beautiful resort. The lake there is rich with arcane power, perfect for an Awakened arcanist like me.

**露西**：它编制灵活，预算独立，唯一需要担忧的是电力供应是否充足。\
**Lucy**: Not only is it a resort, but also an independent team with a good amount of freedom. My only concern is if they have adequate power supply.

**露西**：噢，还有生锈。也许出发前我应当找X研究员借用他最近研发的“超级钛合金除锈机”……\
**Lucy**: Oh, rust might be a problem. Perhaps I should ask Researcher X about his "Titanium Derust Machine."

**哑谜**：……\
**Enigma**: ...

机器兴致盎然地陷入了休假生活的畅想。\
The robot is happily thinking about her vacation plans.

她已经完成了离开的所有准备。\
She has completed all preparations for departure.

**露西**：出发吧，希曼。\
**Lucy**: Time to go, Simone.

**哑谜**：……稍等，露西女士，请您最后过目一下这个。\
**Enigma**: Madam Lucy. Please take a look at this before you go.

一叠装订整齐的报告被递交到了露西面前。\
A stack of reports is handed in front of her.

**哑谜**：这是您在“暴雨”倒计时期间整理的126种副作用与调和卷轴的拟合情况，关于第34类副作用的数据部分，我有一些疑惑。\
**Enigma**: This is the report you compiled during the "Storm" countdown, detailing 126 side effects and how the scroll alleviates them. I have some questions about the data for Type 34.

露西接过了那个出于自己之手的列表，最后尽职地浏览了一遍。\
Lucy flips it open and dutifully goes through the list one last time.

**露西**：嗯，这里的确有一些疏漏。\
**Lucy**: Yes. I can see a few errors in here.

**露西**：但很抱歉，我必须在今天办完交接手续。我想你之后可以请教乌尔里希先生这个问题……\
**Lucy**: Unfortunately, I have to complete all of the handover procedures today. Perhaps you can ask Mr. Ulrich about it later.

她将报告还给了研究员，对方却半天没有接下。\
She hands it back to Enigma, but he does not reach for it.

纸张对面，研究员摇了摇头，声音低沉而悲伤。\
He looks at her, grief-stricken.

**哑谜**：实验还是留下了副作用，是吗？\
**Enigma**: The side effects left a mark on you, didn't they?

**哑谜**：您登记的副作用一共是162种，不是126种。第34类副作用的数据是一个非常明显的抄写失误，我们早就发现并修正了它，用时不过5秒。\
**Enigma**: There are 162 side effects, not 126. There was also an obvious typo in the data for Type 34. We noticed it long ago and corrected it, took only 5 seconds.

**哑谜**：这是您用生命写下的列表，您却没有第一时间看懂。\
**Enigma**: You sacrificed so much for this report, yet you could not see such glaring mistakes.

**哑谜**：您称呼我为霍夫曼研究员——这仅仅发生在八年前您刚接管科算中心时。之后，为了和我姐姐区别开，同僚们都称呼我为阿德勒。\
**Enigma**: You called me Researcher Hofmann earlier—a name you haven't used since you took over Laplace eight years ago. To avoid confusion with my sister, you and our colleagues started calling me Adler instead.

他往前走一步，阴沉地提出了自己的设想。\
Moving closer, he asks grimly.

**哑谜**：您……丢失了多少数据？甚至损伤到了您的科研能力……？\
**Enigma**: How much data did you lose to impair your research abilities like this?

**哑谜**：这才是您必须离开的真正原因吗？\
**Enigma**: Is this why you have to leave Laplace now?

**哑谜**：您推动了所有人的进步，代价却是您自己的退步——！\
**Enigma**: The progress you've made has helped so many, but at what cost to your own well-being!

机器没有回答，她罕见地沉默。\
The robot does not answer, a rare occurrence.

助理希曼上前一步，取走了哑谜迟迟没有接下的那份报告。\
From her side, Simone gently takes the file for her.

**助理希曼**：出发的时间到了，露西女士。\
**Assistant Simone**: We should go, Madam Lucy.

**露西**：嗯。再见，阿德勒研究员。\
**Lucy**: Hm. Goodbye, Researcher Adler.

**露西**：谢谢你纠正我的数据错误。\
**Lucy**: Thank you for correcting my mistake.

她迈着钢铁的脚步离开了，不再回顾遗留的种种。

露西的脚步声，然后过渡到哑谜追上去的跑步声。\
She walks away with steely steps, not looking back.

拉普拉斯科算中心-走廊

**哑谜**：——好吧，好吧！\
**Enigma**: Alright, fine!

研究员扒住门框，枉顾其他人异样的眼光，朝那道背影大喊道。\
He grips the doorframe, ignoring the strange looks from the hallway.

**哑谜**：我会去接受那个职务！我会去做你希望我做的事！我会去和那些我厌烦的委员们打交道——\
**Enigma**: I'll take up that role and do what you've been nagging me to do. I'll take care of those pesky committees.

**哑谜**：但不是为了楼宇顶层的那些俯瞰我们的大人物们——！\
**Enigma**: But just so you know, I'm not doing this for the higher-ups who look down on us,

**哑谜**：——而是为了那些在外面仰慕这座大厦的人！\
**Enigma**: but for the people who look up to us from below!

**露西**：……\
**Lucy**: ...

机器的脚步没有为此停滞。\
The footsteps continue in rhythm.

她在此的职务已经结束了。\
Her duty here is done.

然后，她听到了另一声呼喊。\
Then, another voice calls out.

**破译组长**：——露西女士！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Madam Lucy!

**露西**：……嗯？\
**Lucy**: Hm?

圆形的走廊上站满了人。\
The corridors are bustling with people.

研究员们、文员们、实验室负责人们、警卫们。\
Researchers, clerks, directors, and security ...

科算中心的每个岗位的职员都站到了走廊上，从第一层到最高层。\
Every Laplace employee is in the corridors, from bottom to top floor.

然后，有人发出了第一声高呼。\
The same voice shouts.

**破译组长**：向露西女士——\
**Cryptography Lead**: All attention!

**破译组长**：致敬！\
**Cryptography Lead**: Salute!

纸片纷纷扬扬。\
Papers litter the air like snowflakes.

人们发出不同语言的告别声，整齐划一将怀里的文件一扔而下。\
Everyone says goodbye in their own language, tossing files over the railings.

那是在过去二十四小时内产生的无数演算纸、设计图、审批文件、行政文书。\
The countless drafts, designs, and forms from the past 24 hours rain down.

它们因“暴雨”研究而诞生，也在这之后完成了自己的使命。\
They were created for the "Storm," and have completed their mission.

——一如这台机器。\
Just as did the robot.

**露西**：为什么人们朝我投掷这些文件，希曼？他们是在表示驱逐吗？\
**Lucy**: Simone, why are they throwing papers at me? Are they rejecting me and banishing me?

**助理希曼**：……不，我想他们是在表达尊敬。\
**Assistant Simone**: On the contrary, madam, they are showing their reverence.

**露西**：噢，是这样吗？\
**Lucy**: Oh, I see.

机器今日并未装配业务交流时所需的表情系统，因此她只是转过身去。\
The robot is without a face and emotion module today, so she turns away from the crowd.

阳光照在她金属的棱角上，折射出一片晃眼的金光。\
The sunlight dances on her metallic surface, enveloping her in a golden aura.

**露西**：走吧，希曼。\
**Lucy**: Let us go, Simone.

**露西**：我想念拉普拉斯的充电桩了。\
**Lucy**: I miss the Laplace chargers already.

**露西**：——Z女士引荐的地方，应该也会有230伏特的充电口吧？\
**Lucy**: There is a 230-volt bath at the resort, right?
